# hep-th [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Covariant Holographic Entanglement Entropy Inversion to Reconstruct Bulk Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16459)
*Ji-Seong Chae*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了协变全息纠缠熵（covariant holographic entanglement entropy）在超越标准单函数径向反问题情形下的解析逆变换方法，通过HRT（Hubeny–Rangamani–Takayanagi）族重构稳态径向块，并揭示了交叉叶一致性作为协变问题可积性的隐藏条件。基于对不同熵函数S(Δt,Δx)的末端导数给出的守恒荷E和J以及其特征比κ，建立了Abel反演重构框架，并通过多个时空示例加以验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准的全息纠缠熵反问题局限于等时间径向单函数情形，无法处理协变框架下包含非平凡空间扭曲因子（warp factor）和参考系拖曳（frame dragging）的径向块重构。本文旨在发展一种解析逆变换方法，从HRT（Hubeny–Rangamani–Takayanagi）熵函数中重构稳态径向块结构。

Method: 该方法基于HRT族的区间熵S(Δt,Δx)作为在壳Hamilton–Jacobi泛函的识别：通过对区间端点的导数获得守恒HRT荷E和角动量J，并以比值κ=E/J标记特征叶（characteristic leaf）。对于每个固定的κ，熵定义了径向块的Abel（Abel）重构。通过要求不同κ下得到的候选径向块作为同一径向坐标的函数相一致，建立交叉叶一致性条件，该条件构成协变问题的可积性（integrability）条件。

Result: 当交叉叶一致性成立时，相同数据可确定投影体光锥（projected bulk light cone），从而从纠缠信息中提取参考系拖曳轮廓、光锥开角、视界生成元和能层表面（ergosurface）。当一致性条件不成立时，全息纠缠熵无法在假定的径向HRT约化框架下解释，而需要额外的输入信息。文章通过纯AdS、旋转BTZ、静态翘曲度量、boosted Einstein–标量黑膜、高维条带简并（strip degeneracy）和薄壳阻碍（thin-shell obstruction）等多个示例进行了验证。

Conclusion: 交叉叶一致性是协变全息纠缠熵径向反问题中隐藏的可积性条件。一致性不成立并不意味着全息对偶的失效，而是表明需要更完整的输入信息（如分支分辨、横向密度分离、额外区域数据或真正的时间依赖信息）来完成径向重构。该工作将全息纠缠熵的反问题从等时间情形推广到了包含时空协变效应的更一般框架。

Abstract: We present an analytic inversion of covariant holographic entanglement entropy beyond the usual one-function equal-time radial inverse problem, in which one effective radial coefficient remains after the radial gauge and transverse density are fixed. The formula reconstructs the stationary radial block seen by the HRT family, including a nontrivial spatial warp factor and the shift responsible for frame dragging. On a smooth HRT branch, the interval entropy \(S(Δt,Δx)\) is an on-shell Hamilton--Jacobi functional: its endpoint derivatives give conserved HRT charges \(E\) and \(J\), and the ratio \(κ=E/J\) labels characteristic leaves. For each fixed \(κ\), the entropy defines an Abel reconstruction of a candidate radial block. A single classical radial geometry exists only when the candidates obtained at different \(κ\)'s agree as functions of the same radial coordinate. This cross-leaf agreement is the hidden integrability condition of the covariant problem. When it holds, the same data determine the projected bulk light cone, making the frame-dragging profile, cone opening, horizon generator, and ergosurface visible from entanglement. Failure of the condition is not a failure of holography; it means that the HEE cannot be interpreted within the assumed radial HRT reduction without further input, such as branch resolution, transverse-density separation, additional region data, or genuinely time-dependent information. We illustrate the construction with pure AdS, rotating BTZ, a static warped metric, a boosted Einstein--scalar black brane, a higher-dimensional strip degeneracy, and a thin-shell obstruction. The analysis uses the classical HRT area term.

</details>


### [2] [When Symmetries Twist: Anomaly Inflow on Monodromy Defects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16482)
*Christian Copetti*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了在能隙型SPT相（symmetry-protected topological phases）和无能隙反常对称性理论中的单值性缺陷（monodromy defects），指出其作为拓扑对称性算符的动态终止，由局域背景磁通激发，并受到反常性的影响，只能在对称性生成元与反常诱导的拓扑序之间的畴壁上定义。该拓扑修饰导致了受保护的手征边缘模和绝热泵浦等物理后果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解单值性缺陷在具有反常对称性的系统（包括能隙型SPT相和无能隙理论）中的定义方式和物理性质，特别是背景磁通作为反常源（anomaly source）对缺陷结构的约束作用。

Method: 采用inflow方法（inflow approach）分析反常对称性对单值性缺陷的影响，并在连续模型和格点（lattice）模型中对反常手征对称性（anomalous chiral symmetries）下的单值性缺陷进行具体验证。

Result: 单值性缺陷只能被定义为对称性生成元与反常诱导的拓扑序（topological order）之间的畴壁（domain wall）；缺陷的世界体积（worldvolume）上存在受保护的手征边缘模（chiral edge modes），并伴随局域磁通束缚的无能隙自由度的绝热泵浦（adiabatic pumping）。

Conclusion: 单值性缺陷的拓扑修饰是理解反常对称性下缺陷物理的关键，其在连续和格点模型中的可验证性表明该框架具有普适性。

Abstract: Monodromy defects describe a dynamical termination of topological symmetry operators, and are sourced by a localized background magnetic flux. We study their properties in gapped SPT phases and, by inflow, in gapless theories with an anomalous symmetry. The background flux acts as a source for the anomaly, impacting the definition of the monodromy defect, which can only be defined as a domain wall between the symmetry generator and a topological order induced by the anomaly. The topological dressing has several consequences, such as the presence of protected chiral edge modes on the defect's worldvolume, and the adiabatic pumping of gapless degrees of freedom bound to the localized flux. We verify our predictions in several examples, focusing on monodromy defects for anomalous chiral symmetries, both in the continuum and on the lattice.

</details>


### [3] [Isolated Critical Points for Scherk-Schwarz Compactifications of M-theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16484)
*Zihni Kaan Baykara,Shi Chen,Cumrun Vafa*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了M理论在Scherk-Schwarz紧化（具有非平凡自旋结构的环面紧化）下的模空间势能，发现了孤立的临界点，并推广了扰动弦论中面向离散对称性的反常消除条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在M理论的Scherk-Schwarz紧化中，系统性地寻找模空间势能的孤立临界点，并建立紧化过程中关于离散对称性的反常消除条件。

Method: 通过识别未破缺的对偶群（unbroken duality group），并寻找模空间中被该群元素固定的孤立点，来证明势能孤立临界点的存在。对于反常消除条件，采用对偶协变（duality covariant）的形式，将其推广到Tⁿ被离散ℤ_N对称性（以相位作用于荷格）轨形化（orbifolded）的情形。

Result: 在d=8,6,5,4维时空维度下，具体构造了Scherk-Schwarz紧化的孤立临界点实例。提出了一个对偶协变的M理论反常消除条件，该条件推广了扰动弦轨形中的层次匹配（level matching）要求。

Conclusion: M理论的Scherk-Schwarz紧化在低维模空间上存在势能的孤立临界点，且其反常消除条件可通过对偶协变形式统一描述，为理解非微扰弦紧化提供了重要约束。

Abstract: We consider Scherk-Schwarz compactifications of M-theory (toroidal compactifications with a non-trivial spin structure) in various dimensions and find isolated critical points of the potential on the moduli space. We demonstrate this by identifying the unbroken duality group and finding isolated points on the moduli spaces which are fixed by elements of the unbroken duality group. We work out concrete examples involving compactifications down to $d=8,6, 5$ and $4$ spacetime dimensions. We also conjecture a duality covariant anomaly cancellation condition for M-theory on $T^n$ orbifolded by discrete $\mathbb Z_N$ symmetries acting as phases on the charge lattice. This anomaly cancellation condition generalizes the level matching requirement for perturbative string orbifolds.

</details>


### [4] [5d Trinions and Tetraons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16497)
*Mario De Marco,Michele Del Zotto,Michele Graffeo,Andrea Sangiovanni*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用M理论几何工程（M-theory geometric engineering）将5d SCFT的原子分类方案从双基本（bifundamental）共形物质推广到三叉与四叉结构，构建了具有D型味对称性的非线性广义箭图（non-linear generalized quivers），并排除了E型三叉与四叉结构的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在已有的5d SCFT原子分类方案中，双基本共形物质（bifundamental conformal matter）通过融合可生成线性广义箭图；然而，更丰富、非线性的广义箭图结构尚未被系统构造与分类，这限制了人们对5d超共形场论（5d SCFT）全貌的理解。

Method: 采用M理论几何工程方法，通过构造三叉（trinion）和四叉（tetraon）5d SCFT实现对非线性广义箭图的几何实现，并分析其瞬时子对称性增强（instanton symmetry enhancement）模式。

Result: 成功构建了具有D型味对称性（flavor symmetry of type D）的三叉和四叉5d SCFT，它们对应非线性广义箭图并展现出新颖的瞬时子对称性增强模式。这些结构的融合会产生奇异几何，通常为非环非完全交（non-toric non-complete intersections）。此外，在该框架下排除了E型三叉和四叉结构的存在。

Conclusion: 研究将5d SCFT的原子构造从双基本线性结构推广至三叉与四叉非线性结构，补充了D型味对称性下的分类图景，并明确了E型情形的不可行性，从而拓展了5d SCFT分类学的边界。

Abstract: Recently, an atomic classification scheme of 5d SCFTs has been proposed, relying on the identification of indecomposable building blocks that can be fused together to produce large classes of 5d SCFTs. These novel SCFTs are known as bifundamental 5d conformal matter theories, and their fusion produces linear generalized quivers. We generalize such picture employing M-theory geometric engineering to construct trinions and tetraon 5d SCFTs with flavor symmetry of type D. They correspond to non-linear generalized quivers displaying novel patterns of instantonic symmetry enhancement, and their fusion produces singular geometries that often are non-toric non-complete intersections. Finally, within our setup, we rule out trinions and tetraons of type E.

</details>


### [5] [Interpolating conformal algebra in $(1+1)$ dimensions between the instant form and the light-front form of relativistic dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2601.19251)
*Chueng-Ryong Ji,Hariprashad Ravikumar*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文构建了(1+1)维时空下瞬时形式动力学(IFD)与光前动力学(LFD)之间的插值共形代数，以及对应的4×4插值投影时空矩阵表示。研究发现，在LFD中运动学生成元与动力学生成元的数量发生戏剧性变化，分别最大化为四个和最小化为两个，相较于IFD及其他插值形式中的两个运动学与四个动力学生成元。这一结果证实了LFD在求解(1+1)维量子场论时能显著节省动力学计算量。此外，还给出了(1+0)和(0+1)维共形群的2×2泡利矩阵表示，以及(1+0)维共形群的量子简谐振子产生/湮灭算符表示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解不同动力学形式（瞬时形式与光前形式）下共形代数的生成元结构差异，旨在揭示LFD在简化(1+1)维量子场论求解中的优势。

Method: 构建了(1+1)维插值共形代数，并给出了4×4插值投影时空矩阵表示；同时采用2×2泡利矩阵与简谐振子产生/湮灭算符分别表示低维共形群。

Result: LFD将运动学生成元最大化至四个、动力学生成元最小化至两个，而IFD及其他插值形式则对应两个运动学与四个动力学生成元。

Conclusion: LFD的生成元结构特征显著节省了求解(1+1)维量子场论的动力学计算量，验证了其在低维场论研究中的实用价值。

Abstract: We present the interpolating conformal algebra between the instant form dynamics (IFD) and the light-front dynamics (LFD) in $(1+1)$ dimensions, along with a $4\times4$ interpolating projective spacetime matrix representation. While there are six generators in the $(1+1)$ dimensional conformal algebra, the number of kinematic and dynamic generators dramatically changes in LFD, maximizing (minimizing) the number of kinematic (dynamic) generators to four (two) with respect to two (four) kinematic (dynamic) generators in IFD, as well as in any other forms of dynamics between IFD and LFD. It confirms and signifies the utility of LFD, saving substantial dynamical efforts in solving the $(1+1)$ dimensional quantum field theories. We also present $2\times2$ Pauli matrix representation of $(1+0)$ and $(0+1)$ conformal groups, and creation/annihilation operators of quantum simple harmonic oscillator representations of $(1+0)$ dimensional conformal groups.

</details>


### [6] [Krylov complexity from a simple quantum mechanical model for a radiating black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16507)
*Eric L Graef,Jeff Murugan,Horatiu Nastase,Hendrik J. R. van Zyl*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在一个描述黑洞及其辐射耦合的简化量子力学模型（mini-BMN矩阵模型）中研究Krylov复杂度（Krylov complexity），发现早期呈现混沌量子动力学的典型增长行为，晚期则饱和至平台期，对应黑洞与辐射的平衡化，并指出该平台可由有效路径积分中的欧几里得瞬子（Euclidean instanton）贡献给出半经典解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在在一个可解析求解的简化框架内，明确研究辐射黑洞在信息论层面的行为，特别是Krylov复杂度及其相关熵的动力学，而非复现完整BMN矩阵模型的全部动力学。

Method: 采用受Maldacena近期提议启发的简化“mini-BMN”矩阵模型，结合微扰分析与数值模拟，分别在早期和晚期分析Krylov复杂度与Krylov熵的行为。

Result: 早期Krylov复杂度呈现混沌量子动力学预期的增长；晚期动力学饱和至平台期，与黑洞及其辐射之间的平衡化以及有限熵量子系统的一般预期一致。

Conclusion: 平台期行为可通过有效路径积分中的欧几里得瞬子贡献获得半经典解释；该玩具模型为解析和数值研究这些特征提供了一个可控框架。

Abstract: We investigate Krylov complexity in a simple quantum mechanical model describing a black hole coupled to its radiation. The model is constructed as a simplified ``mini-BMN" matrix system inspired by a recent proposal of Maldacena. Our aim is not to reproduce the full dynamics of the BMN matrix model, but rather to isolate a tractable setting in which the information-theoretic behaviour of a radiating black hole can be studied explicitly. We analyze both the early- and late-time behaviour of Krylov complexity and the associated Krylov entropy. At early times, perturbative and numerical analyses reveal the expected growth characteristic of chaotic quantum dynamics. At late times, however, the dynamics saturates to a plateau, consistent with equilibration between the black hole and its radiation and with general expectations from finite-entropy quantum systems. We argue that this plateau behaviour admits a semiclassical interpretation in terms of Euclidean instanton contributions in an effective path-integral. The toy model studied here offers a controlled framework in which these features can be investigated analytically and numerically.

</details>


### [7] [Strong-coupling results in (non-)conformal $\mathcal{N}=2$ theories with fundamental flavors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16521)
*M. Billo,A. Lerda,A. Testa*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类四维 $\mathcal{N}=2$ SU($N$) 规范理论（gauge theories），包含两个秩二反对称表示的无质量超多重态（hypermultiplets）以及 $0\leq N_f\leq 4$ 个基本味。通过超对称局域化（supersymmetric localization）方法，在 $N_f=4$ 超共形情形和 $N_f<4$ 渐近自由情形下，计算了大 $N$ 极限下的自由能（free energy）和 $\frac12$-BPS 圆形威尔逊环（circular Wilson loop）期望值，并证明大 't Hooft 耦合 $\lambda$ 下的非平面修正可重求和为有效耦合 $\widetilde\lambda$。在超共形情形中，$\widetilde\lambda$ 的展开暗示了 AdS/CFT 对偶中有效耦合应代替 $\lambda$ 作为体弦耦合常数（bulk string coupling）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索四维 $\mathcal{N}=2$ 规范理论在大 $N$ 极限下的非平面修正结构，并建立从局域化矩阵模型到 AdS/CFT 对偶的新联系。

Method: 使用超对称局域化（supersymmetric localization）方法将四球面上的可观测量映射为矩阵模型（matrix model）；在此基础上分析大 $N$ 极限下的自由能和 $\frac12$-BPS 圆形威尔逊环期望值。

Result: 对于所有 $N_f$，证明了在大的 't Hooft 耦合 $\lambda$ 下，非平面修正的无穷级数可用一个有效耦合 $\widetilde\lambda$ 重新求和。在非共形窗口（$0\leq N_f<4$）中，这是首次通过局域化在强 't Hooft 耦合下得到平面极限显式结果；在超共形情形（$N_f=4$）下，$\widetilde\lambda$ 的展开提示了 AdS/CFT 对偶中一个新的字典条目。

Conclusion: 有效耦合 $\widetilde\lambda$ 统一了共形与非共形情形下大 $N$ 极限的非平面重求和，并在超共形情形中暗示 $\widetilde\lambda$ 应作为 AdS/CFT 对偶中的体弦耦合常数，从而修正了标准的 AdS/CFT 字典。

Abstract: We study a class of four-dimensional $\mathcal{N}=2$ SU($N$) gauge theories with two massless hypermultiplets in the rank-two antisymmetric representation and $0\leq N_f\leq 4$ fundamental flavors. These theories are superconformal for $N_f=4$ and asymptotically free otherwise. Supersymmetric localization on the four-sphere applies in both cases and leads to matrix-model representations for a broad class of protected observables. Within this framework, we compute the free energy and the expectation value of the $\frac{1}{2}$-BPS circular Wilson loop in the large-$N$ limit. For any $N_f$, we show that the infinite series of non-planar corrections at large 't Hooft coupling $λ$ can be resummed in terms of an effective coupling $\widetildeλ$. In the non-conformal window ($0\leq N_f<4$), this provides a first example in which localization leads to explicit results in the planar limit at strong 't Hooft coupling. In the superconformal case ($N_f=4$), the large-$N$ expansion in $\widetildeλ$ suggests a refined AdS/CFT dictionary in which $\widetildeλ$, rather than $λ$, plays the role of the bulk string coupling.

</details>


### [8] [3d QFT IR divergences as UV divergences in 4d Holographic Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16587)
*Matheus Cravo,Horatiu Nastase*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过在一个三维玩具模型场论中引入质量项并保持广义共形结构，计算了双圈两点和三点关联函数的红外（IR）结构，论证了微扰论之外可能存在红外有限性，对应于对偶四维宇宙学中的紫外（UV）有限性及宇宙奇点的消除。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究四维全息宇宙学（4d holographic cosmology）中红外发散（IR divergences）的机制，并探索微扰论之外的红外有限性是否可能存在，进而缓解对偶宇宙学中的紫外发散问题（即宇宙奇点）。

Method: 在三维玩具模型场论中引入质量项，同时保持广义共形结构（generalized conformal structure）的特定形式；在此基础上计算了双圈（2-loop）水平的两点和三点关联函数（2- and 3-point functions），并分析其在质量标度以下的红外结构。

Result: 在双圈水平下，关联函数在质量标度以下表现出特定的红外行为；基于此结果，论文论证了微扰论之外可能存在红外有限性（IR finiteness），与格点模拟（lattice results）的结果一致。

Conclusion: 该三维红外场论方法所预示的红外有限性，在对偶的四维宇宙学中对应于紫外有限性（UV finiteness），即宇宙奇点（cosmological singularities）的消除。此外，该方法具有超越本应用的推广潜力。

Abstract: In this paper we consider IR divergences in a 3d toy model field theory for 4d holographic cosmology, and we analyze them by introducing a mass term in a way that preserves a certain form of the generalized conformal structure. This allows us to compute 2- and 3-point functions at 2-loops and study their IR structure below the mass scale, from which we argue for a possible IR finiteness beyond perturbation theory, consistent with lattice results. In the holographically dual 4d cosmology, this corresponds to UV finiteness, i.e., the absence of cosmological singularities. The 3d IR field theory methods could be extended beyond this specific application.

### [9] [Evaporating Black Hole Interior and Complexity Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16619)
*Nicolò Bragagnolo,S. Prem Kumar*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究蒸发黑洞内部演化的子系统复杂度（complexity），在Jackiw-Teitelboim (JT)引力与端世界膜（end-of-the-world brane）的简化模型中，通过纠缠膜内态与辅助辐射系统模拟蒸发过程。基于淬火无序平均（quenched disorder averaging）的计算发现：蒸发黑洞的复杂度演化与不蒸发情形截然不同——早期线性增长，在Page时间达到峰值∼O(S_BH)，随后指数衰减；Page时间后相对涨落大幅上升，失去自平均性（self-averaging），由稀有构型主导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索蒸发黑洞内部的量子引力效应，特别是子系统复杂度（complexity）在黑洞蒸发过程中的演化行为，以理解非平衡量子引力系统中信息与复杂度的动态特征。

Method: 采用Jackiw-Teitelboim (JT)引力与端世界膜（end-of-the-world brane）模型，通过纠缠膜内部态与辅助辐射系统模拟蒸发；利用淬火无序平均（quenched disorder averaging）方法，纳入时空虫洞（spacetime wormholes）与复制虫洞（replica wormholes）的非微扰引力效应，编码对偶随机哈密顿量（random Hamiltonian）与膜态耦合的系综平均。

Result: 蒸发黑洞的子系统复杂度早期线性增长，在Page时间达到最大值∼O(S_BH)，随后指数衰减；复杂度对辐射希尔伯特空间维度有非平凡依赖。Page时间前相对涨落较小，但Page时间后涨落变为O(1)量级并持续增大，系综平均复杂度由稀有构型主导，丧失自平均性（self-averaging）。

Conclusion: 蒸发黑洞的复杂度演化与不蒸发黑洞存在本质差异，Page时间前后的涨落行为揭示了系统统计性质的转变，系综平均在晚期不再代表典型实现的行为。

Abstract: We study the evolution of the interior of an evaporating black hole in a simple model of Jackiw-Teitelboim (JT) gravity with an end-of-the-world (EoW) brane, where evaporation is modeled by entangling the brane's internal states with an auxiliary radiation system. To probe the black hole interior, we consider a geodesic length extracted from a boundary-to-brane two-point function and interpret its renormalised value as a measure of subsystem complexity. Our computation, based on quenched disorder averaging, includes non-perturbative gravitational effects from both spacetime wormholes and replica wormholes, encoding ensemble averaging over the dual random Hamiltonian and brane-state couplings. Unlike non-evaporating black holes where complexity first grows linearly and then plateaus at late times $\sim{\cal O}(e^{S_{\rm BH}})$, we find that complexity evolution of the black hole subsystem in the evaporating case differs drastically, depending nontrivially on the dimension of the emitted radiation Hilbert space. It grows linearly at early times, reaches a maximum at Page time $\sim{\cal O}({S_{\rm BH}})$, and then decays exponentially. We further show that the relative fluctuations of the interior length remain small before the Page time but become of order one and eventually large at later times: this signals a loss of self-averaging, with the ensemble-averaged complexity dominated by rare configurations rather than by typical realisations.

### [10] [On bulk reconstruction in Lorentzian AdS and its flat space limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16641)
*Núria Navarro,Ana-Maria Raclariu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明了四维Lorentzian反德西特时空（AdS₄）中的自由量子场可通过边界三维共形场论（CFT₃）中的初级算符（primary operators）进行重构，并展示了多种等价的表示形式，包括利用时间排序传播子、阴影算符（shadow operators）以及主级数表示（principal series representations），同时揭示了该构造与平直空间正则量子化（canonical quantization）之间的类比关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在AdS/CFT对偶（AdS/CFT correspondence）框架下，深入理解体时空（bulk spacetime）中自由量子场如何由边界共形场论（CFT）中的初级算符（primary operators）重构，并建立与平直空间量子化的明确类比。

Method: 利用体-边传播子（bulk-to-boundary propagators）的适当时间排序构造AdS中Klein-Gordon方程解的正负能量子空间；在余维为一的体超曲面（codimension-1 bulk hypersurface）上用边界区域积分表示体标量场；从表示论（representation theory）角度和平直空间极限（flat space limits）计算两方面验证与平直空间正则量子化的等价性；引入主级数表示（principal series representations）的波函数进行替代分解。

Result: 自由标量场在AdS₄中的体超曲面上可用过去或未来边界区域的积分表示，核函数为时间排序或反时间排序传播子；该构造是平直空间正则量子化的AdS类比；根据标量场尺度维数Δ的选择和边界插入点的位置，可获得平面波基（plane wave basis）或Carroll基（Carrollian basis）的分解；AdS₄中的自由标量还可由so(3,1)子代数的主级数表示波函数分解，并在大AdS半径极限下退化为平直空间中的标量共形初级波函数（scalar conformal primary wavefunctions）。

Conclusion: AdS₄中自由标量场的边界重构存在多种等价表示，且这些构造与平直空间中的正则量子化具有明确的对应关系，同时展示了不同极限下（如Δ→∞或大AdS半径极限）向平直空间标量场表示的平滑过渡。

Abstract: We revisit the reconstruction of a free quantum field in 4-dimensional Lorentzian Anti-de-Sitter (AdS$_4$) spacetime in terms of primary operators in the boundary 3d CFT (CFT$_3$). We show that the positive and negative energy subspaces of solutions to the Klein-Gordon equation in AdS can be spanned with bulk-to-boundary propagators with appropriate time orderings. As a result, free scalar fields on a codimension-1 bulk hypersurface $Σ_τ$ can be expressed in terms of operators integrated over boundary regions in the past or future of $Σ_τ$ with kernels given by time-ordered or anti-time-ordered propagators. We present various equivalent representations for the bulk field in terms of either CFT primaries or their shadows. We show from both a representation theoretic perspective and by direct computation of various flat space limits that our construction is the AdS analog of the canonical quantization of a free scalar in flat space. Depending on the choice of $Δ$ and the location of the boundary insertions one obtains a decomposition of the scalar in either a plane wave basis ($Δ\rightarrow \infty$) or a Carrollian basis (fixed $Δ$). Finally, we show that the free scalar in AdS$_4$ can be alternatively decomposed in terms of wavefunctions associated with principal series representations of dimension $δ= 1 + iλ$ of an $\mathfrak{so}(3,1)$ subalgebra of the AdS$_4$ isometry algebra. We demonstrate that the latter become, in the limit of large AdS radius and for fixed $δ$, scalar conformal primary wavefunctions in flat space.

Abstract: We study the separable master equations for the electromagnetic and gravitational perturbations in five-dimensional Myers-Perry black holes. In the static limit, while the master equation for the electric polarization of the Maxwell field reduces to that of a massless scalar field, the magnetic polarization and gravitational perturbation yield Heun equations for both its angular and radial components. We reconstruct the gauge field using master fields and study its asymptotic behavior. Abstract: We study the gauging of invertible symmetries, particularly in 3 dimensions, using equivariantisation, $G$-crossed braided zesting, and the generalised orbifold construction. We discuss how these methods are related and illustrate them in various examples. We cover all $\mathbb{Z}_2$-symmetries in Dijkgraaf--Witten $\mathbb{Z}_2$-gauge theory $\mathcal{D}(\mathbb{Z}_2)$, the $\mathbb{Z}_2$-symmetries described by Tambara--Yamagami categories, and obstructions to gauging the central symmetry in Chern--Simons $\mathrm{SU}(2)_k$-gauge theory. ### [14] [Five legs @ three loops: N=4 sYM amplitude near mass-shell](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17056)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 发现该红外敏感可观测量具有简洁的表示形式；确认了其在红外项和有限项上的指数化行为；红外双对数（infrared double logarithm）通过八边形反常维度（octagon anomalous dimension）作为控制系数，展现了预期的普适性（universality）。与二圈结果不同，三圈结果表明三个独立运动学结构各自拥有独立的't Hooft耦合函数。

Abstract: We present a three-loop analysis of the scattering amplitude of five nearly massless W-bosons in planar maximally supersymmetric Yang-Mills theory. The basis of the master integrals is established, making use of the unitarity-cut sewing technique in six-dimensional N=(1,1) super-Yang-Mills theory. Its dimensional reduction down to four allows us to generate masses for internal and external states. Employing explicit expressions for all integrals that we calculated in a companion paper, we find a concise representation for this infrared-sensitive observable. We confirm its exponentiation, both for infrared and finite terms. The infrared double logarithm manifests the anticipated universality through the octagon anomalous dimension as its governing coefficient. Unlike our previous two-loop result, this consideration reveals that each of the three independent kinematic structures furnishing the amplitude possesses its own function of 't Hooft coupling.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We calculate the three-loop master integrals contributing to the three-loop five-point amplitude on the special Coulomb branch of $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM theory. For the genuine pentagon integrals, we follow the approach of Ref. [JHEP 12 (2025) 107], which includes a regularization preserving dual conformal invariance (DCI). As a new ingredient, we introduce a simple method, allowing to factor out the dependence on the DCI cross ratios from the contribution of each region. The remaining integrals are then essentially simplified by taking successive limits of vanishing external invariants. For 3 out of 82 regions contributing to the most complicated integral $\mathcal{I}_5^{(3)}$ we were not able to perform the integration even after these simplifications. For these three regions, we perform the integration-by-parts (IBP) reduction in parametric representation and evaluate the resulting locally finite integrals using HyperInt.

*A. Boasso,C. D. Fosco,B. C. Guntsche,F. D. Mazzitelli*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有弯曲边界的平坦流形上无质量标量场的非局域有效作用量。通过热核（heat-kernel）方法，推导了外曲率张量（extrinsic curvature tensor）二次阶非局域贡献的协变展开，该展开在外曲率梯度主导非线性曲率效应的区域内有效。作为应用，计算了2+1维振荡变形环和3+1维振荡变形球面上的粒子产生率（particle-creation rate）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有结果仅适用于蒙日贴片（Monge-patch）嵌入的特定表面，缺乏适用于更一般曲面的几何框架。本文旨在建立一种协变展开方法，既能复现早期结果，又能推广到不满足全局蒙日贴片描述的任意曲面。

Method: 采用热核方法（heat-kernel approach），对平坦流形上弯曲边界问题中无质量标量场的非局域有效作用量进行协变展开，展开到外曲率张量的二次阶。

Result: 导出了外曲率张量二次阶非局域贡献的协变展开式，该展开在外曲率梯度主导非线性曲率效应的区域内成立。计算了2+1维振荡变形环和3+1维振荡变形球面上的粒子产生率。

Conclusion: 所构造的几何框架统一并推广了基于蒙日贴片嵌入的早期结果，适用于更一般的曲面几何。该框架可用于计算弯曲边界系统中的粒子产生等物理效应。

Abstract: We study the nonlocal effective action of a massless scalar field defined on a flat manifold with a curved boundary. Using a heat-kernel approach, we derive a covariant expansion of the nonlocal contribution to quadratic order in the extrinsic curvature tensor. Our construction provides a geometric framework that both reproduces earlier results obtained for Monge-patch embeddings and extends them to more general surfaces that need not admit a global Monge-patch description. The expansion is valid in the regime where gradients of the extrinsic curvature dominate over nonlinear curvature effects. As an application, we compute the particle-creation rate for an oscillating deformed ring in $2+1$ dimensions and an oscillating deformed sphere in $3+1$ dimensions.

</details>


### [17] [Emergent AdS Geometry and Black Hole Thermodynamics from Functional Renormalization Group](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17209)

Method: 在泛函重整化群（FRG）框架内，通过连续迭代威尔逊重整化群（Wilsonian RG）变换，将额外维尺度坐标识别为 emergent (d+1) 维体时空的径向方向；构建双向全息词典，将非微扰涨落直接映射到 emergent 体度规的扭曲因子（warping factors）中。

Result: 在无质量临界构型下，emergent 引力真空自发组织成无坐标奇点的稳定正则 AdS_{d+1} 几何，满足所有局域能量条件；半经典霍金温度与边界场论温度严格相等；近视界热力学势精确满足黑洞热力学第一定律，并自发导出贝肯斯坦-霍金面积律 S_{horizon} = (N/4)𝒜。

Conclusion: 该工作从第一原理自下而上地推导了黑洞热力学与 AdS 几何的出现，为非微扰全息对偶和 emergent 时空提供了严格的泛函重整化群基础。

Abstract: We present a non-perturbative holographic dual description for the \(O(N)\) vector model in \(d\)-dimensional Euclidean space within the functional renormalization group (FRG) framework. By continuously iterating Wilsonian RG transformations, the extra-dimensional scale coordinate is identified as the radial direction of an emergent \((d+1)\)-dimensional bulk spacetime. We construct a bidirectional holographic dictionary that maps non-perturbative fluctuations directly into the emergent bulk metric warping factors. Under the massless critical configuration, the emergent gravitational vacuum spontaneously organizes into a stable, regular Anti-de Sitter (\(\text{AdS}_{d+1}\)) geometry without coordinate singularities, satisfying all foundational local energy conditions. Near the thermal horizon, by systematically eliminating the conical deficit singularity, we rigorously prove that the semiclassical Hawking temperature identically matches the boundary field theory temperature (\(T_H \equiv T\)). Finally, we show that the near-horizon thermodynamic potentials exactly satisfy the First Law of Black Hole Thermodynamics, spontaneously generating the Bekenstein-Hawking area law (\(S_{\text{horizon}} = \frac{N}{4}\mathcal{A}\)) from a first-principles, bottom-up derivation.

### [18] [Functional Renormalization Group as a Ricci Flow: An $\mathcal{F}$-Entropy Perspective on Information Metric Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17215)
*Ki-Seok Kim*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文建立了泛函重整化群（Functional Renormalization Group, FRG）与经微分同胚修正的里奇流（Ricci flow）之间的等价性，证明耦合常数空间上的信息度量演化是一个几何优化过程，并引入场论版本的𝒻-熵泛函（𝒻-entropy functional）作为理论的李雅普诺夫势（Lyapunov potential）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在建立重整化群（renormalization group）与几何演化方程之间的严格等价关系，从而为理解重整化群不动点的稳定性提供几何基础，并桥接量子场论、信息几何（information geometry）与Perelman的几何演化理论。

Method: 将Polchinski精确重整化群方程重新表述为无穷维Fokker-Planck框架；构造场论版本的𝒻-熵泛函（Perelman 𝒻-熵的无穷维类比）；证明连续尺度演化构成该熵的黎曼梯度流（Riemannian gradient flow），从而通过熵景观的参数化海森矩阵（parametric Hessian）形变信息度量。

Result: 有效作用量的对数作为标量势Φ生成所需的微分同胚，确保张量一致性；高能自由度积分有效地平滑信息流形的曲率，驱动系统趋向里奇孤子（Ricci soliton）平衡态。

Conclusion: 该框架为刻画重整化群不动点的稳定性提供了新基础，并在量子场论、信息几何与Perelman几何演化理论之间建立了首性原理层面的桥梁。

Abstract: We establish an equivalence between the Functional Renormalization Group (FRG) and the Ricci flow modified by a diffeomorphism. By reformulating the Polchinski exact renormalization group equation into an infinite-dimensional Fokker-Planck framework, we show that the evolution of the Fisher information metric on the coupling constant space is a geometric optimization process. Central to this mapping is our construction of a field-theoretic $\mathcal{F}$-entropy functional - an infinite-dimensional analogue of Perelman's $\mathcal{F}$-entropy functional - which acts as a Lyapunov potential for the theory. We prove that the continuous scale evolution of the field distribution constitutes a Riemannian gradient flow of this $\mathcal{F}$-entropy, which in turn deforms the information metric on the coupling constant space via the parametric Hessian of the entropic landscape. Crucially, the log of the effective action serves as a scalar potential $Φ$ that generates the diffeomorphisms required to ensure the tensorial consistency of the flow. Our framework demonstrates that successive integration of high-energy degrees of freedom effectively smooths out the curvature of the information manifold, driving the system toward a Ricci soliton equilibrium. These results provide a novel foundation for characterizing the stability of RG fixed points and offer a first-principles bridge connecting quantum field theory, information geometry, and Perelman's theory of geometric evolution.

### [19] [Holographic entanglement entropy in the QCD phase diagram under external magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17438)
*Man-Man Sun,Man-Li Tian,Zhou-Run Zhu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-伸缩子（Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton）模型，研究了外磁场下QCD相图中的全息纠缠熵（holographic entanglement entropy），发现纠缠熵在垂直磁场方向呈现 swallow-tail 结构，在大化学势下出现多值行为，而磁场增强可恢复单值性。结果表明纠缠熵可作为QCD相变的有效探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索外磁场对QCD相图（QCD phase diagram）中全息纠缠熵的影响，并检验纠缠熵能否作为QCD相变（QCD phase transition）的有效探测工具。

Method: 采用爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-伸缩子模型（Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton model），分别考虑赝禁闭相（specious-confinement phase）和退禁闭相（deconfined phase），计算和分析两种磁场取向（垂直和平行）下的纠缠熵行为。

Result: 垂直磁场方向下，条带长度（strip length）出现三个不同分支，纠缠熵呈现 swallow-tail 结构，表明连接与断开纠缠面之间存在转变；平行方向下行为单调，无转变发生。纠缠熵差在小子化势（chemical potential）下随温度平滑变化，在大化学势下变为多值，而增加磁场可恢复单值行为。

Conclusion: 上述结果与黑洞热力学（black hole thermodynamics）和QCD相图一致，表明纠缠熵可作为QCD相变的有效探针。

Abstract: In this work, we explore holographic entanglement entropy in the QCD phase diagram under an external magnetic field using an Einstein-Maxwell-dilaton model. We consider both the specious-confinement and deconfined phases. In the perpendicular magnetic field orientation, the strip length shows three distinct branches, and the entanglement entropy develops a swallow-tail structure, indicating a transition between connected and disconnected entanglement surfaces. For the parallel orientation, the behavior is monotonic and no transition occurs. In addition, the difference in entanglement entropy changes smoothly with temperature at small chemical potential, but becomes multivalued at large chemical potential. Increasing the magnetic field restores single-valued behavior. These results are consistent with the black hole thermodynamics and the QCD phase diagram. Our findings show that entanglement entropy can serve as an effective probe of the QCD phase transition.

### [20] [Krylov Correlators in $\mathfrak{sl}(2,\mathbb R)$ Models: Exact Results and Holographic Complexity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17550)
*Eleonora Alfinito,Matteo Beccaria*

Main category: hep-th

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者推导了具有 sl(2,R) 或海森堡-外尔（Heisenberg-Weyl）对称性的量子系统中 Krylov 关联函数的精确解析结果，并将这些结果应用于复杂度-动量对应关系，计算多时间点 Krylov 速度算符的乱序关联函数（out-of-time-ordered correlators, OTOC）。

Result: 研究发现，两个或更多不同时刻的 Krylov 速度算符的乱序关联函数（OTOC）与落入 AdS₃ 中 BTZ 黑洞的粒子在这些时刻的适当径向动量（proper radial momenta）的组合成比例，从而确立了 Krylov 关联函数与黑洞径向动力学之间的定量对应关系。

Conclusion: 该工作是对原始复杂度-动量关系（original complexity–momentum relation）的第一步推广，为在全息框架下建立更广泛的复杂度与几何量之间的对应关系提供了新的方向。

Abstract: In holography, the complexity--momentum correspondence relates the increasing momentum of a point particle falling into an eternal black hole to the rate of growth of the Krylov complexity of the dual boundary state, a conjecture established exactly for the BTZ black hole in AdS$_{3}$ at the semiclassical level. We examine possible extensions of the correspondence by considering boundary higher Krylov complexities and Krylov correlators encoding fluctuations and temporal correlations of the spreading quantum state. To this end, we derive exact results for Krylov correlators in quantum systems with $\mathfrak{sl}(2,\mathbb{R})$ or Heisenberg-Weyl symmetry and apply them to the complexity--momentum correspondence. We show that certain out-of-time-ordered correlators of two or more Krylov speed operators at different times are proportional to combinations of the proper radial momenta of a particle falling into the BTZ black hole in AdS$_{3}$, evaluated at those times. This represents a first step in the generalization of the original complexity--momentum relation.

Method: 利用时间演化算子（time-evolution operator）的Schwartz核（Schwartz kernel）的振荡积分表示（oscillatory integral representation），结合驻相近似（stationary phase approximation）计算倒谐振子在 $L^{2}(\mathbb{S})$ 空间中的态密度（density of states）。

Conclusion: 本文的谱分析指出并弥合了先前文献中的概念与数学空白，为热化现象的半经典起源提供了更严格的数学基础。

Abstract: We consider an inverted harmonic oscillator in the space $L^{2} (\mathbb{S})$ of square-integrable functions on the circle $\mathbb{S}$ and compute its density of states employing the stationary phase approximation. Our computation is based on an oscillatory integral representation of the Schwartz kernel of the time-evolution operator. This demonstrates thermalisation as a semi-classical manifestation of the classical Lyapunov instability -- reported earlier in [Phys. Rev. D 102, 044006; Phys. Rev. D 102, 124047] using heuristic analytic continuation. Our spectral analysis of the Hamiltonian points out and closes the conceptual and mathematical gaps in the preceding literature.

### [22] [Anomaly-Free Spectra, Unimodular Lattices and 6D R-Symmetry Gauged Supergravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17643)
*Katrin Becker,Qi You*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文对具有规范阿贝尔R对称性（gauged abelian R-symmetry）和一个张量多重态（tensor multiplet）的无反常六维 $\mathcal N=(1,0)$ 超引力（supergravity）进行了分类研究，发现了十一个新模型，并分析了反常系数的算术结构，包括幺模嵌入（unimodular embeddability）、特征向量条件（characteristic-vector condition）和无鬼场条件（ghost-free gauge-field condition），从而界定了无反常六维谱、全局一致性约束与弦论/F-理论（F-theory）紫外实现之间的边界。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用算术结构分析方法，研究反常系数（anomaly coefficients）的整数配对（integral pairings）、在秩二幺模电荷格点（rank-two unimodular charge lattices）中的可嵌入性、特征向量条件以及无鬼场条件；同时详细讨论了 $D_4$ 李代数（Lie algebra）对反常多项式（anomaly polynomial）的贡献。

Conclusion: 无反常的规范 $U(1)_R$ 超引力景观（landscape）可能比先前认识的更为丰富，但依然受到高度约束；研究结果进一步厘清了无反常六维谱、全局一致性约束以及可能源于弦论或F-理论的紫外实现（UV realization）之间的边界。

Abstract: We study the classification problem for anomaly-free 6D $\mathcal N=(1,0)$ supergravities with a gauged abelian R-symmetry and one tensor multiplet. We present eleven new models with gauge group $G_{\mathrm{non-Abelian}}\times U(1)_R$ that satisfy the local Green--Schwarz factorization condition, together with several recently proposed global consistency conditions. In particular, the low-rank models we found are precisely where some of the recent enumeration literature is least directly applicable. These examples suggest that the landscape of anomaly-free gauged $U(1)_R$ supergravities may be richer than previously recognized while still remaining highly constrained. We analyze the arithmetic structure of the anomaly coefficients, including their integral pairings, embeddability into rank-two unimodular charge lattices, the characteristic-vector condition and ghost-free gauge-field conditions. We show that $n_V \equiv 8 \pmod{12}$ is necessary and sufficient for the unimodular embeddability in the rank-two case. For the characteristic-vector condition we verify sufficiency for the branches realized by our examples and identify a remaining branch requiring additional exclusion. We also present a detailed discussion of the contribution to the anomaly polynomial when the $D_4$ Lie algebra is present. These results sharpen the boundary between anomaly-free 6D spectra, global-consistency constraints, and possible UV realization in string theory or F-theory.

### [23] [An Alternative Viewpoint on Kinematic Flow from Tubing Splitting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17751)
*Ji-Yuan Ke,Ping He*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过反转图管（graph tubings）的演化方向，重新表述了共形耦合标量场在幂律宇宙学（power-law cosmology）中波函数系数所满足的微分方程，并发现其基础结构——运动学流（kinematic flow）与图管——可能比微分方程本身更为基本，甚至可推广至tr φ³理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在为运动学流（kinematic flow）提供新的视角，通过反转图管（graph tubings）的演化方向，重新理解共形耦合标量场在幂律宇宙学（power-law cosmology）中波函数系数所满足的微分方程的基础结构。

Method: 将波函数系数满足的微分方程重铸为基函数的迭代微分系统，利用图管（graph tubings）对这些函数进行编码，并通过反转图管演化方向重新表述基函数之间的关系，进而构造等价于树图级（tree level）运动学流（kinematic flow）的拆分规则（splitting rules）来推导微分方程。

Result: 所构建的拆分规则揭示了微分方程背后更丰富的物理结构，包括奇点（singularities）和局域演化（local evolution）。在基于时间排序（time ordering）的替代基底下，这些规则暗示了时间如何从运动学空间（kinematic space）中涌现，且该结论不限于单个费曼图，可推广至tr φ³理论。

Conclusion: 图管（graph tubings）与运动学流（kinematic flow）可能比微分方程更为基本，具有独立于后者之外的自身结构（a life of their own）。

Abstract: The differential equations satisfied by the wavefunction coefficients of conformally coupled scalars in a power-law cosmology can be recast into an iterative differential system of basis functions. These functions can be encoded within graph tubings, and are governed by a set of rules describing how they flow in kinematic space. In this paper we propose a new viewpoint on the kinematic flow by reformulating the relations among these basis functions through reversing the evolution direction of the tubings. The differential equations can then be derived by constructing appropriate splitting rules equivalent to the kinematic flow (at tree level). While the implementation of these rules can be somewhat complicated, they reveal richer physical structures underlying the differential equations, such as singularities and local evolution. Under an alternative basis based on time ordering, these rules offer important implications for how time emerges from kinematic space. This conclusion is even not restricted to individual Feynman diagrams, and can be generalized to the tr $φ^3$ theory. This suggests that the tubings, as well as the kinematic flow, might be more fundamental objects than the differential equations, and have a life of their own.

</details>


### [24] [A Renormalizable and Unitary Approach to Quantum Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17817)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准爱因斯坦-希尔伯特作用量在量子化后存在不可重整化（non-renormalizable）和幺正性（unitarity）问题，需要寻找一种能同时满足这两项要求且与经典广义相对论相容的量子引力模型。

Method: 通过引入一个拉格朗日乘子场来限制单圈阶（one-loop order）的量子修正，从而构造出可重整化且幺正的模型。

Result: 该模型在单圈阶是可重整化（renormalizable）且幺正（unitary）的，并在经典极限下能够重新导出爱因斯坦场方程（Einstein field equations）。

Conclusion: 引入拉格朗日乘子场的方案有望在量子引力（quantum gravity）框架中同时实现可重整性与幺正性，并保持与经典广义相对论的一致。

Abstract: A Lagrange multiplier field restricts the quantum corrections to the Einstein-Hilbert action at one-loop order, yielding a model that is renormalizable and unitary while reproducing the Einstein field equations in the classical limit.

Method: 采用小质量 regime（$-t\sim m^2$）下的4点和5点散射振幅，对所有阶的 $G_N s$ 大修正进行重求和。随后应用 KMOC 公式计算引力冲量（gravitational impulse），并取大质量极限恢复经典高能结果。

Conclusion: 该重求和方法在超相对论极限下有效统一了经典引力冲量的高阶修正，验证了与后闵可夫斯基展开的一致性，并为更高阶 PM 展开提供了预测能力。

Abstract: We compute the gravitational impulse for two classical massive scalars in the ultrarelativistic limit to all orders in Newton's constant $G_N$ at fixed $G_N s/m b$ to $O(m^4/s^2)$. By computing the 4 and 5-point scattering amplitudes in the small-mass regime of $-t\sim m^2$, we are able to resum all large $G_N s$ corrections. Abstract: We investigate field theory models of holographic superconductors in which the condensation of the order parameter is induced by a Robin boundary condition. Using modular invariance, we relate the high- and low-temperature phases, reproducing analytically the results for the zero-winding sector of the holographic model. Moreover, we match the near-critical behaviour of the condensate with an effective Ginzburg--Landau field theory description. Method: 利用黎曼双线性恒等式将变形转化为一个算符穿衣服过程加上一个高亏格大回路积分；基于该提议，计算环面和高亏格黎曼面上的配分函数变形，将其表示为保持模不变性或协变性的核积分（kernel integral）；分析共形权重与守恒荷沿变形的流动，并结合模 $S$-变换（modular $S$-transformation）提出构建穿衣服算符的判据。

Abstract: We propose a reformulation of the conformal perturbation theory of the correlation functions in $J\bar{J}$-deformed CFTs as a dressing on the deformed operators, that matches both bare and renormalized perturbation theory. The key is to use the Riemann bilinear identity to convert the deformation into a dressing and a large-cycle integral for higher genus. Based on the proposal, we calculate the deformation of partition functions on the torus and higher genus Riemann surfaces, which can be written as kernel integrals that preserve modular invariance or covariance. We also calculate the flow of the conformal weights and conserved charges along the deformation. ### [30] [Modular Lower Bounds on Reeh-Schlieder State Preparation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18640)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Reeh-Schlieder定理保证任意量子态可从真空中通过局域算符近似实现，但未给出定量代价。本文旨在填补这一空白，建立制备具有负模能量态的普适性代价下界。

Method: 从Tomita-Takesaki理论中提取一个标准估计式作为模型无关的制备界（preparation bound）；通过将算符重缩放到物理收缩算符，将同一估计转化为后选择开销的下界；在具体几何中利用Bisognano-Wichmann定理和Casini-Huerta-Myers公式分别将边界化为楔形区域的升压能量（boost energy）和共形场论有界区域中的应力张量（stress-tensor）表述。

Result: 具有深度负模能量的目标态需要大尺度局域算符；局域幺正算符（local unitaries）只能到达非负模能量的态；负模扇区必须借助非幺正或后选择操作，从而产生一个制备代价下界，该下界在类型III局域代数（type III local algebras）中与真空盗用（vacuum embezzlement）互补。

Conclusion: Reeh-Schlieder定理所保证的可达性存在定量成本，负模能量态的制备必然伴随算符尺度或后选择代价的增大，该结果对量子场论中的信息提取与通道容量问题具有约束意义。

Abstract: The Reeh-Schlieder theorem says that every target vector can be approximated from the vacuum by an operator localized in an arbitrarily small spacetime region, but it gives no quantitative cost for doing so. This note isolates a standard Tomita-Takesaki estimate as a model-independent preparation bound. Targets with deeply negative modular energy require large local operators. After rescaling such an operator to a physical contraction, the same estimate becomes a lower bound on postselection overhead. In geometries where the modular Hamiltonian is known, the bound becomes explicit. Bisognano-Wichmann turns it into a boost energy statement for wedges, and the Casini-Huerta-Myers formula gives a stress-tensor version for bounded regions of conformal field theories. Local unitaries can only reach states of nonnegative modular energy. Negative modular sectors require nonunitary or postselected outcomes, giving a preparation cost bound that complements vacuum embezzlement in type III local algebras.

### [31] [The classical Yangian symmetry of Auxiliary Field Sigma Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18213)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 推广了由Brezin、Itzykson、Zinn-Justin和Zuber提出的BIZZ递归程序，用于生成非局域荷（non-local charges），并给出了这些荷服从杨-麦克斯特代数（Yangian algebra）的充分条件。该方法适用于一大类可积西格玛模型（integrable sigma models）及其辅助场形变。

Result: 将所提出的方法应用于多个可积西格玛模型及其辅助场形变的实例中，在所有情形下均发现了杨-麦克斯特代数（Yangian algebra）和梅莱括号结构（Maillet bracket structure）。

Conclusion: 该工作为哈密顿量可积性（Hamiltonian integrability）与杨-麦克斯特对称性（Yangian symmetry）在变形西格玛模型中得以保持的现象提供了一个统一的解释。

Abstract: Integrable field theories exhibit infinitely many symmetries which underlie their solvability, but the structure of these symmetries can become obscured after performing an integrable deformation such as $\TT$ or an auxiliary field deformation. In this paper, we present a systematic organizing principle for understanding deformed charges and their Yangian structure in a broad class of integrable sigma models and their auxiliary field deformations. We generalize the recursive procedure of Brezin, Itzykson, Zinn-Justin, and Zuber (BIZZ) for generating non-local charges, and give sufficient conditions under which the resulting charges obey a Yangian algebra. We apply these results to many examples of integrable sigma models and their auxiliary field deformations, finding a Yangian algebra and Maillet bracket structure in all cases. This offers a unified explanation for the persistence of Hamiltonian integrability and Yangian symmetry across a wide landscape of deformed sigma models.

### [32] [From classical Lax ODEs to quantum integrable theories: the moduli](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18695)
*Davide Fioravanti,Marco Rossi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文从经典可积（integrable）偏微分方程出发，通过常微分方程/可积模型对应（ODE/IM correspondence），建立广义 sinh-Gordon 方程与量子可积模型之间的联系，推导出 Y-系统和热力学贝特假设方程（thermodynamic Bethe Ansatz equations），并证明了两个 Zamolodchikov 猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 推导出 Y-系统和热力学贝特假设方程（thermodynamic Bethe Ansatz equations），无需经过散射理论（scattering theory）即可获得，并提供了单值性空间（monodromy space）的不变量参数化。零动量情形下，该模型完整描述了量子齐次正弦-戈登模型（homogeneous sine-Gordon model），对应于 $\mathcal{N}=4$ 超杨-米尔斯（SYM）理论强耦合下的散射振幅或 $AdS_3$ 中的零多边形类光威尔逊环。此外，证明了基于先前结果的两个 Zamolodchikov 猜想。

Abstract: The general idea of this paper is to start from a classical integrable (partial differential) equation which arises as a compatibility condition for a matrix linear differential problem. For definitiveness' sake, a generalised sinh-Gordon equation depending on $2N-1$ complex coefficients or moduli is considered. Then, the connexion coefficients (Wronskians) of different solutions to this problem satisfy, in the spirit of the Ordinary Differential Equation/Integrable Model correspondence, functional relations, which can be considered, -- if supplemented by suitable asymptotic behaviours --, as identifying a specific state of a quantum integrable model: in fact they are the eigenvalues of extensions of Baxter operators $Q$ and $T$, the transfer matrix. Moreover, Y-system and (implementing the asymptotic conditions) thermodynamic Bethe Ansatz equations originate from them, without any passage through the scattering theory, and providing an invariant parametrisation of the monodromy space. The crucial novelty is the modification of all the relations because of their dependence on the moduli. For zero momentum, they fully describe physically the quantum homogeneous sine-Gordon model, {\it i.e.} scattering amplitudes of gauge fields in $\mathcal{N} = 4$ SYM at strong coupling or their dual null polygonal light-like Wilson loops in $AdS_3$. As a direct consequence of the correspondence, two Zamolodchikov's conjectures, based on previous results, are also proven.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究 D1D5 共形场论（CFT）中随机矩阵统计（random-matrix statistics）的出现机制，特别是分析低能近 BPS（near-BPS）扇区中的提升矩阵（lifting matrix）行为。

Method: 比较 N=3 有限 N 提升问题（finite-N lifting problem）与固定轨形共形权重和 R 荷（R charges）下的平面大 N 极限（planar large-N limit），并利用对称性（symmetry）分辨能谱分析不同循环结构之间的混合效应。

Result: 在平面大 N 极限下，单循环态与多循环态之间的混合被抑制，对称分辨的提升谱呈现泊松型能级统计（Poisson-like level statistics）。在有限 N 下，非平面项恢复了不同循环结构之间的混合，伴随能级排斥，与随机矩阵行为一致。

Conclusion: 在可分析的低能近 BPS 扇区中，有限 N 下的非平面循环结构混合与能级排斥及随机矩阵型间隔统计（random-matrix-like spacing statistics）的出现相关。

Abstract: We investigate the emergence of random-matrix statistics in the D1D5 CFT by studying second-order lifting matrices in low-energy near-BPS sectors. We compare the $N=3$ finite-$N$ lifting problems with the planar large-$N$ limit at fixed orbifold conformal weight and R charges. In the planar large-$N$ limit at fixed orbifold energy, mixing between single-cycle and multi-cycle states is suppressed, and the symmetry-resolved lifting spectra display Poisson-like level statistics. At finite $N$, non-planar terms restore this mixing between different cycle structures. Within the resulting symmetry-resolved sectors, this finite-$N$ mixing is accompanied by level repulsion consistent with random-matrix behavior. These results suggest that, in the low-energy near-BPS sectors accessible to our analysis, non-planar cycle-structure mixing at finite $N$ is associated with the onset of level repulsion and random-matrix-like spacing statistics.

</details>


### [34] [Tachyonic (In)stability in Randall-Sundrum Braneworld Scenarios](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18403)
*Abhirup Karmakar,Soumitra SenGupta*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文受Damour-Esposito-Farése (DEF)自发标量化模型启发，在膜世界（braneworld）场景中研究了快子不稳定性（tachyonic instability）与自发标量化（spontaneous scalarization）的可能性。基于两膜Randall-Sundrum (RS)模型，分析了三种情景下额外维辐射子（radion）场的快子（不）稳定性条件，并进一步将形式推广到f(R)引力理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在膜世界（braneworld）框架下实现快子不稳定性（tachyonic instability）和自发标量化（spontaneous scalarization）的可能性，受标量-张量引力（Scalar-Tensor theories）中Damour-Esposito-Farése (DEF)模型的启发。

Method: 基于两膜Randall-Sundrum (RS)模型，将低能有效理论（low-energy effective theory）描述为标量-张量（scalar-tensor）形式，并以额外维辐射子（radion）作为标量场；在三种情形（无势、纯引力势、含稳定场背景）中分析辐射子场的快子（不）稳定性条件，并拓展至FLRW背景及f(R)理论。

Result: 在含体稳定场（bulk stabilizing field）的RS模型中，T>0的膜上物质会改变辐射子场的真空期望值（VEV），破坏规范层级问题（gauge hierarchy problem）的解决；T<0的膜上物质则不影响稳定性与VEV。确定了Planck膜上辐射子场在FLRW背景几何下的精确快子（不）稳定性条件。

Conclusion: 膜世界场景中存在类似标量-张量引力中DEF模型的自发标量化机制；所建立的快子不稳定性分析框架可进一步推广到f(R)引力理论，为暴涨宇宙学（inflationary epoch）时期的4D有效理论提供统一描述。

Abstract: Low-energy effective theories provide a natural description of four-dimensional physics in higher-dimensional geometries, where the imprint of the bulk geometry appears as parameters of the lower-dimensional theory. Inspired by the Damour-Esposito-Farése (DEF) model of spontaneous scalarization in first generation Scalar-Tensor theories of gravity, we investigate the possibility of tachyonic instability and spontaneous scalarization in braneworld scenarios. We consider the two-brane Randall-Sundrum model where the low-energy effective theory on either brane is of scalar-tensor nature with the extra-dimensional radion playing the role of the scalar. We have determined the possibilities for tachyonic (in)stability of the radion field on either branes in three scenarios: the Randall-Sundrum (RS) model with fine-tuning conditions in which the potential of the radion field vanishes identically, the RS model without fine-tunings where the radion potential arises purely from the gravity sector, and the RS model with a bulk stabilizing field that generates a radion potential with a minimum. With the bulk stabilizing field, we have found that on-brane matter with $T>0$ changes the VEV of the radion, destroying the resolution of the gauge hierarchy problem, whereas on-brane matter with $T<0$ does not alter the stability and VEV of the radion. We further determined the exact condition of tachyonic (in)stability of radion field on Planck brane with the FLRW background geometry on the brane. Finally, we have extended the same formalism to study the tachyonic (in)stability conditions of $f(R)$ theories of gravity with the motivation that the 4D effective theory on RS branes can be casted into a $f(R)$ theory on the branes at the inflationary epoch of cosmology.

### [35] [Basis-free neural-network geminal and Jastrow factors for variational Monte Carlo](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17083)
*Jan Kessler,Thomas D. Kühne*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种无基组（basis-free）的Jastrow–AGP神经网络量子态变分蒙特卡罗方法，将反对称双子功率（AGP）行列式与前馈神经网络结合，分别处理节面结构和动态关联。在氢气分子和矩形氢四聚体上实现了亚毫哈特里精度，并揭示了节面自由度不足时的残差限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经网络量子态（neural-network quantum states）能灵活构造紧凑多电子波函数，但其实际精度严重依赖于如何处理费米子反对称性（fermionic antisymmetry）、电子关联（electron correlation）和优化噪声（optimization noise）。现有方法在这些方面仍存在局限，需要更清晰地分离动态关联与静态、多参考关联的误差来源。

Method: 将反对称双子功率（AGP）行列式与前馈神经网络（feed-forward neural networks）结合，用神经网络取代双子（geminal）和两个Jastrow因子构造中的常规基组展开（basis-set expansions）。得到的无基组Jastrow–AGP拟设通过变分蒙特卡罗（variational Monte Carlo）优化，设计思路是将两个任务分离：AGP部分定义节面（nodal surface），神经网络Jastrow因子在固定节面下恢复动态关联（dynamical correlation）。

Result: 在氢气分子和矩形氢四聚体（rectangular hydrogen tetramer）上，当AGP节面足够恰当时，实现了亚毫哈特里（sub-millihartree）精度。在氢四聚体大半径方形几何附近，暴露了残留的节面局限性（residual nodal limitation）。

Conclusion: 该分离式设计能够区分动态关联误差与静态、多参考关联（static, multireference correlation）导致的误差，明确了神经网络构建块在哪些方面能改进紧凑双子拟设，以及在哪些情况下需要额外的节面自由度。

Abstract: Neural-network quantum states offer a flexible route to compact many-electron wave functions, but their practical accuracy depends strongly on how fermionic antisymmetry, electron correlation, and optimization noise are treated. Here we combine an antisymmetrized geminal power (AGP) determinant with feed-forward neural networks that replace conventional basis-set expansions in the geminal and in two Jastrow-factor constructions. The resulting basis-free Jastrow--AGP ansatz is optimized by variational Monte Carlo and is designed to separate two tasks: the AGP part defines the nodal surface, while the neural-network Jastrow factor recovers dynamical correlation at fixed nodes. This separation makes it possible to distinguish errors associated with dynamical correlation from those caused by static, multireference correlation. Applications to the hydrogen molecule and the rectangular hydrogen tetramer show sub-millihartree accuracy when the AGP nodes are adequate, and expose the residual nodal limitation near the large-radius square geometry of the hydrogen tetramer. These results clarify where neural-network building blocks can improve a compact geminal ansatz and where additional nodal flexibility is required.

### [36] [Enriched categories, real metrics and Lorentz manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18088)
*Marco Grandis*

Main category: math.CT

TL;DR: 本文综述性地将基于丰富范畴（enriched categories）的广义度规理论与洛伦兹流形（Lorentz manifolds）两个领域联系起来，通过将相对论时空中的实值度规及其反度规（antimetric）纳入Lawvere度规空间的范畴论框架，展示了如何将带实值度规的空间视为对称幺半闭范畴（symmetric monoidal closed category）上的丰富范畴。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者旨在桥接范畴论与相对论两个领域，将相对论时空的度规结构置于范畴论（category theory）的坚实基础之上，从而推广Lawvere关于度规空间的经典范畴论表述。

Method: 作者将相对论时空中的实值度规ρ(x, y)及其反度规γ(x, y) = -ρ(x, y)（满足反向三角不等式）纳入范畴论框架，将带实值度规的空间视为扩展实数线（extended real line）上的丰富范畴，其中扩展实数线被构造为对称幺半闭范畴。

Result: 论文指出，反度规γ(x, y)作为y的函数，在x的光锥（lightcone）上为零，在x的时间锥（timecone）上为正，在不受x影响的全部事件上为-∞；所有这些性质均可通过范畴论得到严格描述。

Conclusion: 这项工作表明，相对论时空的度规结构可以自然地嵌入Lawvere的范畴论度规空间框架中，为两个领域的交叉研究提供了形式化的理论基础。

Abstract: This expository article brings together two subjects: generalised metrics based on enriched categories, on the one hand, and Lorentz manifolds, on the other, at the price of dealing with details that are well known either in category theory or in relativity.
  The spacetime of relativity can be given a real valued metric $ρ(x, y)$, with values in the extended real line, or better (if equivalently) a real valued `antimetric' $γ(x, y) = - ρ(x, y)$ (satisfying a reverse triangle inequality); the latter, as a function of $y$, is positive on the timecone of $x$, annihilates on its lightcone, and is $- \infty$ on all events which cannot be influenced by $x$.
  All this can be given a well-established base in category theory, extending Lawvere's notion of a metric space. In fact, a space with a real valued metric can be viewed as an enriched category on the extended real line, structured as a symmetric monoidal closed category.

</details>

### [37] [Is the Binary Black Hole Population Inference from Gravitational-Wave Data Robust?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16510)
*Upasana Das,Suvodip Mukherjee*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文研究表明，引力波波形建模的不确定性会显著扭曲双黑洞（binary black holes, BBHs）质量分布中的推断特征，这种系统性误差甚至可能超过统计不确定性，因此在进行天体物理种群分析时必须考虑波形系统误差，以实现可靠的测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波观测已初步揭示双黑洞质量分布中可能存在的精细结构（features），这些特征有望关联不同的BBH形成机制并导出重要的天体物理论断。然而，这些特征是真实的天体物理信号还是源于未知的系统误差，目前尚不明确，因此需要系统评估波形建模不确定性对质量分布推断的影响。

Method: 本文通过对比统计不确定性与波形建模系统误差的尺度，量化分析了波形不确定性对BBH质量分布中特征结构的扭曲程度，并探讨了系统误差的典型标度关系（scaling）。

Result: 波形建模不确定性能够显著扭曲BBH质量分布中的推断特征，其影响幅度甚至超过统计不确定性，在现有探测器水平下尤为明显。该效应在对不稳定超新星（pair instability supernovae, PISN）质量间隙下边缘附近达到峰值，同时也会影响幂律分布的斜率。

Conclusion: 为确认BBH质量分布中天体物理特征的可靠检测，并将其与BBH形成通道建立联系，必须在种群分析中纳入波形系统误差的考量。本文还提出了若干缓解该效应的途径，以提升未来测量的稳健性。

Abstract: Gravitational-wave observations are playing an instrumental role in understanding the population of binary compact objects in the Universe. These observations have begun to hint at the mass distribution of binary black holes (BBHs), with tentative evidence for features in the mass distribution beyond a simple power-law. Such features, hence, can be connected with different formation scenarios of BBHs and lead to important astrophysical conclusions. However, it is crucial to understand whether these features are truly astrophysical or connected with any unknown systematics. We show in this work that waveform modelling uncertainties can significantly distort inferred features in the BBH mass distribution, which can be more pronounced than the statistical uncertainty, even with the current generation detectors, which can peak close to the lower edge of the pair instability supernovae (PISN) mass gap, and also can impact the slope of the power-law distribution. So, in order to have a confirmed detection of astrophysical features in the BBH mass distribution and connecting them with BBH formation channels, it is important to consider waveform systematics in the astrophysical population analysis. We show the typical scaling of the systematic error and discuss a few avenues to mitigate this effect for robust measurements in the future.

### [38] [Nonlinear electrodynamics in magnetars: systematic effects on radius constraints and timing analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17048)
*Gabriel A. Porto,Jonas P. Pereira,Eduardo Bittencourt,Elda Guzmán-Herrera*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文揭示非线性电动力学（Nonlinear Electrodynamics, NLED）显著改变磁星（magnetar）附近光子的传播路径，使其偏离标准零测地线（null-geodesics）。忽略这一效应会导致通过射线追踪（ray-tracing）技术推断的恒星半径产生约10%的相对误差，并引入约350纳秒的系统性最小传播时间延迟，远超NICER等任务100纳秒的时间分辨率。该结果对当前及未来X射线脉冲轮廓（X-ray pulse profiles）观测数据的精确解释至关重要，并指出NLED也可能影响其他天体物理现象（如glitches和antiglitches）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁星表面磁场强度可达10^15高斯，在此超临界尺度下，麦克斯韦线性电动力学被非线性电动力学（NLED）取代。虽然真空双折射（vacuum birefringence）已为NLED效应提供了初步观测证据，但其对光子传播的更广泛影响仍未被充分探索。

Method: 通过理论分析，研究NLED在磁星附近如何改变光子传播，使其偏离标准零测地线；并基于射线追踪技术和传播时间计算量化相关效应。

Result: 忽略NLED修正会导致通过射线追踪技术推断的恒星半径产生约10%的相对误差，并诱导出约350纳秒的系统性最小传播时间延迟，该值已远超NICER任务100纳秒的时间分辨率。

Conclusion: 这些结果对于解释当前及未来观测站（如eXTP）的X射线脉冲轮廓数据至关重要，后者依赖高精度光弯曲（light-bending）和计时模型来确定中子星的质量和半径。此外，磁星可作为研究超致密物质和超临界场物理的重要窗口，NLED也可能影响其他天体物理可观测现象（如glitches和antiglitches）。

Abstract: Magnetars are among the most extreme laboratories in the universe, harboring surface magnetic fields reaching $10^{15}$~G. At these supercritical scales, Maxwell's linear electrodynamics is superseded by Nonlinear Electrodynamics (NLED). While vacuum birefringence has provided initial observational evidence for these effects, its broader impact on photon propagation remains largely unexplored. In this work, we demonstrate that NLED significantly alters photon propagation in the vicinity of magnetars, deviating light from standard null-geodesics. We estimate that neglecting these corrections leads to relative errors in inferred stellar radii by means of ray-tracing techniques of approximately $10\%$. Furthermore, we find that NLED induces a systematic minimal travel-time delay of approximately $350~n$s, a value that already far exceeds the $100$~ns temporal resolution of missions like NICER. These results are critical for the interpretation of X-ray pulse profiles from current and future observatories, such as eXTP, which rely on high-precision light-bending and timing models to determine neutron-star masses and radii. Finally, our results underscore the role of magnetars as a vital window into the physics of superdense matter and supercritical fields, and we briefly highlight other astrophysical observables--such as glitches and antiglitches--that may be affected by NLED.

</details>


### [39] [Higher-order statistics of the stochastic gravitational wave background from supermassive black hole binaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17983)
*Hinano Hisamamtsu,Koutarou Kyutoku*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文提出通过引入物理下限 z_min 解决引力波背景高阶统计量（方差、偏度、峰度）在红移积分中的发散问题，并证明在高阶统计量中，所有超出期望值的统计量仅依赖于啁啾质量的加权平均 <M^{10/3}>，与红移演化模型无关；方差与期望值之比可独立于总合并数提供啁啾质量比的信息，峰度与偏度平方之间存在一致性关系，可用于检验引力波背景的双星起源假说。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统引力波背景分析主要关注频谱幅度和频率依赖，而高阶统计量（如方差、偏度、峰度）有潜力提取更多物理信息，但这些统计量在红移积分延伸至 z=0 时发散。本文旨在解决这一发散问题，并探索高阶统计量如何为引力波背景的物理解释提供新工具。

Method: 提出引入物理驱动的红移积分下限 z_min，该下限由探测单个源（individual sources）的灵敏度定义；在高阶统计量的计算中采用红移最低阶近似（lowest-order approximation with respect to redshift），因其主要由局域源（local sources）贡献。

Result: 所有超出期望值的高阶统计量仅依赖于质量函数通过啁啾质量（chirp mass）的加权平均 <M^{10/3}>，与红移演化模型无关；方差与期望值之比提供 <M^{10/3}>/<M^{5/3}> 的信息，且独立于总合并数；峰度与偏度平方之间存在一致性关系。

Conclusion: 高阶统计量为引力波背景的诠释提供了新视角，能够打破现有简并性并改进对质量函数的理解，同时峰度与偏度平方的一致性关系为检验引力波背景的双星起源假说（binary-origin hypothesis）铺平了道路。

Abstract: Recent progress in gravitational wave observations has positioned Pulsar Timing Arrays as a key tool for detecting the stochastic gravitational wave background in the nanohertz band. It is widely believed that this background is primarily attributed to the cosmic ensemble of inspiraling supermassive black hole binaries. While traditional analyses have predominantly focused on the spectral amplitude and frequency dependence of the gravitational wave background, higher-order statistics such as variance, skewness, and kurtosis could potentially be useful for extracting further physical information. However, these statistical moments are known to diverge when the redshift integration is extended down to z=0. In this study, we propose a strategy to resolve this issue by introducing a physically motivated lower integration limit, z_min, defined by the sensitivity for detecting individual sources. Since higher-order statistics are primarily determined by local sources, we may adopt the lowest-order approximation with respect to redshift in their computations. Under this approximation, we demonstrate that all higher-order statistics beyond the expectation value depend on the mass function only through a weighted average of the chirp mass, <\mathcal{M}^{10/3}>, irrespective of the redshift evolution model. We show that the ratio of the variance to the expectation value provides information on <\mathcal{M}^{10/3}>/<\mathcal{M}^{5/3}> independently of the total number of mergers. We also find a consistency relation between the kurtosis and the squared skewness, paving the way for testing the binary-origin hypothesis of the gravitational wave background. Our findings demonstrate that higher-order statistics provide a new window for interpreting the gravitational wave background, offering a methodology to break existing degeneracies and refine our understanding of the mass function.

</details>


### [40] [A universal framework to identify eccentric binary mergers: GW200105 case study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18742)
*Teagan A. Clarke,Isobel M. Romero-Shaw,Charlie Hoy,Jakob Stegmann,Paul D. Lasky,Eric Thrane*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文以候选偏心（eccentric）中子星-黑洞并合事件GW200105_162426为案例，展示了引力波信号中偏心率的测量结果高度依赖于参考频率（reference frequency）的选取和先验（prior）选择。通过提出一种不依赖参考频率的探测统计量，并边缘化（marginalise）天体物理启发的偏心率分布，发现支持偏心假说的证据减弱，对GW200105_162426的偏心解释提出质疑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波信号中的轨道偏心率（orbital eccentricity）是判别致密双星并合形成通道（formation channel）的重要指标。已有多个双黑洞并合及一个中子星-黑洞（neutron star--black hole）并合事件报告了偏心率迹象，但不同研究对同一事件的识别结果和显著性存在分歧。偏心率测量的结果会因先验选择和参考频率的不同而改变，亟需统一和稳健的统计方法。

Method: 以候选偏心中子星-黑洞并合事件GW200105_162426为案例，采用不同的先验（prior）参考频率（reference frequency）进行比对分析。提出一种不依赖于参考频率的探测统计量（detection statistic），该统计量边缘化（marginalise）了具有天体物理动机（astrophysically-motivated）的偏心率分布，以消除参考频率选择带来的偏差。

Result: 不同研究之间报告的偏心率结果差异，部分可以通过考虑偏心率随参考频率的演化来调和。使用新提出的探测统计量后，对于GW200105_162426，偏心、自旋对齐（aligned-spin）假说相对于准圆（quasi-circular）、进动（precessing）假说的自然对数贝叶斯因子（natural log Bayes factor）ln B ≤ 0.9，支持偏心假说的证据减弱。

Conclusion: 研究结果对GW200105_162426的偏心解释提出质疑，强调在分析引力波信号的偏心率时，必须建模和纳入偏心率的天体物理分布（astrophysical distributions），以避免先验和参考频率选择带来的误导性结论。

Abstract: Orbital eccentricity in gravitational-wave signals from merging compact object binaries is a powerful indicator of their formation channel. Several binary black hole mergers and a neutron star--black hole merger have been reported to exhibit signs of eccentricity, but which events are identified and the significance of the eccentricity differs between studies. Measurements of eccentricity can change depending on the choice of prior. The choice of prior is subtle: eccentricity is commonly measured at an arbitrary reference frequency, which varies from study to study. We use the candidate eccentric neutron star--black hole merger GW200105_162426 as a case study, employing a range of priors and reference frequencies, and find the results to be strongly prior-driven. We show that the varied results reported across different studies can be partially reconciled by accounting for the evolution of eccentricity with reference frequency. In order to make conclusive statements about eccentricity, we propose a detection statistic that does not depend on reference frequency, and which marginalises over astrophysically-motivated distributions in eccentricity. Using this detection statistic, we find reduced support for the eccentric hypothesis for GW200105_162426: we obtain a natural log Bayes factor ln B $\leq$ 0.9 comparing the eccentric, aligned-spin hypothesis to the quasi-circular, precessing hypothesis. Our results cast doubt on the eccentric interpretation of GW200105_162426 and underscore the importance of modelling the astrophysical distributions of eccentricity in nature.

</details>

### [41] [Positive-rate PCA and IPS with stationary Bernoulli measures are rapidly forgetful](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16904)
*Irène Marcovici,Siamak Taati*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文证明了：具有严格正转移概率且存在平稳伯努利测度的概率元胞自动机（probabilistic cellular automaton）是指数遍历（exponentially ergodic）的；有限区域的混合时间（mixing time）随区域直径对数增长。该结论也适用于连续时间下正速率、有限程相互作用粒子系统。证明基于熵（entropy）方法，并将系统表示为带噪声系统的扰动。在二维及更高维中，是否具有此类性质在算法上不可区分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解概率性相互作用系统的遍历行为（ergodic behaviour）及其混合速率的底层机制，特别是噪声积累与局部信息交换之间的竞争如何决定系统的统计力学（statistical mechanics）性质。

Method: 使用熵（entropy）方法，将目标系统表示为另一带噪声系统的扰动（perturbation），通过分析噪声导致的随机性积累与局部信息交换导致的随机性扩散之间的竞争，推导遍历性和混合时间上界。

Result: 证明了正转移概率且存在平稳伯努利测度的概率元胞自动机必然指数遍历，其有限区域混合时间与区域直径成对数关系。该结果同样适用于正速率、有限程相互作用粒子系统。此外，在二维及更高维中，是否满足上述条件的系统在算法上不可区分（algorithmically indistinguishable）。

Conclusion: 噪声的存在足以驱动系统快速混合至平稳状态，且这种混合速度在低维（一维）与高维（二维及以上）之间存在算法可判定性上的根本差异。

Abstract: We prove that every probabilistic cellular automaton with strictly positive transition probabilities that admits a stationary Bernoulli measure is exponentially ergodic. Moreover, the mixing time of any finite region in such a system is logarithmic in the diameter of the region. A similar result holds in continuous time for positive-rate, finite-range interacting particle systems. The proofs use entropy, and rely on a representation of the system as a perturbation of another system with noise. The ergodic behaviour results from a competition between the accumulation of randomness due to noise and the diffusion of randomness due to local information exchange. We show that, in two and higher dimensions, the positive-rate probabilistic cellular automata that admit stationary Bernoulli measures are algorithmically indistinguishable from those that do not.

### [42] [Zero correlations and averaged fields of orthonormal Gaussian functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17296)
*Luís Daniel Abreu,Tomoyuki Shirai*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该论文研究由高斯整函数（Gaussian Entire Function）通过Landau升算子迭代生成的一族高斯随机函数零点过程，发现其归一化配对关联表现出类似于正交多项式零点的交错模式（repulsion for k=1, attraction for k=2, no correlation for k≥3），并证明了平均场的几乎必然收敛及波动的高斯极限定理，为ConceFT等高分辨率时频算法的有效性提供了理论依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于信号处理中的实际问题，特别是验证Flandrin和Bayram-Baraniuk的猜想，并为Daubechies、Wang和Wu提出的高分辨率时频算法ConceFT的效率提供理论解释。

Method: 方法包括：(1) 通过Landau升算子迭代高斯整函数，生成一族在期望意义下逐点正交的高斯随机函数；(2) 分析零点过程的归一化配对关联（normalized pair correlations）；(3) 建立复域紧集上平均场的几乎必然收敛性和相应标度波动的泛函中心极限定理（functional central limit theorem）。

Result: 主要结果：(1) 配对关联函数g_{n,n+k}在w→z时表现出模式：k=1时排斥（repulsion），k=2时吸引（attraction），k≥3时无短程二阶关联；(2) 平均场的几乎必然收敛于常数1；(3) 标度波动收敛到由实白噪声（real white noise）指示函数积分定义的高斯过程。

Conclusion: 结论：零点关联模式与正交多项式零点交错经典现象的相似性，以及与白噪声谱图（spectrogram）的等价性，为ConceFT算法的高分辨率性能提供了理论依据，并确认了Flandrin和Bayram-Baraniuk的猜想。

Abstract: We consider the family of point processes $\{\mathcal{Z}_{f_{n}}\}_{n=0}^{\infty}$ of zeros of Gaussian random functions $\{f_{n}(z,\overline{z})\}_{n=0}^{\infty} $, arising from the Gaussian Entire Function \[ f_{0}(z):=\sum_{k=0}^{\infty} ζ_{k} \frac{z^{k}}{\sqrt{k!}}, \quad ζ_{k} \sim N_{\mathbb{C}}(0,1)\text{ i.i.d.} \] by iteration of the Landau raising operator, and orthonormal at each point in expectation in the sense that \[ \mathbb{E}\left[ e^{-\left\vert z\right\vert^{2}}f_{n}(z,\overline{z})\overline{f_{n^{\prime }}(z,\overline{z})}\right] ={δ}_{nn'}. \] We first show that the normalized pair correlations $g_{n,n+k}(z,w)$ of the pairs $(\mathcal{Z}_{f_{n}},\mathcal{Z}_{f_{n+k}})$ exhibit \emph{a pattern reminiscent of the classical interlacing of zeros of orthogonal polynomials}: when $w\rightarrow z$, $g_{n,n+k}$ displays repulsion for $k=1$, attraction for $k=2$, and no short-range second-order correlation for $k \ge 3$. We complement this with the convergence of real-valued averaged fields on compacts $K \subset \mathbb{C}$, \[ \lim_{N \to \infty} \frac{1}{N}\sum_{n=0}^{N-1}\left\vert f_{n}(z,\overline{z})e^{-\frac{\left\vert z\right\vert^{2}}{2}} \right\vert^{2} \rightarrow 1 \quad \text{ almost surely in $C(K)$}, \] and a functional central limit theorem for the corresponding scaled fluctuations, which converge to the Gaussian process \[\mathcal{G}(z) = \frac{1}{\sqrtπ} \int_{\mathbb{C}} \mathbf{1}_{B(z,1)}(u) dW_{\mathbb{R}}(u), \] where $W_{\mathbb{R}}$ denotes real white noise on $\mathbb{C}$ and $B(z,1)$ is the unit disk centered at $z$. The results are motivated by problems in signal processing. Due to an identification with white noise spectrograms, they confirm conjectures of Flandrin and Bayram-Baraniuk and provide a rationale for the efficiency of high resolution time-frequency algorithms, namely \emph{ConceFT}, by Daubechies, Wang and Wu.

</details>


### [43] [Limit theorems for random walks with spatio-temporal drift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17725)
*Ngo P. N. Ngoc,Tuan-Minh Nguyen*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类离散时间随机游走（discrete-time random walk），其条件漂移（conditional drift）随时间呈多项式衰减、随当前位置到原点距离呈多项式增长。在矩条件假设下，分析了线性情形中的相变（phase transition）以及非线性情形中三种不同行为分区的极限分布。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此类随机游走与多个自相互作用随机过程（self-interacting random processes）模型相关，理解其渐近行为具有理论意义。

Method: 假设增量具有 p>2 阶矩，分析漂移的线性和非线性两种情形。线性情形中研究归一化过程收敛到高斯极限（Gaussian limit）的相变；非线性情形中识别出由一条临界线（critical line）划分的三个不同分区。

Result: 线性情形中，归一化过程依分布收敛到高斯极限存在相变。非线性情形中，三个分区分别表现出：依分布收敛到高斯分布、收敛到随机微分方程（stochastic differential equation）平稳分布给出的非高斯极限、以及几乎必然局域化（almost sure localization）于超球面（hypersphere）上。

Conclusion: 该随机游走模型在漂移的线性和非线性情形下均展现出丰富的渐近行为，包括相变和多分区特性，揭示了漂移形式对极限分布的深刻影响。

Abstract: We study a class of discrete-time random walks in $\mathbb{R}^d$ whose conditional drift decays polynomially in time and grows polynomially with the distance from the origin to the current position. This class is related to several models of self-interacting random processes. We determine the asymptotic behavior of the walk under the assumption that its increments have moments of order $p$ for some $p>2$. In the linear case, where the drift depends linearly on the current position, we establish a phase transition in the convergence in distribution of the normalized process to Gaussian limits. In the nonlinear case, we identify three distinct regimes separated by a critical line and show that the normalized process exhibits qualitatively different behaviors in each regime, including convergence in distribution to a Gaussian law, convergence to a non-Gaussian limit given by the stationary distribution of a stochastic differential equation, and almost sure localization on a hypersphere.

### [45] [On transposed Poisson conformal superalgebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17747)
*Hao Fang,Lamei Yuan*

Main category: math.RA

TL;DR: 本文引入并研究了转置泊松共形超代数（transposed Poisson conformal superalgebras）及其非交换变体，证明了其张量积结构、与Hom-李共形超代数的关系，以及基于已知李共形超代数分类的全部兼容结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将转置泊松代数（transposed Poisson algebras）推广到共形超代数（conformal superalgebras）的Z₂分次（Z₂-graded）框架下，填补该领域在超代数与共形结构交叉方向的研究空白。

Method: 通过转置共形超-莱布尼茨法则（transposed conformal super-Leibniz rule）推导恒等式族；在C[∂]上构造张量积（tensor product）并证明其自然继承转置泊松共形超代数结构；利用Hom-李共形超代数（Hom-Lie conformal superalgebras）建立关联；修改李共形括号（modified Lie conformal brackets）以及来自Novikov-Poisson、pre-Lie交换、微分Novikov-Poisson、pre-Lie泊松共形超代数的构造。

Result: 导出由转置共形超-莱布尼茨法则强制的一组恒等式；证明两个此类超代数的张量积仍具有转置泊松共形超代数结构；揭示其与Hom-李共形超代数的密切关系，并给出泊松共形超代数与转置泊松共形超代数之间的兼容条件（compatibility conditions）；基于秩为(1+1)的李共形超代数（Lie conformal superalgebras）分类，确定其上的所有兼容结构。

Conclusion: 转置泊松共形超代数是一类结构丰富的代数对象，其张量积封闭性及与多种已知代数结构（如Hom-李共形超代数、Novikov-Poisson共形超代数等）的兼容性表明该理论具有良好的延展性和应用潜力。

Abstract: We introduce and study transposed Poisson conformal superalgebras, the $\mathbb Z_2$-graded conformal analogues of transposed Poisson algebras, as well as their noncommutative variants. We derive a family of identities forced by the transposed conformal super-Leibniz rule and prove that the tensor product over $\mathbb C[\partial]$ of two such superalgebras again carries a natural transposed Poisson conformal superalgebra structure. Moreover, we display a close relationship between transposed Poisson conformal superalgebras and Hom-Lie conformal superalgebras, and give the compatibility conditions between a Poisson conformal superalgebra and a transposed Poisson conformal superalgebra. In addition, several constructions are obtained from modified Lie conformal brackets and from Novikov-Poisson, pre-Lie commutative, differential Novikov-Poisson, and pre-Lie Poisson conformal superalgebras. Finally, using the known classification of Lie conformal superalgebras of rank (1+1), we determine all compatible transposed Poisson conformal superalgebra structures on such superalgebras.

### [46] [Notes on obstructions in the hyperbolic Clifford algebra bundle structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16558)
*J. M. Hoff da Silva,E. Notte-Cuello*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文从障碍类（obstruction classes）的一般分析出发，研究了双曲克利福德代数（hyperbolic Clifford algebra）丛结构相关的障碍问题。通过考虑惠特尼和（Whitney sum）的特殊性，证明了与经典切丛（tangent bundle）情况不同，双曲标架丛（hyperbolic frame bundle）在没有任何拓扑障碍（topological obstruction）的情况下允许提升（lifting），从而使得在双曲克利福德丛（hyperbolic Clifford bundle）中总能定义旋量结构（spinor structure）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典切丛中定义旋量结构（spinor structure）常受到拓扑障碍（topological obstruction）的限制；本文旨在探索在双曲克利福德丛（hyperbolic Clifford bundle）的框架下是否能够规避这些障碍。

Method: 从障碍类（obstruction classes）的一般分析出发，结合双曲克利福德代数（hyperbolic Clifford algebra）的丛结构，并考虑惠特尼和（Whitney sum）带来的特殊性，对双曲标架丛（hyperbolic frame bundle）的提升条件进行拓扑分析。

Result: 与经典切丛（tangent bundle）情况不同，双曲标架丛（hyperbolic frame bundle）在提升过程中不存在任何拓扑障碍（topological obstruction）。

Conclusion: 由于双曲标架丛的提升不存在拓扑障碍，双曲克利福德丛（hyperbolic Clifford bundle）中总是可以定义旋量结构（spinor structure）。

Abstract: Starting from a general analysis of obstruction classes, we develop the investigation of obstructions associated with the bundle structure of the hyperbolic Clifford algebra. By taking into account particularities arising from the Whitney sum, it is shown that, unlike classical tangent bundle cases, the hyperbolic frame bundle admits lifting without any topological obstruction. This leads to the possibility of always defining spinor structures in hyperbolic Clifford bundles.
