### [47] [Long-time stability for nonlinear Maryland models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16624)
*Ruijie Cui,Zhiyan Zhao*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对d维非线性Maryland模型，证明在合适的丢番图条件下，当非线性强度和初始扰动足够小时，加权的多项式ℓ²-范数在长达ε^{-1}ε^{-M_*}的时间尺度上保持有界稳定性，证明基于Birkhoff正则型方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非线性系统（nonlinear system）在长时演化中是否保持稳定性是动力学核心问题之一，特别对于拟周期离散系统（quasiperiodic discrete system），如Maryland模型，其长期行为尚不完全清楚。本文旨在建立此类系统在加权范数下的多项式长时间稳定性（polynomial long-time stability）。

Method: 采用Birkhoff正则型方法（Birkhoff normal form procedure）进行证明。该方法通过逐步正则化消去非线性项中产生共振的低阶部分，从而在足够长的时间尺度上控制解的范数增长。

Result: 对于满足丢番图条件（Diophantine condition）的频率向量ϖ，且相位参数x属于R/Z的几乎全测度子集（almost full-measure subset），当耦合参数|ε|充分小时，初始加权ℓ²-范数\|q(0)\|_s为O(ε)量级的解，在时间|t| ≤ ε^{-1}ε^{-M_*}内满足\|q(t)\|_s = O(ε)，其中M_*可任意取正整数。

Conclusion: 本文证明了高维非线性Maryland模型在拟周期位势下存在多项式长时间的范数稳定性，将传统一维结果推广到任意维度；该稳定性时间尺度随初始小量ε的负幂次增长，且可通过调整参数M_*任意延长。

Abstract: For the $d-$dimensional nonlinear Maryland model \begin{equation}\label{eq-abs} \ri\partial_t q_n=\tanπ(n\cdot\varpi+x)q_n+ε(Δq)_n+|q_n|^2q_n,\quad n\in{\Z^d}, \end{equation} with $d\in\N^*$, $ε\in \R$ and $\varpi\in\R^d$ satisfying a suitable Diophantine condition, we establish polynomial long-time stability of polynomially weighted $\ell^2$-norm $$\|q(t)\|_s:=\left(\sum_{n\in{\Z^d}}|q_n|^2 (1+|n|^2)^{s}\right)^{\frac{1}{2}},\quad s>0. $$ More precisely, given any $M_*\in\N^*$, for phase parameters $x$ belonging to an almost full-measure subset of $\R/\Z$, if $|ε|$ is sufficiently small, then solutions $q(t)$ of Eq. (\ref{eq-abs}) with high-order weighted $\ell^2$-norm $\|q(0)\|_s$ of sufficiently small size $\varepsilon$ satisfy $$\|q(t)\|_s=\CO(\varepsilon),\quad \forall \ |t|\leq ε^{-1}\varepsilon^{-M_*}. $$ The proof relies on a Birkhoff normal form procedure.

</details>


### [48] [Resolving the viscosity operator ambiguity on Riemannian manifolds via a kinematic selection principle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17502)
*Zhi-Wei Wang,Samuel L. Braunstein*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究黎曼流形上Navier-Stokes方程的不同粘性算子表述，指出变形拉普拉斯算子（deformation Laplacian）由运动学构造唯一确定，而霍奇拉普拉斯算子（Hodge Laplacian）在运动学步骤中被排除。在薄膜极限下，算子的选择取决于边界条件：无应力条件恢复变形拉普拉斯算子，霍奇边界条件恢复霍奇拉普拉斯算子。变形的拉普拉斯在负曲率曲面上的能量不等式和弱解适定性方面具有优势，而霍奇拉普拉斯则存在分析障碍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在一般黎曼流形上，Navier-Stokes方程存在多种不等价的粘性算子表述，但缺乏统一的选择准则。本文旨在从运动学构造和薄膜极限两个角度澄清哪种算子是物理上和数学上自然的选择，并解决霍奇拉普拉斯在负曲率流形上能量不等式失效的分析障碍。

Method: 采用拉格朗日运动学构造（Lagrangian kinematic construction），通过李拖曳（Lie-dragged）连接向量内积变化率构建应变率（strain rate），并利用内积几何的对称性排除霍奇拉普拉斯。进一步通过三维环境流的薄膜极限分析，结合边界条件（无应力与霍奇边界）的显式分解，识别出不同算子对应的物理情境。

Result: 变形拉普拉斯算子由运动学构造唯一选出，霍奇拉普拉斯在运动学步骤中被排除。在薄膜极限下，无应力（Navier slip）边界条件恢复变形拉普拉斯，霍奇边界条件恢复霍奇拉普拉斯。在双曲平面 $\HH^2$ 上，变形拉普拉斯满足能量不等式而霍奇拉普拉斯不满足；在任何高斯曲率有负上界（negative constant）的完备二维流形上，带变形拉普拉斯的不可压Navier-Stokes方程存在唯一全局弱解且能量指数衰减。

Conclusion: 黎曼流形上的Navier-Stokes方程应优先采用变形拉普拉斯算子作为粘性算子，因其具有运动学自然性、边界条件一致性以及更好的数学适定性（well-posedness）。霍奇拉普拉斯在负曲率情形下存在根本性的分析缺陷，不适合作为流体粘性算子。

Abstract: On a general Riemannian manifold the Navier-Stokes equations admit several inequivalent formulations, differing in the choice of viscous operator: the Hodge Laplacian, the Bochner Laplacian, or the deformation Laplacian. We show that a Lagrangian kinematic construction, in which the strain rate is built from the rate of change of inner products of Lie-dragged connecting vectors, uniquely selects the deformation Laplacian for fluids whose configuration space is intrinsically the manifold. The Hodge Laplacian is excluded at the kinematic step (before introducing constitutive assumptions) because the strain rate constructed from inner-product geometry is symmetric and has no antisymmetric part. We further show that when the fluid arises as a thin-shell limit of an ambient three-dimensional flow, the operator that emerges depends on the boundary condition imposed in the normal direction: stress-free (Navier slip) conditions recover the deformation Laplacian, while Hodge boundary conditions recover the Hodge Laplacian, via an explicit decomposition of the ambient Bochner Laplacian into intrinsic and extrinsic pieces. The intrinsic piece is the deformation Laplacian regardless of the boundary condition. As an analytical confirmation, we show that the kinematic selection is consistent with the known failure of the energy inequality for the Hodge Laplacian on the hyperbolic plane $\HH^2$: the deformation Laplacian is coercive on $\HH^2$ while the Hodge Laplacian is not, because the Ricci term has the opposite sign in the two operators. We further prove that on any complete two-dimensional manifold with Gaussian curvature bounded above by a negative constant, the incompressible Navier-Stokes equation with the deformation Laplacian admits a unique global weak solution with exponential energy decay, resolving the analytical obstruction preventing the corresponding result for the Hodge Laplacian.

</details>


### [49] [Where solitons are in a KdV soliton gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18093)
*Benjamin Doyon*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对KdV孤子气体在有限密度下孤子位置的定义问题，提出了一种基于流体胞投影（fluid-cell projection）的新方法，证明了其在不引入辐射修正的情况下保持KdV场性质，并建立了与广义流体动力学（Generalised Hydrodynamics）中半经典Bethe方程的联系，为非随机性孤子气体动力学提供了严格数学基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: KdV方程作为可积经典场（integrable classical field）的典范模型，其孤子气体（soliton gas）的核心分析对象——态密度（density of states）——依赖于单位长度的孤子数目。然而，当多个孤子彼此靠近时，其形状发生畸变，无法直接从KdV场中显式识别孤子位置。因此，需要在宏观极限（macroscopic limit）下为有限密度孤子定义合理的位置判据。

Method: 本文提出一种流体胞投影（fluid-cell projection）方法：将在介观区域（mesoscopic region）外的孤子投影掉，使得KdV场在该区域内保持不变，并支撑于一个多孤子场（multi-soliton field）上。核心工具是本文首次引入的多孤子KdV场的tau函数（tau function），该函数还用于推导多孤子支撑集增长的新界以及场及其导数的上确界（supremum）界。

Result: 证明了所定义孤子位置与流体胞投影满足预期性质，且不引入辐射修正（radiative corrections）；验证了守恒密度的弱极限（weak limit）可通过态密度计算；在大尺度上，孤子位置满足广义流体动力学框架下的半经典Bethe方程（semi-classical Bethe equations），该方程体现了二体散射位移（two-body scattering shift）和因子化散射（factorised scattering）；非严格推导重现了Gennady El于2003年利用Witham调制理论从有限能隙解得到的KdV孤子气体动力学方程。

Conclusion: 本结论在谱参数的简单条件和冲击参数（impact parameters）的物理自然条件下成立，且无需随机性假设。多孤子KdV场tau函数的方法有望推广至其他孤子模型（solitonic models）。

Abstract: The Korteweg-De Vries (KdV) equation is a paradigmatic model of integrable classical fields, admitting solitoning solutions. When many solitons are near to each other, their shapes are modified, and it is not manifest, from the KdV field, where they are. This is a key problem in the analysis of a soliton gas, as its main object, the density of states, is a number of solitons per unit length. How to define solitons' positions at finite densities in the macroscopic limit? A sensible criterium is that, projecting out solitons lying outside a mesoscopic region, the KdV field is unchanged in this region, and the result is a multi-soliton field supported there. In the context of emergent hydrodynamics, this is referred to as a fluid-cell projection. In this paper we solve this problem. We define solitons' positions and a fluid-cell projection, and show that it has these properties, without introducing radiative corrections. We show that the weak limit of conserved densities can be evaluated using the density of states. On large scales the solitons' positions satisfy the semi-classical Bethe equations introduced in the context Generalised Hydrodynamics, that accounts for the two-body scattering shift and encodes factorised scattering. A non-rigorous derivation reproduces the kinetic equation of the KdV soliton gas, first proposed by Gennady El in 2003 using Witham modulation theory from finite-gap solutions. The results hold under simple conditions on spectral parameters, and certain physically natural conditions on impact parameters. No randomness is required. Our proof is based on a novel tau function for the multi-soliton KdV field, which also allows us to obtain new bounds on the growth of the multi-soliton support and on the supremum of the field and its derivatives. We believe the methods are generalisable to other solitonic models.

</details>


### [50] [Arbitrary-genus dark soliton gases in the defocusing nonlinear Schrödinger hydrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18651)
*Marco Bertola,Deng-Shan Wang,Peng Yan,Dinghao Zhu*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次引入暗孤子气体（dark soliton gas）的任意亏格势（arbitrary-genus potential），通过无穷多暗孤子极限构造，利用Deift-Zhou非线性最速下降法解析研究其大空间渐近行为与长时间演化，揭示了从调制/未调制高亏格区域到平面区域的级联行为，并得到数值验证的完美支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 聚焦非线性薛定谔（defocusing nonlinear Schrödinger）流体动力学在有限密度边界条件下支持精确暗孤子，但暗孤子气体的相互作用系综尚未被研究。作者旨在填补这一空白，系统刻画暗孤子气体的统计与动力学行为。

Method: 考虑$\mathcal{N}$个暗孤子解在$\mathcal{N}\to\infty$极限下的渐近行为，构造暗孤子气体的任意亏格势。采用Deift-Zhou非线性最速下降法（nonlinear steepest descent approach）解析分析该势的大空间渐近形式与长时间演化。此外，通过数值模拟验证理论结果。

Result: 亏格-$N$（genus-$N$）暗孤子气体势在$x\to-\infty$时趋近于亏格-$N$有限间隙解（finite-gap solution），在$x\to+\infty$时趋近于背景$1$。长时间演化中，随自相似变量$\xi=x/t$增大，气体构型表现出级联行为：从未调制与调制的亏格-$N$区域依次过渡，逐步降至平面区域（未调制亏格-$0$区域）。低亏格孤子气体的演化可嵌入高亏格气体中，在特定区域内呈现相同动力学。数值结果与理论预测完全吻合。

Conclusion: 暗孤子气体势从高亏格到低亏格的级联演化行为可通过潜在谱（underlying spectra）编码，揭示了不同亏格孤子气体之间的动力学嵌入关系，为孤子气体理论提供了新的解析框架与数值验证。

Abstract: The defocusing nonlinear Schrödinger hydrodynamics supports exact dark solitons under finite density boundary conditions. However, the dark soliton gas, an interacting ensemble of dark solitons, has not yet been studied. In this work, we introduce an arbitrary-genus potential of dark soliton gases by considering the limit of the $\mathcal{N}$-dark soliton as $\mathcal{N}\to \infty$. The large-space asymptotics and long-time evolution of this dark soliton gas potential are analytically investigated through Deift-Zhou nonlinear steepest descent approach. The genus-$N$ dark soliton gas potential approaches the genus-$N$ finite-gap solution as $x \to -\infty$ and the background $1$ as $x \to +\infty$. In the long-time evolution, as the self-similar variable $ξ=x/t$ increases, the gas configuration exhibits a cascade of behaviours, passing from unmodulated and modulated genus-$N$ regions and progressively reducing the genus down to the planar region (unmodulated genus-$0$ region). Notably, the evolution of lower-genus soliton gases can be embedded within that of higher-genus gases, exhibiting identical dynamics within specific regimes. This phenomenon is encoded by the underlying spectra. We also include numerical validations, in perfect agreement with the theoretical predictions.

</details>


### [51] [Traveling Waves and Bumps in $p$-adic NNs]{Pseudo-Traveling Waves and Bumps in Quantum and Classical Hierarchical Cellular Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18717)
*W. A. Zúñiga-Galindo; B. A. Zambrano-Luna,Chayapuntika Indoung*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究定义在 p-adic 整数环上的两类层级蜂窝神经网络（CNN）的伪行波与凸起解的存在性，涵盖经典反应-扩散模型及其 Wick 旋转量子对应模型，并辅以数值模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将经典 Chua-Yang 蜂窝神经网络推广至 p-adic 框架，探索非阿基米德（non-Archimedean）背景下行波（traveling wave）行为的根本差异，并引入伪行波（pseudo-traveling wave）概念以处理层级无限网络中的有限截断问题。

Method: 在 p-adic 整数环上建立两类层级 CNN：一类由反应-扩散方程（reaction-diffusion equation）描述，另一类通过 Wick 旋转（Wick rotation）得到其量子模拟；状态由 p-adic 上的积分-微分方程（integro-differential equations）控制。引入伪行波作为 p-adic 球面上无限独立模式集合的有限截断。

Result: 证明了经典网络与量子网络中伪行波的存在性；同时证明了两种模型均存在与时间无关的凸起解（bumps）；数值模拟给出了量子 CNN 伪行波解的近似结果。

Conclusion: p-adic 层级 CNN 中的行波与阿基米德（Archimedean）情形存在本质差异，伪行波与凸起解的存在性为理解非阿基米德结构上的神经网络动力学提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We study the existence of pseudo-traveling waves and bump solutions for two classes of hierarchical cellular neural networks (CNNs) defined over the ring of $p$-adic integers $\mathbb{Z}_{p}$. The first type is a $p$-adic CNN described by a reaction-diffusion equation, while the second type is its quantum analog obtained via Wick rotation. The $p$-adic CNNs are hierarchical versions of the classical Chua-Yang CNNs; these networks have a tree-like hierarchical architecture with infinitely many cells and hidden layers. The states are governed by integro-differential equations on $% \mathbb{Z}_{p}$. The $p$-adic traveling waves behave fundamentally differently from their Archimedean counterparts. A traveling wave restricted to a $p$-adic sphere yields a countably infinite collection of independent patterns. We introduce the notion of pseudo-traveling waves as finite truncations of this structure and prove their existence for both the classical and quantum networks. We further establish the existence of time-independent solutions (bumps) for both models. Our theoretical results are complemented by numerical simulations that approximate pseudo-traveling-wave solutions for quantum CNNs.

</details>

### [52] [Photoluminescence of resin-based solder flux residue under ultraviolet excitation from 120 nm to 310 nm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16845)

TL;DR: 该研究测量了液氙探测器中常用商用焊剂（solder flux）残渣在真空紫外（VUV）光照射下的光致发光（photoluminescence）光谱和强度，发现所有测试的焊剂残渣在暴露于VUV光时均在可见光波段发光，可能对粒子探测器的本底（background）和事件重建（event reconstruction）造成干扰。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用紫外（UV）和真空紫外（VUV）光照射不同种类商用焊剂（solder flux）残渣，这些焊剂常用于液氙探测器，并测量其光致发光（photoluminescence）光谱和强度。

Result: 所有测试的焊剂残渣在暴露于真空紫外（VUV）光时，均在可见光（visible）波段产生光致发光（photoluminescence）。

Conclusion: 焊剂残渣的光致发光效应可能成为液氙等惰性液体粒子探测器中的意外本底信号来源，需要在探测器设计与事件重建中加以考虑。

Abstract: Nuisance photoluminescence is a potential source of background in particle detectors that use noble liquids as target material for galactic dark matter particles and neutrinos. Liquid argon and xenon scintillate in the vacuum ultraviolet (VUV) wavelength range in response to particle interactions. Photoluminescent materials that absorb these photons can cause unexpected signals that may impede event reconstruction in these detectors. We illuminated residue from different types of commercial solder flux commonly used in liquid xenon detectors with ultraviolet and VUV light and measured their photoluminescence spectra and intensities. We find that all tested flux residues photoluminesce in the visible spectral region when exposed to VUV light.

Method: 系统基于实验物理及工业控制系统（EPICS）框架构建，采用嵌入探测器的PT100铂电阻温度计监测液闪温度，实时采集温度数据以实现全面的热学监测；报警程序采用基于触发的机制（trigger-based mechanism），设置多级阈值（multi-level thresholds），在温度偏离安全范围时即时向操作人员发出警报。

Result: 该系统已稳定运行六个月，累计生成超过一千条报警记录，证明了其在保障实验安全稳定运行方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 该低温监测与报警系统能够满足TAO实验的实时温度监控和安全报警需求，为实验的可靠运行提供了重要保障。

Abstract: The Taishan Antineutrino Observatory (TAO) is a near-site experiment for the Jiangmen Underground Neutrino Observatory (JUNO). Its primary goal is to provide a precise reference reactor antineutrino energy spectrum, thereby eliminating the model dependence in reactor neutrino spectrum predictions and enhancing the sensitivity of the neutrino mass ordering measurement. To ensure accurate data acquisition and safe operation of the TAO experiment, a low-temperature monitoring and alarm system has been developed. Built on the Experimental Physics and Industrial Control System (EPICS) framework, the system employs PT100 platinum resistance thermometers embedded in the detector to monitor the temperature of the liquid scintillator. Real-time temperature data are acquired, enabling comprehensive thermal monitoring. The alarm program adopts a trigger-based mechanism with multi-level thresholds, providing instant alerts to operators when the temperature deviates from the safe range. The system has been operating stably for six months, accumulating over one thousand alarm records, and has proven effective in ensuring the safe and stable operation of the experiment.

### [54] [Wire-by-Wire Tracking Efficiency Plots: A New Diagnostic for the Belle~II Central Drift Chamber](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17381)
*Suryanarayan Mondal*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于逐丝（wire-by-wire）探测效率的诊断方法，用于Belle II中心漂移室（CDC）的径迹性能监测。该方法通过外推参考径迹（helix）到每一丝层，计算击中关联比例作为效率，能从蒙特卡洛模拟中揭示传统通道级诊断无法定位的局部径迹失效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型探测器通常只在通道级别（漂移时间、收集电荷、击中映射图）进行监测，这只能验证硬件是否工作，无法评估径迹重建性能。现有方法缺乏一种能够在单丝层面直接衡量径迹探测效率的诊断手段。

Method: 该方法模拟了基于外推的效率测量标准（extrapolation-based efficiency measurement standard），该标准最初为印度中微子观测站（INO）的阻性板室（RPC）探测器堆叠开发。具体步骤为：将一条参考径迹（螺旋线）外推到每个丝层（wire layer）；统计经过该层的径迹中，有多少条关联到实际击中（hit），计算比值作为该丝的效率。该方法已部署在Belle II的数据质量监测（DQM）框架中。

Result: 在蒙特卡洛模拟中，通过引入受控的死丝（dead-wire）条件进行了验证。结果表明，该方法能够发现传统通道级诊断无法察觉的局部径迹失效。所生成的结果图可直接为运行选择（run selection）、运行操作和长期老化研究提供反馈。

Conclusion: 该逐丝径迹效率诊断方法弥补了通道级硬件事后监测与径迹性能评估之间的空白，为探测器运行状态评估和老化跟踪提供了更精细、更直接的工具。

Abstract: Large detectors are often monitored at the channel level (drift time, collected charge, and hit maps), which validates hardware but not tracking performance. A wire-by-wire tracking efficiency diagnostic is presented for the Belle~II Central Drift Chamber~(CDC). The method is directly analogous to the extrapolation-based efficiency measurement standard in resistive-plate-chamber~(RPC) stacks developed for the India-based Neutrino Observatory~(INO). A reference track (helix) is extrapolated to each wire layer; the fraction of crossings that contain an associated hit defines the per-wire efficiency. Implemented in the Belle~II Data Quality Monitoring~(DQM) framework and validated on Monte Carlo simulation with controlled dead-wire conditions, the method reveals localised tracking failures that are invisible to conventional channel-level diagnostics. The resulting plots provide direct feedback for run selection, operations, and long-term ageing studies.

</details>


### [55] [Low-field carrier mobilities in silicon irradiated to extreme fluences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18581)
*I. Bloch,B. Bruers,C. -T. Klein,H. Lacker,P. Li,M. Ullan,Y. Unno,I. Mandić,C. Scharf*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 该论文测量了<100>硅中载流子迁移率随1 MeV中子等效注量（最高至10¹⁸ cm⁻²）及温度（230–260 K）的变化，利用电离杂质散射迁移率模型拟合电流数据，并结合TCAD仿真估算载流子浓度。模型在注量和温度维度均与实验高度吻合。在预期用于未来环形对撞机（FCC-hh）最内层探测器的注量（6×10¹⁷ cm⁻²）下，电子和空穴迁移率之和下降约60%。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在230–260 K温度范围内，测量不同1 MeV中子等效注量（最高至10¹⁸ cm⁻²）下的电流-电压特性；采用电离杂质散射迁移率模型（mobility model for scattering at ionized impurities）对电流数据进行拟合；并借助技术辅助设计（Technology-aided Design, TCAD）仿真估算拟合所需的载流子浓度参数。

Result: 拟合模型在注量和温度两个维度上均与实验数据吻合良好；在FCC-hh最内层探测器预期注量（6×10¹⁷ cm⁻²）下，电子与空穴迁移率之和下降约60%。

Conclusion: 所采用的迁移率模型能够有效描述辐照后硅中载流子迁移率的退化行为；极高注量下迁移率的大幅下降将对FCC-hh最内层探测器的信号收集效率产生显著影响。

Abstract: The low-field carrier mobilities in <100> silicon were quantified as a function of the 1$\,$MeV neutron-equivalent fluence up to $10^{18}\,$cm$^{-2}$ and for temperatures between 230$\,$K and 260$\,$K. Current measurements were fitted using a mobility model for scattering at ionized impurities. Technology-aided design (TCAD) simulations were compared to measurements and used to estimate the carrier concentrations, which are parameters in the fit. The fit model describes the data very well, both as a function of fluence and the temperature. At a fluence of $6 \cdot 10^{17}\,$cm$^{-2}$, which is expected for the innermost detector layers at the proposed Future Circular Hadron Collider (FCC-hh), the sum of the mobilities of electrons and holes was found to decrease by $\sim60$%.

</details>

### [56] [Dense $\mathrm{QC_2D_2}$ with uniform matrix product states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17183)
*Kohei Fujikura,Yoshimasa Hidaka*

Main category: hep-lat

TL;DR: 本研究采用规范不变变分均匀矩阵乘积态（gauge-invariant variational uniform matrix product state ansatz）在热力学极限下对(1+1)维冷致密单味SU(2)规范理论进行第一性原理研究，发现其红外行为符合Tomonaga-Luttinger液体（Tomonaga-Luttinger liquid），且Luttinger参数从稀密度的K≈1连续变化到高密度的K≈1/2，预示着夸克子交叉（quarkyonic crossover），并通过夸克分布首次从第一性原理实现了夸克子图像（quarkyonic picture）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 致密QCD（dense QCD）体系存在符号问题（sign problem），阻碍了传统蒙特卡洛方法的第一性原理研究。本文旨在建立一种无符号问题的变分方法，从第一性原理出发研究致密强子物质的红外行为与夸克子图像的微观实现。

Method: 采用规范不变变分均匀矩阵乘积态在热力学极限下对(1+1)维冷致密单味SU(2)规范理论进行计算，该方法无符号问题，属于第一性原理方法。

Result: 有限重子数密度下，红外行为与Tomonaga-Luttinger液体一致：中心荷（central charge）确定为c=1，重子数密度两点函数（two-point function）呈现空间调制，波数符合Tomonaga-Luttinger液体理论预期。Luttinger参数（Luttinger parameter）从稀重子区域（dilute-baryon regime）的K≈1平滑变化到高密度区域的K≈1/2。夸克分布同时展现了夸克费米海（quark Fermi sea）与重子红外描述（baryonic infrared description）的共存。

Conclusion: Luttinger参数的连续变化暗示存在夸克子交叉（quarkyonic crossover），而夸克分布中费米海与重子描述共存的现象首次从第一性原理实现了夸克子图像（quarkyonic picture）。该方法为无符号问题的致密QCD研究提供了有效途径。

Abstract: We study cold dense single-flavor $\mathrm{SU}(2)$ gauge theory in $(1+1)$ dimensions in the thermodynamic limit using a gauge-invariant variational uniform matrix product state ansatz. This formulation provides a sign-problem-free, first-principles approach to dense QCD. We show that, at finite baryon density, the infrared behavior is consistent with a Tomonaga--Luttinger liquid: the central charge is determined to be $c=1$, and the two-point function of the baryon-number density exhibits spatial modulation with the wavenumber predicted by Tomonaga--Luttinger liquid theory. The Luttinger parameter varies smoothly from $K\simeq 1$ in the dilute-baryon regime to $K\simeq 1/2$ at higher densities, suggesting a quarkyonic crossover. Furthermore, the quark distribution reveals the coexistence of a quark Fermi sea with a baryonic infrared description, thereby realizing the quarkyonic picture from first principles.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 成功构建了由紧致第二可数群G的G-核导出的连续自同态范畴（continuous category of endomorphisms），从而将原有离散群框架推广到了连续群情形。

Conclusion: 该连续自同态范畴为研究子因子理论与连续群表示论之间的相互作用提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: We generalize the construction of tensor categories of endomorphisms of a type III factor $M$ associated with a $G$-kernel, from the case of a discrete group $G$ to that of a compact second countable group. Our approach is based on the construction of a unitary tensor functor from a category of $C(G)$-modules to the category of endomorphisms of $M$. This functor maps a $C(G)$-module, realized as the space of square-integrable functions on a measure space, to a continuous family of endomorphisms of $M$. The resulting structure is a continuous category of endomorphisms, which provides a new framework for studying the interplay between subfactor theory and the representation theory of continuous groups.

### [58] [Shifted quantum toroidal algebra of type $\mathfrak{gl}_{1|1}$ and the Pieri rule of the super Macdonald polynomials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16773)
*Hiroaki Kanno,Ryo Ohkawa,Jun'ichi Shiraishi*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将超Macdonald多项式与量子环面代数$\mathcal{U}_{q,t}(\widehat{\widehat{\mathfrak{gl}}}_{1|1})$的超Fock模联系起来，并揭示其背后的Pieri规则和超对称结构。

Method: 利用代数$\mathcal{U}_{q,t}(\widehat{\widehat{\mathfrak{gl}}}_{1|1})$的超荷（super charges）作用推导超Macdonald多项式的Pieri规则；将Pieri规则用幂和$p_k$与费米子幂和（fermionic power sums）$\pi_k$的微分算子表示，进而转化为自由玻色子和自由费米子Fock空间上的算子；从Pieri规则出发通过超荷的反对易子（anti-commutator）计算超对称哈密顿量。

Result: 成功将超Macdonald多项式的Pieri规则表达为幂和与费米子幂和的微分算子形式，并从中恢复了文献中已有的超对称哈密顿量结果；发现必须处理一个平移后的量子环面代数（shifted quantum toroidal algebra）。

Conclusion: 超Macdonald多项式为量子环面代数的零级超Fock模提供了基，其Pieri规则自然导出超对称哈密顿量，且该代数结构需考虑平移（shifted）版本。

Abstract: The super Macdonald polynomials indexed by the super partitions form a basis of the level zero super Fock module (combinatorial representation) of the quantum toroidal algebra $\mathcal{U}_{q,t}(\widehat{\widehat{\mathfrak{gl}}}_{1|1})$. The action of the super charges of $\mathcal{U}_{q,t}(\widehat{\widehat{\mathfrak{gl}}}_{1|1})$ implies the Pieri rule of the super Macdonald polynomials. We can express the Pieri rule in terms of differential operators in the power sums $p_k$ and the fermionic power sums $π_k$, which leads to the operators on the Fock space of a free boson and a free fermion. From the Pieri rule we compute the supersymmetric Hamiltonians given by the anti-commutator of the super charges and recover the results previously obtained in the literature. It is remarkable that we have to deal with a shifted quantum toroidal algebra.

### [59] [A Weighted Spectral Quantum Fidelity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17167)
*Cong Trinh Le,The Khoi Vu,Minh Toan Ho,Trung Hoa Dinh*

Main category: math.FA

TL;DR: 本文引入并研究了一族基于加权谱几何均值的保真度型量——加权谱保真度\( \mathsf{F}_t^{\mathrm{spec}}(ρ,σ) \)，该族在\( t=0,1 \)时的平凡重叠与\( t=\frac12 \)时的Uhlmann保真度之间光滑插值，并建立了其核心结构性质、显式的数据后处理不等式违例以及关于态变量的凹性等结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子信息论中已有的保真度（fidelity）和Rényi型散度族在结构性质（如可乘性、凹性）和数据后处理不等式（data processing inequality, DPI）的满足情况上各有优劣，缺乏一个能同时实现从平凡重叠到Uhlmann保真度光滑插值、且在中点处满足DPI而在其他点显式违例的统一框架。本文旨在填补这一空白，定义并分析一种新的保真度族。

Method: 定义了一族基于加权谱几何均值（weighted spectral geometric mean）\( ρ^{-1}\sharpσ \)的保真度型量\( \mathsf{F}_t^{\mathrm{spec}}(ρ,σ)=\Tr[ρ(ρ^{-1}\sharpσ)^{2t}] \)，其中\( t\in[0,1] \)。通过分析该量的酉不变性、张量稳定性和可乘性、翻转对称性、端点行为及正交性判据等结构性质来刻画其行为，并推导其在纯态和布洛赫坐标下qubit系统中的闭式表达式。

Result: 该族在\( t=\frac12 \)处恢复为Uhlmann根保真度，在其他\( t \)点显式违例数据后处理不等式（DPI）；在态变量上具有各自分离的凹性；将第一个Fuchs–van de Graaf不等式推广至所有\( t\in[0,1] \)，但第二个不等式在中点以外失效。

Conclusion: 加权谱保真度族提供了一个区别于夹逼Rényi（sandwiched Rényi）族的新插值框架，其在中点处满足DPI而在其他点故意违例的特性，为研究量子信息处理中的资源理论、量子态区分和统计推断等问题的保真度选择提供了新的结构视角和数学工具。

Abstract: We introduce and study a one-parameter family of fidelity-type quantities based on the weighted spectral geometric mean, which we call the \emph{weighted spectral fidelity} \( \mathsf{F}_t^{\mathrm{spec}}(ρ,σ):=\Tr\!\big[ρ(ρ^{-1}\sharpσ)^{2t}\big],\ t\in[0,1]. \) This family interpolates smoothly between the trivial overlap ($t=0,1$) and the Uhlmann (root) fidelity at $t=\tfrac12$, and it is distinct from the sandwiched Rényi family except at this midpoint. We establish core structural features-unitary invariance, tensor stabilization and multiplicativity, flip symmetry, endpoint behavior, and a orthogonality criterion. We further show explicit \emph{violations of DPI} for generic $t\neq\tfrac12$. For concavity in the state variables we obtain concavity in each variable separately. Closed forms are obtained for pure states and for qubits in Bloch coordinates. We also extend the first Fuchs--van de Graaf inequality to $\mathsf{F}_t^{\mathrm{spec}}$ for all $t\in[0,1]$, while the second inequality fails away from the midpoint.

</details>


### [60] [Nonuniform Periodic Wavelet Frames on Non-Archimedean Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17323)
*Owais Ahmad*

Main category: math.FA

TL;DR: 本文在非阿基米德域（non-Archimedean field）上引入非均匀周期小波框架（nonuniform periodic wavelet frame）的概念，并基于傅里叶变换（Fourier transform）技术和酉延拓原理（unitary extension principle）提出了相应的构造方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实际应用中的信号并非来自均匀平移（uniform shifts），因此需要一个稳定的数学工具来分析与分解这类信号。Gabardo、Nashed 和 Yu 通过非均匀多尺度分析（nonuniform multiresolution analysis）和基于谱对（spectral pairs）理论的非均匀小波填补了这一空白，但其工作主要在实数域上展开。本文旨在将这一框架推广到非阿基米德域上。

Method: 借助傅里叶变换（Fourier transform）技术以及酉延拓原理（unitary extension principle），本文提出了一种在非阿基米德域（non-Archimedean field）上构造非均匀周期小波框架（nonuniform periodic wavelet frame）的方法。

Result: 在非阿基米德域上成功引入了非均匀周期小波框架的定义，并建立了系统的构造途径。

Conclusion: 本文将在实数域上发展的非均匀小波（nonuniform wavelet）理论拓展到了非阿基米德域，为该域上的非均匀信号分析提供了新的数学工具。

Abstract: In real life application all signals are not obtained from uniform shifts; so there is a natural question regarding analysis and decompositions of these types of signals by a stable mathematical tool. Gabardo and Nashed and Gabardo and Yu filled this gap by the concept of nonuniform multiresolution analysis and nonuniform wavelets based on the theory of spectral pairs for which the associated translation set $Λ=\left\{ 0,r/N\right\}+2\,\mathbb Z$ is no longer a discrete subgroup of $\mathbb R$ but a spectrum associated with a certain one-dimensional spectral pair and the associated dilation is an even positive integer related to the given spectral pair. In this paper, we introduce a notion of nonuniform periodic wavelet frame on non-Archimedean field. Using Fourier transform technique and the unitary extension principle, we propose an approach for the construction of nonuniform periodic wavelet frames on non-Archimedean fields.

</details>

### [61] [Universal dynamics from a single-particle dark state](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16494)
*Ruben Daraban,Arghavan Safavi-Naini,Johannes Schachenmayer,Mohammad Maghrebi*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文研究受关联耗散作用的自旋链中，单粒子暗态（single-particle dark state）如何以 $1/\log t$ 的慢衰减律及通用标度形式（universal scaling form）显著影响多体长时动力学，并通过数值模拟验证其普适性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开放量子系统（open quantum systems）中暗态或亚辐射态（subradiant states）在少激发（few-excitation）区域已被广泛研究，但其对多体动力学（many-body dynamics）的影响尚不清楚。

Method: 研究一个受相邻位点关联耗散（correlated dissipation）作用的自旋链，该体系在单粒子层面上存在零动量暗态（dark state at zero momentum）。通过分析耗散诱导的非线性（dissipation-induced nonlinearity）对暗态的修饰效应，推导动量分布与总密度的标度形式，并使用矩阵乘积态（matrix product state, MPS）模拟进行验证。

Result: 单粒子暗态在长时多体动力学中会引起慢衰减行为：零动量模以 $1/\log t$ 衰变；动量分布（momentum distribution）呈现关于 $k\sqrt{t}$ 的通用标度形式（universal scaling form）；总密度（total density）以 $1/\sqrt{t}\log t$ 方式衰减。该普适行为（universal behavior）在软核相互作用（soft-core interactions）下依然成立。

Conclusion: 单粒子暗态通过耗散诱导的非线性显著改变多体长时动力学，并呈现普适标度律。该结果有助于澄清近期文献中相互矛盾的结论，且普适行为对相互作用细节不敏感。

Abstract: Open quantum systems can host dark or subradiant states whose decay is highly suppressed. While these states have been extensively studied in the few-excitation regime, their impact on the many-body dynamics remains largely unexplored. Here, we study a spin chain subject to correlated dissipation on neighboring sites, which admits a single-particle dark state at zero momentum. We show that the single-particle dark state qualitatively alters the many-body dynamics at long times, and identify its distinct universal behavior. While the zero-momentum mode is dark at the single-particle level, it decays slowly as $1/\log t$ as it becomes dressed by other modes through a dissipation-induced nonlinearity. We demonstrate that the momentum distribution takes a universal scaling form in $k\sqrt{t}$, and the total density decays as $1/\sqrt{t}\log t$. Our results further elucidate the origin of the conflicting results in recent works. Finally, we corroborate the analytics with matrix product state simulations and show that the same universal behavior persists for soft-core interactions, underscoring the universality of the emergent dynamics.

</details>


### [62] [Temperature-Controlled Resonance in a Heteronuclear Quantum Gas Mixture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17931)
*Xiaoyi Yang,Tianyu Xu,Shengli Ma,Zhigang Wu,Ren Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出通过控制异核混合气体温度来实现连续可调的单通道共振（single-channel resonance）机制，称为温度控制共振（TCR），并在淬火动力学中解释了近期实验的温度依赖性耗散特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单通道共振是原子散射中的基本过程，但其产生在很大程度上是偶发的，缺乏系统性的控制手段。

Method: 将类Casimir介质相互作用（Casimir-like mediated interaction）推广至有限温度，利用费米面（Fermi surface）的热涂抹（thermal smearing）效应重塑杂质间的有效势，从而在宽参数范围内实现温度控制的共振。

Result: 共振位置随温度变化系统性地移动；浸入费米海（Fermi sea）的玻色气体（Bose gas）的淬火动力学（quench dynamics）中的温度依赖性耗散特征与TCR机制一致。

Conclusion: 温度可作为超冷量子气体中单通道共振的简单且实验可访问的控制旋钮（control knob）。

Abstract: Single-channel resonances are fundamental processes in scattering of atoms, yet their occurrence is largely incidental and lacks systematic control. In this Letter, we propose a mechanism to realize a continuously tunable single-channel resonance by controlling the temperature of the heteronuclear mixture. By extending the Casimir-like mediated interaction to finite temperature, we demonstrate that thermal smearing of the Fermi surface reshapes the effective potential between impurities, giving rise to a temperature-controlled resonance (TCR) over a wide parameter range. As a direct consequence, the resonance position shifts systematically with temperature variation, providing a clear experimental signature of this mechanism. We further investigate the quench dynamics of a Bose gas immersed in a Fermi sea and demonstrate that the observed temperature-dependent loss features in recent experiments are consistent with the TCR mechanism. Our results establish temperature as a simple and experimentally accessible control knob for single-channel resonances in ultracold quantum gases.

</details>


### [63] [Shapiro steps of superfluid Fermi gases in a ring trap across the BCS--BEC crossover](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17940)
*Hikaru Kuriki,Masaya Kunimi,Tetsuro Nikuni*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究通过含时Bogoliubov–de Gennes方程模拟环形阱中超流费米气体在运动势垒下的约瑟夫森结动力学，在BCS‑BEC渡越中观测到低阶Shapiro台阶，并揭示其来源于势垒处周期性孤子产生所介导的同步相位滑移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究环形阱中超流费米气体在BCS‑BEC渡越范围内的输运性质，特别是非平衡相位动力学如何受相互作用强度调控，并为具有非平凡拓扑的原子电子学（atomtronics）系统提供微观物理见解。

Method: 采用含时Bogoliubov–de Gennes（BdG）方程模拟由直流（DC）和交流（AC）电流共同偏置的约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction）在环形阱中的动力学过程，并在从BCS到BEC的渡越区间扫描相互作用强度。

Result: 在相位相干区域内，观察到势垒速度‑化学势差中清晰的低阶Shapiro台阶（Shapiro-step plateaus），其中时间平均化学势差以$\hbarω/2$为整数单位量子化；该$1/2$因子源于BdG框架中按单个费米子定义化学势的约定。

Conclusion: 这些基本台阶源于势垒处周期性孤子（soliton）产生所介导的同步相位滑移（synchronized phase slips）。该结果阐明了相互作用区间在环形阱费米超流非平衡相位动力学中的作用，并为未来研究具有非平凡拓扑的原子电子学系统提供了微观层面的参考。

Abstract: We investigate the transport properties of a superfluid Fermi gas confined in a ring trap with a moving potential barrier across the Bardeen-Cooper-Schrieffer (BCS) to Bose-Einstein condensate (BEC) crossover. Employing time-dependent Bogoliubov--de Gennes (BdG) equations, we simulate the dynamics of a Josephson junction biased by both DC and AC currents. Over a wide range of interaction strengths, we observe clear low-order Shapiro-step plateaus in the barrier-velocity--chemical-potential-diffenrence, within the phase-coherent regime, where the time-averaged chemical potential difference is quantized in units of $\hbarω/2$. This factor of $1/2$ reflects our convention of defining the chemical potential per single fermion in the BdG framework. Microscopic analysis reveals that these fundamental steps originate from synchronized phase slips mediated by periodic soliton generation at the barrier. Our findings clarify the role of interaction regimes in the nonequilibrium phase dynamics of ring-trapped fermionic superfluids and provide microscopic insights relevant to future studies of atomtronic systems with nontrivial topology.

</details>


### [64] [Jones-Roberts solitary waves and the onset of rotation in a spherical surface condensate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18297)
*Noel Cuadra,Thomas Gasenzer,Davide Proment,Alberto Villois*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文研究了稀薄玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate）在薄球壳约束下旋转启动过程中的非线性激发，揭示了从涡旋偶极子（vortex dipole）到无涡旋的Jones-Roberts孤子（Jones-Roberts soliton）的转变，并确定了由Landau临界速度（Landau critical velocity）设定的角速度上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解球壳几何中稀薄玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体的旋转启动机制，特别是其中非线性激发（如孤子和涡旋）的行为及其与约束几何的关联。

Method: 对薄球壳约束下的稀薄玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体进行理论分析，研究以恒定角速度绕球旋转的孤立波（solitary wave）激发及其随角速度演化的行为。

Result: 低角速度下激发表现为带有相反环量的单量子化涡旋偶极子（dipoles of singly quantized vortices）；高角速度下演化为无涡旋的Jones-Roberts孤子；进一步增加角速度时，这些激发与赤道约束模式（equatorially confined modes）发生混合，其方位波数由以愈合长度（healing length）为单位的球半径决定。

Conclusion: 这些模式的传播速度起到Landau临界速度的作用，从而设定了整个Jones-Roberts孤子家族的角速度上限。

Abstract: The nonlinear excitations underlying the onset of rotation in a dilute Bose-Einstein condensate confined to a thin spherical shell are studied. These excitations correspond to solitary waves rotating about the sphere at constant angular speed: at low speeds they appear as dipoles of singly quantized vortices with opposite circulation, while at higher speeds they evolve into vortex-free Jones-Roberts solitons. With further increase of the angular speed, these excitations hybridize with equatorially confined modes whose azimuthal wave number is set by the sphere radius measured in units of the healing length. The propagation speed of these modes is shown to play the role of a Landau critical velocity, thereby setting the upper limiting angular speed of the entire Jones-Roberts family.

</details>


### [65] [A study of the dimer-trimer crossover in a driven three-component Fermi gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18405)
*Ronnie Slowinski,Gaël Servignat,Frédéric Chevy,Carlos Lobo*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个三组分可区分原子系统的有效场论（Effective Field Theory, EFT），通过变分法计算了真空中和单费米海（Fermi sea）背景下两体与三体的结合能。研究发现，真空中和介质中的二聚体与三聚体分支之间存在交叉现象，其交叉位置可通过外部驱动调控原子间耦合来加以控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在多体物理中，理解由多种可区分原子物种构成的系统中的束缚态行为具有重要意义。作者希望建立一个系统的有效场论框架，用以描述一个非普适的闭通道二聚体（closed-channel dimer）与第三种原子（作为介质）之间的耦合，并探究这种耦合如何影响真空中与介质中的二聚体和三聚体结合能，以及是否存在类似于极化子-分子问题中的分支交叉现象。

Method: 采用有效场论方法，假设前两种原子物种之间存在受外部驱动调控的相互作用，从而产生一个可独立调节耦合强度的非普适闭通道二聚体。其余相互作用（二聚体与第三种原子之间）被建模为接触相互作用（contact interaction）。通过变分计算（variational calculation），推导出真空中和介质中二聚体与三聚体结合能的解析表达式。

Result: 得到了真空中和介质中二聚体与三聚体结合能的解析形式。在介质情况下，预测了二聚体与三聚体分支之间随原子-二聚体散射长度（atom-dimer scattering length）变化而发生的分支交叉（crossing）。此外，该交叉的位置可通过改变由外部驱动产生的原子-原子耦合来加以调控。

Conclusion: 本文结果揭示了多组分费米体系中束缚态分支交叉的可调性，为类比于通常的极化子-分子问题提供了新的可控自由度，并对理解相关超冷原子系统中的多体物理现象具有参考意义。

Abstract: We develop an Effective Field Theory (EFT) for a system with three distinguishable atomic species and present a variational calculation of the two and three-body binding energies in vacuum and in the presence of a single Fermi sea. Specifically, we consider the case where the interaction between first two atomic species is externally driven so as to produce a (non-universal) closed-channel dimer whose coupling can be controlled independently of all other interactions. We then model the remaining interactions as a contact interaction between the dimer and a third atomic species which forms the medium. We derive analytical expressions for the dimer and trimer binding energies in vacuum and in medium, and in the latter case we predict a crossing between the dimer and trimer branches as a function of the atom-dimer scattering length, analogous to the usual polaron and molecule problem. Furthermore, we show that the position of this crossing can be controlled by varying the atom-atom coupling that results from the external drive and we discuss the implications of these findings.

### [66] [Relativistic theory for coupled orbital and spin angular momentum dynamics in magnetic systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16830)
*Subhadip Santra,Ritwik Mondal,Marco Berritta,Peter M. Oppeneer*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 该论文建立了一个完整的相对论性理论框架，用于描述磁性系统中电子自旋角动量（spin angular momentum）和轨道角动量（orbital angular momentum）的耦合动力学，并分析了总角动量在不同条件下的守恒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论对磁性系统中自旋和轨道角动量动力学的描述尚不完整，缺乏从相对论狄拉克框架出发的统一推导，特别是在电磁场作用下两者耦合行为的严格理论。

Method: 从相对论性的狄拉克-库恩-沈（Dirac-Kohn-Sham）哈密顿量出发，通过幺正变换（unitary transformation）得到推广的泡利哈密顿量（extended Pauli Hamiltonian），进而推导轨道和自旋角动量的运动方程，并引入原子海森堡近似（atomistic Heisenberg approximation）处理交换相互作用。

Result: (1) 在无自旋极化Kohn-Sham交换场时，总角动量J守恒，但施加电磁场后J不再守恒；(2) 在原子海森堡近似下，即使存在电磁场，总角动量J仍守恒，但自旋和轨道角动量各自不守恒。

Conclusion: 该理论自洽地描述了磁性系统中自旋与轨道角动量的耦合动力学，并揭示了不同近似条件下总角动量守恒性的关键差异，为理解超快磁动力学（ultrafast magnetodynamics）等过程提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We develop a complete relativistic theory to describe the dynamics of electronic angular momentum including both spin (S) and orbital (L) contributions in magnetic systems. We start with the relativistic Dirac-Kohn-Sham Hamiltonian under the influence of an electromagnetic field and apply a unitary transformation to formulate the extended Pauli Hamiltonian. Using the transformed semirelativistic Hamiltonian, we derive the angular momentum dynamics for the orbital and spin angular momenta. Thereby, we formulate the coupled dynamics of orbital and spin moments consistent with the relativistic Dirac framework. Considering especially the conservation of the total angular momentum, J = S +L, we show first that J is conserved in the absence of a spin-polarized Kohn-Sham exchange field, but is no longer conserved under the application of an electromagnetic field, e.g., laser pulse, THz field, etc. Second, considering magnetic systems with atomic spin and orbital momenta, we derive the coupled equations of motion of angular momenta dynamics whilst making the atomistic Heisenberg approximation for the exchange interaction. Our results suggest that, under these assumptions, the total angular momentum remains conserved, even with electromagnetic field, but atomic spin and orbital angular momenta individually are not conserved.

</details>


### [67] [Coherent spectroscopy of collective excitations in superfluid helium far from equilibrium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17835)
*Gabriel Voith,Alexander A. Milner,Valery Milner*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文利用飞秒脉冲序列对超流氦中Landau激发谱的多个分支（包括maxon对和Pitaevskii plateau激发）进行了超快相干控制光谱学测量，揭示了maxon对具有异常强的结合能、极短的寿命以及准粒子有效质量对相干响应相位的影响，证明了通过非平衡动力学提取强相互作用量子流体中集体激发信息的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超流体中集体激发的超快动力学在roton（旋子） regime之外仍 largely unexplored（很大程度上未被探索），然而理解这些系统的非平衡过程具有重要意义。

Method: 使用飞秒脉冲序列对超流氦进行 ultrafast coherent control（超快相干控制），通过 time-resolved optical birefringence（时间分辨光学双折射）测量，追踪maxon对、Pitaevskii plateau激发以及先前已研究的roton对的非平衡动力学。

Result: 发现了maxon对具有surprisingly strong binding energy（异常强的结合能）和 extremely short lifetime（极短的寿命），并揭示了quasiparticle effective mass（准粒子有效质量）对相干响应相位的影响。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，通过探测强相互作用量子流体在飞秒到皮秒时间尺度上的非平衡动力学，可以提取此前无法获得的关于集体激发的信息。

Abstract: Ultrafast dynamics of collective excitations in superfluids remains largely unexplored beyond the roton regime, despite its importance for understanding nonequilibrium processes in these systems. Here, we employ ultrafast coherent control with sequences of femtosecond pulses to perform spectroscopy of multiple branches of the Landau excitation spectrum in superfluid helium far from equilibrium. By measuring the time-resolved optical birefringence, we track the nonequilibrium dynamics of maxon pairs and Pitaevskii plateau excitations alongside the previously studied roton pairs, revealing surprisingly strong binding energy of maxon pairs, their extremely short lifetime, and the influence of the quasiparticle effective mass on the phase of the coherent response. These results demonstrate the ability to extract previously inaccessible information about collective excitations in a strongly interacting quantum fluid by probing its nonequilibrium dynamics on femtosecond and picosecond timescales.

### [68] [Chern classes of Laughlin bundles on the quasihole moduli space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18089)
*Florent Dupont,Semyon Klevtsov*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文研究了任意亏格（genus）黎曼曲面（Riemann surface）上具有准空穴（quasihole）激发态的分数量子霍尔效应（fractional quantum Hall effect），使用Grothendieck-Riemann-Roch定理构造并分析了准空穴态的向量丛（vector bundle）的陈特征（Chern character），并在亏格零和一情形下通过显式波函数验证了贝里相位（Berry phase）的分解与预测一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将分数量子霍尔态的研究从平坦几何推广到任意亏格的黎曼曲面，旨在理解准空穴激发在弯曲流形上的拓扑性质，并建立贝里相位（Berry phase）的纯几何分解。

Method: 对于m个准空穴构型，在黎曼曲线的m次对称积（symmetric power）上构造向量丛，使得纤维对应准空穴定域在给定位置的状态；利用Grothendieck-Riemann-Roch定理计算陈特征（Chern character）；在亏格零和一情形下构造显式波函数并验证陈联络（Chern connection）的曲率与预测陈类（Chern classes）一致。

Result: 在完全填充态（粒子数最大）中，向量丛满足投射平坦性（projective flatness）；所得陈类逐项匹配贝里相位在准空穴交换下的预测分解，即广延的Aharonov-Bohm贡献与分数统计（fractional statistics）贡献之和；该结果推广至多层与多准空穴类型情形。

Conclusion: 论文从几何上统一了分数量子霍尔系统中准空穴激发的贝里相位结构，验证了其在任意亏格曲面上的投射平坦性与统计分解，为进一步理解分数统计的几何基础提供了严格框架。

Abstract: We study fractional quantum Hall states with quasihole excitations, on Riemann surfaces of arbitrary genus. For configurations with $m$ quasiholes we construct a vector bundle above the $m$-th symmetric power of the curve so that the fiber at a point $\lbrace w_1,\dots,w_m \rbrace$ corresponds to the state with quasiholes localized at these positions. We determine the Chern character of this bundle via the Grothendieck-Riemann-Roch theorem and show that in the completely filled state, i.e. when the number of particles is maximal, the vector bundle is compatible with the condition of projective flatness. Furthermore, we obtain a generalization of this result to the case of multiple layers and multiple quasihole types. In genus zero and one, we construct explicit wave-functions and verify that the curvature of the associated Chern connection reproduces the predicted Chern classes. The Chern classes obtained match, term by term, the predicted decomposition of the Berry phase under quasihole exchange, into an extensive Aharonov--Bohm contribution and a fractional statistical contribution.

### [69] [2-dimensional finite-gap Schrödinger operator whose spectrum admits two involutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18388)

Main category: math.AG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对具有两个以上分支点的光滑双覆盖，其Prym簇不再是主极化（principally polarized）的，Fay引入了与其同源（isogenic）的主极化簇——即isoPrym簇。本文旨在为这类更一般的情形建立新的势性条件，以识别这些isoPrym簇。

Method: 本文提出了一套新的势性条件，适用于某个特定类别的曲线上的光滑双覆盖（smooth double coverings），且覆盖具有两个以上的分支点（branch points）。该条件与Fay讲义中引入的isoPrym簇相关联。

Result: 给出了针对具有两个以上分支点的光滑双覆盖的isoPrym簇识别的新势性条件，从而将此前仅适用于两个分支点的Riemann–Schottky问题的解法推广到更一般的覆盖情形。

Conclusion: 新的势性条件为识别具有多个分支点的光滑双覆盖的isoPrym簇提供了有效的代数和几何刻画，推进了有限能级薛定谔算子与代数曲线理论之间关联的研究。

Abstract: Two-dimensional Schrödinger operators that are finite-gap at one energy level are introduced in 1976 by Dubrovin, Krichever and Novikov. In two subsequent works by Novikov and Veselov the potentiality conditions for them have been studied, that are conditions for the magnetic term to be absend. Besides their physical importance, these works played a crucial role in solving out the Riemann--Shottki problem of indetification of Prymians of smooth coverings with two branch points in the class of principally polarized Abelian varieties, going back to 80s, and completed in Krichever'06, and Krichever and Grushevsky'07.
  For smooth coverings with more than two branch points, the Prym varieties are no longer principally polarized. In wellknown Fay's lectures, certain isogenic to them principally polarized varieties are introduced, which we refer to as isoPrymians. In the present work we propose the new potentiality conditions for the Schrödinger operators in question, and a related approach to identification of isoPrymians of smooth double coverings of curves of a certain class, with more than two branch points.

### [70] [Hydrodynamic cascade drives tumbling in sheared colloidal rod suspensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16723)
*Lucas H. P. Cunha,Paul F. Salipante,Peter D. Olmsted,Steven D. Hudson*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过粒子模拟和标度分析发现，胶体棒（colloidal rods）悬浮液中的流体动力学耦合（hydrodynamic coupling）会驱动级联翻转事件（cascade of tumbling events），破坏流动取向并显著增加粘度和法向应力差，这与近期实验定性一致，表明现有本构模型需要修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 胶体棒动力学建模是软物质物理学（soft-matter physics）的核心挑战，其各向异性和长程相互作用使问题复杂。以往假设流体动力学相互作用（hydrodynamic interactions）在半稀薄体系中被屏蔽或太弱而可忽略，但该假设在实验常见剪切速率和浓度下是否成立尚不明确。

Method: 采用基于粒子的模拟（particle-based simulations）和标度分析（scaling analysis），研究胶体棒悬浮液在剪切流中的集体动力学行为。

Result: 发现相邻棒之间的流体动力学耦合会触发级联翻转事件；该集体动力学破坏流动取向（flow alignment），并导致粘度（viscosity）和法向应力差（normal stress differences）显著增加，结果与近期实验定性一致。

Conclusion: 流体动力学促进的级联效应（hydrodynamically-promoted cascade effect）表明，现有胶体棒本构模型需要修正。流体动力学耦合应被视为高各向异性悬浮液中集体动力学的关键机制。

Abstract: Modeling the dynamics of colloidal rods remains a central challenge in soft-matter physics due to the anisotropic and long-ranged nature of their interactions. Hydrodynamic interactions in rods suspensions are often assumed to be screened or too week to play any role in semi-dilute regimes, yet we find here these assumptions to break down at shear rates and concentrations that are often attained in experiments. Using particle-based simulations and scaling analysis, we uncover a cascade of tumbling events driven by hydrodynamic coupling among neighboring rods. This collective dynamics disrupts flow alignment and leads to a pronounced increase in viscosity and normal stress differences, in qualitative agreement with recent experiments. The discovery of this hydrodynamically-promoted cascade effect calls for a revision of existing constitutive models for colloidal rods and highlights hydrodynamic coupling as a key mechanism governing collective dynamics in highly anisotropic suspensions.

### [71] [Global space correlations of polarization, charge density, and electric field in electrolytes under the fixed-potential condition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17346)
*Akira Onuki*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文研究了平行金属电极间稀电解液中极化强度、电荷密度和电场的热涨落，揭示了这些涨落随膜厚与德拜屏蔽长度相对大小变化的全局关联特性，并得出了有效介电常数与膜厚及屏蔽长度的依赖关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在固定外加电势差条件下，理解受限几何中电解质涨落行为的微观物理机制，尤其是极化、电荷密度和电场的全局空间关联如何受薄膜厚度与德拜屏蔽长度（Debye screening length）之比的影响。

Method: 采用统计力学（statistical mechanics）方法，在平行金属电极之间固定电势差 $Φ_a$ 的边界条件下，解析分析稀电解质的极化 $p$、电荷密度 $ρ$ 和电场 $E$ 的热涨落（thermal fluctuations）及其空间关联结构，并区分膜厚 $H$ 小于或远大于德拜屏蔽长度 $κ^{-1}$ 两种情形。

Result: 当 $H < κ^{-1}$ 时，沿表面法向的 $p_z$ 和 $E_z$ 的空间关联出现与膜体积 $V$ 成反比的全局分量；当 $H ≫ κ^{-1}$ 时，双电层外的体区域中 $p_z$ 和 $ρ$ 的全局关联变小，但 $E_z$ 的全局关联几乎不受离子影响。有效介电常数 $ε_{\rm eff}$ 依赖于 $H$ 和 $κ$，并可用 $p_z$、$ρ$ 及非局域表面电荷密度的涨落方差表达。

Conclusion: 稀电解质的涨落行为在受限几何中由膜厚与德拜屏蔽长度的相对尺度决定，其中电场涨落在固定电势差下具有全局性和鲁棒性，而有效介电常数可统一由若干涨落方差的组合表征。

Abstract: We examine the thermal fluctuations of the polarization $p$, the charge density $ρ$, and the electric field $E$ in dilute electrolytes inserted between pararell metallic electrodes, where we fix the applied potential difference $Φ_a$ between the two electrodes. If the film thickness $H$ is shorter than the Debye screening length $κ^{-1}$, the space correlation of the polarization $p_z$ and the electric field $E_z$ along the surface normal (in the $z$ direction) acuire global components inversely proportional to the film volume $V$, which vary slowly along the $z$ axis and are homogeneous in the $xy$ plane. The areal charge density on each electrode surface also has a component homogeneous on the surface, which produces the global electric fluctuations. On the other hand, if $H$ much exceeds $κ^{-1}$, the global correlations of $p_z$ and $ρ$ become small in the bulk region outside the electric double layers, but that of $E_z$ remains almost unchanged by ions in the whole cell at fixed $Φ_a$. The dielectric constant $ε_{\rm eff}$ depends on $H$ and $κ$ and is expressed in terms of the fluctuation variances of $p_z$ and $ρ$ and that of the noblocal surface charge density at fixed $Φ_a$.

</details>


### [72] [Getting rid of the ghosts: a toy-model of membrane melting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17579)
*Olivier Coquand*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文重新审视了晶态膜（crystalline membrane）中的热涨落理论，详细分析了重整化群（renormalization group）相图中两个通常被忽略的不稳定临界区域，指出固定点P2是描述晶态膜熔化的良好候选，并通过从二维晶体熔化生成流体膜的方式，避免了通常 Canham-Helfrich 作用量中 Monge 参数化带来的鬼场（ghost）问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 晶态膜重整化群相图中存在两个在某一方向上不稳定的临界区域，以往研究常将其排除讨论。本文旨在深入分析这两个区域，以更全面地理解晶态膜的热涨落行为及其熔化机制。

Method: 通过围绕每个临界区域进行适当的 Goldstone 模计数，分析主导大尺度谱的涨落性质，并将熔化膜的特性与流体膜的特性进行比较。

Result: 固定点 P2 是描述晶态膜熔化的良好候选。此外，通过熔化二维晶体生成流体膜的方式，可以构建其关联函数（correlation functions），从而避免传统 Canham-Helfrich 作用量中因采用 Monge 参数化而必然出现的鬼场问题。

Conclusion: 对晶态膜熔化过程的深入分析不仅为描述熔化相变提供了候选固定点，还提出了一种无鬼场的流体膜关联函数构造方法，具有理论意义。

Abstract: The theory of thermal fluctuations in crystalline membranes is put under scrutiny. In particular, the two critical regimes of the renormalisation group diagram, which are often left out of the discussion because of their instability in one direction, are examined in details. After studying the proper Goldstone mode counting around each of them, the properties of the fluctuations dominating the large scale spectrum are analysed. This shows that the fixed point P2 is a good candidate to describe the melting of a crystalline membrane. The properties of the melted membrane are then compared to the known properties of fluid membranes. As a byproduct of this analysis, we show that the generation of a fluid membrane by melting a bidimensional crystal allows to formulate its correlation functions without being plagued by the ghosts that inevitably show up in the usual Canham-Helfrich action relying on the Monge parametrisation.

</details>


### [73] [Structure of the twist-bend nematic phase with respect to the orientational molecular order of the thioether-linked dimers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17523)
*Antoni Kocot,Barbara Loska,Yuki Arakawa,Katarzyna Merkel*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过分析液晶二聚体（liquid crystal dimers）中官能团（介晶基元和连接基团）的红外（IR）吸收光谱，测定了向列相（nematic phase）和扭曲-弯曲向列相（twist-bend nematic phase）中的取向有序度（orientation order）以及偶极相互作用（dipole interactions）的信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究液晶二聚体在向列相与扭曲-弯曲向列相中分子长轴和短轴的取向有序度变化规律，以及偶极子间的轴向与横向相互作用行为，从而加深对扭曲-弯曲向列相中双轴取向（biaxial ordering）和螺旋形变（helical deformation）机制的理解。

Method: 采用红外吸收光谱（IR absorbance）分析技术，对液晶二聚体的分段官能团（介晶基元与连接基团）进行检测，通过测量不同温度下的吸光度变化来推断分子取向有序度和偶极相互作用。

Result: 在向列相中，长轴取向有序度随温度降低而增加，但增速远慢于经典向列相；进入扭曲-弯曲向列相后，由于分子倾斜，该趋势发生逆转。短轴在向列相中各向同性均匀旋转并保持单轴排列（uniaxial alignment），而在扭曲-弯曲向列相中则出现显著的双轴取向（biaxial ordering）。在相变点，纵向偶极的吸光度下降，表明偶极子间产生反平行轴向相互作用（antiparallel axial interaction）；横向偶极的吸光度在340 K以下保持不变，之后转为平行关联（parallelly correlated）。

Conclusion: 扭曲-弯曲向列相中分子倾斜导致了长轴有序度的反转，并诱导出双轴取向行为；偶极相互作用的轴向反平行与横向平行关联模式，与指向矢（director）的螺旋形变密切相关。

Abstract: An analysis of the IR absorbance for the segmented functional groups of liquid crystal dimers: mesogen and linker, enabled the orientation order to be determined and information about the dipole interactions in the nematic and twist-bend nematic phases to be obtained. The long axis orientational order increases as the temperature decreases in the nematic phase, although much more slowly than for the classical nematics, and then reverses this trend in the twist-bend nematic phase due to the tilt of the molecules. In the nematic phase, the short axis of the molecule performs an isotropic uniform rotation and has a uniaxial alignment. In the twist-bend nematic phase, however, biaxial ordering occurs and grows significantly in accordance with the helical deformation of the director. Changes in the mean absorbance in the twist-bend nematic phase were observed: a decrease for the longitudinal dipole at the nematic-twist-bend nematic phase transition, thus emphasizing the antiparallel axial interaction of the dipoles, while the absorbance of the transverse dipoles remains unchanged up to 340 K, and then the latter become parallelly correlated.

### [74] [Topological Data Analysis combined with Machine Learning for Predicting Permeability of Porous Media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17581)
*Ebru Dagdelen,Catherin Neena Lalu,Aakash Karlekar,Manav Arora,Matthew Illingworth,Jonathan Jaquette,Linda Cummings,Lou Kondic*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于标准解析或数值方法难以处理多孔介质中的流动问题，而合成多孔介质的表示易于生成且实验数据日益丰富，因此该问题非常适合引入机器学习（ML）技术来研究。

Method: 从多孔介质数据中提取三类特征：描述几何的结构度量（structural measures）、描述连通性的拓扑度量（topological measures），以及通过将多孔介质简化为孔隙网络（pore networks）获得的网络度量（network measures）。将这些特征作为标准ML算法的输入变量，以预测合成多孔材料的渗透率，并利用单独计算出的精确渗透率（ground truth）进行对比。

Result: 通过比较不同输入变量组合的实验结果，验证了各类特征在基于多孔介质结构预测渗透率方面的效用。特别地，拓扑数据分析（TDA）提供了一套有用特征，且易于与ML结合产生有意义的预测结果。

Conclusion: 拓扑数据分析（TDA）为多孔介质渗透率的机器学习预测提供了一套高效且易于集成的特征，有助于深化对结构-渗透率关系的理解。

Abstract: Flow in porous media is difficult to address using standard analytical or numerical methods due to its complexity. However, since synthetic representations of porous media are easy to produce and data from physical experiments are becoming more widely available, the problem is well-suited to studies that include machine learning (ML) techniques. We discuss a number of features that can be extracted from such data, and their utility as input variables into a standard ML algorithm. These features include structural measures describing the geometry of the porous media, topological measures describing the connectivity, and network measures obtained by modeling the porous media as simplified pore networks. These features enable the prediction of the permeability of the considered (synthetic) porous materials using ML techniques that also leverage the separately computed exact permeability (ground truth). Comparing results obtained using different input variables helps develop a better understanding of the utility of various measures for predicting permeability based on the porous media structure. We show, in particular, that topological data analysis (TDA) provides a useful set of features that can be easily combined with ML to yield meaningful results.

Abstract: We study an agent-based model of self-propelled particles with a velocity-dependent alignment rule. This interaction is orientation weighted and acts along the line connecting neighboring particles. Tuning the alignment strength produces several distinct collective regimes, including disordered gas-like motion, coherent flocking, jammed high-density states, and densely ordered moving clusters with active-crystal-like behavior. These results show that a simple local alignment rule can generate a broad range of nonequilibrium collective dynamics within a single microscopic model.

### [76] [Mpemba effect in a sheared granular gas with velocity-dependent restitution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17881)
*Makoto R. Kikuchi,Yuria Kobayashi,Satoshi Takada*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该论文通过动力学理论（kinetic theory）研究了稀疏剪切颗粒气体中的姆潘巴效应（Mpemba effect），发现即使初始温度更高，从各向同性状态出发的系统比从剪切稳态出发的系统能更快弛豫，并首次揭示了由速度依赖的恢复系数（restitution coefficient）引入的额外内禀时间尺度导致了多重粘度姆潘巴效应（viscosity Mpemba effect）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在具有速度依赖恢复系数的稀疏剪切颗粒气体中是否存在姆潘巴效应，并分析其弛豫动力学机制。

Method: 采用基于Grad矩方法（Grad's moment method）的动力学理论，分析剪切率突变后系统的弛豫动力学。

Result: 发现了温度演化中的姆潘巴效应，以及剪切粘度弛豫曲线中的粘度姆潘巴效应；速度依赖的恢复系数引入了额外内禀时间尺度，导致多重交叉（multiple crossings）现象的出现。

Conclusion: 速度依赖的恢复系数为驱动颗粒气体中的多重姆潘巴效应提供了一个最小化动力学机制（minimal kinetic mechanism）。

Abstract: We investigate the Mpemba effect in a dilute sheared granular gas with a velocity-dependent restitution coefficient. Using kinetic theory based on Grad's moment method, we analyze the relaxation dynamics following a sudden change in the shear rate. We show that, despite having a higher initial temperature, a system starting from an isotropic state can relax faster than a system prepared in a sheared steady state, demonstrating a clear Mpemba effect in the temperature evolution. We further demonstrate the emergence of a viscosity Mpemba effect, characterized by crossings in the relaxation curves of the shear viscosity. Remarkably, multiple crossings arise due to an additional intrinsic timescale introduced by the velocity dependence of the restitution coefficient, providing a minimal kinetic mechanism for multiple Mpemba effects in driven granular gases.

### [77] [Lateral hydrodynamics in supported membranes: The Evans-Sackmann model and its extensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17917)
*Yuto Hosaka,David Andelman,Shigeyuki Komura*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文综述了Evans-Sackmann流体动力学模型在支撑流体膜（supported fluid membranes）侧向输运中的理论发展与现代应用，从原始公式出发，涵盖边界条件扩展、支撑膜迁移率张量（mobility tensor）的统一框架，以及面向活性手性膜（active and chiral membranes）的最新推广。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 支撑流体膜中的侧向输运对于理解膜内嵌入物（如蛋白质、脂质结构域或示踪粒子）的扩散与动力学至关重要。Evans-Sackmann模型通过引入线性动量衰减项（linear momentum decay term）来刻画膜-基底耦合，为定量解释支撑双层膜（supported bilayers）中的示踪扩散测量提供了理论基础。

Method: 摘要采用综述性论述，首先回顾Evans-Sackmann模型的原始公式，重点分析描述膜-基底耦合的线性动量衰减项；随后总结在嵌入物周界处放宽标准边界条件的理论扩展，包括圆盘拖拽（drag of a disk）、液态结构域拖拽以及膜相分离（phase separation）动力学；最终引入支撑膜迁移率张量作为统一工具，系统处理准二维环境中的关联扩散、聚合物动力学、相分离动力学及多体相互作用，并延伸至具有奇黏度（odd viscosity）的活性手性膜。

Result: 该模型能够定量解释支撑双层膜中的示踪扩散测量。支撑膜迁移率张量作为统一工具，可系统处理准二维环境中的多种动力学问题。在手性膜扩展中，奇黏度提供了横向流体动力学响应（transverse hydrodynamic response），为检测二维流体中的手性（chirality）提供了可能途径。

Conclusion: Evans-Sackmann流体动力学模型从最初的膜-基底耦合框架发展为统一的迁移率张量方法，能够处理准二维膜环境中从简单扩散到多体相互作用的广泛动力学问题；向活性手性膜的扩展进一步拓展了其在探测二维流体手性等方面的应用前景。

Abstract: We review the theoretical development and modern applications of the Evans-Sackmann hydrodynamic model for lateral transport in supported fluid membranes. We first cover the original formulation, emphasizing the linear momentum decay term that captures membrane-substrate coupling mediated by a thin lubricating fluid layer. This coupling term enables quantitative interpretation of tracer diffusion measurements in supported bilayers. Building on this foundation, we survey theoretical extensions that relax standard boundary conditions at the inclusion perimeter, where inclusions refer to embedded objects such as proteins, lipid domains, or tracer particles within the membrane. We discuss the drag of a disk and a liquid domain, as well as the dynamics of membrane phase separation. We further highlight how the supported-membrane mobility tensor serves as a unifying tool for systematic treatments of correlated diffusion, polymer dynamics, phase separation kinetics, and many-body interactions in quasi-two-dimensional environments. Finally, we discuss recent extensions to active and chiral membranes, where odd viscosity provides a transverse hydrodynamic response and offers a possible route for detecting chirality in two-dimensional fluids.

</details>


### [78] [Coalescence of Polymer Droplets Moving on a Surface with Stiffness Gradient](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18279)
*Divyansh Tripathi,Vimal Kishore,Panagiotis E. Theodorakis,Swarn Lata Singh*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文研究了软表面上同向移动两个液滴的合并过程，该运动由表面刚度梯度驱动。通过考察不同速度比、液滴间及液滴内相互作用强度等参数，分析了桥接高度随时间增长的幂律行为，发现了从毛细主导到粘弹性主导的两种幂律增长区间转变。结果表明合并动力学与程度强烈依赖于相互作用参数，对微流控和喷墨打印等应用具有潜在意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解软表面上由刚度梯度（即趋硬性，durotaxis）驱动的液滴合并现象，填补对运动状态下液滴合并动力学认识的不足。

Method: 研究了软表面上同向运动液滴的合并，并以均匀表面上对应不同刚度值的静态合并作为参照。考虑了前导与后随液滴速度比的合理范围，以及液滴-液滴和液滴内部相互作用强度的变化，分析了桥接高度（bridge height, $h$）随时间（$t$）的幂律增长（$h \sim t^α$）。

Result: 桥接高度的幂律指数 $\alpha$ 随时间从高值向低值转变，表明存在两种不同的幂律增长区间：从毛细（capillarity）主导区过渡到粘弹性（viscoelasticity）主导区。合并动力学与合并程度强烈依赖于液滴间及液滴内的相互作用参数。

Conclusion: 研究结果有助于深入理解趋硬性驱动的聚合物液滴合并机制，对微流控（microfluidics）和喷墨打印（ink-jet printing）等基底性质变化的实际应用具有参考价值，同时可为生物表面上多细胞聚集体之间的相互作用提供基础认识。

Abstract: Here, we study the coalescence of two droplets that are moving in the same direction on a soft surface; the motion of the droplets is caused by a gradient in the surface stiffness. As reference, stationary coalescence of the same droplets is also studied on the corresponding uniform surfaces for different stiffness values. To describe the coalescence phenomenon on a surface with stiffness gradient, a relevant range of velocity ratios of the leading and the trailing droplet was considered to elucidate the effect of this parameter on coalescence. Moreover, to analyze the dynamics of the process, the temporal growth of the bridge height $(h)$ was investigated, which follows a power law $(h \sim t^α)$, before eventually attaining a constant value. The obtained values of $α$ show a transition from a higher to a lower value as a function of time, pointing to the presence of two distinct power-law growth regimes, where the transition signifies the crossover from the capillarity-dominated regime to the viscoelasticty-dominated regime of coalescence. In addition, varying attractive strengths for droplet--droplet and intra-droplet interactions were considered. The results indicate that both the dynamics and the degree of the coalescence strongly depend on these interaction parameters. Thus, we anticipate that our results will shed more light on the durotaxis-driven coalescence of polymeric droplets for various relevant system parameters, which will have practical implications for applications ranging from microfluidics to ink-jet printing, where substrate properties may vary. In addition, results may add to the fundamental understanding of the interactions among multicellular aggregates moving on biological surfaces.

</details>


### [79] [Coherent modeling of double-folded ring polymers and their underlying random tree structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18355)
*Pieter H. W. van der Hoek,Angelo Rosa,Elham Ghobadpour,Ralf Everaers*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文证明了拓扑约束类基因组聚合物（genome-like polymers）的双重折叠描述——环聚合物（ring polymers）与随机树（random trees）——在构型熵上等价，差异仅源于单棵树的缠绕计数，并提出了自由切换两种表示的连贯框架。该等价性在一致处理相互作用下可推广至相互作用系统，并引入了一个泛化的Amoeba蒙特卡洛算法（Amoeba Monte Carlo algorithm），其静态性质采样比动态环模拟快O(N)，同时可用于制备平衡初态以研究动力学性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑约束下的类基因组聚合物常呈现双重折叠的树状构型，现有两种独立描述（环聚合物层次与随机树层次）虽已获得受控分支活性系综下的构型熵表达式，但两者之间的等价关系尚未明确建立，阻碍了两种表示的自由转换与统一分析框架的形成。

Method: 通过解析推导证明两种描述的构型熵等价，差异仅在于单棵树的不同缠绕计数（wrappings of a single tree）贡献；在此基础上建立自由切换两种表示的连贯框架，并提出一种泛化的Amoeba蒙特卡洛算法以生成尺寸波动的所需树系综。

Result: 环层次与树层次的描述在构型熵上等价，且该等价性在一致处理相互作用时可扩展至相互作用系统。泛化的Amoeba算法能够生成树系综，其静态性质采样结果与动态环模拟一致，但计算复杂度低O(N)；同时，该算法可用于制备平衡初态以支持环模型研究动力学性质。

Conclusion: 本文建立的等价框架统一了环与树两种描述，为拓扑约束聚合物的静态与动态性质研究提供了高效的计算工具，展示了树算法在静态采样上的速度优势以及环模型在动力学研究中的实用性。

Abstract: Topologically constrained genome-like polymers often double-fold into tree-like configurations, which can be modelled on the level of folded (ring) polymers or on the level of the underlying random trees. For both descriptions, we have recently obtained expressions for the configurational entropy in ensembles with controlled branching activity. Here we demonstrate that they are equivalent up to a contribution originating from the number of distinct wrappings of a single tree. This allows us to develop a coherent framework for freely switching between the two representations. Importantly, the equivalence extends to interacting systems provided the interactions are treated consistently on the tree and on the ring level. To demonstrate the utility of the scheme, we introduce a generalization of the Amoeba Monte Carlo algorithm capable of generating the required ensembles of trees with fluctuating sizes. While the tree algorithm reproduces results obtained by dynamic simulations of the corresponding ring model, it is $O(N)$ faster for the purpose of sampling static properties and leverages the utility of the ring model for the study of dynamical properties, when used for the preparation of equilibrated starting states.

### [80] [Ultrasonic determination of crystallographic texture by transmitted field fitting regardless of medium dispersivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16556)
*Diego A. Cowes,Juan I. Mieza,Martín P. Gómez*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种全波场波形拟合策略（full-field wave fitting strategy），通过模拟透射超声场并与实验测量直接对比，实现对晶体学织构（crystallographic texture）的非破坏性测定。该方法不依赖体波或板波近似，适用于多种样品厚度，且无需正交对称性假设，可表征一般各向异性材料。采用Hashin-Shtrikman均匀化框架计算有效弹性响应，结合GPU加速优化求解非线性反问题，在约10分钟内完成测量与反演，实验结果与独立衍射测量一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统超声织构反演方法（体波与导波技术）受几何约束限制：体波方法难以用于薄样品，导波方法仅适用于较小厚度；此外，许多方法假设集合体具有正交对称性（orthotropic symmetry），限制了在高各向异性材料（highly anisotropic materials）中的应用。因此需要一种不依赖上述近似和对称性假设的通用织构测定方法。

Method: 采用全波场波形拟合策略，直接模拟透射超声场并与实验测量对比。有效弹性响应通过Hashin-Shtrikman均匀化框架（homogenization framework）计算，该框架提供比经典Voigt-Reuss-Hill平均值更紧的界（tighter bounds），从而在优化中约束可行搜索空间。非线性反问题采用GPU加速优化方案求解。

Result: 该方法在六方（hexagonal）和立方（cubic）晶体对称性材料上进行了验证，覆盖多种样品厚度。反演得到的织构系数（texture coefficients）与独立衍射测量结果一致。弱弹性各向异性（weak elastic anisotropy）织构也被成功恢复。完整测量与反演在约10分钟内完成。

Conclusion: 提出的全波场波形拟合策略消除了对样品厚度和宏观对称性假设的限制，适用于一般各向异性材料。该方法在精度和效率上均有良好表现，展现了鲁棒性和通用性，为工程材料的快速、非破坏性织构表征提供了一种可行方案。

Abstract: The determination of crystallographic texture through elastic wave propagation offers a cost-effective, nondestructive means of obtaining through-thickness information with minimal sample preparation. Existing ultrasonic approaches rely on either bulk-wave or guided-wave velocity measurements for texture inversion. These strategies impose geometric constraints: bulk-wave methods become impractical for thin specimens, whereas guided-wave techniques are limited to relatively small thicknesses. Furthermore, many formulations assume orthotropic symmetry of the aggregate, thereby restricting their applicability to materials with higher anisotropy. In this work, a full-field wave fitting strategy is developed in which the transmitted ultrasonic field is simulated and directly compared to experimental measurements. Because the approach does not rely on bulk-wave or plate-wave approximations, it remains applicable across a broad range of specimen thicknesses. Furthermore, no macroscopic symmetry assumptions are imposed on the aggregate, enabling the characterization of generally anisotropic materials. The effective elastic response is computed using a Hashin-Shtrikman homogenization framework, which provides tighter bounds than classical Voigt-Reuss-Hill averages and constrains the admissible search space during optimization, thereby improving convergence. The nonlinear inverse problem is solved using a GPU-accelerated optimization scheme. The methodology is validated on materials with hexagonal and cubic crystal symmetry over a range of specimen thicknesses. The inferred texture coefficients show consistent agreement with independent diffraction measurements. Additionally, textures with weak elastic anisotropy are successfully recovered, demonstrating the robustness and versatility of the proposed method. Complete measurement and inversion are achieved within approximately 10 minutes.

</details>


### [81] [Crystal growth and characterization of the ultra-high temperature substrate $\mathrm{Ta_{1-x}Hf_{x}C_{0.5}}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16583)
*Evan N. Crites,Sharad Mahatara,Joshua R. Hummel,Sydney R. Laywell,Ahamed Raihan,Shivashree S. Gowda,Ethan A. Scott,Amitayush Jha Thakur,Jessica L. McChesney,Patrick E. Hopkins,MVS Chandrashekhar,Michael G. Spencer,Stephan Lany,Satya K. Kushwaha,Tyrel M. McQueen*

Result: Laue 衍射证实生长晶锭具有大尺寸单晶区域。单晶 X 射线衍射表明材料具有 AA 型堆叠的层状结构，属三方空间群 P-3m1，晶格参数 a=3.1168(4) Å，c=4.9644(4) Å。XPS 显示 Hf:Ta 比接近名义值 0.8:0.2。DFT 计算表明该结构由碳空位形成能（carbon-vacancy formation energy）所稳定。表面抛光将 RMS 粗糙度从 130 nm 降至 7 nm。室温热导率 κ=18.1(4) W·m⁻¹·K⁻¹。

Abstract: Incorporation of $\mathrm{Al_{y}Ga_{1-y}N}$ (AGN) semiconductors into high power electronics offers efficiency improvements in power transmission, generation, and use, if approaches to eliminate the defects arising from film-lattice mismatch can be established. Here, we report the optical floating zone crystal growth of $\mathrm{Ta_{1-x}Hf_{x}C_{0.5}}$ (x = 0.2), a new metallic substrate material family lattice matched to the ultra-wide-band-gap, Al-rich side (y = 0.91) of the AGN solid solution. Laue diffraction demonstrates large single crystal domains in the as-grown boule. Single crystal x-ray diffraction at T = 213 K in conjunction with first principles calculations shows that the material adopts a layered crystal structure with AA-type stacking of (Ta/Hf)-C-(Ta/Hf) trilayers described in the trigonal space group P-3m1 (#164), with a = 3.1168(4) Å, c = 4.9644(4) Å, and $β$ = 120.0°. X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy (XPS) measurements show the Hf:Ta ratio to be close to the nominal value of 0.8:0.2 in the grown crystal. Density Functional Theory calculations reveal that this structure is stabilized by the low energy of carbon-vacancy formation of a hypothetical $\mathrm{(Ta/Hf)_{1}C_{1}}$ anti-NiAs structure type, and imply flexibility in interface structure with an overlayer nitride film. ### [82] [Machine Learning Approaches to Point Defects in Non-Metallic Materials: A Review of Methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16611)
*Yu Kumagai,Shin Kiyohara*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文综述了机器学习（machine learning, ML）在非金属材料点缺陷中的应用，重点聚焦于缺陷形成能的预测。现有方法分为直接ML模型和机器学习势（MLPs）两类。文章指出数据集质量是实际模型性能的主导因素，并将带电缺陷形成能视为核心前沿问题，强调需谨慎处理费米能级对齐、有限尺寸修正和长程静电效应以实现跨材料的可迁移预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非金属材料中点缺陷的形成能是材料性能的关键参数，但传统计算方法（如第一性原理）计算成本高，难以高效处理大量候选材料。机器学习方法有望加速缺陷形成能的预测，因而亟需系统梳理现有ML方法的进展与瓶颈，明确关键挑战与未来方向。

Method: 综述将现有方法归纳为两类：(1) 直接ML模型，基于局域结构表示（local structural representations）直接预测缺陷能量学；(2) 机器学习势（machine-learning potentials, MLPs），通过近似含缺陷的势能面（potential energy surface）进行预测。

Result: 研究发现，数据集质量（dataset quality）通常是决定实际模型性能的主导因素。同时，带电缺陷形成能（charged-defect formation energies）被识别为当前的核心前沿问题，涉及费米能级对齐（Fermi-level alignment）、有限尺寸修正（finite-size corrections）以及长程静电效应（long-range electrostatics）等关键环节。

Conclusion: 为了实现不同材料间有意义的比较与可迁移的预测（transferable predictions），未来的研究必须谨慎且一致地处理带电缺陷形成能中的费米能级对齐、有限尺寸修正和长程静电问题。数据集质量的提升也是突破当前瓶颈的关键。

Abstract: We review recent machine-learning (ML) approaches for point defects in non-metallic materials, with an emphasis on defect formation energies. Existing studies largely fall into two categories: direct ML models that predict defect energetics from local structural representations, and machine-learning potentials (MLPs) that approximate the defect-containing potential energy surface. We summarize key achievements as well as persistent bottlenecks, emphasizing that dataset quality often dominates practical model performance. We further identify charged-defect formation energies as a central frontier, where Fermi-level alignment, finite-size corrections, and long-range electrostatics must be handled carefully and consistently to enable meaningful comparisons and transferable predictions across different materials.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用多物理场仿真（multiphysics simulation）进行了有限元分析（finite element analysis），利用完全三维模型（fully 3D model）对破坏圆柱对称性（broken cylindrical symmetry）的单匝线圈进行了有限元法计算。

Conclusion: 单匝线圈中的电流、温度和磁场表现出强烈的非线性扩散特性，是导致其内部磁场时空分布不均匀的根本原因。

Abstract: The single-turn coil method is a destructive pulsed magnet for generating over 100 T with a few $μ$-second pulse duration, and it inevitably causes the coil to explode. The temporal and spatial distributions of the electric current and magnetic field are highly inhomogeneous, arising from the skin effect, rapid temperature rise, and coil deformation. To grasp the dynamic phenomena in the single-turn coil, we conducted a finite element analysis using multiphysics simulation. We employed finite element method calculations using a fully 3D model of the single-turn coil with broken cylindrical symmetry. The calculated result revealed highly nonlinear diffusion of electric current, temperature, and magnetic fields, which are the sources of the inhomogeneous magnetic fields inside the single-turn coil in time and space.

### [84] [Learning inelastic constitutive models from stress-strain data under hard thermodynamic constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16837)
*Filippo Masi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 提出了一种热力学约束学习框架（thermodynamics-constrained learning framework），将非平衡热力学（non-equilibrium thermodynamics）、客观性（objectivity）和稳定性（stability）作为硬约束（hard constraints）嵌入模型架构，用于从标准宏观数据中学习本构模型（constitutive models）。框架在解析基准和颗粒介质模拟中展现出对不可见加载路径的良好泛化能力，并能自主恢复可解释的内变量（interpretable internal variables）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于物理的机器学习方法大多仅部分满足物理和热力学要求，在材料行为的广泛一致性及对未见加载路径（unseen loading paths）的鲁棒泛化方面存在不足，尤其是在仅有有限测量数据时问题更为突出。

Method: 该方法通过将非平衡热力学原理、客观性和稳定性作为硬且可扩展的约束嵌入神经网络架构，构建热力学约束学习框架；利用应力-应变加载路径（stress-strain loading paths）的分析基准进行训练，并将框架应用于基于离散元法（discrete element method）数值模拟的颗粒介质（granular media）实验。

Result: 在解析基准上，该方法学习了热力学一致且鲁棒的本构模型，并能泛化至更具挑战性的未观测路径，自主恢复捕捉路径依赖演化的内变量。在颗粒介质应用中，模型发现了底层本构方程，预测了循环加载（cyclic loading）响应，包括训练数据中不存在的迟滞现象（hysteresis）。

Conclusion: 通过硬约束强制执行非平衡热力学是实现数据驱动本构模型（data-driven constitutive models）发现中鲁棒性、一致性和可扩展性的一种原则性途径。

Abstract: Machine learning approaches informed by physics have offered new insights into the discovery of constitutive models from data, helping overcome some limitations of traditional constitutive modelling while reducing the cost of otherwise computationally intensive simulations. Yet, most existing approaches only partially enforce the requirements of physics and thermodynamics, leaving open questions about their consistency across a broad range of material behaviours and their ability to generalise robustly to unseen loading paths when only limited measurements are available.
  This work establishes a thermodynamics-constrained learning framework whose architecture embeds the principles of non-equilibrium thermodynamics, objectivity and stability as hard, scalable constraints to learn constitutive models from standard macroscopic data. Analytical benchmarks involving stress-strain loading paths demonstrate that the method learns thermodynamically consistent and robust constitutive models for a range of inelastic materials of increasing complexity. At inference, the resulting models generalise to more demanding, unobserved paths and can autonomously recover interpretable internal variables that capture path-dependent evolution. The framework is then applied to granular media, prototypical heterogeneous and history-dependent materials for which constitutive modelling remains challenging. Trained on numerically simulated experiments based on the discrete element method, the model discovers the underlying constitutive equations and predicts responses under cyclic loading, including the emergence of hysteresis absent from the training data, relying solely on macroscopic stress-strain histories. The findings indicate that enforcing non-equilibrium thermodynamics through hard constraints represents a principled route to robust, consistent, and scalable data-driven discovery of constitutive models.

### [85] [An Efficient Approach for Calculating Free Energy in Molecular Dynamics: Demineralization of Hydroxyapatite as a Case Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16957)
*Mahdi Tavakol,Jin-Chong Tan,Alexander M. Korsunsky*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究针对分子动力学模拟中时间尺度受限的问题，提出了一种基于Jarzynski方程的自适应非平衡功自由能计算方法，通过结合高质量与低质量自由能值构建完整自由能曲线，证明初始结构的质量和平衡程度比模拟数量更关键，在最优情况下显著降低了计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分子动力学（Molecular Dynamics）模拟在材料科学、物理学和生物学中能提供微观细节的洞见，但其最大瓶颈是时间尺度受限——模拟时间尺度比真实过程低数个数量级。自由能计算（free energy calculations）理论上可克服这一障碍，尤其适用于生物矿化（biomineralisation）等稀有事件（rare events）和长时间尺度现象的建模，但该领域尚缺乏最佳实践规范。

Method: 本研究比较了基于Jarzynski方程（Jarzynski equation）的非平衡功自由能计算结果与在48核Intel Xeon Platinum 8268 CPU上每次耗时75天的可逆拉动模拟（reversible pulling simulations）结果。设计了一种自适应自由能计算方法（adaptive free energy calculation methodology），将高质量、高计算成本的自由能值与低质量、低成本的值相结合，逐步构建完整的自由能曲线（free energy profile）。

Result: 研究表明，自由能计算的准确性关键在于初始结构（initial structures）的质量和平衡程度（equilibration），而非模拟数量的多少。所提出的自适应方法在最优情况下，相较于常规非平衡功方法和可逆模拟，均大幅降低了计算成本。

Conclusion: 通过关注初始结构的质量而非模拟数量，非平衡功自由能计算方法的计算效率可以得到显著提升。自适应方法为长时间尺度分子动力学模拟中的自由能估算提供了一种更高效的技术路径。

Abstract: Despite the strength of Molecular Dynamics simulations in providing insights into the microscopic details of phenomenon in many fields in materials science, physics and biology, the biggest barrier is its limited timescale which is several orders of magnitude lower than the timescale of the real-world processes and phenomena being modeled. Free energy calculations are designed as a remedy to this problem that in theory can overcome this barrier. This is particularly relevant for biomineralisation processes such as tooth mineral formation and dissolution, while reflecting a broader challenge in accurately modelling rare events and long-timescale phenomena across complex molecular systems. However, due to the novelty of the field, a number of questions remain outstanding pertaining to the best practice of applying this method. The non-equilibrium work approach based on the Jarzynski equation is one of the most promising free energy calculation methods. However, the biggest challenge for the broader use of this method is the question of how many simulations are required for an accurate free energy estimation. Comparing the free energy results with very long reversible pulling simulations of atom clusters from the surface, each taking 75 days on the 48-core Intel Xeon Platinum 8268 CPUs, in this study we showed that this question is irrelevant and higher quality and better equilibrated initial structures is the proper approach than simply based on the number of simulations. We designed a new adaptive free energy calculation methodology which combines high quality, high computational cost free energy values with lower quality, lower cost values to build up the entire free energy profile. In the best case scenario this method lowers manifold the computational cost required for the non-equilibrium work free energy calculations compared to both the regular method and the reversible simulation.
