### [86] [First-principles calculations of electrical conductivities of edge-modified graphene nanoribbons: strain effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16965)
*Sanjay Prabhakar,Roderick Melnik*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究基于第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations），系统分析了应变工程（strain engineering）对三种扶手椅型石墨烯纳米带（armchair graphene nanoribbons, aGNRs）——原始型（7aGNRsH）、硼掺杂型（7aGNRsH-B）和单碳原子空位型（7aGNRsH-V）——电学性质及贝里曲率（Berry curvature）的影响，发现应变可使原本不导电的半导体型纳米带转变为宽谱段导电材料，并在金属型纳米带中观察到贝里曲率分布的非平凡特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 石墨烯纳米带在传感器和光电器件中具有潜在应用价值，而应变工程是调控其电学性质的有效手段。本文旨在通过第一性原理计算，深入理解应变对不同类型扶手椅型石墨烯纳米带电导率和贝里曲率的影响机制。

Method: 选择了三种具有7个锯齿形边缘（zigzag edges）的扶手椅型石墨烯纳米带：原始型（7aGNRsH）、硼掺杂型（7aGNRsH-B）和单碳原子空位型（7aGNRsH-V），以及双原子硼掺杂的p型体系（7aGNRsH-2B）。基于第一性原理计算，分析了应变作用下各体系的电导率和贝里曲率变化。

Result: 未施加应变时，原始7aGNRsH呈非导电态；施加应变后，其在红外（IR）、可见光（visible）至紫外（UV）的宽能谱范围内转变为导电态。金属型的7aGNRsH-B和7aGNRsH-V在应变前后均表现出非零电导率。贝里曲率分析显示，半导体型无应变7aGNRsH的费米子（fermions）遍布整个布里渊区（Brillion zone），而施加应变引起面外变形后，费米子局域在Γ点附近；金属型7aGNRsH-B和7aGNRsH-V的费米子则远离Γ点。此外，双原子硼掺杂的7aGNRsH-2B在红外能谱区间出现大的电导率峰，该信号可能在实验中可检测。

Conclusion: 应变工程可显著调控扶手椅型石墨烯纳米带的电学性质，特别是使半导体型体系在宽波段内实现导电性转换；贝里曲率分布对应变和掺杂/缺陷类型敏感，反映了费米子在倒易空间（reciprocal space）中不同的局域化特征。双硼掺杂体系在红外波段的高电导率峰具有实验可观测性，为相关传感器和光电器件设计提供了指导。

Abstract: We investigate the influence of strain on the electrical properties of graphene nanoribbons that have potential applications in making sensors and other optoelectronic devices. In particular, we chose pristine armchair graphene nanoribbons with 7 zigzag edges (7aGNRsH), boron doped armchair graphene nanoribbons with 7 zigzag edges (7aGNRsH-B) and armchair graphene nanoribbons with 7 zigzag edges that have one carbon atom vacancy (7aGNRsH-V). Based on first-principles calculations, results show that pristine unstrained 7aGNRsH is electrically nonconductive but turns to be electrically conductive in a wide range of energy spectrum, e.g., from IR to visible to UV, due to the application of strain engineering. In metallic unstrained and strained 7aGNRsH-B and 7aGNRsH-V, non-vanishing electrical conductivity in the IR, visible and UV energy spectrum regimes are observed. We also investigate the influence of strain on the Berry curvature of 7aGNRsH, 7aGNRsH-B and 7aGNRsH-V nanoribbons. The results show that fermions are spread through out the Brillion zone in the reciprocal space for semiconducting unstrained 7aGNRsH but localized near the $Γ$-point for strained 7aGNRsH that have out-of-plane deformations due to strain engineering. For metallics 7aGNRsH-B and 7aGNRsH-V, Berry curvature plots show that fermions are localized far away from the $Γ$-point. In two atom boron doped p-type armchair graphene nanoribbons with 7 zigzag edges (7aGNRsH-2B), large peaks in electrical conductivity at IR energy spectrum regimes can be observed. These peaks of electrical conductivities in 7aGNRSH-2B may be detectable in experimentally synthesized structure in Reference, JACS 137, 8872 (2016).

### [87] [Frequency renormalization and its effects in nonlinear phononics with $Q_RQ_{IR}^{2}$-type coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17241)
*Yijie Zeng*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过微扰方法研究具有最低阶耦合形式 $Q_RQ_{IR}^2$ 的双声子系统，解析地得到了声子位移和频率的结果。红外（IR）活性模的频率重整化导致拉曼（Raman）模的整流效应在强泵浦场下趋于饱和。对于简并红外模与耦合形式 $Q_R(Q_{IR,x}^2-Q_{IR,y}^2)$ 的情况，在椭圆或线偏振超短中红外脉冲共振泵浦下，红外模频率会发生分裂，同时实现拉曼整流和磁化。这些结果揭示了一种第一性原理计算无法捕捉的非线性声子学（nonlinear phononics）动力学效应，将动态多铁性（dynamical multiferroicity）拓展至具有耦合 $Q_R(Q_{IR,x}^2-Q_{IR,y}^2)$ 的系统，且该方法可推广至更高阶耦合。强泵浦场下的振幅饱和效应为克服这一非线性效应提供了未来研究方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用微扰方法（perturbation method）对具有最低阶耦合 $Q_RQ_{IR}^2$ 的双声子系统进行分析，推导出声子位移和频率的解析解。对简并红外模情况，考虑耦合形式 $Q_R(Q_{IR,x}^2-Q_{IR,y}^2)$，并引入椭圆或线偏振超短中红外脉冲作为共振泵浦。

Result: 红外活性模的频率重整化（frequency renormalization）导致拉曼模整流效应在强泵浦场下出现饱和；在简并红外模系统中，椭圆或线偏振共振泵浦引发红外模频率分裂，同时实现拉曼整流与磁化。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了一种第一性原理计算无法捕捉的非线性声子学动力学效应，并将动态多铁性推广至具有 $Q_R(Q_{IR,x}^2-Q_{IR,y}^2)$ 耦合的系统。所提出的方法可适用于更高阶耦合情况。强泵浦场下的振幅饱和效应为后续研究克服该非线性限制提供了方向。

Abstract: A two-phonon system with lowest-order coupling of form $Q_RQ_{IR}^2$ is studied by perturbation method, and analytic results for both phonon displacements and frequencies are obtained. The frequency renormalization of infrared (IR) active mode brings the rectification of Raman mode to saturate at high pump field. For degenerate IR mode with coupling of form $Q_R(Q_{IR,x}^2-Q_{IR,y}^2)$, the frequency of IR mode will split when resonantly pumped by elliptically or linearly polarized ultrashort mid-IR pulse, realizing Raman rectification and magnetization simultaneously. Our results reveal a dynamical effect of nonlinear phononics not captured by first-principles calculation, extend the dynamical multiferroicity to systems with coupling $Q_R(Q_{IR,x}^2-Q_{IR,y}^2)$, and the method can be readily applied to higher-order couplings. The amplitude saturation under strong pump field stimulates future researches to overcome this nonlinear effect.

### [88] [Causal Anomaly Detection for Lithium-Ion Battery Degradation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17334)
*Dieter W. Heermann,Hagen Heermann*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 提出CausalHealth框架，利用因果图发现和k近邻转移熵从锂离子电池常规循环遥测数据中提取三种信号类异常分数，构建置信度加权的综合健康指数，实现早期退化检测，在七种电池上达到100%检测率，并用电化学阻抗谱实验验证了物理合理性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 锂离子电池早期退化检测需要健康指标兼具物理可解释性，且能从常规循环遥测数据中计算，无需访问退化区域内部信息。现有方法在这两方面存在不足。

Method: 应用因果图发现（causal graph discovery）和k近邻转移熵（k-nearest-neighbour transfer entropy）处理每周期电压、电流、温度和电阻时间序列；将12个异常评分组织为三类信号束（幅度-偏移、预测-残差、复杂度-熵），并构建置信度加权综合健康指数（RWMHI）进行跨束融合。

Conclusion: CausalHealth框架能够从常规遥测数据中实现高可靠性的早期退化检测，且经电化学阻抗谱验证具有物理基础，适用于多种电池化学体系。

Abstract: Reliable early detection of lithium-ion battery degradation requires health indicators that are physically interpretable and computable from routine cycler telemetry without access to the degradation region. We introduce \textsc{CausalHealth}, a framework that applies causal graph discovery and $k$-nearest-neighbour transfer entropy to per-cycle voltage, current, temperature, and resistance time series, and organises twelve resulting anomaly scores into three signal-class bundles (Magnitude-shift, Predictive-residual, Complexity-entropy) -- with Isolation Forest reported separately as it falls below the bundle reliability threshold -- to characterise detection sensitivity across ten commissioning fractions (5--30\,\%). The Magnitude-shift class achieves 100\,\% detection across all seven tested cells spanning LFP (MIT--Stanford MATR) and LCO (NASA PCoE, CALCE CS2) chemistries, with a lead time of up to 402 cycles before conventional capacity-threshold failure on gradual-fade cells. A Reliability-Weighted Master Health Index (RWMHI) -- a cross-bundle fusion of five high-reliability detectors weighted by inverse coefficient of variation -- improves lead time by 15--52 cycles over the class median on long-lived cells while maintaining 100\,\% detection. Validation against electrochemical impedance spectroscopy on an NMC prismatic cell provides independent physical grounding: transfer entropy $\mathrm{TE}(R \!\to\! V)$ correlates with charge-transfer resistance $R_{\mathrm{ct}}$ (pooled $r = +0.990$; temperature-controlled partial $r = +0.898$), and an Arrhenius analysis of both quantities yields an activation energy consistent with published NMC charge-transfer kinetics. These results are evaluated on seven cells across three benchmark datasets.

*Kristýna Repček,Tomáš Grabec,David Mareš,Pavla Stoklasová,Petr Sedlák,Jakub Kušnír,Petr Veřtát,Oleg Heczko,Sebastian Fähler,Klara Lünser,H. Seiner*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用瞬态光栅光谱学（transient grating spectroscopy, TGS）对3微米厚的外延NiTi薄膜进行原位表征，测量其在热致相变温度循环（奥氏体→R相→马氏体→奥氏体）中的弹性系数和热扩散率。

Result: 弹性性质表现出剪切模量交叉（shear moduli crossover）：在奥氏体中c' < c44，在马氏体中c' > c44。热扩散率在R相与奥氏体之间变化高达450%。该剧烈变化以及R相与奥氏体之间无滞后的特性使NiTi成为热开关的候选材料。

Conclusion: 热扩散率的变化源于R相的异常热容（anomalous heat capacity）。TGS研究提供了模拟基于NiTi的热管理微系统所需的温度依赖热学和弹性性质。

Abstract: Shape memory alloys like NiTi are at the core of emerging thermal management applications, including elastocaloric refrigeration, thermoelastic harvesting, and latent heat storage. Most of these applications benefit from a small scale due to the accelerated heat exchange, but obtaining precise functional properties of films is challenging. Here we demonstrate that transient grating spectroscopy (TGS) enables characterization of elastic coefficients and thermal diffusivity of a 3 $μ$m thick epitaxial NiTi film during a thermally induced phase transformation. The in-situ measurement of a complete austenite$\rightarrow$R-phase$\rightarrow$martensite$\rightarrow$austenite temperature cycle reveals that the elastic properties exhibit a crossover of the shear moduli (from $c^\prime < c_{44}$ in austenite to $c^\prime > c_{44}$ in martensite) and that the thermal diffusivity changes by 450 $\%$ between the R-phase and austenite. This dramatic change, together with the absence of hysteresis between the R-phase and austenite, makes NiTi a promising material candidate for thermal switches. The results indicate that the change in thermal diffusivity originates from an anomalous heat capacity of the R-phase. Furthermore, our TGS study provides temperature-dependent thermal and elastic properties required for simulating thermal management microsystems using this material.

### [90] [Microstructure evolution during rapid solidification of hypoeutectic Al-Ag alloys near absolute stability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17576)
*Brian Rodgers,Mingwang Zhong,Trevor Lyons,John Roehling,Joseph T. McKeown,Alain Karma,Amy J. Clarke*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过动态透射电子显微镜（Dynamic Transmission Electron Microscopy, DTEM）、相场（phase-field, PF）模拟和锐界面线性稳定性分析，证明在足够浓缩的亚共晶Al-Ag合金中，可在远低于增材制造（additive manufacturing, AM）典型生长速率（约1 m/s）的条件下达到绝对稳定极限（absolute stability limit, V_abs），从而实现无微观偏析（microsegregation-free）微观结构的形成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用动态透射电子显微镜（DTEM）对激光点熔化Al-Ag薄膜后的快速凝固前沿演化进行实时观测，并结合事后微观结构表征（postmortem microstructural characterization）。同时，开展相场（PF）模拟，并利用从PF模型中提取的非平衡、依赖速度的相图（velocity-dependent phase diagram），进行锐界面线性稳定性分析（sharp-interface linear stability analysis）。

Result: 分析预测V_abs随Ag浓度的变化趋势与混溶间隙（miscibility gap）相似，先增大后减小。预测的V_abs值在整个亚共晶成分范围内与PF模拟结果定量吻合，并且在三种浓缩合金的实验中也得到了验证。

Conclusion: 这些结果为指导和控制在增材制造（AM）条件下、接近绝对稳定极限的浓缩合金中微观结构的形成提供了依据。

Abstract: Microsegregation-free microstructures can form by solidifying at velocities beyond the absolute stability limit ($V_{\text{abs}}$), where solute partitioning is suppressed by a stable, planar solid-liquid interface. Producing such microstructures is of considerable practical interest; however, $V_{\text{abs}}$ typically exceeds the ${\sim}1$ m/s growth rates encountered in additive manufacturing (AM). Here we demonstrate the absolute stability limit can be reached in sufficiently concentrated hypoeutectic Al-Ag alloys at growth rates well below the 1~m/s typically encountered in additive manufacturing. Dynamic Transmission Electron Microscopy (DTEM) of rapid solidification front evolution -- following laser spot melting of Al-Ag thin films -- combined with postmortem microstructural characterization, enables detailed quantitative comparison with both phase-field (PF) simulations and a sharp-interface linear stability analysis that uses a non-equilibrium, velocity-dependent phase diagram extracted from the PF model. The analysis predicts that $V_{\text{abs}}$ follows a trend similar to that of the miscibility gap, first increasing and then decreasing with Ag concentration. Predicted values of $V_{\text{abs}}$ are in good quantitative agreement with PF simulations over the entire hypoeutectic concentration range and with experiments for three concentrated alloys. These results inform the prediction and control of microstructural development in concentrated alloys near the absolute stability limit under AM conditions.

*Laku Dorjee Tamang,Shivraj Gurung,Bhanu Chettri,Nguyen Thanh Tien,Le Huu Nghia,Darwin Barayang Putungan,Ranjit Thapa,Kailash Chandra Bhamu,Dibya Prakash Rai*

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算，系统研究了二维同质双层NbOX₂（X=Cl, Br, I）的结构、电子、光学及光催化性质。

Abstract: Motivated by our previous work on bulk NbOX2 , where we have reported its high 1dielectric polarisation and finite piezoelectric response, this work extends to its 2D homo bilayer system to explore its potential for photocatalytic water splitting. Herein, density functional theory (DFT) were employed in probing the structural, electronic, optical, and photocatalytic properties of 2D homo bilayer NbOX2 (X = Cl, Br, and I). Our results show that structurally, NbOCl2 and NbOBr2 prefer AC bilayer stacking,while AB stacking was preferred by NbOI2 . All the considered bilayers are dynamically, thermally, and mechanically stable. From the analysis of electronic structure we have found a decreasing trend in the energy band gap as X goes down the group from Cl to I, with the position of the valence band maximum shifting upward along the high symmetry points. In terms of carrier mobility, all 2D bilayer systems possess high carrier mobility comparable to known 2D materials. It also exhibits an anisotropic carrier transfer property by which charge carriers are separated efficiently. These materials show similar trends to BiOI and PtSe2 , in which photocatalytic efficiency was increased by forming the multiple layers. The materials under investigation are suitable for photocatalytic water splitting under visible and ultraviolet regions with absorption coefficients of 105 cm-1.

### [92] [Finite-width adiabatic shear banding and dislocation patterning in mesoscale polycrystalline aggregates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17619)
*Siddharth Singh,Rajat Arora,Janith Wanni,Charles Adkins,Raymond Rasmussen,Noah J. Schmelzer,Dan J. Thoma,Curt A. Bronkhorst,Amit Acharya*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用介观位错力学模型，引入与GND密度相关的硬化长度尺度，并结合经典晶体塑性模型（crystal plasticity model）和Voce各向同性硬化律。进行二维（截面）和三维（包含100万有限单元的模拟）统计代表性体积元（statistically representative volume element）模拟，结果与实验样品对比验证。

Abstract: Dynamic shear banding under adiabatic conditions in a mesoscale polycrystalline aggregate is studied using a model of mesoscale dislocation mechanics and experiments. The model involves a length scale related to hardening induced by excess/polar/geometrically necessary dislocation (GND) density, and utilizes a simple classical crystal plasticity model with isotropic Voce law hardening. Simulations of statistically representative volume elements of a polycrystal determined from experimental samples are conducted. Studies in 2-d (section) and 3-d capture the experimentally observed finite-width shear bands and the formation of low-angle subgrain boundaries even in the absence of heat conduction in the model, as well as size-dependent strengthening for grain sizes from 1 to 20 $μ$m. The 2-d and large-scale 3-d simulations, the latter involving 1 million finite elements, provide access to the progressive evolution of material strength, stress state, and temperature in the course of large deformations. GND distributions accumulate at grain boundaries and form patterned structures within grain interiors, offering insight into the microstructural changes that precede failure in adiabatic shear bands. Mesh-converged, delocalized and localized plastic flow to very large deformations without softening is observed for a significant range of parameters, reflecting a competition between GND hardening and thermal softening in setting the non-softening steady state in the absence of other ductile damage mechanisms in the model.

### [93] [Ferroelectric polarization controlled orbital Hall conductivity in a higher-order topological insulator: \textit{d1T}-phase monolayer MoS$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17722)
*Yingjie Hu,Heng Gao,Wei Ren*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文预测单层 d1T 相 MoS₂ 是一种高阶拓扑绝缘体（higher-order topological insulator），同时具备铁电特性。研究展示了其非平庸拓扑指数、体带隙内的角态及量化分数电荷，发现了能隙内非零的轨道霍尔电导（orbital Hall conductivity）平台，并揭示了铁电极化方向可调制轨道霍尔电导的正负值，为外电场可控的轨道电子学（orbitronics）提供了理论与材料候选。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高阶拓扑绝缘体是传统拓扑绝缘体的推广，但其材料实现仍然有限；同时，探索拓扑态与铁电性之间的耦合关系，对于实现电场可调的轨道电子学功能具有重要意义。

Method: 基于理论分析与第一性原理计算，研究单层 d1T-MoS₂ 的拓扑性质与电子结构。通过计算拓扑不变量（topological index）验证非平庸拓扑性，识别体带隙内的角态（corner states）及量化分数电荷；计算轨道霍尔电导平台以表征高阶拓扑序，并分析铁电极化方向对轨道霍尔电导的调制作用。

Result: 验证了 d1T-MoS₂ 的高阶拓扑绝缘体性质，观察到体带隙内的角态与量化分数电荷；在能隙内发现非零轨道霍尔电导平台；铁电极化方向可调控轨道霍尔电导 σ_{\rm{OH}}^x 的正负值。

Conclusion: 该工作为铁电性可调的轨道霍尔效应提供了理论与具体材料候选，有望推动外电场可控的轨道电子学器件发展。

Abstract: The higher-order topological insulator is an extended concept of the conventional topological insulator, which obeys the generalization of the standard bulk-boundary correspondence. In our paper, we predict the monolayer \textit{d1T}-phase transition metal dichalcogenide MoS$_2$ to be a higher-order topological insulator, while also possessing intriguing ferroelectric characteristics. We explicitly demonstrate the nontrivial topological index and reveal the hallmark corner states with quantized fractional charge within the bulk band gap. Second, we show the existence of a nonzero orbital Hall conductivity plateau within the energy gap which is a signature to identify higher-order topology system. Additionally, we investigate the relationship between the ferroelectricity and the orbital Hall conductivity of \textit{d1T} MoS$_2$ and find that the direction of ferroelectric polarization can modulate the positive and negative values of the orbital Hall conductivity $σ_{\rm{OH}}^x$. Our findings provide the theory and material candidate for ferroelectricity tunable orbital Hall effect which is promising to realize the external electric field controllable orbitronics.

</details>


### [94] [Thermal Transport in Defective Uranium Nitride: Effects of Point Defects, Anharmonicity, and Electronic Contributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17726)
*Beihan Chen,Marat Khafizov,Zilong Hua,David H. Hurley,Miaomiao Jin*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文利用机器学习原子间势（MLIP）结合Green-Kubo（GK）和简正模分析（NMA）方法，系统研究了点缺陷对铀氮化物（UN）在300-1500 K范围内热输运的影响，揭示了四声子散射在高温非简谐声子输运中的必要性，以及不同点缺陷对声子散射的选择性作用和电子-缺陷散射对总热导率的关键影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解点缺陷对UN热输运的影响对于核燃料材料的热管理至关重要，但此前缺乏统一的微观机制解释，尤其是不同类型缺陷（间隙和空位）对声子和电子输运的差异化作用尚不清晰。

Method: 采用机器学习原子间势（machine learning interatomic potential, MLIP）结合Green-Kubo（GK）方法和简正模分析（normal mode analysis, NMA）方法，在300-1500 K范围内进行计算；同时利用ShengBTE程序包含三声子和四声子散射过程，并通过半经典电子-缺陷散射模型引入缺陷-电子贡献。

Result: 在完美UN中，四声子散射（four-phonon scattering）对高温非简谐声子输运是必要且充分的；在缺陷体系中，所有点缺陷均显著降低低温热导率，其中铀间隙（IU）在宽声子谱上引起强散射，而其他缺陷产生选择性散射；总热导率与实验吻合，600 K以上电子贡献占主导；缺陷对热导率的退化程度排序为IU > VU > IN > VN，且缺陷体系中电子-声子耦合可忽略。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了UN中依赖于点缺陷类型的热输运的统一理解，阐明了四声子散射、缺陷-声子散射以及电子-缺陷散射在不同温度区间和缺陷类型下的相对重要性，为核燃料材料的热设计提供了微观理论基础。

Abstract: The impact of point defects on thermal transport in uranium nitride (UN) is investigated using a MLIP combined with Green-Kubo (GK) and normal mode analysis (NMA) methods over 300-1500 K. In pristine UN, temperature-dependent calculations of lattice thermal conductivity reveal that four-phonon scattering is essential yet sufficient to accurately capture high temperature anharmonic phonon transport, as evidenced by close agreement between GK and ShengBTE calculations including three- and four-phonon processes. In defective systems, all types of point defects significantly reduce thermal conductivity at low temperature. Mode-resolved analysis further shows that interstitial defects introduce new phonon states due to a stronger local strain effect. Notably, the uranium interstitial leads to strong defect-phonon scattering over broad phonon spectrum, while the other point defects produce more selective scattering, with even reduced phonon scattering for some acoustic modes. The optical contribution to thermal conductivity remains nearly constant in the presence of IU, but decreases with increasing temperature for pristine and the other defect types. The total thermal conductivity, incorporating electron-phonon coupling and an estimated electronic contribution, yields excellent agreement with experiment in the pristine system, with electronic contributions dominating thermal transport above 600 K. Moreover, with defect-electron contribution introduced through a semiclassical electron-defect scattering model, it is found that (i) the total conductivity degradation follows IU, VU, IN, and VN in descending order, and (ii) electron-phonon coupling becomes negligible in defective systems. These results provide a unified understanding of defect-dependent thermal transport in UN.

### [95] [Anomalies in the thermal conductivity of honeycomb antiferromagnet MnPS$_{3}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17785)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究对象为蜂巢晶格反铁磁体（honeycomb antiferromagnet）MnPS₃（奈尔温度T_N=78 K），在极低温（<0.01T_N）至高温区间测量其热霍尔电导率和纵向热导率随外磁场的变化。

Conclusion: 上述低温异常归因于磁振子能带中贝里曲率的重新分布（redistribution of Berry curvature）。该结果证明了热霍尔测量在探测磁性绝缘体（magnetic insulators）中贝里曲率分布方面具有优越性能。

Abstract: Intrinsic two-dimensional magnets serve as a good platform to explore collective, charge-neutral and low-energy excitations. Distinguishing the crucial role of them in experimental aspect remains a challenge for decades. Here, we study the thermal transport in honeycomb antiferromagnet MnPS$_{3}$ with $T_N$=78 K down to very low temperatures (<0.01$T_N$). At high temperatures (>0.1$T_N$), the field dependence of the thermal Hall conductivity exhibits a linear phonon Hall effect and a peak associated with the spin-flop transition due to a strong spin-lattice coupling, well reproducing the previous report (Phys. Rev. B 110, 165147 (2024)). Notably, below 2 K, we find that the field dependence of the thermal Hall conductivity exhibits sign reversals within the spin-flop phase, at which the field dependence of the longitudinal thermal conductivity also shows multiple valleys. We suggest that these anomalies are caused by the redistribution of Berry curvature in magnon bands, demonstrating the superior performance of the thermal Hall measurements to detect the Berry curvature distributions in magnetic insulators.

Conclusion: 无金属杂原子掺杂是一种有效且可持续的策略，可通过调控电荷分离和反应选择性来提升C₃N₄的光催化H₂O₂生成性能。

Abstract: The photocatalytic production of hydrogen peroxide (H$_2$O$_2$) from water is a promising strategy for solar-to-chemical energy conversion. Mechanistic studies indicate that oxygen activation mainly follows a two-electron (2e$^{-}$) pathway driven by charge-carrier modulation and reactive oxygen species dynamics, with singlet oxygen and photogenerated holes playing a dominant role. In addition, S-doped C$_3$N$_4$ retained over 95\% of its activity after five cycles. ### [97] [Indicators for phonon hydrodynamics from first principles predictions of thermal conductivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17947)
*Nikhil Malviya,Navaneetha K. Ravichandran*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出以完整线性化佩尔斯-玻尔兹曼方程（LPBE）与弛豫时间近似（RTA）计算的热导率之比（κ_LPBE/κ_RTA）作为声子流体动力学（phonon hydrodynamics）的低成本指示器，并指出该比值随布里渊区（BZ）采样密度增大而下降，需谨慎收敛；传统基于Normal和Umklapp散射率的方法不足以预测该现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 流体动力学热流（hydrodynamic heat flow）在石墨中被实验观察到，但为加速发现其他具备该非傅里叶热流（non-Fourier heat flow）行为的材料及适宜实验条件，需要一种计算高效、基于第一性原理（first principles）的指示指标。

Method: 通过比较完整线性化佩尔斯-玻尔兹曼方程（linearized Peierls-Boltzmann equation, LPBE）与弛豫时间近似（relaxation time approximation, RTA）求解所得热导率之比（κ_LPBE/κ_RTA），作为判断声子流体动力学（phonon hydrodynamics）强弱的标准。

Result: 集体漂移的非平衡声子会放大κ_LPBE/κ_RTA比值，而小比值对应扩散主导的声子输运；该比值随布里渊区（Brillouin zone, BZ）采样密度增大而下降，影响若干超高导热材料在低温下的流体动力学特征强度；传统基于Normal与Umklapp散射率的RTA和Callaway近似不足以预测声子流体动力学。

Conclusion: κ_LPBE/κ_RTA是一个计算成本低廉且有效的声子流体动力学指示器，可加速新型非常规热流材料的发现；同时强调BZ采样收敛研究对确保可靠预测的必要性。

Abstract: Hydrodynamic heat flow, where out-of-equilibrium phonons collectively drift in response to an applied temperature differential, has attracted renewed interest following its experimental observation in graphite at temperatures as high as 300 K. To accelerate discovery of material alternatives to graphite and suitable experimental conditions for realizing this non-Fourier heat flow regime, computationally efficient indicators derived from predictive first principles approaches are necessary. Here we show that the ratio of thermal conductivity ($κ$) obtained from the complete solution of the linearized Peierls-Boltzmann equation (LPBE) for phonon transport ($κ_{LPBE}$), to that from the relaxation time approximation (RTA) for phonon decay ($κ_{RTA}$), is a low cost indicator for phonon hydrodynamics. We show that collectively drifting non-equilibrium phonons amplify the ratio of $κ_{LPBE}$ to $κ_{RTA}$, while a small $κ_{LPBE}/κ_{RTA}$ correlates with predominantly diffusive phonon transport. On the other hand, we find that conventional approaches that rely only on momentum-conserving Normal and momentum-dissipating Umklapp scattering rates, such as the RTA and the Callaway approximations to the LPBE, are inadequate to predict phonon hydrodynamics. Furthermore, our study reveals that the indicator ratio - $κ_{LPBE}/κ_{RTA}$, and therefore the strength of hydrodynamic signatures, decrease with increasing Brillouin zone (BZ) sampling density for several ultrahigh-$κ$ materials at low temperatures, thus underscoring the need for careful BZ sampling convergence studies to ensure robust predictions of phonon hydrodynamics. This computationally inexpensive indicator of phonon hydrodynamics will accelerate the search for new materials that exhibit such unconventional heat flow regimes.

</details>


### [98] [Real-time Multi-instrument Autonomous Discovery of Novel Phase-change Memory Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18033)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出MAD框架，采用多输出模型（multi-output model），通过协同区域化核（co-regionalization kernel）同时融合XRD与电阻测量数据；利用非负矩阵分解（non-negative matrix factorization, NMF）最大化晶体结构分布的知识，同时并行寻找最大电阻值的成分。

Conclusion: 该框架为大型自主设施开辟了新研究路径，未来实验可并行运行而非独立进行。

Abstract: Autonomous labs enable the integration of automated experiment execution, data analysis and decision making. The main challenge remains the integration of diverse data streams from multiple instruments, where the data is often heterogeneous and unsynchronized. The standard learning process of undetermined synthesis-process-structure-property relationships (SPSPR) usually relies on post-experiment analysis after data is fully collected, not during live experiments, and decision making is carried out independently across characterization equipment. Here, we demonstrate the Multi-instrument Autonomous Discovery (MAD) framework -- combining structural property mapping and functional property optimization simultaneously in a closed-loop manner. As an example, we applied MAD to phase change memory (PCM) materials, and, in particular on the Mn-Sb-Te ternary, a previously unexplored materials system for PCM. A multi-output model is employed to merge data from x-ray diffraction (XRD) and electrical resistance measurements simultaneously through a co-regionalization kernel that models the relationship between them. The output probabilistic posterior and uncertainty quantification facilitate decision making with shared knowledge, while the goals are different across tasks. We aimed to maximize the knowledge of crystal structure distribution using non-negative matrix factorization (NMF), while in parallel, we find the composition with the maximum resistance value, an important figure of merit for PCM. Leveraging MAD, we found promising electrical PCMs and identified the SPSPR within 25 closed-loop iterations, corresponding to a seven-fold speed-up. The framework opens a new path of study in large-scale autonomous facilities, where future experiments can be run in parallel together, not independently.

### [99] [Why hole polaron formation on oxygen is limiting the Fermi level in Fe acceptor doped BaTiO$_{3}$ under oxidizing conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18258)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density-functional theory, DFT），结合占据矩阵控制（occupation-matrix control）和基于分段线性（piecewise-linearity）的Hubbard修正（DFT+U）处理O-2p态，对Fe掺杂BaTiO₃中氧化空穴的定位进行第一性原理计算。

Yet, the experimentally accessible picture based on electron-paramagnetic resonance (EPR) is dominated by Fe$^{3+}$-related signatures, while Fe$^{4+}$ is not a straightforward observable. Here we show that this apparent discrepancy reflects the preferred location of the oxidizing hole: not on Fe, but on oxygen. Using density-functional theory with with occupation-matrix control and a piecewise-linearity-based Hubbard correction (DFT+$U$) for O-2$p$ states, we find that an oxygen-centered hole polaron is forming a Fe$^{3+}$-O$^{-}$ complex that is lower in energy than the formal Fe$^{4+}$ configuration. Our results identify ligand-hole formation as a favorable charge-compensation mechanism in oxidized Fe-doped BaTiO$_3$ and provide an explanation for the predominance of Fe$^{3+}$-based centers in spectroscopy. *Kai D. Röseler,Geo Sciarini,Felix Eder,Samuel Moody,Vladimir Pomjakushin,Fabian O. von Rohr*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过溶剂热阳离子交换法首次合成了此前未被报道的碲化物 Cu$_{1-x}$CrTe$_2$（$x \approx 0.3$），该材料仅在约 90 °C 的窄温窗内形成，在 239 K 发生磁结构转变进入反铁磁态，并在 250 °C 分解为尖晶石相 CuCr$_2$Te$_4$，强调了低温拓扑化学路径在合成亚稳态含 Cu(I) 碲化物中的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在层状铜铬二硫属化物系列 CuCr$X_2$ 中，氧化物、硫化物和硒化物已有报道，但碲化物 CuCrTe$_2$ 始终未能合成；本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 采用低温溶剂热阳离子交换法（solvothermal cation exchange），以 K$_{1-x}$CrTe$_2$（$x \approx 0.3$）和 CuBr 为前驱体，在约 90 °C 的窄温度窗口内合成目标产物。

Result: 成功合成了 Cu$_{1-x}$CrTe$_2$（$x \approx 0.3$），其在奈尔温度（Néel temperature）$T_\mathrm{N}=239$ K 发生磁结构转变（magnetostructural transition）进入反铁磁（antiferromagnetic）态，该 $T_\mathrm{N}$ 值高于其他 $A$CrTe$_2$ 相，并与铁磁全脱嵌的 CrTe$_2$ 相当。该化合物为亚稳态，在低至 250 °C 时即分解形成尖晶石（spinel）CuCr$_2$Te$_4$。

Conclusion: 低温拓扑化学（topochemical）路线对于获取传统固态合成无法获得的亚稳态含 Cu(I) 碲化物至关重要。

Abstract: In the layered copper chromium dichalcogenide series CuCr$X_2$, the oxide, the sulfide, and the selenide analogues have been reported, but the telluride CuCrTe$_2$ has remained unsynthesized so far. Here, we report the synthesis of Cu$_{1-x}$CrTe$_2$ ($x \approx 0.3$), which forms only within a narrow temperature window near 90 °C by solvothermal cation exchange of K$_{1-x}$CrTe$_2$ ($x \approx 0.3$) and CuBr. Cu$_{1-x}$CrTe$_2$ undergoes a magnetostructural transition to an antiferromagnetic state at $T_\mathrm{N}=239$ K, a Néel temperature that is high relative to other $A$CrTe$_2$ phases and comparable to that of ferromagnetic, fully-deintercalated CrTe$_2$. Cu$_{1-x}$CrTe$_2$ is metastable and decomposes at temperatures as low as 250 °C to form spinel CuCr$_2$Te$_4$. These results highlight the importance of low-temperature topochemical routes for accessing metastable Cu(I)-containing tellurides that are inaccessible by conventional solid-state synthesis.

</details>

# cond-mat.mes-hall [[Back]](#toc)

### [102] [Nonlinear Ohmic electromagnetic response](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16367)
*Anwei Zhang,Zheng Cai,C. M. Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文在松原格林函数（Matsubara Green's function）框架下系统研究了二次谐波产生与双线性磁电效应中的非线性欧姆响应，发现并预言了一种由能带几何（band geometry）引起的本征欧姆电导，并基于二维狄拉克模型（two-dimensional Dirac model）论证了其可观测性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对非线性欧姆响应（nonlinear Ohmic response）的微观机制理解尚不充分，尤其是在双线性磁电效应（bilinear magnetoelectric effect）中由能带几何诱导的贡献未被识别，因此需要建立统一的理论框架加以描述。

Method: 采用松原格林函数形式论（Matsubara Green's function formalism）对二次谐波产生（second-harmonic generation）和双线性磁电效应中的非线性欧姆电导进行系统分析；利用二维狄拉克模型（two-dimensional Dirac model）进行数值验证。

Result: 光学非线性欧姆电导包含一个类德鲁德（Drude-like）的非线性部分和一个由全对称归一化量子度量偶极（fully symmetrized normalized quantum metric dipole）决定的本征项；在双线性磁电响应中预言了一种此前未被认识的、源自能带几何（band geometry）的本征欧姆电导，其横向行为与光学对应类似。

Conclusion: 该几何诱导的非线性欧姆响应在高费米速度（high Fermi velocity）与窄带隙（narrow band gaps）材料中可观测，为凝聚态系统中非线性欧姆输运（nonlinear Ohmic transport）提供了系统的量子场论描述框架。

Abstract: We systematically investigate nonlinear Ohmic responses in second-harmonic generation and bilinear magnetoelectric effects within the Matsubara Green's function formalism. The optical nonlinear Ohmic conductivity is shown to consist of a nonlinear Drude-like part and an intrinsic term determined by the fully symmetrized normalized quantum metric dipole. Notably, we predict a previously unrecognized intrinsic Ohmic conductivity arising from band geometry in the bilinear magnetoelectric response, which exhibits transverse behavior similar to its optical counterpart. Using a two-dimensional Dirac model, we demonstrate that this geometrically induced nonlinear Ohmic response is observable in materials with high Fermi velocity and narrow band gaps. Our work provides a systematic quantum field-theoretic framework for describing nonlinear Ohmic transport in condensed matter systems.

</details>


### [103] [Long Spin Relaxation Times in CVD-Grown Nanodiamonds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16394)
*Jeroen Prooth,Michael Petrov,Alevtina Shmakova,Michal Gulka,Petr Cigler,Jan D'Haen,Hans-Gerd Boyen,Milos Nesladek*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文报道了一种先进的荧光纳米金刚石（fluorescent nanodiamond, FND）生长技术，通过在预设计位点上进行异质成核，制备出平均尺寸约60 nm、纵向相干时间（T₁）均值达800 μs（最高超过1.8 ms）的高质量FND。该性能相比同类商用纳米金刚石提升了近十倍，并进一步探讨了面向近表面传感应用的壳层结构制备及可扩展性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前荧光纳米金刚石（FND）在生物传感（biosensing）应用中，其对外部场的灵敏度受限于晶格缺陷，这些缺陷显著影响自旋纵向弛豫时间（T₁）和自旋横向弛豫时间（T₂）等关键量子态特征。因此，亟需改进FND生长工艺以提升相干时间性能。

Method: 采用一种先进的FND生长技术，通过在预设计位点上进行异质成核（heterogeneous nucleation on pre-engineered sites）来控制金刚石的成核与生长过程。同时，制备了重氮掺杂的纳米金刚石壳层（heavy-N doped nanodiamond shells），并基于{111}晶面上的再成核（re-nucleation）和孪晶（twinning）机制对其进行了讨论。

Result: 制备的FND平均尺寸约60 nm，纵向相干时间（T₁）均值达800 μs，最大值超过1.8 ms，接近块体（bulk）理论值。相较于同尺寸范围（50–150 nm）的商用纳米金刚石，性能实现了近十倍的显著提升。

Conclusion: 该方法大幅提升了FND的自旋相干时间，使其接近块体理论极限，为高灵敏度量子传感应用提供了材料基础。同时，文章讨论了重氮掺杂壳层结构及其在近表面传感中的潜力，并指出了实现规模化生产以满足传感应用需求所需解决的可扩展性（scalability）问题。

Abstract: Currently, the primary applications of fluorescent nanodiamonds (FNDs) are in the area of biosensing, by using photoluminescence or spin properties of colour centres, mainly represented by the Nitrogen Vacancy (NV) point defect. The sensitivity of NV-FNDs to external fields is, however, limited by crystallographic defects, which influence their key quantum state characteristics - the spin longitudinal (\textit{T$_1$}) and spin transversal (\textit{T$_2$}) relaxation and coherence times, respectively. We report on utilising an advanced FND growth technique consisting of heterogeneous nucleation on pre-engineered sites to create FNDs averaging around 60 nm in size, with mean longitudinal coherence times of 800 $μ$s and a maximum over 1.8 ms, close to bulk theoretical values. This is a major, nearly ten-fold improvement over commercially available nanodiamonds for the same size range of 50 to 150 nm. Heavy-N doped nanodiamond shells, important for sensing events in nm proximity to the diamond surface, are fabricated and discussed in terms of re-nucleation and twinning on \{111\} crystal facets. We also discuss scalability issues in order to enable the production of FND volumes matching the needs of sensing applications.

</details>


### [104] [Berry-phase in a periodically driven single molecule magnet transistor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16635)
*Gabriel Gonzalez*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文利用 Floquet 和 Landauer 形式理论，计算了在横向磁场和交流门电压作用下单分子磁体晶体管的电子输运性质，发现时间周期势诱导的零透射共振随横向磁场振荡，该振荡源于两条量子隧道路径间的贝里相位干涉，并可在特定能量电子的电导中检测到。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究在横向磁场和交流驱动门电压共同作用下，单分子磁体晶体管（single molecule magnet transistor）的电子输运行为，特别关注时间周期势对量子干涉和电导特性的影响。

Method: 采用 Floquet 形式理论和 Landauer 形式理论，计算电导随电子能量和横向磁场的变化关系。

Result: 发现时间周期势（time periodic potential）会导致零透射共振（zero transmission resonances）出现，该共振随横向磁场呈现振荡行为。这种振荡源于两条量子隧穿路径（two quantum tunneling paths）之间的贝里相位干涉（Berry phase interference）。

Conclusion: 贝里相位振荡（Berry phase oscillations）可以在特定能量入射电子的电导随横向磁场变化的关系中被实验检测到。

Abstract: We consider the electron transport through a single molecule magnet transistor in the presence of a local transverse magnetic field and ac-driven gate voltage. We calculate the conductance as a function of the electron energy and transverse magnetic field by using the Floquet and Landauer formalism. We show that the time periodic potential causes zero transmission resonances that oscillate as a function of the transverse magnetic field due to the Berry phase interference associated with two quantum tunneling paths. We find that these Berry phase oscillations can be detected in the conductance as a function of the transverse magnetic field for an incoming electron with a specific energy.

</details>


### [105] [Emergent impedance due to antiferromagnetic domain wall dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16778)
*Yuta Yamane,Jotaro J. Nakane,Yasufumi Araki,Jun'ichi Ieda*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文理论上研究了反铁磁体（antiferromagnets）中由畴壁动力学（domain-wall dynamics）诱导的涌现阻抗（emergent impedance），并导出了交流电流下反铁磁畴壁电响应的解析表达式，揭示了两种不同动力学模式对涌现阻抗的贡献及其竞争机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 涌现阻抗此前已在螺旋磁体（spiral magnets）中被预测和观察到，但反铁磁畴壁中的涌现阻抗机制尚不明确，需要发展相应的理论形式来描述其电响应行为。

Method: 发展了交流电流下反铁磁畴壁电响应的理论形式（formalism），并推导了涌现阻抗的解析表达式。

Result: 发现两种动力学模式对涌现阻抗起不同作用：畴壁中心的平移运动（translational motion）产生与速度成正比的贡献，类似螺旋磁体；另一种反铁磁畴壁特有的贡献来源于运动畴壁内局域子晶格磁化强度（sublattice magnetizations）的时间依赖性倾斜（time-dependent canting），其大小与反铁磁交换耦合常数成反比。两者竞争决定了亚共振频率下涌现阻抗虚部的符号和大小。

Conclusion: 该结果为反铁磁体中的电子输运提供了基础物理洞察，并为基于反铁磁体的新型自旋电子学（spintronics）器件开辟了可能性。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate emergent impedance induced by domain-wall dynamics in antiferromagnets. Emergent impedance, arising from a combined action of spin-transfer torque and spinmotive force, was previously predicted and observed in spiral magnets. Here we develop a formalism for the electrical response of an antiferromagnetic domain wall under ac currents, and obtain analytical expressions for the resulting emergent impedance. We find that two dynamical modes play separate roles in the emergent impedance: Translational motion of the domain-wall center generates a contribution proportional to its velocity, analogous to that arising from the corresponding motion of a spiral magnet. Another contribution, unique to antiferromagnetic domain walls, originates from the time-dependent canting of the sublattice magnetizations localized within the moving domain wall, whose magnitude is inversely proportional to the antiferromagnetic exchange coupling constant. The competition between these two distinct contributions determines the sign and magnitude of the imaginary part of the emergent impedance at sub-resonant frequencies. Our results provide a fundamental insight into electron transport in antiferromagnets, and open avenues for novel antiferromagnet-based spintronics devices.

</details>


### [106] [New Source of Spin-hot spot in displaced silicon double quantum dots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16947)
*Sanjay Prabhakar*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文分析了声学声子形变势引起的自旋弛豫，发现单量子点在低面内磁场下弛豫率高度敏感，而双量子点中出现一种新型自旋热点（spin-hot spot），其弛豫率比传统单量子点低约三个数量级；当量子点间距约60 nm时，还可观测到自旋热点振荡，弛豫率较传统高场热点低约四个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在双量子点中控制电子自旋是实现下一代固态量子比特（solid-state qubit）器件的关键，理解自旋弛豫机制（尤其是自旋热点行为）对于优化量子比特的相干时间和操作保真度至关重要。

Method: 研究基于理论分析，利用声学声子（acoustic phonon）的形变势（deformation potential）机制，分析单量子点（single quantum dot）和双量子点（double quantum dot）中的自旋弛豫（spin relaxation）行为。研究考虑了面内（in-plane）和面外（out-of-plane）磁场的影响，并通过改变量子点间距和磁场强度进行参数化计算。

Result: 单量子点中，自旋弛豫率对低于1 T的面内磁场高度敏感，并在自旋热点区域收敛。双量子点中，当量子点被拉开时出现新型自旋热点，自旋弛豫率比传统单量子点低约三个数量级。在磁场约束主导的位移量子点中，两个不同的自旋热点出现在不同面内磁场强度下，弛豫时间从毫秒到皮秒不等。量子点间距约60 nm时，随面内磁场变化出现自旋热点振荡，弛豫率比传统高场自旋热点（约4.5 T）低约四个数量级。

Conclusion: 双量子点中极低的自旋弛豫率使得在自旋热点处制备量子比特（qubit）叠加态成为可能，为量子计算与信息处理提供了有利条件。

Abstract: Controlling electron spins in double quantum dots allows individual electrons to be trapped and manipulated for next-generation solid-state qubit devices. In this paper, the study analyzes spin relaxation due to deformation potentials of acoustic phonon in single and double quantum dots under in-plane and out-of-plane magnetic fields, showing that in single quantum dots the relaxation rate is highly sensitive to low in-plane magnetic fields ($<1T$) but converges near a spin-hot-spot region. In a single quantum dot, the spin-hot spot arises from well-understood level crossings between singlet and triplet states. In double quantum dots, a new and unusual spin-hot spot appears as the dots are pulled apart from the origin, with spin-relaxation rates three orders of magnitude lower than conventional single quantum dots. In displaced quantum dots dominated by magnetic confinement, two distinct spin-hot spots appear at different in-plane magnetic field strengths, where spin-relaxation time varies from millisecond to picosecond. When quantum dots are separated by about 60 nm, calculations predict oscillations in spin-hot spots as the in-plane magnetic field changes. These unusual spin-hot spot oscillations occur at low magnetic fields ($<1T$), resulting in spin-relaxation rates about four orders of magnitude lower than those of conventional high-field spin-hot spots ($\approx 4.5T$). The extremely low spin-relaxation rate at the spin-hot spot enables the preparation of qubit superposition states for quantum computing and information processing.

</details>


### [107] [Observation of a Mott quantum spin Hall insulator in twisted WSe2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17335)
*Yifei Jin,Yaqi Ma,Aoqian Zhang,Nan Zhang,Ulf Lampe,Ivana Wong,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Tze Kin Cheung,Ning Wang,Kaifei Kang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文报道在2.29度扭曲WSe2器件的第二个莫尔能带半填充处，观测到磁场稳定的莫特绝缘态（Mott insulating state）中存在量子自旋霍尔（QSH）边缘输运。该态与单粒子QSH态具有相同的电阻平台，表明相同的螺旋边缘通道数量；输运测量显示近量子化电阻对电场、垂直磁场及5K以下温度不敏感，非局域输运和负面内磁导进一步证实了强关联体系中的鲁棒边缘输运。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，量子自旋霍尔绝缘体（QSH insulator）和莫特绝缘体（Mott insulator）被视为两种截然不同的绝缘相，分别源于能带拓扑和强库仑相互作用。本研究旨在探究强关联（strongly correlated）的莫特绝缘态中能否存在拓扑保护的QSH边缘输运，从而建立相互作用鲁棒性拓扑输运的物理机制。

Method: 采用2.29度扭曲WSe2器件，在第二个莫尔能带半填充处通过外加磁场稳定莫特绝缘态，开展电输运测量，包括电阻平台对比、垂直电场和垂直/面内磁场依赖、非局域输运（nonlocal transport）以及温度依赖的霍尔测量（Hall measurement）。

Result: 该莫特绝缘态在半填充时表现出与第一莫尔价带全填充单粒子QSH态相同的电阻平台，近量子化电阻对垂直电场、垂直磁场和5K以下温度不敏感；非局域输运显著，面内磁导呈现强负性；温度依赖霍尔测量给出约10K的特征温度尺度，对应约1meV的能量尺度。

Conclusion: 结果表明，自旋守恒的QSH边缘态可以在半填充的强关联绝缘相和外加磁场条件下持续存在，为在莫尔量子材料（moire quantum materials）中实现抗相互作用的拓扑输运开辟了新路径。

Abstract: Quantum spin Hall (QSH) insulators and Mott insulators are conventionally regarded as distinct insulating phases, arising from band topology and strong Coulomb interactions, respectively. Here, we report the observation of QSH edge transport in a magnetic-field-stabilized Mott insulating state at half filling of the second moire band in a 2.29 degree twisted WSe2 device. This state exhibits a resistance plateau identical to that of the single-particle QSH state at full filling of the first moire valence band, indicating the same number of helical edge channels. Electrical transport measurements reveal nearly quantized resistance that is insensitive to vertical electric field, out-of-plane magnetic field, and temperature below 5 K. Pronounced nonlocal transport and strong negative in-plane magnetoconductance further support helical edge conduction, establishing robust edge transport in the strongly correlated regime. Temperature-dependent Hall measurements reveal a characteristic temperature scale of approximately 10 K, corresponding to an energy scale of about 1 meV. Our results demonstrate that spin-conserved QSH edge states can persist in a half filled, strongly correlated insulating phase and under external magnetic field, opening a route toward interaction-resilient topological transport in moire quantum materials.

</details>


### [108] [Durable Enhancement of $\mathbf{MoS_2}$ Single-Layer Photoluminescence by Ultraviolet Laser Treatment Under Ambient Conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17363)
*Mahan Bakhshikhah,Jiří Liška,Rahul Kesarwani,Jindřich Mach,Ondřej Červinka,Petr Dub,Jiří Spousta,Jan Přibyl,Jana Kalbáčová Vejpravová,Tomáš Šikola*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出一种非破坏性紫外激光处理方法，可将剥离和化学气相沉积（CVD）生长的单层二硫化钼（MoS₂）的光致发光（photoluminescence, PL）强度增强8倍以上，并在环境条件下保持长期稳定（CVD样品72天、剥离样品32天），同时实现PL特性的空间可控调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单层二硫化钼（MoS₂）在纳米光电子学中具有重要潜力，但实现高强度、长期稳定的光致发光（PL）发射仍是一个挑战。

Method: 采用非破坏性紫外（UV）激光处理方法，对剥离法和CVD生长的单层MoS₂进行处理；并在氩气、氮气和氧气等可控气氛环境中进行对照实验，以区分氧气作为PL处理剂的作用。

Result: PL强度最大增强超过8倍；PL信号出现三子（trion）到中性激子（neutral exciton）的转变；拉曼E₂ᵍ¹和A₁ᵍ振动模式发生蓝移，分别表明电子耗尽（p型掺杂）和Mo-O键形成；PL增强效果可在环境条件下保持长期稳定（CVD样品72天，剥离样品32天）；可实现UV激光处理区域的精准空间控制。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一种可靠的、可永久调控单层MoS₂ PL特性的处理路径，为面向实用化高性能纳米光子器件迈出了关键一步。

Abstract: Single-layer molybdenum disulfide ($MoS_2$) possesses significant potential for nanoscale optoelectronics, but achieving high-intensity, long-term-stable photoluminescence (PL) emission remains a challenge. In this work, we demonstrate a remarkably robust, more than 8-fold maximum enhancement in the PL intensity of exfoliated and CVD-grown single-layer $MoS_2$ via a non-destructive ultraviolet (UV) laser treatment method. This substantial increase in radiative efficiency is accompanied by a trion-to-neutral exciton transition in the PL signal and a corresponding blue shift of the Raman $E_{2g}^1$ and $A_{1g}$ vibrational modes, signaling successful electron depletion (p-doping) and formation of Mo-O bonds, respectively. Furthermore, we demonstrate precise spatial control over PL properties by confining PL treatment exclusively to the UV laser-treated area. Crucially, the enhanced PL performance shows exceptional longevity; the CVD sample and the exfoliated sample remained stable for the entire monitoring period (72 and 32 days, respectively) under ambient conditions. We further investigated UV laser treatment in a controlled-environment chamber under argon, nitrogen, and oxygen atmospheres, distinguishing the influence of oxygen as the PL treatment agent. These findings establish a reliable pathway for the permanent treatment of single-layer $MoS_2$ PL properties, an essential step toward practical, high-performance nanophotonic devices.

</details>


### [109] [Geometry-Driven Nonlinear Orbital Magnetoelectric Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17462)
*Jinxiong Jia,Zhenhua Qiao,Jian Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种非线性轨道磁电效应（nonlinear orbital magnetoelectric effect），可在中心对称材料中产生轨道磁化二次方响应，并为实验观测提供了理论框架和可区分判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 线性轨道磁电效应在中心对称材料（centrosymmetric materials）中被严格禁止，现有框架无法在此类系统中实现轨道磁电耦合。

Method: 采用扩展半经典表述（extended semiclassical formulation），推导出规范不变（gauge-invariant）的微观理论，分离本征（intrinsic）与非本征（extrinsic）贡献，并建立它们对弛豫时间（relaxation time）的不同依赖关系。

Result: 在二维系统中，非线性响应受面外旋转对称性（out-of-plane rotational symmetries）的约束远小于线性效应，显著扩大了可实现的材料范围；微观上主导贡献由厄米连接结构（Hermitian-connection structure）控制；非线性轨道磁电效应的量级处于当前先进磁光克尔测量（magneto-optical Kerr measurements）的灵敏度范围内。

Conclusion: 该非线性轨道磁电效应为中心对称材料中实现轨道磁电耦合提供了新途径，其弛豫时间依赖特性可作为实验区分的判据，且实验可测性良好。

Abstract: We propose a nonlinear orbital magnetoelectric effect, which generates orbital magnetization quadratically in centrosymmetric materials where the linear orbital magnetoelectric effect is strictly forbidden. Using extended semiclassical formulation, we derive a gauge-invariant microscopic theory that separates intrinsic and extrinsic contributions and establishes their distinct dependence on the relaxation time, providing an experimental discriminator. In two-dimensional systems the nonlinear response is far less constrained by out-of-plane rotational symmetries than the linear orbital magnetoelectric effect, substantially enlarging the materials platform. Microscopically, the dominant contributions are governed by a Hermitian-connection structure. Finally, we estimate that the magnitude of the nonlinear orbital magnetoelectric effect lies within the sensitivity of state-of-the-art magneto-optical Kerr measurements.

Method: 基于连续弹性力学（continuum elasticity），推导面内位移场的自洽方程，并利用微扰方法（perturbative method）获得层分辨的面内位移场解析表达式。

Result: 解析结果与完整数值解在实验相关参数范围内高度一致；发现异质双层在接近对齐时可能出现由莫尔弛豫引起的压缩面内应变驱动的屈曲不稳定性（buckling instability）。

Abstract: We develop an analytical theory for lattice relaxation in twisted moiré heterobilayers, accounting for lattice mismatch, twist, external biaxial heterostrain, and different elastic constants. Starting from continuum elasticity, we derive the self-consistent equations for the in-plane displacement fields and obtain simple perturbative expressions for the layer-resolved in-plane displacement fields induced by lattice relaxation. We apply our theory to graphene on hBN and representative 2H transition metal dichalcogenide heterobilayers, including MoTe$_2$/WSe$_2$ and WSe$_2$/WS$_2$. Our analytical results agree very well with full numerical solutions over experimentally relevant parameters. We further show that heterobilayers can exhibit a buckling instability near alignment, driven by compressive in-plane strain due to moiré relaxation. Our results provide a simple theoretical framework for incorporating lattice relaxation in realistic moiré heterostructures.

Abstract: Crystalline rhombohedral multilayer graphene (RMG) has emerged as an ideal platform for studying unconventional superconductivity. Here, we report the observation of superconductivity in moiréless rhombohedral heptalayer graphene (RHG) at zero magnetic field. The superconducting phases emerge at low displacement electric fields (|D| < 0.2 V/nm) and are symmetrically distributed about D = 0, with one robust state exhibiting zero resistance and two weaker superconducting features. These results highlight the strong dependence of superconductivity on layer number and electronic structure in RMG systems and provide new insights into its microscopic origin.

### [112] [Geometric symmetry and size-dependent skyrmion phase transitions in magnetic nanostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17939)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用对比分析方法，研究三种几何形状的纳米结构——纳米圆盘（nanodisks）、纳米方形（nanosquares）和纳米矩形（nanorectangles），分别分析其在不同尺寸和垂直外磁场条件下的磁斯格明子态演化行为。

Conclusion: 几何对称性（geometric symmetry）是调控斯格明子稳定性与功能性的关键设计参数，可为多态存储和可重构逻辑器件等自旋电子学应用提供重要指导。

Abstract: We investigate the interplay of geometric symmetry, size, and external magnetic fields in regulating individual skyrmion states within magnetic nanostructures. By analyzing nanodisks, nanosquares, and nanorectangles, we demonstrate that rotational symmetry in nanodisks enables rich topological phase transitions, from ferromagnetic states to skyrmions, skyrmioniums, and multi-states, as their diameter increases. In contrast, square and rectangular structures exhibit suppressed topological complexity due to corner-induced demagnetization effects and reduced symmetries. Under perpendicular magnetic fields, nanodisks show field-driven transitions between skyrmionium and skyrmion states. By leveraging asymmetry, square and rectangular nanostructures stabilize skyrmions over a broader parameter range than nanodisks. These findings highlight geometric symmetry as a critical design parameter for tailoring skyrmion stability and functionality in spintronic applications such as multi-state memory and reconfigurable logic devices.

### [113] [Multi-rotational switching in a noncollinear antiferromagnet by spin-orbit torque](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18009)
*Yuma Sato,Yutaro Takeuchi,Yuta Yamane,Shun Kanai,Shunsuke Fukami*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文报告了一种由自旋轨道矩驱动的非共线反铁磁纳米点中的新型多旋转开关动力学（multi-rotational switching），该过程对脉冲持续时间表现出非传统的阈值电流密度不敏感性，揭示了电流驱动非共线反铁磁体开关的微观机制，为下一代自旋电子学技术提供了新路径。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用非共线反铁磁纳米点（noncollinear antiferromagnetic nanodot），施加宽范围时长和振幅的电脉冲，观测自旋轨道矩（spin-orbit torque）驱动的开关行为。结合理论分析，揭示多旋转开关（multi-rotational switching）的物理机制，包括电流驱动的相干旋转、场致净磁化重定向以及热涨落（thermal fluctuations）三者的相互作用。

Result: 实验发现，在回切事件（switch-back events）中，阈值电流密度（threshold current density）对脉冲持续时间表现出非传统的（unconventional）不敏感性。这一现象归因于一种此前未被认识的过程：非共线反铁磁序（noncollinear antiferromagnetic order）在完成反转前经历多次旋转，称为多旋转开关（multi-rotational switching）。

Conclusion: 多旋转开关（multi-rotational switching）源于三个关键因素的相互作用：电流驱动的非共线反铁磁序相干旋转（coherent rotation）、场致非补偿净磁化（uncompensated net magnetization）的重定向以及热涨落（thermal fluctuations）。这些发现建立了非共线反铁磁体中电流驱动开关的微观机制，为纳米器件中反铁磁序（antiferromagnetic order）的控制开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Spintronics has advanced through discoveries of various electrically-driven spin dynamics in nanomagnets. Here, we report a novel switching dynamics of spin systems driven by spin-orbit torque, using a noncollinear antiferromagnetic nanodot. With electric pulses spanning a wide range of durations and amplitudes, we find an unconventional insensitivity of a threshold current density to pulse duration in switch-back events. This observation is attributed to a previously unrecognized process, in which the noncollinear antiferromagnetic order undergoes multiple rotations before completing reversal, a phenomenon we term multi-rotational switching. Our theoretical analysis reveals that multi-rotational switching arises from the interplay of three key factors: current-driven coherent rotation of the noncollinear antiferromagnetic order, field-induced reorientation of the uncompensated net magnetization, and thermal fluctuations. These findings establish a microscopic mechanism governing current-induced switching in noncollinear antiferromagnets, a topic of growing interest for next-generation spintronics technologies, opening a new route to controlling antiferromagnetic order in nanodevices.

Here, we experimentally demonstrate an approach to realizing strong mechanical nonlinearity in nanomechanical resonators, fully controlled through optical laser drives. Moreover, we demonstrate that the nonlinear optical spring mediates effective interactions between mechanical modes coupled to a common cavity, inducing tunable nonlinear interactions between them that impact spectral response and dynamics. ### [115] [Kapitza-like modulation of near-field radiative heat transfer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18322)
*Mauro Antezza*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于卡皮查机制（Kapitza mechanism）的近场辐射传热（near-field radiative heat transfer）方法，证明对任意控制参数（如真空间隙或材料响应）进行快速调制，会在慢速热动力学中产生二次时间平均修正。该修正分为静态项和动态项，可诱导可测量的温度偏移并改变有效热导，从而稳定或失稳稳态。以SiC平板间的间隙调制为例，推导了解析标度律，预测的温度偏移可在现有实验平台上实现，仅需约Ω≈10⁴ rad/s的低调制频率。研究建立了卡皮查机制的热学类比，为微纳尺度辐射热流控制提供了通用路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索近场辐射传热的动态调控机制，受经典卡皮查热阻（Kapitza resistance）现象的启发，寻求通过参数快速调制来实现对热流的主动控制。

Method: 引入卡皮查式机制：对影响热通量的任意参数（如真空间隙或材料响应）施加快速调制，推导出慢速热动力学中的二次时间平均修正；将该理论应用于SiC平板间的间隙调制，推导解析标度律并预测温度偏移。

Result: 调制产生的修正分为频率无关的静态项和低通动态项；可导致可测量的温度偏移和有效热导（effective thermal conductance）的改变，进而稳定或失稳稳态；在SiC平板间隙调制情形下，预测的温度偏移量在现有实验平台上完全可测量，仅需约Ω≈10⁴ rad/s的低调制频率。

Conclusion: 建立了卡皮查机制在热辐射领域的类比，为微纳尺度平台上的辐射热流控制提供了一条通用路线。

Abstract: We introduce a Kapitza-like mechanism for the near-field radiative heat transfer and show that fast modulation of any parameter controlling the flux, such as the vacuum gap or a material response, produces a quadratic, time-averaged correction in the slow thermal dynamics. This correction splits into a frequency-independent static term and a low-pass dynamical term, yielding sizable modulation-induced temperature shifts and modified effective thermal conductances that can stabilize or destabilize the steady state. Applying the theory to gap modulation between SiC slabs, we derive analytical scaling laws and predict temperature shifts that are fully measurable with existing experimental platforms, requiring only readily accessible low modulation frequencies of order $Ω\approx 10^4~\mathrm{rad/s}$. Our results establish a thermal analogue of the Kapitza mechanism and provide a general route for controlling radiative heat flow in micro- and nanoscale platforms.

### [116] [Qumus: Realization of An Embodied AI Quantum Material Experimentalist](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18407)
*Lihan Shi,Zhaoyi Joy Zheng,Xinzhe Juan,Yimin Wang,Ming Yin,Mayank Sengupta,Kristina Wolinski,Yanyu Jia,Jingzhi Shi,Derek Saucedo,Neill Saggi,Haosen Guan,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Ali Yazdani,Mengdi Wang,Sanfeng Wu*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: Qumus是一个物理具身化（physically embodied）于机器人微型实验室中的多智能体系统（multi-agent system），具备多模态（multimodal）信息处理能力。该系统能够自主完成从假设生成、实验方案规划、多步实验执行、结果分析到报告撰写的完整科学循环（full scientific cycle），并具备自主纠错（autonomous error correction）与闭环实验（closed-loop experimentation）能力。

Result: 该系统首次实现了由AI自主创建石墨烯（graphene），并首次通过AI完成了复杂纳米器件的制造，包括基于范德华堆叠（van der Waals stacking）的原子级薄膜场效应晶体管（field-effect transistors）。Qumus通过展示自主纠错和闭环实验能力，在这些任务中表现出色。

Conclusion: 该研究成果建立了一个可推广的框架（generalizable framework），用于实现能够直接从量子世界中学习的自改进具身化AI系统（self-improving embodied AI systems），为加速量子材料、电子学及更广领域的科学发现开辟了路径。

Abstract: While modern Large Language Models (LLMs) and agentic artificial intelligence (AI) have demonstrated transformative capabilities in digital domains, the realization of embodied AI capable of real-world scientific discovery remains a difficult frontier. The advancements are hindered by the inherent complexity of integrating high-level reasoning, multimodal information processing and real-time physical execution. Here we introduce Qumus, the first AI quantum materials experimentalist. Physically embodied within a robotic mini-laboratory, Qumus is an intelligent, multimodal, and multi-agent system designed for the creation and nano-processing of atomically thin two-dimensional (2D) materials and stacked van der Waals (vdW) structures. Qumus autonomously navigates the full scientific cycle, from hypothesis generation and protocol planning to multi-step experimental execution, result analysis and reporting, acting as an experimentalist. Markedly, the system has achieved, for the first time, the AI-creation of graphene, as well as the first AI-fabrication of complex nanodevices including atomically thin field-effect transistors via vdW stacking. Qumus excels at these tasks by demonstrating autonomous error correction and closed-loop experimentation. Our results establish a generalizable framework for self-improving embodied AI systems that learn directly from the quantum world, opening a pathway toward accelerated discovery in quantum materials, electronics and beyond.

</details>


### [117] [Spin and orbital mixing of edge states in a quantum Hall system proximitized by a superconductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18411)
*S. Maji,M. P. Nowak*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过数值模拟Bogoliubov-de Gennes方程，研究了超导体邻近化量子霍尔系统中的手性Andreev边缘态的形成与输运性质，揭示了Andreev反射导致的边缘模混合、Zeeman分裂、自旋-轨道耦合效应以及电子透射概率的鲁棒简并性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究超导体邻近化的二维量子霍尔系统中手性Andreev边缘态的形成机制及其输运特性，特别是多模和自旋ful系统中非局域电导与透射概率的行为。

Method: 采用Bogoliubov-de Gennes（BdG）方程对系统进行数值建模，分析非局域电导（non-local conductance）和透射概率（transmission probabilities），并分别引入Zeeman相互作用和Rashba自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）进行考察。

Result: Andreev反射过程会导致高阶填充因子下量子霍尔边缘模发生混合；Zeeman相互作用使Andreev边缘态分裂为自旋正交且不混合的独立自旋通道；单独的自旋-轨道耦合引起轻微自旋退极化，但与面内磁场结合时驱动复杂的自旋混合；电子透射概率展现出源于幺正性约束和粒子-空穴对称性的鲁棒简并性。

Conclusion: 超导邻近化量子霍尔系统中Andreev边缘态的输运行为受Andreev反射、Zeeman效应和自旋-轨道耦合的复杂调控，且系统的散射矩阵在磁场和自旋-轨道耦合下受幺正性和粒子-空穴对称性约束，导致透射概率出现稳健的简并特征。

Abstract: We investigate the formation and transport properties of chiral Andreev edge states in a two-dimensional quantum Hall system proximitized by a superconductor. By numerically modeling the system using the Bogoliubov-de Gennes equations, we analyze the non-local conductance and transmission probabilities of multimode and spinful systems. We demonstrate that the Andreev reflection process induces a mixing of the quantum Hall edge modes at higher filling factors, a phenomenon strictly prohibited in clean, purely electronic systems. When incorporating the Zeeman interaction, we show that the Andreev edge states split into uncoupled spin species, maintaining spin orthogonality that prevents mixing between opposite spin sectors. Furthermore, we explore the impact of Rashba spin-orbit coupling. While the spin-orbit interaction alone causes slight spin depolarization, its combination with an in-plane magnetic field drives complex spin mixing among all chiral Andreev bands, fundamentally altering the conductance oscillations. Finally, we reveal that the electron transmission probabilities exhibit robust degeneracies, which emerge as a direct consequence of the unitarity constraints and the particle-hole symmetry of the system's scattering matrix in a magnetic field and the presence of spin-orbit interaction.

</details>

### [118] [Anomalous Diffusion as Structural Memory: An Extended Structural Dynamics Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16337)
*Patrick BarAvi*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文提出，生物系统中常见的次扩散（sub-diffusion）现象并非真正的反常（anomalous），而是由于将三维可变形实体（而非点粒子）的完整动力学投影到平动子空间后自然产生的记忆效应所致。基于扩展结构动力学（Extended Structural Dynamics, ESD）框架，次扩散指数可由内禀模式谱（internal mode spectrum）独立确定，无需拟合扩散数据，并给出了四个可证伪的定量预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统理论将生物系统中的次扩散归因于反常扩散（anomalous diffusion），需要引入分数阶导数（fractional derivatives）、重尾等待时间（heavy-tailed waiting times）或拟合的记忆核（fitted memory kernels）。作者认为这种“反常”实为相空间（phase space）不完整的伪象：标准框架将扩散粒子视为质点，而生物分子是具有三维结构的可变形实体，其位置、取向和内部结构是不可约化的物理属性。

Method: 提出扩展结构动力学（Extended Structural Dynamics, ESD）框架，将每个粒子视为具有平动（translational）、取向（orientational）和形变（deformational）自由度的原始结构实体（primitive structured entity）。当完整相空间上的动力学被投影到平动子空间时，记忆核（memory kernel）自然涌现，无需任何现象学假设。次扩散指数由内禀模式谱（internal mode spectrum）决定，可通过B因子（B-factors）、核磁共振序参数（NMR order parameters）或分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulations）独立测量。

Result: 给出了四个可证伪的定量预测：(1) 次扩散强度与分子柔韧性（molecular flexibility）相关；(2) 温度驱动向正常扩散的交叉，其特征能量尺度由内禀模式频率设定；(3) 非零的旋转-平动交叉相关谱（rotation-translation cross-correlation spectrum）编码了内部动力学信息，在点粒子模型中恒为零；(4) 记忆时间尺度（memory timescales）与粒子尺寸的平方成比例。利用独立估计的结构参数，论文展示了与拥挤环境中蛋白质实验观测的定量一致性。

Conclusion: 从点粒子视角看似反常的次扩散，实际上是结构化物质（structured matter）被投影到贫瘠描述后的预期行为。反常不在于物理本身，而在于所采用的相空间。该工作主张将粒子的内禀结构作为不可忽略的物理属性纳入动力学描述。

Abstract: Sub-diffusion in biological systems is conventionally treated as anomalous, requiring fractional derivatives, heavy-tailed waiting times, or fitted memory kernels. We argue that this anomaly is an artifact of an incomplete phase space. Standard frameworks model diffusing particles as points. Biological molecules are not points. They are three-dimensional deformable entities whose position, orientation, and internal structure are irreducible physical properties, not modeling conveniences appended to a point mass. Within the Extended Structural Dynamics (ESD) framework, each particle is a primitive structured entity with translational, orientational, and deformational degrees of freedom. When dynamics on this full phase space are projected onto the translational subspace alone, a memory kernel emerges from the projection without phenomenological postulate. The subdiffusion exponent is determined by the internal mode spectrum, independently measurable from B-factors, NMR order parameters, or molecular dynamics simulations, without fitting to transport data. Four falsifiable predictions follow: subdiffusion strength correlates with molecular flexibility; temperature drives crossover to normal diffusion at a characteristic energy scale set by internal mode frequencies; a non-zero rotation-translation cross-correlation spectrum encodes internal dynamics, identically zero in point-particle models; and memory timescales scale as the square of particle size. Quantitative consistency with experimental observations for proteins in crowded media is demonstrated using independently estimated structural parameters. What appears anomalous from the point-particle perspective is the expected behavior of structured matter projected onto an impoverished description. The anomaly is not in the physics. It is in the phase space.

</details>


### [119] [A Unified Critical Scaling Theory for Macroscopic Lightning and Quantum Avalanches: From Three-Dimensional Directed Percolation to Testable Predictions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16368)
*Zhe Li*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文建立了闪电与超导体磁通雪崩之间基于三维有向渗流（3D-DP）普适类的统一理论框架，证明两者属于同一临界普适类（universality class），共享一致的关键临界指数，并提出量子相位相干性与经典几何之间的映射关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 闪电与量子超导体中的磁通雪崩在尺度上相差二十个数量级，却表现出显著的分形相似性，表明这可能并非表面类比，而是深层的物理统一性。现有理论缺乏连接这两种现象的统一框架。

Method: 将两种系统映射到同一个三维反应-扩散-平流方程（reaction-diffusion-advection equation），该方程基于非平衡统计物理（non-equilibrium statistical physics）；通过理论分析确定两者均属于三维有向渗流（3D-DP）普适类；并引入各向异性与湍流耦合来适应真实雷暴环境。

Result: 证明闪电和磁通雪崩共享统一的关键临界指数，例如雪崩大小分布指数 $τ≈1.41$ 和分形维数 $D_f≈2.5$；预测了闪电通道的各向异性分形结构以及湍流对临界指数的系统性偏移；建立了超导体微观量子相位相干性与闪电通道宏观曲率及扭转分布之间的严格几何对应关系。

Conclusion: 该框架不仅为跨尺度的耗散结构提供了统一范式，还通过七个可检验的预测，开辟了利用实验室量子系统模拟自然闪电以及发展新型物理预警方法的途径。

Abstract: Lightning, the most colossal discharge in nature, and flux avalanches in quantum superconductors--phenomena separated by twenty orders of magnitude in scale--display striking fractal similarity. We demonstrate that this is no mere analogy but reveals a deep physical unity. Here, we establish a universal theoretical framework that connects them. By mapping both onto the same three-dimensional reaction-diffusion-advection equation grounded in non-equilibrium statistical physics, we show they belong to the same critical universality class. We demonstrate that both systems belong to the three-dimensional Directed Percolation (3D-DP) universality class near their critical point, sharing a unified set of universal critical exponents (e.g., avalanche size distribution exponent $τ\approx 1.41$ , fractal dimension $D_f \approx 2.5$). Furthermore, by incorporating the anisotropy and turbulence coupling intrinsic to real thunderstorm environments, we predict novel effects such as anisotropic fractality of lightning channels and the systematic shift of critical exponents by turbulence. The core theoretical breakthrough lies in proposing a geometric correspondence of quantum phase information: through a rigorous mapping, the microscopic quantum phase coherence of superconductors is translated into the curvature and torsion distributions of macroscopic lightning channels, revealing a quantum statistical fingerprint emergent in classical geometry. This framework not only provides a unified paradigm for understanding dissipative structures across scales but also, via seven testable predictions, opens avenues for simulating natural lightning with laboratory quantum systems and developing novel physical early-warning methods.

</details>


### [120] [Irreversibility from Self-Reference: Gradient Flow and an H-Theorem for a Self-Referential Statistical Operator Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16400)
*Lucio Marassi*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文是 arXiv:2605.06705 的续篇，对自指算子 Omega 进行了多方面的拓展分析：在局域核近似（LKA）之外进行一阶微扰展开并证明 Tsallis 指数 q = α + β 的结构稳定性；定义迭代动力学方案并利用 Fréchet 谱半径分析收敛性；在 LKA 框架下严格建立了离散迭代与连续梯度流的 H 定理；最后刻画了自耦合参数 κ 的非微扰作用，识别出 κ > κ* ≈ 0.50 ± 0.05 时的重入无序相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前序工作（arXiv:2605.06705）在局域核近似（local kernel approximation, LKA）下引入了自指算子 Omega（self-referential operator Omega），并导出了 Tsallis 指数 q = α + β 作为不动点条件。本文旨在解决该工作中遗留的四个问题：超越 LKA 的微扰稳定性、迭代动力学的收敛性分析、H 定理的严格证明以及自耦合参数 κ 的非微扰效应。

Method: 采用一阶微扰展开（first-order perturbative expansion）将 Omega 算子拓展至 LKA 之外，分析其在 (ξ/L)^2 主导阶下的结构稳定性；定义迭代动力学方案 Ψ_{n+1} = Ω[Ψ_n] 并通过 Fréchet 谱半径（Frechet spectral radius）分析收敛性；在 LKA 框架下，对离散迭代和连续梯度流（continuous gradient flow）分别建立 H 定理，显式计算沿流的 dF/dτ 并识别负半定耗散项（negative semi-definite dissipation term），利用前文证明的 F 的严格凸性完成严格证明，并对 N=80 的离散系统在 53 次迭代中给出 F[Ψ_n] 单调递减的数值证据；通过数值方法刻画 κ 的非微扰作用，确定重入无序相（re-entrant disordered phase）的临界值 κ* ≈ 0.50 ± 0.05。

Result: 第一，在 LKA 之外的一阶微扰展开中，q = α + β 在 (ξ/L)^2 的主导阶下具有结构稳定性。第二，Fréchet 谱半径为迭代动力学的收敛性提供了分析框架。第三，在 LKA 内，离散迭代与连续梯度流均满足 H 定理：dF/dτ 可显式计算，耗散项为负半定，且 N=80 系统的数值实验验证了 F[Ψ_n] 在 53 次迭代中单调递减。第四，发现当 κ > κ* ≈ 0.50 ± 0.05 时存在重入无序相。

Conclusion: 本文明确了哪些结果是严格证明的、哪些是基于数值建立的，以及为超越 LKA 的完整解析证明仍需解决的开放问题。该工作为自指算子框架下的 Tsallis 统计力学（Tsallis statistics）提供了更丰富的理论支撑，同时揭示了自耦合参数 κ 在相行为中的关键非微扰角色。

Abstract: This paper is a direct companion to arXiv:2605.06705, where the self-referential operator Omega was introduced and the Tsallis index q = alpha + beta was derived as a fixed-point condition within the local kernel approximation (LKA). Here we address four aspects deferred from the previous work. First, we carry out the first-order perturbative expansion of Omega beyond the LKA and demonstrate structural stability of q = alpha + beta at leading order in (xi/L)^2. Second, we define the iterative dynamical scheme Psi_(n+1) = Omega[Psi_n] and analyze convergence via Frechet spectral radius. Third, and centrally, we establish an H-theorem rigorously within the LKA for both the discrete iteration and the continuous gradient flow: we compute dF/dtau explicitly along the flow, identify the negative semi-definite dissipation term, establish the result rigorously in the LKA using strict convexity of F proved in the companion paper, and provide numerical evidence showing monotone decrease of F[Psi_n] across 53 iterations on an N = 80 discrete system. Fourth, we characterize the non-perturbative role of the self-coupling parameter kappa, identifying a re-entrant disordered phase at kappa > kappa* approximately 0.50 +/- 0.05. The paper is explicit about what is proved, what is established numerically, and what open problems remain for a complete analytical proof beyond the LKA.

</details>


### [121] [The problem of relaxation to equilibrium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16417)
*Silvina Limandri,Silvina Segui,Bruno Castellano,Ignacio Belitzky,Gustavo Castellano*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文证明，通过在容器壁相互作用中引入海森堡不确定性原理（Heisenberg's uncertainty principle）作为非严格边界条件，一个简单的经典气体系统无需额外假设即可自发演化到热力学平衡态（thermodynamic equilibrium）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热力学系统解除约束后最终会进入平衡态，但无论是经典哈密顿方程（Hamilton's equations）还是量子薛定谔方程（Schrödinger equation）描述这一弛豫过程时，均需要引入额外假设才能成功。论文旨在克服这一理论困境。

Method: 论文对一个简单的经典气体系统施加非严格边界条件（non-strict boundary conditions），即气体与容器壁的所有相互作用必须遵循海森堡不确定性原理。

Result: 在该非严格边界条件下，经典气体系统能够自发达到平衡态，无需依赖任何额外的辅助假设。

Conclusion: 通过将量子不确定性原理引入经典系统的边界条件，可能为描述热力学弛豫（relaxation to thermodynamic equilibrium）提供一条无需额外假设的理论路径。

Abstract: When a thermodynamic system is released from any constraint, after some time its evolution will render it into an equilibrium state. Although the description of this relaxation to thermodynamic equilibrium has been attempted through both classical (Hamilton's equations) or quantum (Schrödinger equation) approaches, no success has been achieved without recurring to additional hypotheses. The present work demonstrates the possibility of reaching equilibrium states in a simple classical gaseous system, by imposing non-strict boundary conditions, in the sense that all interactions with the container walls must occur according to Heisenberg's uncertainty principle.

</details>


### [122] [Thermodynamic and statistical properties of a multifractional modified dispersion relation via the grand-canonical ensemble](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16424)
*A. A. Araújo Filho*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文在巨正则系综框架下研究了由多分形修正色散关系 $\omega^{2}=k^{2}+4E_{*}^{-1/2}k^{5/2}$ 所描述气体的热力学与统计性质，推导了状态密度、巨势、配分函数及主要热力学量，分析了玻色子和费米子两体系在红外和紫外区间的非标准标度行为，并探讨了热稳定性、涨落、玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚及简并费米气体极限等物理效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多分形（multifractional）理论是量子引力候选框架之一，但现有研究对其热力学与统计物理后果的刻画尚不充分。本文旨在系统分析多分形修正色散关系如何改变气体的相空间分布和热力学标度行为，填补对该类修正在统计力学（statistical mechanics）层面系统理解的空白。

Method: 在巨正则系综（grand-canonical ensemble）框架下，从多分形修正色散关系出发，推导修正后的状态密度（density of states）、巨势（grand potential）、配分函数（partition function），并分别对玻色子（bosonic）和费米子（fermionic）体系计算主要热力学量。

Result: 红外（infrared）区间恢复标准相对论性气体行为，修正项正比于 $(T/E_{*})^{1/2}$ 的幂次；紫外（ultraviolet）区间状态密度标度为 $\varrho(\omega)\propto \omega^{7/5}$，对应有效状态密度维数 $d_{\mathrm{eff}}=12/5$；Stefan-Boltzmann 定律变形为 $u\propto E_{*}^{3/5}T^{17/5}$；物态方程参数接近 $w=5/12$ 而非标准辐射值 $w=1/3$；多分形修正提高了守恒玻色气体的临界温度，并改变了简并费米气体的费米能、压强、声速及低温热容。

Conclusion: 多分形修正色散关系在紫外和红外区间均产生可观测的热力学偏离，改变了状态密度的有效维度和标度律，并对玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（Bose-Einstein condensation）及简并费米气体（degenerate Fermi gas）的物性产生定量修正。

Abstract: We study the thermodynamic and statistical properties of a gas governed by a multifractional modified dispersion relation of the form $ω^{2}=k^{2}+4E_{*}^{-1/2}k^{5/2}$, where $E_{*}$ sets the characteristic scale of the multifractional correction. Working within the grand-canonical ensemble, we derive the modified density of states, the grand potential, the partition function, and the main thermodynamic quantities for both bosonic and fermionic sectors. The deformation changes the available phase-space distribution and produces nonstandard thermal scalings controlled by the ratio $T/E_{*}$. In the infrared regime, the usual relativistic gas behavior is recovered with leading corrections proportional to powers of $(T/E_{*})^{1/2}$. In the ultraviolet regime, the density of states scales as $\varrho(ω)\propto ω^{7/5}$, corresponding to an effective density-of-states dimension $d_{\mathrm{eff}}=12/5$. As a consequence, the Stefan-Boltzmann law is deformed from $u\propto T^{4}$ to $u\propto E_{*}^{3/5}T^{17/5}$, while the equation-of-state parameter approaches $w=5/12$ instead of the standard radiation value $w=1/3$. We also analyze thermal stability, particle number and energy fluctuations, Bose-Einstein condensation, and the degenerate Fermi gas limit. The multifractional correction increases the critical temperature of a conserved bosonic gas and modifies the Fermi energy, pressure, sound speed, and low-temperature heat capacity of degenerate fermions.

</details>


### [123] [From bulk to interface dynamics, in and out of equilibrium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16503)
*Lila Sarfati,Julien Tailleur,Frédéric van Wijland*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文从相分离场的涨落流体力学出发，研究弱变形界面分离两种稳定相的动力学，通过界面精确定义与动力学作用量形式推导线性弛豫和涨落，并推广至非平衡系统，同时揭示活性场论中常用假说的危险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有界面动力学理论多基于平衡态假设，无法直接适用于活性物质等非平衡系统，且常用假说在活性场论中缺乏控制，亟需建立一种普遍适用于平衡与非平衡系统的界面动力学推导框架。

Method: 采用精确定义的界面概念与动力学作用量（dynamical-action）形式描述路径概率，从相分离场的涨落流体力学（fluctuating hydrodynamics）出发，推导界面的线性弛豫及其附近的涨落，并系统计算非线性项（以模型A及活性模型A为例演示）。

Result: 该方法在平衡动力学中恢复并补充了现有结果，并成功推广至非平衡对应系统；发现一种在平衡中严格成立但在活性场论中不受控制的流行假说（popular ansatz）存在危险。

Conclusion: 本文建立的界面动力学推导框架兼具普遍性与系统性，为平衡与非平衡系统提供了统一分析工具，并警示活性场论领域不能盲目沿用基于平衡假设的界面动力学假说。

Abstract: We study the dynamics of weakly deformed interfaces separating two stable phases, starting from the fluctuating hydrodynamics of the phase-separating fields. Using a well-chosen definition for the interface and the dynamical-action formalism to represent path probabilities, we derive the linear relaxation of the interface and the fluctuations around it for a large class of models. Our method applies to equilibrium dynamics, where it recovers and complements existing results, but also extends to their non-equilibrium counterparts. We explain how non-linear terms can be systematically computed and illustrate their derivations in the case of (active) model A. We highlight the danger of a popular ansatz used to derive interface dynamics, which was rigorously established in equilibrium but is uncontrolled for active field theories.

### [124] [Data-driven analysis of metastability in a stochastic bistable system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16574)

Method: 采用库普曼算子（Koopman operator）的形式化框架，通过分析算子谱中次主导模式（subdominant mode）的时间演化与衰减率，替代直接追踪系统轨迹的方法，从而在弱噪声极限（weak-noise limit）下量化逃逸时间（escape time）的统计特性。进一步利用深层模式区分阱内变异性与从鞍点（saddle）向吸引子（attractor）的逃逸动力学。

Abstract: We study the metastability properties of a simple prototypical bistable system using the formalism of the Koopman operator. Instead of studying noise-induced transitions by following the trajectories of the system, we track them by studying the time evolution and the decay rate of the subdominant mode of the Koopman operator, thus in a geometry-agnostic framework. The subdominant Koopman mode also allows for an accurate reconstruction of the competing basins of attraction. Going deeper in the Koopman spectrum, we are able to recognise modes that are associated with intrawell variability as well as with the escape of trajectories from the saddle towards the attractor, both in the equilibrium and nonequilibrium case. Our methodology, being grounded in purely data-driven techniques, could be helpful for studying high-dimensional metastable systems.

### [125] [Path-Extrema Upper Bounds on Mean Entropy Production](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17074)
*Surachate Limkumnerd*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文证明，对于稳态过程中熵产生（entropy production）的路径极值（path extrema），仅知道正向运行最大值无法改进平凡的端点下界；通过引入运行下确界和上确界，推导出路径极值上包络（upper envelope），并建立了平均熵产生的精确恒等式，将波动关系（fluctuation relation）通常提供的下界角色拓展为熵产生的定量上界理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 波动关系给出了熵产生均值⟨Σ_T⟩≥0的下界，但尚不清楚路径极值是否能为熵产生均值提供非平凡的上界约束。本文旨在利用熵产生鞅（martingale）M_t=e^{-Σ_t}的运行极值信息，建立熵产生的上界理论，补充波动关系的下界角色。

Method: 利用熵产生鞅M_t=e^{-Σ_t}的运行下确界L_T=inf M_t和上确界H_T=sup M_t，推导路径极值上包络U_ext。将松弛包络问题（relaxed envelope problem）视为连续背包问题（knapsack problem），按单位鞅成本（martingale cost）的熵增益ln(H_T/L_T)/(H_T-L_T)对实现区间排序。最终建立恒等式⟨Σ_T⟩=U_ext−A−C，其中A为跨包络类的分配缺口（allocation gap），C为包络内曲率缺口（curvature gap）。

Result: 仅知道Σ_t的正向运行最大值对均值上界无改进，因为稀疏的负熵产生涨落仍可携带波动关系所需的指数权重。路径极值上包络U_ext由运行极值决定，而分配缺口A和曲率缺口C分别量化了实际动力学如何将终态结果分配至不同包络类以及在每个包络内放置终值。

Conclusion: 路径极值信息可转化为熵产生的定量上界理论，与波动关系的下界角色形成互补。该框架揭示了路径极值如何通过包络结构约束熵产生均值，并给出了严格的恒等分解。

Abstract: Fluctuation relations imply the second-law inequality $\langleΣ_T\rangle\ge0$, but path extrema can also constrain how large the mean entropy production can be. For steady-state processes with entropy-production martingale $M_t=e^{-Σ_t}$, we show that knowing only the positive running maximum of $Σ_t$ gives no improvement over the trivial endpoint bound: rare negative entropy-production excursions can still carry the exponential weight required by the fluctuation relation. Using the running extrema $L_T=\inf M_t$ and $H_T=\sup M_t$, we derive a path-extrema upper envelope $\mathcal{U}_{\rm ext}$. The relaxed envelope problem ranks realized intervals by the entropy gain per martingale cost, $\ln(H_T/L_T)/(H_T-L_T)$, giving a continuous knapsack problem. The actual mean satisfies the exact identity $\langleΣ_T\rangle=\mathcal{U}_{\rm ext}-\mathcal{A}-\mathcal{C}$, where $\mathcal{A}$ is an allocation gap across realized envelopes and $\mathcal{C}$ is a curvature gap within each envelope. Thus path extrema set the upper envelope, while the two gaps quantify how actual dynamics allocate terminal outcomes across envelope classes and place terminal values within each realized envelope. This turns path-extrema information into a quantitative upper-bound theory for entropy production, complementary to the usual lower-bound role of fluctuation relations.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将Euler-Maruyama离散化随机微分方程（stochastic differential equations）的方法推广至非维纳过程；利用Lévy过程子集生成非高斯噪声，同时适用于加性噪声（additive noise）和乘性噪声（multiplicative noise）。加性噪声的结果通过Kramers-Moyal展开推导为等价的主方程（master equation）。

Result: 非高斯噪声的生成方式简单且具有更强的物理合理性；在示例中，该方法相比几何布朗运动（geometric Brownian motion）给出了更优的物理结果。

Conclusion: 推广后的Euler-Maruyama方法能有效处理非维纳过程，Lévy过程子集生成的非高斯噪声在物理建模中具有优势，且加性噪声情形可通过Kramers-Moyal展开与主方程建立等价关系。

Abstract: Descriptions of complex physical or biological systems often include stochastic contributions, and these are commonly simulated using Wiener processes. In many cases however, non-Gaussian fluctuations may originate from non-Wiener processes which remain less explored. The Euler-Maruyama method of discretising stochastic differential equations to non-Wiener processes is generalised. Non-Gaussian noise generated from a subset of Lévy processes can be used simply and often with more physical justification, for both additive and multiplicative noise. An example of this is provided that gives superior physical results compared to using geometric Brownian motion. Finally the results of the additive noise are shown to be equivalent to a derived master equation via the Kramers-Moyal expansion.

  <summary>Details</summary>
