Result: 在d_u=6以下，临界SCC呈现非平凡分形维数d_SCC，尺寸分布满足~s^{-τ_SCC}且超标度关系τ_SCC=1+d/d_SCC成立；d≥d_u时恢复平均场行为，d_SCC/d=1/3。完全图中SCC尺寸分布呈现双标度结构，大SCC服从平均场指数τ_SCC=4，小SCC遵循不同幂律指数τ'=1。临界巨入簇和巨出簇也具有分形性，其维数与标准逾渗簇相同。

Abstract: We study the percolation of strongly connected clusters (SCCs), in which sites are mutually reachable through directed paths, in systems with randomly oriented bonds by extensive simulations on hypercubic lattices from dimension $d=2$ to $7$ and complete graphs. Below the upper critical dimension $d_u=6$, the critical SCCs exhibit nontrivial fractal dimension $d_{\rm SCC}$, and the size distribution scales as $\sim s^{-τ_{\rm SCC}}$ with the hyperscaling relation $τ_{\rm SCC}=1+d/d_{\rm SCC}$. For $d \ge d_u$, mean-field behavior is recovered with $d_{\rm SCC}/d=1/3$, consistent with complete-graph results. However, in contrast to hypercubic lattices, complete graphs exhibit a double-scaling structure in the SCC size distribution: large SCCs are governed by mean-field value $τ_{\rm SCC}=4$, while small SCCs follow a distinct power law with exponent $τ'=1$. At criticality, the giant in- and out-clusters are also fractal, sharing the same dimension as standard percolation clusters. These results show that critical SCCs remain well-defined fractal objects across dimensions, while their approach to the mean-field limit involves nontrivial changes in cluster statistics.

TL;DR: 本文求解了一个具有环面边界条件的广义三链伊辛管（TCGIT）模型，该模型在基本棱柱上包含20个独立耦合常数（包括外磁场）。通过8×8转移矩阵得到精确配分函数及热力学极限下的各种热力学量，并在多种特殊情况下化简了解析形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We obtain an exact solution for a generalized three-chain Ising tube (TCGIT) of length $L$ with toroidal boundary conditions and the most general $C_3$-invariant Hamiltonian on an elementary prism, containing 20 independent coupling constants, including an external magnetic field. Using an $8\times 8$ transfer matrix, we derive the exact partition function of the finite system and obtain the free energy, internal energy, specific heat, magnetization, magnetic susceptibility, and entropy in the thermodynamic limit $L\to\infty$. In the general case, $λ_{\max}$ is determined by a quartic equation, whereas in the principal special case with even-spin interactions (PSC) the spectrum simplifies substantially: the characteristic polynomial factorizes, and $λ_{\max}$ is given by the root of a quadratic equation. For mirror-symmetric subfamilies, we derive explicit formulas for the pair correlation functions and express the magnetization in terms of the components of the eigenvector associated with $λ_{\max}$; in the even-spin case with $h=0$, the magnetization vanishes. Important special cases include the width-three planar model with nearest-neighbor, next-nearest-neighbor, and plaquette interactions, including the entropy limit $S(T\to0^+)=(\ln 2)/3$ for $k\ge 0$ and $S(T\to0^+)=0$ for $k<0$, as well as the width-three planar triangular model with distinct nearest-neighbor couplings, three-spin interactions involving neighboring triangles, and an external field.

### [130] [Variational Boundary Fluctuations as a First-Principles Origin of Langevin Noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17621)
*Francisco Monroy*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文从变分原理出发，指出哈密顿原理中端点数据的涨落会导致壳上作用量（on-shell action）的涨落，进而通过哈密顿-雅可比传播（Hamilton--Jacobi propagation）产生有效的朗之万力（Langevin force）。该力并非自由指定，其振幅由哈密顿主函数（Hamilton's principal function）的海森矩阵（Hessian）过滤，产生乘法性与状态依赖的噪声；均匀加性朗之万力仅作为马尔可夫粗粒化极限（Markovian coarse-grained limit）恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，随机力（stochastic forces）要么被直接假定，要么通过消去环境自由度获得。该论文试图为随机力提供一个更根本的变分起源（variational origin），即来自哈密顿原理中端点数据的涨落。

Method: 利用哈密顿-雅可比理论（Hamilton--Jacobi theory）传播边界涨落印记，并分析壳上作用量的涨落结构，通过海森矩阵的过滤作用推导有效随机力。

Result: 生成的朗之万力是乘法性与状态依赖的噪声（multiplicative and state-dependent noise），其振幅由哈密顿主函数的海森矩阵决定；均匀加性朗之万力（homogeneous additive Langevin force）仅作为马尔可夫粗粒化极限恢复。

Conclusion: 随机力具有变分起源，而非自由假设；该框架将随机力的形式与变分原理的内在几何结构联系起来，并揭示加性噪声是粗粒化近似下的特例。

Abstract: Stochastic forces are usually postulated or obtained by eliminating environmental degrees of freedom. Here we identify a variational origin: fluctuating endpoint data in Hamilton's principle induce fluctuations of the on-shell action. Hamilton--Jacobi propagation transports this boundary imprint, whose gradient generates an effective Langevin force inherited from boundary-action fluctuations. The resulting force is not freely specifiable: its amplitude is filtered by the Hessian of Hamilton's principal function, yielding multiplicative and state-dependent noise. Homogeneous additive Langevin forcing is recovered only as a Markovian coarse-grained limit.

### [131] [Iterative maps emerging from cohomological structure of primes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17622)
*Marzena Ciszak*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 素数出现在统计力学（statistical mechanics）、量子力学（quantum mechanics）和动力系统（dynamical systems）等多种物理语境中，但控制其序列中不规则性的机制以及它们与物理系统的联系尚不明确。

Method: 分析不同分离距离下的素数间隙，证明其遵循一个依赖于该距离的函数，并可通过一个迭代映射（iterative map）描述；进一步分析剩余涨落，揭示其背后的上同调结构。

Result: 素数间隙的确定性函数关系成立，仅存在小幅衰减涨落；素数具有长程关联和局部跳跃，编码了潜在的上同调结构；该上同调方程的解是对数积分函数。

Conclusion: 素数可被视为一个渐近趋于确定性的系统的状态，其序列中的规则性和涨落均可由上同调结构统一解释。

Abstract: Prime numbers appeared in contexts spanning statistical mechanics, quantum mechanics and dynamical systems. However, the mechanisms governing the irregularities observed in their sequence and linking them to physical systems remained unclear. Here, it is shown that prime gaps at different separation distances follow a function depending on that distance and can be described by an iterative map which predicts the primary growth of successive primes. On the other hand, the analysis of remaining fluctuations reveals the existence of a well-defined cohomological structure, where the deterministic functional relation holds for primes up to small decaying fluctuations. In consequence, the long-range correlations as well as local jumps in primes encode the underlying cohomological structure where prime numbers are states of a given system that becomes deterministic asymptotically. Remarkably, the solution to this cohomological equation turns out to be the logarithmic integral function.

</details>


### [132] [Theory of melting lines with a variable enthalpy of fusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17631)
*Anthony N. Papathanassiou*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于修正Clausius-Clapeyron方程的两相解析模型，通过引入固体非简谐效应（anharmonicity）将熔化潜热与共存相比容关联，推导出熔化线（melting line）的近似抛物线标度律，其参数仅由基本热物理性质定义，并从全新的理论视角支持了熔化曲线的普适抛物线性质。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Clausius-Clapeyron关系推导相边界时通常采用恒潜热近似以维持升华线和沸腾线的解析函数形式，但固-液相变的热力学更为复杂。本文旨在解决这一问题，发展一个能够处理沿熔化线可变熔化焓（variable enthalpy of fusion）的两相解析模型。

Method: 通过修正Clausius-Clapeyron方程，引入可变潜热，并利用近期理论与实验进展——即晶体在熔点附近的等压热容（isobaric heat capacity）以非简谐、体积依赖成分为主导——将潜热与共存相比容（specific volumes）关联。对修正后的CC关系求导，得到控制熔化线的二阶微分方程，并施加适当的边界条件，推导出物理上可接受的近似抛物线解析解。

Result: 所得解析函数的参数完全由共存相的体积模量（bulk moduli）、热膨胀系数（thermal expansion coefficients）、比容以及固体的等压热容等基本热物理性质定义。推导出的近似抛物线标度律与基于液体声子理论（Phonon Theory of Liquids）推导的普适模型一致。

Conclusion: 该工作从固体非简谐性这一完全不同的理论基础出发，支持了熔化曲线具有普适抛物线性质（universal parabolic nature）的结论，为理解固-液相变热力学提供了新的解析框架。

Abstract: Conventional derivations of phase boundaries from the Clausius-Clapeyron (CC) relation often employ the constant latent heat approximation to maintain analytical functions of the sublimation and boiling curves. To address the complex thermodynamics of the solid-liquid transition, we develop a two-phase analytical model by modifying the CC equation to account for a variable enthalpy of fusion along the melting line (ML). Our methodology utilizes recent theoretical and experimental progress demonstrating that the isobaric heat capacity of crystalline solids near the melting point features a dominant anharmonic, volume-dependent component. Consequently, the latent heat is correlated to the specific volumes of the coexisting phases. Differentiation of this modified CC relation yields a second-order differential equation governing ML. By imposing appropriate e boundary conditions, physically acceptable approximate parabolic solutions are derived. The parameters of these analytic functions are defined exclusively by fundamental thermophysical properties, including the bulk moduli, thermal expansion coefficients, and specific volumes of the coexisting phases, as well as the isobaric heat capacity of the solid. Our derivation, rooted in solid-state anharmonicity, yields approximate parabolic scaling laws that corroborate with a recent universal model derived from the Phonon Theory of Liquids [K. Trachenko, Phys. Rev. E 109, 034122 (2024)], supporting the universal parabolic nature of melting curves from a completely distinct theoretical foundation.

### [133] [Universal interface fluctuations in absorbing-state phase transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17781)
*Yohsuke T. Fukai,Keiichi Tamai,Tetsuya Hiraiwa*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过数值研究(1+1)维界面在(2+1)维吸收相变(APT)模型中的表现，发现从短时APT主导的涨落到长时Kardar-Parisi-Zhang (KPZ)涨落之间存在普适交叉(crossover)，并证明KPZ增长参数完全由APT的基本性质决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管展示吸收相变(absorbing phase transition, APT)的模型与展示Kardar-Parisi-Zhang (KPZ)增长的模型在形式上具有相似性，但两者普适涨落之间的内在联系长期以来尚不明确。

Method: 采用数值方法研究(2+1)维APT模型（包括有向渗流(directed percolation, DP)类和紧致有向渗流(compact directed percolation, CDP)类）在活性边界条件下的(1+1)维界面；利用APT关联时间和关联长度对时间和长度进行重新标度，并分析界面高度分布累积量的塌缩行为；对比离散Domany-Kinzel模型与连续随机Fisher-Kolmogorov-Petrovsky-Piskunov (sFKPP)方程的涨落性质。

Result: 短时涨落由APT控制，长时涨落则服从KPZ行为，两者之间存在普适交叉。对时间与长度进行APT标度后，界面高度分布累积量塌缩为单一标度函数。离散与连续模型涨落性质一致，表明KPZ增长参数仅由APT的基本属性决定。在CDP类sFKPP方程中，存在一个无量纲参数同时调节临界界面分布和KPZ参数，且偏向选民模型(biased voter model)的界面性质在极限情形下得以恢复。

Conclusion: 这些结果揭示了非平衡标度不变现象中两类普适性范式之间的内在联系：APT涨落在长时间极限下涌现出KPZ涨落，从而将两种普适性范畴统一起来。

Abstract: Despite similarities between models exhibiting absorbing phase transitions (APTs) and those showing Kardar-Parisi-Zhang (KPZ) growth, the relationship between these universal fluctuations has remained elusive. We numerically study (1+1)-dimensional interfaces of (2+1)-dimensional models showing APTs of directed percolation (DP) and compact directed percolation (CDP) classes with an active boundary, finding a universal crossover from short-time APT-governed fluctuations to long-time KPZ fluctuations. Upon rescaling time and length by the APT correlation time and length, the cumulants of the interface height distributions collapse onto a single scaling function. The fluctuation properties of the discrete Domany-Kinzel model and the continuum stochastic Fisher-Kolmogorov-Petrovsky-Piskunov (sFKPP) equation coincide, indicating that the KPZ growth parameters are determined solely by fundamental properties of the APT. For the CDP sFKPP equation, a dimensionless parameter tunes both the critical interface distribution and the KPZ parameters, with the interface properties of the biased voter model recovered in a limiting case. These results uncover a universal crossover in which KPZ fluctuations emerge from APT fluctuations at long times, linking paradigmatic universality classes of nonequilibrium scale-invariant phenomena.

### [134] [Network analysis for steady-state current fluctuations under finite affinity: Application to Brownian computation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17838)
*Yasuhiro Utsumi*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过图论（graph theory）分析主方程（master equations）在有限热力学力（affinity）下的稳态电流噪声。通过引入扭曲回路矩阵（twisted circuit matrices）恢复正交性，将信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio）表达为扭曲回路电流的二次优化问题。在布朗计算模型（Brownian computation model）中，当计算路径长度趋于无穷时，复位电流的Fano因子（Fano factor）在亲和力等于对数分支因子时从无噪声行为过渡到泊松行为，对应计算时间复杂度的易-难相变（easy-hard transition），该转变点精确刻画了逻辑不可逆计算（logically irreversible computation）的热力学代价。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究尚未充分揭示有限热力学力作用下主方程稳态电流噪声的图论结构，尤其是有限亲和力（finite affinity）会破坏标准配边矩阵（incidence matrix）与循环空间（cycle space）的正交性，从而影响信噪比分析。此外，热力学不确定关系（thermodynamic uncertainty relation）无法捕捉计算时间复杂度的易-难相变，促使本文从图论视角重新建立噪声分析与计算代价之间的定量联系。

Method: 采用图论方法，将有限亲和力扭曲的配边矩阵与标准循环空间的正交缺失问题转化为扭曲回路矩阵的构建，借助扭曲回路矩阵得到类似干涉（interference-like）的效应，进而将信噪比重新表达为关于扭曲回路电流（twisted-cycle currents）的二次优化问题。将该框架应用于树状状态转移图（tree-like state-transition diagram）上的布朗计算模型，该模型具有指数级后向分支（exponential backward branching）、每步有限亲和力以及单一复位循环（single reset cycle）。

Result: 在无限长计算路径极限下，复位电流的Fano因子在亲和力达到对数前驱数（$α$）时，从无噪声（noiseless）行为转变为泊松（Poissonian）行为。该转变点对应于计算时间复杂度的易-难相变，而热力学不确定关系无法捕捉该相变。当亲和力为零时，复位代价（reset cost）随路径长度对数增长（$\ln \ell$）；达到转变点时，每步需施加量级为$\ln α$的热力学力以抵消后向分支。

Conclusion: 本文建立的图论框架为有限亲和力下主方程电流噪声分析提供了新的数学工具，明确了逻辑不可逆计算中热力学代价与计算复杂度相变之间的定量关系。该转变点精确表征了在树状状态转移图中实现可靠计算所需的最小热力学力，揭示了超越传统热力学不确定关系的新物理边界。

Abstract: A graph-theoretic analysis of the steady-state current noise in master equations under a finite thermodynamic force (affinity) is presented. The incidence matrix twisted by a finite affinity is not orthogonal to the standard cycle space, motivating the introduction of twisted circuit matrices to restore the orthogonality. The resulting twisted-cycle matrix yields an interference-like effect, enabling us to express the signal-to-noise ratio as a quadratic optimization problem in terms of twisted-cycle currents. We apply this framework to a Brownian computation model on a tree-like state-transition diagram with exponential backward branching, finite affinity at each step, and a single reset cycle. In the limit of an infinitely long intended computation path $\ell$, the Fano factor of the reset current undergoes a transition from noiseless to Poissonian behavior at an affinity equal to the logarithm of the number of immediate predecessors $α$. This corresponds to an easy-hard transition in the computational time complexity [K. Okajima, K. Hukushima, arXiv:2512.24728 ], which is not captured by the thermodynamic uncertainty relation. This transition point precisely characterizes the thermodynamic costs of logically irreversible computation: in the absence of affinity, the reset cost scales as $\ln \ell$, whereas reaching the transition point requires a thermodynamic force of order $\ln α$ per step to counteract backward branching.

### [135] [Global resetting and emergent correlations: exit statistics in an interval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17906)
*Paul C Bressloff*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了受全局随机重置（global stochastic resetting）驱动的多个非相互作用布朗粒子（Brownian particles）在有吸收边界区间内的逃逸统计问题。通过推广伊藤引理（Itô's lemma）推导出联合分裂概率（joint splitting probability）的边值问题（BVP）层次结构，并显式求解了两粒子（M=2）情形，揭示了对关联（pairwise correlations）的产生。进一步，将多粒子分裂概率的边值问题映射到含重置的随机扩散方程（stochastic diffusion equation with resetting）的矩方程，建立了研究全局驱动粒子系统逃逸问题的通用数学框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前学界对受公共涨落环境或驱动作用的非相互作用布朗粒子群体中统计关联（statistical correlations）的产生机制存在浓厚兴趣，但多数工作集中于平稳联合概率密度的解析结构。本文旨在将随机门控域（stochastically gated domains）中多粒子逃逸统计的已有研究推广至两端均具吸收边界的区间内全局重置情景，以揭示关联产生的数学根源。

Method: 采用广义伊藤引理（generalised Itô's lemma）推导所有粒子从同一端逃逸的联合分裂概率所满足的边值问题（BVP）层次结构；该BVP关于初始粒子数$M$形成嵌套序列。对$M=2$情形进行显式求解以展示两两关联的产生。最后，将$M$个布朗粒子的分裂概率BVP映射到含重置的随机扩散方程的$M$阶矩方程。

Result: 建立了多粒子分裂概率BVP的嵌套层次结构，并给出了两粒子情形的显式解，由此证明即使粒子间原本无相互作用，全局重置也会诱导出两两关联。此外，建立了多粒子逃逸问题与含重置随机扩散方程矩方程之间的等价映射关系。

Conclusion: 本文为研究全局驱动粒子系统的逃逸问题提供了一个通用数学框架，揭示了全局随机重置如何在非相互作用粒子群体中产生统计关联，并为后续探索更复杂驱动情景下的多体逃逸统计奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: There is considerable current interest in the emergence of statistical correlations within a population of otherwise non-interacting Brownian particles subject to a common fluctuating environment or drive. Examples include global stochastic resetting, switching confining potentials, fluctuating diffusivities, and stochastically gated boundaries. Most studies have focused on the analytical structure of the stationary joint probability density (assuming it exists). In this paper, we extend previous work on the exit statistics of multiple particles in stochastically gated domains to the case of global resetting in an interval with absorbing boundaries at both ends. First, we use a generalised Itô's lemma to derive a hierarchy of boundary value problems (BVPs) for the joint splitting probability that all particles exit from the same end of the interval. The BVPs form a nested sequence with respect to the initial number of particles $M$. We explicitly solve the BVP for a pair of particles ($M=2$) and use this to illustrate the emergence of pairwise correlations. Second, we show how the BVP for the splitting probability of $M$ Brownian particles can be mapped onto the $M$th order moment equation of a stochastic diffusion equation with resetting. We thus establish a general mathematical framework to study exit problems for globally-driven particle systems.

Abstract: The quantum Mpemba effect concerns with anomalous relaxation of quantum states that evolves either under unitary or non-unitary dynamics. In the context of open quantum systems, while most studies focus on quantum states evolving under completely positive trace-presing dynamics described by the Gorini-Kossakowski-Sudarshan-Lindblad (GKSL) master equation, we demonstrate that an analogous effect can arise at the level of operators. In particular, we show that operators that evolves under the adjoint Liouvillian -- despite not being a trace-preserving map -- can still exhibit a genuine Mpemba effect. We derive general conditions under which this phenomenon can occur and validate our predictions for three different open quantum setups. Our results broaden the scope of the Mpemba effect in quantum systems and provide a framework for controlling the relaxation of physically relevant observables.

### [137] [Entropy additivity from exponential decay of correlations: a coarse-grained operator approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17956)
*Bob Osano*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文从微观粒子对势条件出发，不预设热力学广延性公设（thermodynamic extensivity postulate），而是通过粗粒化算子（coarse-graining operator）和Ursell集团展开（Ursell cluster expansion），在稳定性（stability）、温和性（temperedness）和指数簇分解（exponential cluster decomposition）条件下，推导出粗粒熵（coarse-grained entropy）的加和性，并以显式算子语言恢复Ruelle-Fisher热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）。对于长程相互作用系统，非加和性通过互信息（mutual information）定量刻画，并讨论了熵密度的非线性平均问题与广义Euler关系（generalised Euler relation）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热力学广延性（thermodynamic extensivity）通常作为热力学势的一次齐次性公设引入，而非从微观第一性原理推导而来。本文旨在填补这一逻辑缺口，从经典统计力学（statistical mechanics）的微观对势（pair potential）条件出发，为广延性提供构造性推导，并量化其失效情形。

Method: 基于$N$体正则系综（canonical ensemble）Gibbs态的1-粒子和2-粒子约化密度（reduced densities），引入单粒子相空间（phase space）$\mathcal{M}=\Lambda\times\mathbb{R}^3$上的组合粗粒化算子$\mathcal{C}$，将相空间划分为动量和空间胞格$\{V_i\times\Pi_\alpha\}$，生成无量纲的介观概率（mesoscopic probabilities）。运用Ursell集团展开（Ursell cluster expansion），在稳定性、温和性和指数簇分解（关联长度$\xi$）三项条件下，推导粗粒熵的加和性及指数衰减修正项。

Result: 粗粒熵满足$S_{\mathrm{CG}}=\sum_i S_i+O\!\left(\frac{|Λ|}{\ell^d}e^{-\ell/ξ}\right)$，其中胞格直径$\ell\gg\xi$，每个胞格上的修正呈指数压制，使熵近似加和，并以显式算子语言恢复Ruelle-Fisher热力学极限。对于长程相互作用（long-range interactions）系统，温和性条件被违反，修正项不消失，非加和性通过胞格间互信息量化。此外，空间平均与非线性热力学泛函（如熵密度）不交换，导出含表面修正项的广义Euler关系（generalised Euler relation）。

Conclusion: 本文证明，在适当的微观对势条件下，热力学广延性可以从底层统计力学构造性地推导出来，而非仅作为公设；非加和性可借助互信息精确量化。这一框架还为热力学中的平均问题提供了与宇宙学平均问题（cosmological averaging problem）类似的分析视角。

Abstract: Thermodynamic extensivity is commonly introduced as a postulate -- the homogeneity of degree one in thermodynamic potentials. We provide a constructive derivation of this property from microscopic conditions on the pair potential, without assuming it. Working with the one- and two-particle reduced densities of the $N$-body canonical Gibbs state, we introduce a combined coarse-graining operator $\mathcal{C}$ on single-particle phase space $\mathcal{M}=Λ\times\mathbb{R}^3$, producing dimensionless mesoscopic probabilities over spatial--momentum cells $\{V_i\timesΠ_α\}$. Under three conditions on the pair potential -- stability, temperedness, and exponential cluster decomposition with correlation length $ξ$ -- we show, using the Ursell cluster expansion, that the coarse-grained entropy satisfies \[S_{\mathrm{CG}}=\sum_i S_i+O\!\left(\frac{|Λ|}{\ell^d}e^{-\ell/ξ}\right),\] where $\ell\ggξ$ is the cell diameter. The correction is exponentially suppressed per cell, making entropy additive and recovering the thermodynamic limit of Ruelle and Fisher in explicit operator language. For systems with long-range interactions, where temperedness fails, the correction does not vanish, and non-additivity is quantified through inter-cell mutual information. We further show that spatial averaging does not commute with nonlinear thermodynamic functionals such as the entropy density -- a thermodynamic analogue of the cosmological averaging problem -- and we derive the generalised Euler relation with explicit surface corrections.

</details>


### [138] [Energy-Weighted Site Percolation in Two Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18312)
*Sayan Sircar,Kabir Ramola*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过引入最近邻占据位点之间的键能（bond energy）$\varepsilon$，推广了二维格点逾渗（site percolation）模型，建立了从铁磁稠密团簇经经典逾渗到稀疏孤立团簇的连续谱系。结合蒙特卡洛模拟与实空间重整化群分析，揭示了键能对逾渗阈值、关联长度、团簇尺寸分布及临界指数$\nu$的系统性影响，并发现各向异性键能可导致定向团簇生长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典逾渗模型仅考虑占据位点的随机连接，未引入能量驱动的相互作用。本文通过在最近邻占据位点之间赋予能量成本$\varepsilon$，旨在研究熵驱动团簇生长与能量抑制（或增强）连通性之间的竞争机制，构建更丰富的逾渗相图。

Method: 采用蒙特卡洛模拟与实空间重整化群（real-space renormalization-group, RG）方法（含Kadanoff块递归）进行分析。同时讨论了晶格气体（lattice gas）重整化群方法及键能跨尺度重整化的情形。

Result: 键能$\varepsilon$使逾渗阈值（percolation threshold）连续移动；能量加权关联长度（energy-weighted correlation length）在经典逾渗阈值处保持有限，且随$\varepsilon$增大而收缩。团簇尺寸分布呈现能量依赖的截断。关联长度指数$\nu$从$\nu=1/2$（稠密团簇）演变为$\nu=4/3$（经典逾渗），趋近$\nu=1$（稀疏孤立团簇），与环模型（loop model）的Coulomb-gas预言一致。大$\varepsilon$下最近邻键抑制导致反铁磁子格序；各向异性键能产生定向团簇生长。

Conclusion: 引入键能丰富了逾渗模型的物理内涵，实现了从铁磁到逾渗再到孤立团簇的连续相变谱系。重整化群分析表明键能可重新标度环的赝势能（loop fugacity）。各向异性情形为控制团簇定向连通性提供了可能。

Abstract: We study a generalization of two-dimensional site percolation by assigning an energy cost $\varepsilon$ to bonds between nearest-neighbor occupied sites. This leads to a competition between entropy-driven cluster growth and energetic suppression (or enhancement) of connectivity. Varying $\varepsilon$ continuously interpolates between dense ferromagnetic-like clusters, ordinary classical percolation, and a dilute regime of minimally connected isolated clusters. Using Monte Carlo simulations and real-space renormalization-group (RG) methods, we show that bond energy shifts the percolation threshold smoothly. We define an energy-weighted correlation length that remains finite at the classical site occupation threshold ($p_c(\varepsilon=0)$) and shrinks with increasing $\varepsilon$, capturing the energetic suppression of large-scale connectivity. The cluster size distribution exhibits an energy-dependent cutoff that drives the transition from percolation-like clusters to isolated clusters. A real-space RG with Kadanoff block recursions reveals a systematic evolution of the correlation-length exponent $ν$ from $ν=1/2$ (dense clusters) to $ν=4/3$ (classical percolation), approaching $ν=1$ (minimally connected isolated clusters), in agreement with Coulomb-gas predictions for loop models where bond energy renormalizes loop fugacity. For large values of \(\varepsilon\) (isotropic case), the suppression of nearest-neighbor bonds results in the emergence of antiferromagnetic sub-lattice ordering at high densities. Additionally, anisotropic bond energies lead to directionally selective cluster growth. Finally, we also discuss a lattice gas RG approach and scenarios where bond energy is renormalized across different scales.

</details>


### [139] [Ordering, correlation functions and phase transitions in molecular systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18326)
*Yashwant Singh*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文综述了近年来发展起来的用于计算破缺对称相（broken symmetry phases）的对关联函数（pair correlation functions, PCFs）的方法，并将其纳入巨势（grand potential）与内禀自由能（intrinsic free-energy）的表达式中，从而构建了精确的经典密度泛函理论（classical density functional theory, DFT）框架。该理论被应用于多种流体的冻结相变以及高阶对称性有序相向低阶对称性相的转变，并通过与模拟结果的比较验证了其准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管非均匀流体的经典密度泛函理论（DFT）在四十多年前就已提出，但将其应用于分子系统的破缺对称相（broken symmetry phases）一直面临挑战。以往提出的近似自由能泛函无法准确描述相间的相对稳定性、相变（phase transitions）以及由对称性破缺导致的物性。

Method: 本文综述了近年来发展的计算破缺对称相对关联函数（PCFs）的方法，并将其纳入巨势和内禀自由能的表达式中，从而构建了一个精确的DFT。同时，文中还包含了对统计力学（statistical mechanics）基础知识的简要介绍以增强自洽性。

Result: 该精确DFT被应用于多种流体冻结为有序相（ordered phases）的过程，以及从高对称性有序相向低对称性有序相的转变。不同DFT版本的结果与模拟结果进行了比较，揭示了各方法的准确性。

Conclusion: 通过纳入破缺对称相对关联函数的贡献，可以构建精确的经典DFT，从而更准确地描述对称性破缺相（symmetry broken phases）的相变与相对稳定性。

Abstract: Although the classical density functional theory (DFT) of inhomogeneous fluids was formulated more than four decades ago, its application to broken symmetry phases of molecular systems remained a challenge. Approximate free energy functionals proposed in the past failed to give accurate description of relative stability of phases, phase transitions, and of properties arising due to broken symmetry. In a DFT pair correlation functions (PCFs) play a fundamental role. While in the case of homogeneous fluids, PCFs are routinely determined using experimental, theoretical or simulation methods, determination of PCFs of broken symmetry phases remained a problem. Breaking of symmetry at the transition point gives rise a new contribution to correlation functions which may differ significantly from that of the coexisting higher symmetry phase. We review methods which have been developed in the last few years to calculate PCFs of broken symmetry phases and their inclusion in the expressions of the grand potential and the intrinsic free-energy. This leads to formulation of an exact DFT. We describe application of the theory to freezing of variety of fluids into ordered phases and transition from an ordered phase of higher symmetry to a phase of lower symmetry. Comparison of results found from different versions of DFT and simulations reveal their accuracy. A brief description of basics of statistical mechanics is included to make the article self-contained.

</details>

### [140] [Reducing the Complexity of Density-Matrix Functionals in a Real-Space-Decomposed DF+RDMF Scheme with the Adaptive Cluster Approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16666)
*Konstantin Tamoev,Robert Schade,Thomas D. Kühne*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 提出了一种实空间分解的DF+RDMF方案，结合自适应簇近似（ACA）压缩局域密度矩阵泛函，仅对强关联部分进行显式修正，并以C₃O₂分子弯曲势为例验证了该方法在定性上符合光谱观测的准线性行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 约化密度矩阵泛函理论（RDMFT）虽可超越传统密度泛函近似处理电子关联，但其显式评估仍随活性单粒子态数量呈指数增长，亟需降低计算代价。

Method: 提出DF+RDMF方案：将库仑相互作用在实空间局部分解，仅对强关联部分施加RDMF修正；进一步通过自适应簇近似（ACA）对局域密度矩阵泛函进行压缩，在保持局域相互作用的同时通过幺正旋转截断浴子空间以减少显式关联的浴态数量。

Result: 以C₃O₂分子弯曲势为测试：半局域PBE泛函偏向线性构型，而DF+RDMF/ACA修正稳定了弯曲构型，与光谱实验推得的准线性行为定性一致。

Conclusion: 该方法为在扩展或空间非均匀体系中结合密度泛函与显式关联的密度矩阵修正提供了一种系统性的嵌入层级框架。

Abstract: Reduced density-matrix functional theory (RDMFT) provides a variational route to electronic correlations beyond conventional density-functional approximations, but explicit evaluations of density-matrix functionals still scale exponentially with the number of active one-particle states. We formulate and assess a real-space-decomposed density-functional plus reduced-density-matrix-functional (DF+RDMF) scheme in which the Coulomb interaction is partitioned locally in real space and the RDMF correction is evaluated only for the strongly correlated part of the interaction. The resulting local density-matrix functionals are further compressed using the adaptive cluster approximation (ACA), which performs a unitary rotation of the bath subspace before truncation and therefore preserves the local interaction while reducing the number of explicitly correlated bath states. As a molecular test case, we consider the bending potential of carbon suboxide, C$_3$O$_2$. While semilocal PBE favors a linear molecule, the DF+RDMF/ACA correction stabilizes a bent configuration in qualitative agreement with the quasilinear behavior inferred from spectroscopy. The approach provides a systematic embedding hierarchy for combining density functionals with explicitly correlated density-matrix corrections in extended or spatially inhomogeneous systems.

</details>

### [141] [Geometric Phase Transition Enables Extreme Hippocampal Memory Capacity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17199)
*Prashant C. Raju*

Main category: q-bio.NC

TL;DR: 本文发现，优越的空间记忆源于海马群体编码从无序"雾态"到刚性"晶态"的几何相变。通过比较囤食山雀与非囤食斑胸草雀，并结合计算建模，揭示了拓扑刚性（topological rigidity）是实现记忆容量的数学前提，并提出了"几何税"（geometric tax）作为维持神经流形稳定性的代价。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管相似的硬件约束（hardware constraints），不同物种的记忆系统能够存储的信息量差异巨大，但其背后的神经编码机制尚不清楚。

Method: 对比囤食山雀（food-caching chickadee）与非囤食斑胸草雀（non-caching zebra finch）的海马神经活动，测量几何稳定性（geometric stability）和时间相干性（temporal coherence）指标；使用Valiant的稳定内存分配器（Stable Memory Allocator）进行双重分离分析；在10,000种配置下进行计算建模。

Result: 囤食山雀海马呈现拓扑刚性的"晶态"几何，几何稳定性（0.245 vs 0.166）和时间相干性（0.393 vs 0.209）显著更高；晶态编码在超过1,000个位置上保持高保真读出，而雾态编码在低于10个位置时即失效，容量差异超100倍；晶态需要169倍的表征冗余作为"几何税"以抵抗生物噪声。

Conclusion: 几何稳定性是生物记忆的一个候选组织原则：进化通过塑造神经编码自身的几何结构而非增加神经元数量来实现高容量记忆。

Abstract: Memory systems can store vastly different amounts of information despite similar hardware constraints. Here, we show that superior spatial memory emerges from a discrete stiffening of hippocampal population geometry-a transition from disorganized to crystalline collective coding. Comparing food-caching chickadees to non-caching zebra finches, we found that the caching hippocampus maintains a topologically rigid, "crystalline" geometry with significantly higher geometric stability (Shesha 0.245 v 0.166) and nearly two-fold greater temporal coherence (Shesha 0.393 v 0.209), while the non-caching hippocampus resembles a disorganized "mist." This stability is actively constructed by synergistic circuit dynamics: excitatory neurons form the spatial scaffold while inhibitory populations contribute orthogonal decorrelation, a circuit motif in which excitatory and inhibitory populations occupy largely non-overlapping representational subspaces. A double dissociation with Valiant's Stable Memory Allocator, a model predicting that dedicated neuron ensembles underlie each memory, confirms this advantage reflects continuous topological organization rather than discrete neuron allocation: caching networks exhibit near-zero split-half allocation reliability despite their geometric superiority. Computational modeling across 10k configurations reveals topological rigidity as the mathematical prerequisite for scale: crystalline codes sustain high-fidelity readout beyond M=1k locations while mist codes fail below M=10, a >100-fold capacity advantage. This capacity requires a 169fold representational redundancy: a "geometric tax" stabilizing the manifold against biological noise. These results establish geometric stability as a candidate organizing principle of biological memory: evolution achieves high-capacity memory not by proliferating neurons, but by engineering the geometry of the neural code itself.

</details>

### [142] [Feasibility of Low-Energy True Muonium Photoproduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16557)
*Ivo Schulthess,Benjamin Banto Oberhauser,Paolo Crivelli*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文对在固定靶上通过近阈值光生过程产生真μ子素（true muonium）进行了可行性研究。研究表明，CERN的伽马工厂（Gamma Factory）能提供所需的光子能量和通量，通过基于截断（cut-based）的选择方法可将本底压低至预期信号水平以下，并讨论了首次观测后的物理机遇，包括寿命、超精细分裂（hyperfine splitting）和兰姆移位（Lamb shift）的测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真μ子素（true muonium）——μ子和反μ子的束缚态——在理论上已被充分理解，但至今未被实验观测到。其纯轻子性质使其成为检验束缚态量子电动力学（bound-state quantum electrodynamics）以及超越标准模型（Standard Model）物理的灵敏探针，因此首次实验观测具有重要的基础物理意义。

Method: 研究采用近阈值光生（near-threshold photoproduction）方法在固定靶上产生低能真μ子素。具体包括对信号和主要本底过程进行模拟，估算所需的光子通量，并评估可能的伽马射线源。同时采用基于截断的选择方法（cut-based selections）来抑制本底。

Result: 结果显示，CERN拟议的伽马工厂（Gamma Factory）能够提供真μ子素产生所需的光子能量和速率。基于截断的选择方法能够将本底抑制到低于预期的信号水平，表明在该设施上实现首次观测是可行的。

Conclusion: 本文证实了利用伽马工厂在生产能量和速率方面具备产生真μ子素的可行性，且本底可被有效抑制。首次观测成功后，后续可开展对真μ子素寿命、超精细分裂（hyperfine splitting）和兰姆移位（Lamb shift）的精密测量，进一步探索束缚态量子电动力学及新物理。

Abstract: True muonium, the bound state of a muon and an antimuon, is a theoretically well-understood but experimentally unobserved exotic atom. Its purely leptonic nature makes it a sensitive probe for bound-state quantum electrodynamics and possible physics beyond the Standard Model. We present a feasibility study of low-energy true muonium production via near-threshold photoproduction on a fixed target. The study includes simulations of the signal and dominant background processes, estimates of the required photon fluxes, and an overview of possible gamma sources. We show that the proposed Gamma Factory at CERN could provide the necessary photon energies and rates for the production of true muonium. Furthermore, cut-based selections are shown to suppress the background below the expected signal level. Finally, we discuss possible physics opportunities beyond the first observation, including measurements of its lifetime, hyperfine splitting, and Lamb shift.

</details>


### [143] [Search for the nonresonant production of a pair of additional Higgs bosons in the Type-X two-Higgs-doublet model in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16655)

Main category: hep-ex

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准模型（Standard Model）中缪子反常磁矩的理论计算与实验测量之间存在潜在张力，而Type-X双希格斯二重态模型（two-Higgs-doublet model, 2HDM）的alignment场景可能提供超出标准模型（BSM）的解释。本研究旨在通过搜索离壳Z玻色子产生两个额外希格斯玻色子并衰变到τ轻子对的过程，检验该模型的正确性。

Method: 基于CMS探测器在大型强子对撞机（LHC）上采集的质子-质子对撞数据，质心能量为13 TeV，积分亮度为138 fb⁻¹。搜索过程涉及一个离壳Z玻色子（off-shell Z boson）产生两个额外希格斯玻色子，这两个粒子均衰变为τ轻子对（τ lepton pair）。

Result: 未观测到超出标准模型背景的偏差。针对Type-X双希格斯二重态模型（two-Higgs-doublet model, 2HDM）的alignment场景设定了排除限（exclusion limits）。

Conclusion: 该结果排除了Type-X 2HDM alignment场景作为缪子反常磁矩（muon anomalous magnetic moment）实验值与理论值之间潜在张力的解释。表明该模型在该搜索通道中不再成立。

Abstract: A search is presented for the production of two additional Higgs bosons from an off-shell Z boson, where both additional particles decay to $τ$ lepton pairs. The search is performed with a data sample collected with the CMS detector from proton-proton collisions at the LHC at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 138 fb$^{-1}$. No deviation from the standard model background is observed. Exclusion limits are set on the Type-X two-Higgs-doublet model alignment scenario. These results rule out this model as an explanation to the potential tension between the experimental and theoretical values of the muon anomalous magnetic moment.

### [144] [Global Fit of KamLAND Data and the Daya Bay Antineutrino Energy Spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16915)
*Guihong Huang*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个弱依赖反应堆反中微子通量模型的全局分析框架，使用大亚湾实验独立测量的铀-235和钚-239裂变反中微子谱与KamLAND公开数据，分析发现采用大亚湾实测谱后，质量平方差Δm²₂₁和混合角tan²θ₁₂的最佳拟合值均下降，与JUNO最新测量结果更为一致，表明反应堆反中微子谱的差异可能是两个实验间张力的重要原因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: JUNO实验最近公布的太阳中微子振荡参数测量结果与KamLAND 2013年结果存在约0.2σ的偏差；同时，短基线反应堆中微子振荡实验（Daya Bay、RENO、Double Chooz）在5 MeV附近观测到实测反中微子谱与Huber-Müller模型预测之间存在显著偏差。为进一步探究这些偏差对反应堆中微子振荡参数测量的影响，本研究构建了一个弱依赖反应堆反中微子通量模型的分析框架。

Method: 基于大亚湾实验独立测量的²³⁵U和²³⁹Pu裂变反中微子谱，结合KamLAND公开数据，构建全局分析框架。首先使用Huber-Müller模型成功复现KamLAND 2013结果（误差在0.1σ以内），随后在联合分析中用大亚湾实测反中微子谱替代Huber-Müller模型进行拟合。

Result: 采用大亚湾实测谱后，质量平方差Δm²₂₁的最佳拟合值从(7.53⁺⁰·¹⁷₋₀.₁₆)×10⁻⁵ eV²下降至(7.50⁺⁰·¹⁹₋₀.₁₈)×10⁻⁵ eV²，混合角tan²θ₁₂的最佳拟合值也呈现下降趋势。该结果与JUNO最新测量结果更为一致。

Conclusion: 反应堆反中微子谱的预测差异可能是导致KamLAND与JUNO两个实验之间张力的重要原因。采用基于实测谱的分析框架有助于缓解这一矛盾。

Abstract: Recently, the JUNO experiment published its measurement of the solar neutrino oscillation parameters $Δm^2_{21}$ and $\sin^2θ_{12}$ based on 59 days of data, with central values differing by $0.2σ$ from those released by the KamLAND experiment in 2013. Meanwhile, short-baseline reactor neutrino oscillation experiments such as Daya Bay, RENO, and Double Chooz have observed significant deviations between the measured antineutrino spectrum and the Huber-Müller model prediction around 5~MeV. To further investigate the impact of these deviations on the measurement of reactor neutrino oscillation parameters, we construct a global analysis framework that is weakly dependent on the reactor antineutrino flux model. This framework is based on the independently measured $^{235}\mathrm{U}$ and $^{239}\mathrm{Pu}$ fission antineutrino spectra from the Daya Bay experiment, combined with the public data from KamLAND. First, using the Huber-Müller model, we successfully reproduce the KamLAND 2013 results to within $0.1σ$. Then, replacing the Huber-Müller model with the Daya Bay measured antineutrino spectra in a combined analysis, we find that the best-fit value of the mass-squared difference $Δm^2_{21}$ decreases from $7.53^{+0.17}_{-0.16}\times10^{-5}\,\mathrm{eV^2}$ to $7.50^{+0.19}_{-0.18}\times10^{-5}\,\mathrm{eV^2}$, while the best-fit value of the mixing angle $\tan^2θ_{12}$ also shows a decreasing trend. This result is in better agreement with the latest JUNO measurement, suggesting that differences in the predicted reactor antineutrino spectra may be an important cause of the tension between the two experiments.

</details>

Zhao,J. Y. Zhao,J. Z. Zhao,L. Zhao,Lei Zhao,M. G. Zhao,R. P. Zhao,S. J. Zhao,Y. B. Zhao,Y. L. Zhao,Y. P. Zhao,Y. X. Zhao,Z. G. Zhao,A. Zhemchugov,B. Zheng,B. M. Zheng,J. P. Zheng,W. J. Zheng,W. Q. Zheng,X. R. Zheng,Y. H. Zheng,B. Zhong,C. Zhong,X. Zhong,H. Zhou,J. Q. Zhou,S. Zhou,X. Zhou,X. K. Zhou,X. R. Zhou,X. Y. Zhou,Y. X. Zhou,Y. Z. Zhou,A. N. Zhu,J. Zhu,K. Zhu,K. J. Zhu,K. S. Zhu,L. X. Zhu,Lin Zhu,S. H. Zhu,T. J. Zhu,W. D. Zhu,W. J. Zhu,W. Z. Zhu,Y. C. Zhu,Z. A. Zhu,X. Y. Zhuang,M. Zhuge,J. H. Zou,J. Zu*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 基于BESIII探测器采集的约27.12亿ψ(3686)事例，首次观测到η_c→Σ^0\bar{Σ}^0强子衰变过程，发现分支比显著依赖于干涉模式（constructive/destructive interference），同时未观测到h_c→Σ^0\bar{Σ}^0信号并设置了上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 首次尝试通过ψ(3686)的辐射跃迁（radiative transition）观测粲偶素（charmonium）态η_c的强子衰变η_c→Σ^0\bar{Σ}^0，并探索干涉模式对分支比的影响。

Method: 利用BESIII探测器在BEPCII对撞机上采集的(2712.4±14.3)×10^6个ψ(3686)事例，通过ψ(3686)的辐射跃迁过程分析η_c衰变，并对ψ(3686)→π^0 h_c的强子跃迁（hadronic transition）中h_c→Σ^0\bar{Σ}^0信号进行搜索。

Result: 在相消干涉（destructive interference）和相长干涉（constructive interference）假设下，η_c(1S)→Σ^0\bar{Σ}^0的分支比分别为(2.59±0.14(stat)±0.44(syst))×10^{-3}和(1.18±0.12(stat)±0.21(syst))×10^{-3}。h_c→Σ^0\bar{Σ}^0未观测到显著信号，在90%置信水平（confidence level）上设上限为1.02×10^{-4}。

Conclusion: 首次实现了η_c→Σ^0\bar{Σ}^0衰变的观测，并揭示了分支比对η_c(1S)与非η_c(1S)过程之间干涉模式敏感的依赖关系；同时为h_c→Σ^0\bar{Σ}^0衰变提供了实验上限。

Abstract: Using $(2712.4 \pm 14.3) \times 10^6~ψ(3686)$ events collected by the BESIII detector operating at the BEPCII collider, the hadronic decay $η_{c}\toΣ^{0}\bar{Σ^{0}}$ is observed for the first time via the radiative transition from $ψ(3686)$. It is found that the branching fraction has a significant dependence on the interference pattern between $η_c(1S)$ and non-$η_c(1S)$ processes. They are determined to be $\displaystyle\mathcal{B}(η_c(1S) \to Σ^{0}\bar{Σ^{0}}) = (2.59 \pm 0.14(stat) \pm 0.44(syst)) \times 10^{-3}$ and $(1.18 \pm 0.12(stat) \pm 0.21(syst)) \times 10^{-3}$, for the destructive and constructive interference scenarios, respectively. No significant signal is observed for the decay $h_{c}\toΣ^{0}\bar{Σ^{0}}$ in the hadronic transition $ψ(3686)\toπ^0h_{c}$, and an upper limit on its branching fraction is set to be $1.02\times 10^{-4}$ at the 90\% confidence level.

</details>


### [146] [ML-based Fast Simulation of FARICH Responses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17635)
*Foma Shipilov,Alexander Barnyakov,Vladimir Bobrovnikov,Artem Ivanov,Sergey Kononov,Fedor Ratnikov*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 提出一种基于条件生成对抗网络（cGAN）的轻量卷积架构，用于快速模拟聚焦气凝胶环成像切伦科夫探测器（FARICH）响应，在保持真实性的同时显著加速传统蒙特卡罗模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高能物理（high-energy physics, HEP）中探测器响应的快速模拟至关重要，传统蒙特卡罗（Monte-Carlo）方法计算成本高昂，亟需更高效的替代方案。

Method: 采用条件生成对抗网络（conditional Generative Adversarial Network, cGAN），以粒子径迹（track）和动量（momentum）为条件，生成探测器矩阵上的光子击中（photon hits）样本；网络采用轻量卷积架构以提升计算效率。

Result: cGAN 方法在概率图和重建速度分布（velocity distributions）指标上与线性统计基线模型对比，能够生成逼真的样本，并实现相对于蒙特卡罗模拟的显著加速。

Conclusion: 基于 cGAN 的轻量卷积架构可有效替代传统蒙特卡罗方法，实现聚焦气凝胶环成像切伦科夫探测器（FARICH）响应的快速、逼真模拟。

Abstract: A fast simulation of the detector response is a vital task in high-energy physics (HEP). Traditional Monte-Carlo methods form the backbone of modern particle physics simulation software but are computationally expensive. We present a machine-learning-based approach to fast simulation of the Focusing Aerogel Ring Imaging Cherenkov (FARICH) detector response. Given a particle track and momentum, the goal is to generate realistic samples of photon hits on the detector matrix. We propose a conditional Generative Adversarial Network (cGAN) with a lightweight convolutional architecture that reproduces the projected detector response conditioned on particle parameters. We compare the cGAN against a linear statistical baseline using metrics applied to probability maps and to the reconstructed velocity distributions. The cGAN produces realistic samples and provides a significant speed-up over Monte-Carlo simulation.

</details>


### [147] [Flavour Changing Neutral Current decays at LHCb](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18084)
*Christoph Langenbruch*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文总结了LHCb实验在味改变中性流（FCNC）衰变方面的最新结果，重点介绍了利用LHC Run 1和Run 2共计8.4 fb⁻¹数据对关键衰变$B^0\to K^{*0}μ^+μ^-$的遗留测量，并讨论了与标准模型（SM）预测之间存在的长期张力及其对新物理（NP）的启示。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 味改变中性流（FCNC）衰变在标准模型（Standard Model, SM）的最低阶微扰（perturbative order）下被禁止，仅通过量子圈（quantum loops）允许发生，因此受到强烈压制。这使得该类衰变对新物理（New Physics, NP）极为敏感，是探索超越标准模型信号的重要窗口。特别地，半轻子衰变$b\to s(d)\ell^+\ell^-$和辐射衰变$b\to s(d)γ$不仅可用于寻找NP的存在，还能通过分支比、角观测（angular observables）、CP不对称性（CP-asymmetries）以及轻子味普适性（lepton flavour universality）测试等多种可观测量，探测NP的潜在算符结构（operator structure）。在$b\to sμ^+μ^-$衰变中，数据与SM预测之间已观察到长期存在的张力，激发了本文的研究动机。

Method: 本文基于LHCb实验在LHC Run 1和Run 2期间采集的总积分亮度为8.4 fb⁻¹的数据，对味改变中性流（FCNC）衰变进行实验分析。研究聚焦于关键衰变通道$B^0\to K^{*0}μ^+μ^-$的遗留测量（legacy measurement），涵盖分支比测量、角分析以及CP不对称性等可观测量。分析中特别考虑了标准模型（SM）预测中强子不确定性（hadronic uncertainties）对观测张力量著性（significance）的影响，以此评估结果对NP解释的可靠性。

Result: 在$b\to sμ^+μ^-$衰变中，数据与标准模型（SM）预测之间存在长期张力，该张力在分支比测量和角分析（angular analyses）中均一致地出现。然而，这些张力的统计显著性（significance）高度依赖于SM预测中对强子不确定性（hadronic uncertainties）的假设。本文呈现了来自LHCb实验的最新的味改变中性流（FCNC）衰变结果，包括对$B^0\to K^{*0}μ^+μ^-$衰变的遗留测量。

Conclusion: 味改变中性流（FCNC）衰变因其对量子圈过程的敏感性，是检验标准模型（SM）和探寻新物理（NP）的重要探针。$b\to sμ^+μ^-$衰变中观测到的数据与SM预言的张力为NP的存在提供了潜在迹象，但该结论的可靠性受限于对强子不确定性（hadronic uncertainties）的理解。LHCb实验利用8.4 fb⁻¹数据对$B^0\to K^{*0}μ^+μ^-$衰变的遗留测量，为这一领域提供了关键的实验约束。

Abstract: Flavour Changing Neutral Current (FCNC) decays are forbidden at lowest perturbative order in the Standard Model (SM) and only allowed via quantum loops. These transitions are therefore heavily suppressed in the SM, and New Physics (NP) can give significant contributions through virtual corrections. Of particular interest are semileptonic $b\to s(d)\ell^+\ell^-$ and radiative $b\to s(d)γ$ decays that allow to not only to search for the presence of NP, but also probe its potential operator structure through a multitude of observables. These observables include measurements of branching fractions, angular observables, CP-asymmetries and tests of lepton flavour universality. Long-standing tensions of data with SM predictions have been observed in $b\to sμ^+μ^-$ decays, consistently in measurements of branching fractions and angular analyses. However, the significance of these tensions depends on assumptions on hadronic uncertainties in the SM prediction. These proceedings summarise the most recent results on FCNC decays from the LHCb experiment, including the legacy measurement of the key decay $B^0\to K^{*0}μ^+μ^-$, using $8.4\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$ of data from the LHC Run 1 and 2.

</details>


<div id='physics.class-ph'></div>

# physics.class-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [148] [Variational Openness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17032)
*Francisco Monroy*

Main category: physics.class-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种“变分开放性（variational openness）”的保守延拓框架，用以处理力学、场论与几何分析中边界变化与体变化耦合的变分问题。通过区分可分离开放系统与受调控开放系统，该框架统一了固定边界、自然边界和经典自由边界的变分形式，并导出了受调控系统中的谱移位判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典变分原理通常设定在封闭容许类（closed admissible classes）上，边界变分要么被固定，要么通过自然边界条件（natural boundary conditions）独立消去。然而在许多物理和几何问题中，体（bulk）与边界（boundary）的变分之间存在不可忽略的耦合。本文旨在建立一种能够容纳这种体-边界耦合变分的广义变分框架。

Method: 核心方法是将“变分开放性”定义为经典封闭设置的保守延拓（conservative extension）。其关键前提是：平稳性只要求总一阶变分（total first variation）消去，而不必要求体贡献与边界贡献分别独立消去。据此划分两类系统：可分离开放系统（separable open systems）中体与边界变分仍可独立测试，平稳性给出内域方程与开放边界平衡；受调控开放系统（regulated open systems）中容许变分构成一个图子空间（graph subspace），体与边界位移由相容性算子（compatibility operator）连接，平稳性变为在容许交换空间（admissible exchange space）上的投影平衡。二阶分析中，开放作用量定义图空间上的封闭二次型；对于压力型边界耦合，开放Hessian由稳定几何形式减去经相容性算子拉回的边界-压力形式得到，进而导出Rayleigh–Ritz阈值判据。

Result: 给出了受调控系统中正定性与强制性丧失（loss of positivity and coercivity）的临界阈值。通过最小球面例子（minimal spherical example）展示了对应的受调控谱移位（regulated spectral shift）。该框架将固定边界、自然边界和经典自由边界问题作为极限情形包含在内，同时将平稳性延拓到受调控的体-边界交换类中。

Conclusion: 所提出的变分开放性框架提供了一种统一且保守的延拓方式，能够系统地处理体-边界耦合的变分问题，并在二阶层面通过开放Hessian的谱分析给出稳定性判据。该框架具有普适性，可涵盖多种经典边界类型作为特例。

Abstract: Variational principles in mechanics, field theory and geometric analysis are usually formulated on closed admissible classes, where boundary variations are either fixed or independently cancelled through natural boundary conditions. Variational openness is formulated here as a conservative extension of this setting. Its central premise is that stationarity requires cancellation of the total first variation, not necessarily separate cancellation of bulk and boundary contributions. Separate Euler--Lagrange and boundary equations arise only when admissible variations are independently localizable. Two regimes are distinguished. In separable open systems, bulk and boundary variations remain independently testable, and stationarity yields the usual interior equation together with an open boundary balance. In regulated open systems, admissible variations form a graph subspace in which bulk and boundary displacements are linked by a compatibility operator. Stationarity then becomes a projected balance on the admissible exchange space, allowing nontrivial bulk--boundary action exchange before total cancellation occurs. At second order, the open action defines a closed quadratic form on the admissible graph space. For pressure-like boundary couplings, the open Hessian is obtained by subtracting from the stabilizing geometric form a boundary-pressure form pulled back through the compatibility operator. A Rayleigh--Ritz criterion then yields a critical threshold at which positivity and coercivity are lost. A minimal spherical example illustrates the corresponding regulated spectral shift. The framework contains fixed-boundary, natural-boundary and classical free-boundary problems as limiting cases, while extending stationarity to regulated bulk--boundary exchange classes.

</details>

### [149] [Bridging the Gap on AI-Assisted Scientific Software Development Through Transparency and Traceability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17675)
*Chaitanya Bhave,Pierre-Clément A. Simon,Casey Icenhour,Lin Yang,Cody J. Permann,Daniel Schwen*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文针对科研软件中已普遍存在但缺乏规范的AI辅助开发行为，提出一套在严格软件质量保证（SQA）和核质量保证一级（NQA-1）标准下的结构化治理框架。以聚变能源中的氚迁移开源代码TMAP8为演示平台，通过AI辅助的验证与确认（V&V）案例开发来建立可追溯、可审计、可问责的治理规范，强调在客观可测正确性的场景中确立披露与审查标准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI辅助开发在科研软件中已被广泛使用，但缺乏正式工作流和发表成果中的认可与指导。这种临时且不受管控的使用方式对科研软件质量构成系统性风险，尤其在需要严格软件质量保证（Software Quality Assurance, SQA）乃至核质量保证一级（Nuclear Quality Assurance Level 1, NQA-1）标准的安全相关建模与仿真工具中。因此，科研软件社区面临的核心问题不是是否允许AI辅助开发，而是如何负责任地管控它。

Method: 本文提出面向严格软件质量保证场景下AI辅助代码开发的指导规范。以TMAP8（一个面向聚变能源的开源氚迁移代码）作为演示平台，构建一个用于AI辅助验证与确认（verification and validation, V&V）案例开发的结构化框架。V&V案例由于具有已知解、正确性可客观测量、错误可被设计识别、产物可完全审计，成为建立治理机制的理想实验场。该指导规范基于文中描述的实践经验开发，运行在NQA-1要求框架内。

Result: 提出了一个在NQA-1标准下运行的AI辅助科研软件开发治理框架，以TMAP8的V&V案例开发为具体验证平台。该框架保留人类问责制（human accountability），并建立了负责任的AI辅助科研软件开发所要求的披露（disclosure）与审查（review）标准。

Conclusion: 科研软件社区必须正视AI辅助开发的现实存在，而非回避或禁止。通过在严格质量保证标准（如NQA-1）下建立结构化的治理框架，并以V&V案例开发作为切入点，可以在保留人类问责制的前提下实现负责任的AI辅助科研软件开发。V&V案例因其可审计、可验证的特性，是建立此类治理机制的最佳实践场所。

Abstract: The widespread adoption of AI-assisted development in scientific software is not a future concern -- it is a present reality. Researchers are already using large language models to write code, generate test cases, and draft documentation, yet this practice remains largely unacknowledged and unguided in formal workflows and published work. This ad hoc, ungoverned use of AI represents a systemic risk to scientific software quality, particularly in safety-relevant modeling and simulation tools subject to strict Software Quality Assurance (SQA), or even Nuclear Quality Assurance Level 1 (NQA-1) standards, for which traceability, independent verification, and documented procedures are paramount. The question facing the scientific software community is, therefore, not whether to permit AI-assisted development, but how to govern it responsibly. This paper proposes guidance for AI-assisted code development in the context of strict software quality assurance. Using TMAP8 -- an open-source tritium migration code for fusion energy -- as a demonstration platform, we propose a structured framework for AI-assisted verification and validation (V&V) case development. V&V case development represents the ideal proving ground for establishing that governance: because validation cases have known solutions, correctness is objectively measurable, errors are identifiable by design, and the artifacts are fully auditable. The proposed guidance, developed based on practical experience described herein, operates within NQA-1 requirements, preserves human accountability, and establishes the disclosure and review standards that responsible AI-assisted scientific software development demands.

</details>

### [150] [PRISMat: Policy-Driven, Permutation-Invariant Autoregressive Material Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16612)
*Claire Schlesinger,Circe Hsu,Peter Schindler,Robin Walters*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种名为 PRISMat 的置换不变（permutation-invariant）模型，用于低成本、高通量地筛选具有目标属性的候选材料。实验表明，PRISMat 在推理时间更短的情况下，在晶体表面性质预测任务上超越了大型语言模型（LLMs），将现有最佳模型的误差降低了 4 倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 快速识别具有目标属性的候选材料已成为材料科学的关键任务。尽管大型语言模型（Large Language Models, LLMs）已被用于材料筛选，但由于其参数量大、训练与推理计算成本高，不适合高通量（high-throughput）任务。这种低效源于语言模型的过度参数化以及将材料生成框架化为序列学习问题（sequence learning problem）的困难。

Method: 本文提出了 PRISMat，一种成本效益高且具有置换不变性（permutation-invariant）的模型。该模型摒弃了传统语言模型对序列顺序的依赖，直接对材料结构进行建模，以降低计算开销并提升高通量筛选效率。

Result: PRISMat 在推理时间更少的条件下，在基于材料关键表面性质生成晶体切面（crystal slabs）方面优于大型语言模型。在目标材料发现任务中，解理能（cleavage energy）和功函数（work function）的预测平均绝对误差（mean absolute error）分别达到 0.188 eV/Å² 和 2.79 eV，将现有最佳模型的误差降低了 4 倍。

Conclusion: PRISMat 通过引入置换不变性解决了现有大语言模型在材料筛选中的计算成本高和序列表示困难的问题，为高通量材料发现提供了一种更高效的替代方案。

Abstract: Rapid identification of candidate materials with target properties has become a key task in materials science. Machine learning has emerged as an alternative to physics-based simulation, offering a faster and cheaper way to filter materials based on their stability and other target properties, reducing the number of candidates that reach the costly synthesis stage. Recently, Large Language Models (LLMs) have been applied to this role, but these models are parameter-heavy and computationally expensive both during training and at inference time, making them unsuitable for high-throughput tasks. This inefficiency stems from both the large over-parameterization of language models and the difficulty of framing material generation as a sequence learning problem. In this paper, we present PRISMat, a cost-effective, permutation-invariant model, which addresses these limitations. We show that PRISMat, despite taking less time for inference, is able to outperform LLMs in generating crystal slabs conditioned on critical materials' surface properties. In targeted material discovery, we achieve mean absolute errors of 0.188 eV/A$^2$ and 2.79 eV for cleavage energy and work function tasks, respectively, reducing the error of the next best model by 4$\times$.

</details>


### [151] [A Practical Noise2Noise Denoising Pipeline for High-Throughput Raman Spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18511)
*David Martin-Calle,Cesar Alvarez Llamas,Vincent Motto- Ros,Christophe Dujardin,Jérémie Margueritat,David Rodney*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出一种轻量级、可复现的高通量拉曼光谱去噪流程，基于一维卷积自编码器与Noise2Noise训练策略，无需外部光谱库或高信噪比参考谱，即可从短曝光重复采集子集中学习去噪，在异质矿物样品上验证了5 ms/谱的极短积分时间仍能获得高保真度光谱和化学一致性图谱，兼顾了光谱质量与采集速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高通量拉曼光谱采集常受限于噪声，传统去噪方法依赖高信噪比参考谱或外部光谱库，获取成本高且难以适应快速采集场景。现有方法在极短积分时间（如毫秒级）下难以兼顾光谱保真度与化学信息完整性。

Method: 构建一维卷积自编码器（1D convolutional autoencoder），采用Noise2Noise策略进行训练，仅需重复短曝光采集的低信噪比光谱作为训练子集，无需外部光谱库或高信噪比参考标准。模型从成对噪声观测中学习重构清洁光谱，以消除随机噪声。

Result: 在异质矿物样品上，使用5 ms/谱的积分时间（通常不足以可靠判读），去噪后的光谱在RMSE、SNR、SSIM等量化保真度指标上高度接近参考数据；基于无监督K-means分类的任务导向评估表明，去噪后的光谱仍能生成化学一致性的空间分布图谱。

Conclusion: 该方法在光谱质量与采集速度之间实现了实用权衡，支持快速、可适配的拉曼工作流，适用于常规实验室使用；同时为一维光谱学模态提供了可迁移的去噪框架。

Abstract: A lightweight and reproducible denoising pipeline for high-throughput Raman spectroscopy is presented. The approach relies on a one-dimensional convolutional autoencoder trained using a Noise2Noise strategy, requiring neither external spectral libraries nor high signal-to-noise reference spectra for training. From a reduced training subset composed of repeated short-exposure acquisitions, the model learns to reconstruct Raman spectra while efficiently suppressing stochastic noise. The method is evaluated on a heterogeneous mineral sample, using both quantitative spectral fidelity metrics (RMSE, SNR, SSIM) and task-oriented criteria based on unsupervised K-means classification. Results demonstrate that integration times as short as 5 ms per spectrum, which are typically insufficient for reliable interpretation, yield denoised spectra with high fidelity to the reference data while preserving chemically coherent maps. This work provides a practical trade-off between spectral quality and acquisition speed, enabling fast, adaptable Raman workflows compatible with routine laboratory use. It also offers a transferable framework for other one-dimensional spectroscopic modalities.

</details>

### [152] [Circular polarization of the cosmic microwave background induced by the optical Magnus effect on gravitational lensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16945)
*Yusuke Nishida*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出光学马格努斯效应（optical Magnus effect）作为引力透镜（gravitational lensing）中产生宇宙微波背景（CMB）圆极化（circular polarization）的新机制。圆极化由温度涨落通过光的螺旋度依赖的横向位移产生，尽管信号远低于当前探测能力，但建立了这一基础性物理机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CMB极化包含早期宇宙及晚期大尺度结构的信息，现有研究主要关注线极化，圆极化产生机制尚不完整。本文旨在探索引力透镜中光学马格努斯效应能否成为CMB圆极化的新来源。

Method: 将光学马格努斯效应纳入引力透镜框架，分析光的偏振态（helicity）导致轨迹横向偏移（transverse shift），使得同一观测点的右旋和左旋分量来自最后散射面（surface of last scattering）的不同位置，从而从CMB温度涨落中诱导出圆极化。

Result: 理论分析表明该机制确实能产生CMB圆极化，但产生的信号强度远低于当前探测灵敏度。

Conclusion: 光学马格努斯效应在引力透镜中的作用是产生CMB圆极化的新基础机制，为未来相关研究提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Polarization of the cosmic microwave background (CMB) brings out information not only on the early universe but also on the late-time large-scale structure via weak gravitational lensing. Here, we show that circular polarization is induced in principle from CMB temperature fluctuations when the optical Magnus effect is incorporated into gravitational lensing. This is a consequence of the transverse shift of a trajectory of light depending on its helicity that requires right-handed and left-handed components at the same observation point to be sourced from different points of the surface of last scattering. Whereas the resulting circular polarization is found far beyond the scope of current detection, our work establishes the optical Magnus effect on gravitational lensing as a new fundamental mechanism to produce circular polarization of CMB.

</details>


### [153] [Gravitational lensing time delay beyond the Shapiro/geometry split](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18182)
*Luca Teodori,Kfir Blum,Zhaoyu Bai*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究从精确的施瓦西-德西特（Schwarzschild-de Sitter）度规零测地线出发，推导了强引力透镜系统中时间延迟的理论表达式。标准公式在小角度展开下作为首项被恢复，并识别出几何延迟与夏皮罗延迟（Shapiro delay）分离之外的首个高阶修正项，该修正不引入新的宇宙学依赖，仅源于时空度规的施瓦西部分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强引力透镜（strong gravitational lensing）系统中的时间延迟是重要的可观测量，其理论表达式通常被写为几何延迟（geometrical delay）与夏皮罗延迟（Shapiro delay）之和，宇宙学通过角直径距离（angular diameter distances）和红移前置因子进入表达式。然而，该结构的严格推导及其高阶修正尚待澄清。

Method: 作者从施瓦西-德西特（Schwarzschild-de Sitter）度规的精确零测地线（null geodesics）出发进行严格推导，并通过小角度展开（small-angle expansion）恢复标准公式，进而识别出首个高阶修正项。

Result: 标准时间延迟公式在小角度展开下作为首项被恢复；识别出首个偏离几何延迟-夏皮罗延迟分离结构的高阶修正项。该修正不引入新的宇宙学依赖，仅对应于度规施瓦西部分的内禀高阶修正。

Conclusion: 在该阶数下，宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）仅通过未透镜化的角直径距离（unlensed angular diameter distances）及未透镜化的透镜红移前置因子（unlensed lens-redshift prefactor）进入时间延迟表达式，未引入额外的宇宙学参数。

Abstract: Time delays are a key observable in strong gravitational lensing systems. Their theoretical expression is usually written as a sum of a geometrical delay and a Shapiro delay, with cosmology entering through angular diameter distances and a redshift prefactor. In this work we derive this structure from the exact null geodesics of the Schwarzschild-de Sitter metric. The standard formula is recovered as the leading term in a small-angle expansion, and we identify the first correction to the usual geometrical-plus-Shapiro split. Such correction does not introduce any new cosmological dependence: it corresponds instead to a higher-order correction intrinsic to the Schwarzschild part of the metric. As a consequence, up to this order, the cosmological constant enters only through the unlensed angular diameter distances and the unlensed lens-redshift prefactor.

</details>


### [154] [Primary gravitational waves at high frequencies II: Emergence of the exponential cut-off in the power spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18286)
*Alipriyo Hoory,Jerome Martin,Arnab Paul,L. Sriramkumar*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文利用玻恩近似（Born approximation）研究原初引力波（PGWs）的功率谱（PS）在经过从暴涨到辐射和物质主导时期的光滑相变后的正则化行为。结果表明，随着相变函数越来越光滑，小尺度上的功率谱抑制愈加显著；对于无穷可微的“有效势”，功率谱呈指数级抑制，这种指数衰减可用于确定暴涨的能量标度和结束时间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在暴胀（inflation）过程中，原初引力波（PGWs）的功率谱（PS）在小尺度上存在非物理的二次增长（$k^2$），需要正则化处理以消除这一发散行为。前期工作已在线性和简单光滑过渡情形下分析了正则化后的功率谱行为，但更一般的光滑相变对功率谱的影响尚不清楚，亟需系统研究。

Method: 采用玻恩近似（Born approximation）方法，将暴涨到辐射主导和物质主导时期的相变从瞬时过渡逐步平滑为连续光滑过渡，包括线性函数平滑和无穷可微（infinitely differentiable）的“有效势”（effective potential）过渡情形，通过求解引力波运动方程来分析正则化后的原初引力波功率谱在小尺度上的行为。

Result: 随着过渡函数越发平滑，小尺度（高频率）上的正则化功率谱抑制愈加显著；当过渡由无穷可微的“有效势”描述时，正则化功率谱在小尺度上呈现指数级抑制（exponential suppression）。

Conclusion: 原初引力波功率谱在小尺度上的指数衰减特征可用于推断暴涨的能量标度（energy scale）和暴涨结束的时间（time of the end of inflation）。该发现为未来引力波观测提供了潜在的理论诊断手段。

Abstract: [Abridged] In slow roll inflation, the power spectrum (PS) of primary gravitational waves (PGWs) generated from the quantum vacuum rises as $k^2$ over wave numbers $k$ which never leave the Hubble radius. In fact, over such small scales, the PS exhibits a similar behavior at any time after inflation. In a recent work, we had argued that the PS of PGWs has to be regularized to truncate the unphysical quadratic rise at large wave numbers. Assuming instantaneous transitions from inflation to the epochs of radiation and matter domination, we had shown that the regularized PS oscillates with a constant amplitude about a vanishing mean over small scales during these epochs. We had also smoothed the transition (actually, the `effective potential' governing the equation of motion of GWs) from inflation to radiation domination using a linear function and evaluated the regularized PS of PGWs post inflation. In such a case, we had shown that, over small scales, while the regularized PS continues to oscillate about zero, its amplitude decreases as $k^{-1}$. In this work, using the Born approximation, we examine the behavior of the regularized PS of PGWs over small scales when they are evolved through smoother and smoother transitions from inflation to the epochs of radiation and matter domination. We illustrate that, at small scales or high frequencies, the suppression in the regularized PS of PGWs occurs more and more sharply as the transition is smoothed further and further. With the help of examples, we also show that, in the case of transitions described by infinitely differentiable `effective potentials', the regularized PS of PGWs exhibits an exponential suppression on small scales. We argue that the observation of the exponential drop in the PS of PGWs can help us determine the energy scale and the time of the end of inflation. We clarify related issues and discuss the wider implications.

</details>

# cond-mat.supr-con [[Back]](#toc)

### [155] [Bipolaronic High-Temperature Superconductivity from Phonon-Modulated Hopping: A Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16625)
*John Sous*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文综述了一种绕过传统声子介导超导转变温度上限的途径，核心在于Peierls模型（Su-Schrieffer-Heeger模型）中电子-声子耦合调制电子跳跃而非势能，从而形成轻双极化子（light bipolaron），并通过无符号问题的量子蒙特卡洛模拟证明其可显著突破传统Tc/Ω上限，且对库仑排斥具有鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观念认为声子介导超导的转变温度Tc受限于约十分之一声子频率Ω，根源在于Migdal-Eliashberg理论在中耦合下的失效以及密度耦合模型中双极化子（bipolaron）质量过大。本文旨在探索一种绕过该上限的物理机制。

Method: 采用无符号问题量子蒙特卡洛模拟（sign-problem-free quantum Monte Carlo simulations）研究二维和三维正方格点上的键-Peierls模型（bond-Peierls model），并结合半经典瞬子分析（semi-classical instanton analysis）解释强耦合下双极化子质量差异的物理原因。

Result: 该模型下稀薄双极化子液体形成s波超导体，Tc/Ω显著超过传统上限；该结论对屏蔽库仑排斥（screened Coulomb repulsion）具有鲁棒性；即使存在强长程库仑排斥，Tc/Ω虽降低但仍高于传统上限。

Conclusion: 通过调制电子跳跃而非势能的电子-声子耦合，可以绕过传统声子介导超导的Tc上限。该物理机制可能在铁基砷化物超导体（iron-based pnictide superconductors）等材料中实现，并可作为设计高性能超导体的指导原则。

Abstract: Phonon-mediated superconductivity is conventionally thought to be capped at a transition temperature $T_{\mathrm{c}}$ no larger than roughly one-tenth of the phonon frequency $Ω$, a bound rooted in the breakdown of Migdal-Eliashberg theory at intermediate coupling and in the heaviness of bipolarons formed in standard models with phonons that couple to the electron density. In this review I describe a route to phonon-mediated high-$T_{\mathrm{c}}$ superconductivity that bypasses this bound. The key ingredient is a class of electron-phonon couplings in which lattice distortions modulate the electron hopping and therefore its kinetic energy rather than its potential energy, known as the Peierls model (also known as Su-Schrieffer-Heeger model). In these models phonon exchange generates an interaction that binds two electrons into a small but unusually light bipolaron. Using sign-problem-free quantum Monte Carlo simulations of a bond-Peierls model on the square and cubic lattices, my collaborators and I have shown that a dilute liquid of such bipolarons forms an $s$-wave superconductor with a $T_{\mathrm{c}}/Ω$ that significantly exceeds the conventional bound, that this conclusion is robust against screened Coulomb repulsion, and that $T_{\mathrm{c}}/Ω$ -- despite being reduced -- remains above bound in presence of strong long-range Coulomb repulsion. A semi-classical instanton analysis explains why, at strong coupling, bipolarons in models with phonon-modulated hopping are lighter than their density-coupled (Holstein) counterparts. I close with a discussion of materials in which this physics may be operative, in particular the iron-based pnictide superconductors, and of design principles that follow from it.

</details>


### [156] [Incommensurate Antiferromagnetic Order in the Fe-substituted Bi-2201 Cuprate in the Heavily Overdoped Regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16988)
*Y. Komiyama,Y. Ikeda,T. Taniguchi,T. J. Williams,M. Matsuda,S. Asai,T. Masuda,H. Kuwahara,H. Kuroe,T. Kawamata,I. Watanabe,M. Fujita,T. Adachi*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 通过弹性中子散射实验，在非超导的重度过掺杂5% Fe替代Bi-2201铜氧化物中发现了不相称反铁磁峰，其不相称度（incommensurability）δ~0.21与过掺杂Fe替代Bi-2201中观测到的值相当，表明在超导拱形区域（superconducting dome）之外仍存在稳健的反铁磁关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究重度过掺杂（heavily overdoped）非超导区域铜氧化物中是否仍存在反铁磁（antiferromagnetic）有序，以理解超导拱形区域（superconducting dome）之外磁关联的稳定性。

Method: 对5% Fe替代的Bi-2201铜氧化物在非超导重度过掺杂区域进行弹性中子散射（elastic neutron scattering）实验，测量磁峰的峰位、不相称度（incommensurability）及磁关联长度（magnetic correlation length）。

Result: 观测到不相称反铁磁峰（incommensurate antiferromagnetic peaks），不相称度δ~0.21，与过掺杂Fe替代Bi-2201中的值相当；过掺杂与非超导重度过掺杂区域的磁关联长度也相近。

Conclusion: Fe在重度过掺杂区域诱导并稳定了不相称反铁磁有序，表明在超导拱形区域之外仍存在稳健的反铁磁关联（robust antiferromagnetic correlation）。

Abstract: Elastic neutron scattering experiments showed incommensurate antiferromagnetic peaks in 5% Fe-substituted Bi-2201 cuprate in the non-superconducting heavily overdoped regime. The incommensurability delta~0.21 is comparable to that observed in Fe-substituted Bi-2201 in the overdoped regime. [Hiraka et al., Phys. Rev. B 81, 144501 (2010).] The magnetic correlation length is comparable between the overdoped and non-superconducting heavily overdoped regimes. It is plausible that incommensurate antiferromagnetic order is induced and stabilized by Fe in the heavily overdoped regime, which suggests a robust antiferromagnetic correlation beyond the superconducting dome in the phase diagram.

### [157] [Bogoliubov sum rules and the Knight-shift ellipsoid in noncentrosymmetric superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17030)
*Yi Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文证明，在强锁定（strong-locking）机制下，非中心对称超导体的残余零温奈特移位（Knight shift）完全由自旋锁定方向（spin-locking direction）的费米面投影子（projector）Π_{μν}=⟨n̂_μ n̂_ν⟩_{FS}决定，导出张量恒等式χ_{μν}(0)=χ_N[δ_{μν}−Π_{μν}]，该恒等式独立于配对对称性、能隙幅值和费米面形状。基于此构建了“奈特移位椭球”（Knight-shift ellipsoid）分类方案，并给出了包括Bogoliubov求和规则、动力学对应（自旋Ferrell–Glover–Tinkham求和规则）和去耦口袋多带基线在内的完整理论框架及六项实验协议，最后应用于K₂Cr₃As₃的⁷⁵As NMR数据，识别出c轴锁定和有限q铁磁自旋涨落能隙形成的证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非中心对称超导体（noncentrosymmetric superconductor）的残余零温奈特移位作为自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling, SOC）和配对对称性的敏感探针，需要一个不依赖于具体配对机制和费米面细节的统一理论描述。该工作旨在揭示奈特移位与自旋锁定纹理（locking texture）之间最普适的张量结构关系。

Method: 从Bogoliubov–de Gennes（BdG）框架出发，推导出对所有动量成立的正交求和规则：∑|M_{ph,O}|²+∑|M_{pp,O}|²=Tr_s(O²)，该规则是幺正不变性的BdG加倍形式。由此严格证明零温下奈特移位张量完全由自旋锁定方向在费米面上的投影子Π_{μν}=⟨n̂_μ n̂_ν⟩_{FS}决定。进一步构造了s波SOC闭式插值、有限场强锁定恒等式、自旋Ferrell–Glover–Tinkham求和规则、1/T₁消失投影定理以及去耦口袋多带基线等可控扩展。

Result: 张量恒等式χ_{μν}(0)=χ_N[δ_{μν}−Π_{μν}]被严格证明，且因Tr Π=1，三个主奈特移位落在二维单形（simplex）上，即“奈特移位椭球”，其顶点、边界和内部可分类所有正则配对类。应用于K₂Cr₃As₃的⁷⁵As NMR数据，观测椭球位于扁轴顶点(0,0,1)，饱和迹界（trace bound）；去耦口袋SOC纹理基线在归一化单位下被排除约0.5，要求三个口袋共同具有c轴锁定；沿c轴的1/T₁抑制由消失投影定理识别为有限q铁磁自旋涨落能隙形成指纹。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个不依赖于配对对称性和能隙结构的普适理论框架，将奈特移位分类问题归结为自旋锁定纹理的几何分类。通过六项实验协议，该理论可直接用于解析非中心对称超导体的NMR数据，揭示了K₂Cr₃As₃中各向异性自旋响应与铁磁涨落的微观关联。

Abstract: We show that the residual $T=0$ Knight shift of a noncentrosymmetric superconductor in the strong-locking regime is completely determined by a single Fermi-surface average -- the projector $Π_{μν}=\langle\hat n_μ\hat n_ν\rangle_{\rm FS}$ of the spin-locking direction $\hat n_{\mathbf{k}}$ -- giving the tensor identity $χ_{μν}(0)=χ_{N}[δ_{μν}-Π_{μν}]$ independently of pairing symmetry, gap magnitude, and Fermi-surface shape. Because $\mathrm{Tr}\,Π=1$, the three principal Knight shifts at $T=0$ lie on a two-dimensional simplex of locking textures, the \emph{Knight-shift ellipsoid}, whose vertices, edges, and interior classify every canonical pairing class. The identity follows from a Bogoliubov sum rule, $\sum|M_{ph,O}|^{2}+\sum|M_{pp,O}|^{2}=\mathrm{Tr}_{s}(O^{2})$, valid at every momentum for every Hermitian single-particle operator $O$ as the BdG-doubled form of unitary invariance. Around the central theorem we develop controlled departures (a closed-form $s$-wave SOC interpolation, a finite-field strong-locking identity), a dynamical counterpart (a spin Ferrell--Glover--Tinkham sum rule and a rigorous vanishing-projection theorem for $1/T_{1}$), and a decoupled-pocket multiband baseline, packaged into six experimental protocols. Applied to the $^{75}$As NMR data on K$_{2}$Cr$_{3}$As$_{3}$, the observed ellipsoid sits at the oblate-axial vertex $(0,0,1)$ and saturates the trace bound; the decoupled-pocket SOC-texture baseline is excluded by $\sim 0.5$ in normalized units, requiring a common $\hat c$-axis locking on all three pockets, and the suppression of $1/T_{1}\parallel\hat c$ is identified, via the vanishing-projection theorem, as a fingerprint of finite-$\mathbf{q}$ ferromagnetic spin-fluctuation gap formation.

</details>


### [158] [Supercurrent spin Hall effect enabled nanopillar Josephson diodes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17066)
*Debashree Nayak,Dimple Rani,Prasanjit Samal,Kartik Senapati*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过在重金属（Pt）约瑟夫森势垒中利用超流自旋霍尔效应（supercurrent spin-Hall effect）实现非平衡自旋分离，在液氦温度以上获得了高达17%的场可调约瑟夫森二极管效率，优于此前基于Rashba自旋轨道耦合和外磁场的传统方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管约瑟夫森效应（Josephson effect）本身具有内在对称性，但近年来已可实现类二极管的非互易电流-电压响应。然而，传统方案依赖Rashba自旋轨道耦合（Rashba spin-orbit coupling）和外磁场以分别打破空间反演对称性和时间反演对称性，其效率通常低于10%且工作温度多在100 mK以下。因此，本文旨在探索新的机制以提高约瑟夫森二极管（Josephson diode）的效率和工作温度。

Method: 本文采用新途径，通过重金属（Pt）约瑟夫森势垒中内在的自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling, SOC）所诱导的超流自旋霍尔效应来产生非互易性。具体制备了Nb-Pt-Nb纳米柱（nanopillar）约瑟夫森结进行测量。

Result: 实验演示了场可调约瑟夫森二极管的效率高达17%，且在液氦温度（液氦温度以上）即可实现测量。这一高效率得益于Pt势垒中的超流自旋霍尔效应实现了净非平衡自旋分离（non-equilibrium spin segregation）。诱导自旋矩的方向由偏置电流决定，外磁场使相关相位在相反电流方向上以相反符号相加，从而产生跨结的非互易超流。

Conclusion: 利用超流自旋霍尔效应替代传统Rashba SOC方案，可显著提升约瑟夫森二极管的效率和工作温度，为开发高性能超导二极管器件提供了新思路。

Abstract: In the recent years it has been possible to achieve diode-like, non-reciprocal current-voltage response in Josephson junctions, despite the intrinsic symmetry of the Josephson effect itself. This is typically achieved by incorporating Rashba spin-orbit coupling into the Josephson junction as a strong inversion symmetry breaking component, and external magnetic field as a tuneable time-reversal symmetry breaking component. However, the efficiencies of the external field tuneable Josephson-diodes have remained limited to less than 10 \%, often measured below 100 mK temperature. In this work we take a new approach where non-reciprocity is induced by intrinsic SOC in a heavy metal Josephson barrier via the predicted supercurrent spin-Hall effect. By measuring a series of Nb-Pt-Nb nanopillar junctions we demonstrated field tuneable Josephson diode efficiencies as high as 17\%, measured above liquid Helium temperature. This was possible by the realization of a net non-equilibrium spin segregation in the Pt barrier, due to the supercurrent spin-Hall effect in the Pt barrier, analogous to the normal spin-Hall effect. As the direction of the induced spin moment is determined by the bias current, an external magnetic field causes the associated phases to add with opposite signs for opposite current directions, resulting in a nonreciprocal supercurrent across the junction.

### [159] [Disorder effect on the superfluid density and the origin of the pseudogap end point in the cuprate superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17227)
*Rong Cheng,Tao Li,Jianhua Yang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文针对铜氧化物超导（cuprate superconductivity）中赝隙端点（pseudogap end point）的起源问题，发展了一种针对无序 t-J 模型的变分理论（variational theory），用于计算零温超流密度（superfluid density）。研究发现，该理论计算出的超流密度对无序效应（disorder effect）高度鲁棒，且随掺杂浓度（doping concentration）单调递增，与欠掺杂区实验一致，但与过掺杂区行为严重不符，从而支持了在赝隙端点附近存在从掺杂莫特绝缘体金属（doped-Mott-insulating metal）到费米液体金属（fermi-liquid-like metal）的莫特转变（Mott transition）的假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铜氧化物超导中赝隙端点的起源尚不明确，且该临界掺杂浓度恰好对应超流密度最大值。超流密度随掺杂的非单调变化与德鲁德权重（Drude weight）的单调增加形成鲜明对比，一般认为这源于强关联（strongly correlated nature）和无序效应（disorder effect）的耦合。

Method: 首先对无序 t-J 模型（disordered $t-J$ model）的 RVB 变分基态（RVB variational ground state）进行无限制变分优化；然后构造描述该 RVB 态上顺磁电流响应（paramagnetic current response）的变分态，通过外部电磁场下变分基态能量的曲率提取零温超流密度 ρ_s(0)。

Result: 计算得到的 ρ_s(0) 对无序效应高度鲁棒，随掺杂浓度 x 单调递增，且与总光学权重（total optical weight）呈线性关系。该结果与欠掺杂铜氧化物（underdoped cuprates）的观测一致，但与过掺杂铜氧化物（overdoped cuprates）的行为强烈矛盾。

Conclusion: 欠掺杂与过掺杂区域中无序效应的显著差异，有力地支持了之前提出的关于赝隙端点附近存在莫特转变（Mott transition）的结论，即欠掺杂区为掺杂莫特绝缘体金属（doped-Mott-insulating metal），过掺杂区为类费米液体金属（fermi-liquid-like metal）。

Abstract: A major puzzle in the study of the cuprate superconductivity is the origin of the pseudogap end point. Intriguingly, such a critical doping is also where the superfluid density of the system reaches its maximum. A non-monotonic doping dependence of the superfluid density is rather unusual since the Drude weight of the cuprate system is found to increase monotonically with the doping concentration. It is generally believed that such a peculiar behavior should be attributed to both the strongly correlated nature of the cuprate system and the disorder effect. In this work, we develop a variational theory for the zero temperature superfluid density of the disordered $t-J$ model. This is achieved in two steps. First, we perform an unrestricted variational optimization of an RVB variational ground state for the disordered $t-J$ model. Second, we construct the variational state that describes the paramagnetic current response on such an RVB state. The zero temperature superfluid density $ρ_{s}(0)$ is then extracted from the curvature of the variational ground state energy of the system as a function of the external electromagnetic field. We find that $ρ_{s}(0)$ computed in this way is remarkably robust against the disorder effect. More specifically, we find that $ρ_{s}(0)$ is a monotonically increasing function of doping concentration $x$ and scales linearly with the total optical weight. This is consistent with the observation in the underdoped cuprates but is strongly at odd with the behavior in the overdoped cuprates. The strong contrast between the disorder effect in the underdoped and the overdoped regime lends strong support to our previous proposal that there exist a Mott transition between a doped-Mott-insulating metal in the underdoped regime and a fermi-liquid-like metal in the overdoped regime around the pseudogap end point.

</details>


### [160] [Enhancement of superconductivity by polarization of magnetic impurities in disordered films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17408)
*Gleb S. Seleznev,Yakov V. Fominov*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文在Kharitonov与Feigelman（KF）理论的基础上，利用Gor'kov图解技术发展了适用于含磁杂质脏超导薄膜的理论框架，将KF理论推广到任意温度以及多种超导可观测量，并考虑了任意磁场方向，成功解释了平行磁场增强垂直上临界场$H_{c2}^{\perp}$、抑制伦敦穿透深度$\lambda_L$的实验现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: KF理论预测平行磁场可通过极化磁杂质自旋增强超导临界温度$T_c$，该效应近期已被实验验证；但实验还观察到平行磁场增强垂直上临界场$H_{c2}^{\perp}$并抑制伦敦穿透深度$\lambda_L$，这些量在原始KF理论中未被涉及，因此需要发展更全面的理论框架来解释实验发现。

Method: 基于Gor'kov图解技术（Gor'kov's diagrammatic technique）为脏超导体（dirty superconductors）建立理论框架，在两个方向上扩展KF理论：一是推广到任意温度$T<T_c$及多种超导可观测量，二是推广到任意磁场方向。

Result: 理论推导出平行磁场可抑制伦敦穿透深度$\lambda_L$并增强垂直上临界场$H_{c2}^{\perp}$，与Llanos等人的实验观测结果一致。

Conclusion: 所发展的理论框架弥补了原始KF理论在描述超导可观测量上的不足，揭示了平行磁场通过极化磁杂质自旋对超导性质的多方面影响，为理解脏超导薄膜中的磁杂质效应提供了更完整的理论基础。

Abstract: Dirty superconducting films with magnetic impurities can exhibit nontrivial behavior in a magnetic field that polarizes the impurity spins. As predicted by Kharitonov and Feigelman (KF) [JETP Lett. 82, 421 (2005)], this polarization reduces the exchange scattering rate. Consequently, a parallel magnetic field can enhance the critical temperature $T_c$ when magnetic-field pair breaking is weak, as realized for strong spin-orbit scattering and small film thickness. Recently, Llanos et al. [Nat. Phys. (2026)] observed a pronounced enhancement of $T_c$ consistent with the KF theory. The same experiment also reported an enhancement of the perpendicular upper critical field $H_{c2}^{\perp}$ and a suppression of the London penetration depth $λ_L$ by a parallel magnetic field. These quantities were not considered in the original KF theory. To address this gap, we develop a theoretical framework based on Gor'kov's diagrammatic technique for dirty superconductors. We extend the KF theory in two experimentally relevant directions: (i) to arbitrary temperatures $T<T_c$ and several superconducting observables, and (ii) to arbitrary magnetic-field orientations. As a result, we demonstrate theoretically the suppression of $λ_L$ and the enhancement of $H_{c2}^{\perp}$ by a parallel magnetic field, in agreement with experiment.
