<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 ΛCDM 模型虽能解释晚期宇宙加速膨胀，但其暗能量本质仍未解决；对称遥平行 f(Q,𝒯) 引力作为修改引力理论（modified gravity theory）的一种推广，有望在不引入暗能量的前提下描述宇宙加速膨胀。

Method: 采用空间平坦的 Friedmann-Robertson-Walker (FRW) 度规，选取 f(Q,𝒯) = αQ + β𝒯 的具体函数形式，推导引力场方程；通过模型无关（model-independent）方法对哈勃参量 H(z) 进行参数化，并利用 H(z) 观测数据和 Pantheon+ 超新星样本对模型参数进行观测约束（observational constraint）。

Result: 模型参数约束结果显示宇宙存在从减速膨胀到加速膨胀的相变（transition）；通过能量密度、状态方程参数（equation of state parameter）以及热力学性质等宇宙学诊断（cosmological diagnostics）检验，表明该模型在物理上具有可行性。

Conclusion: f(Q,𝒯) 引力能够自洽地解释当前宇宙的加速膨胀，可作为 ΛCDM 模型的一致性替代方案。

Abstract: This work investigates the dynamical evolution of the universe within the framework of symmetric teleparallel $f(Q,\mathcal{T})$ gravity, where $Q$ is the non-metricity scalar and $\mathcal{T}$ is the trace of the energy-momentum tensor. We consider a spatially flat Friedmann-Robertson-Walker (FRW) metric and explore a specific functional form $f(Q,\mathcal{T}) = αQ + β\mathcal{T}$ to derive the gravitational field equations. To characterize the late-time cosmic acceleration, we utilize a model-independent approach by adopting a particular Hubble parameter $H(z)$ parametrization. The model parameters are constrained using the latest observational datasets, including the Hubble ($H(z)$) measurements and Pantheon+ samples. Our results indicate a transition from a decelerated to an accelerated expansion phase. We further examine the physical viability of the model through various cosmological diagnostics such as energy density, the equation of state parameter and thermodynamic properties. The analysis demonstrates that $f(Q,\mathcal{T})$ gravity provides a consistent alternative to the $Λ$CDM model in explaining the current accelerated expansion of the universe.

</details>


### [193] [Particle Dynamics, Shadow and Hawking Sparsity of a Kalb-Ramond Black Hole Coupled to Nonlinear Electrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16461)
*Faizuddin Ahmed,Ahmad Al-Badawi,İzzet Sakallı*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了由Kalb–Ramond（KR）场耦合非线性电动力学（NED）所驱动的静态球对称黑洞的类时和类光测地线结构、光子环、阴影、Lyapunov指数、似正规振荡频率以及霍金辐射稀疏性特征，并利用事件视界望远镜（EHT）对M87*和Sgr A*的观测数据约束了模型参数空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有黑洞解大多基于广义相对论的简单情形，而对洛伦兹破坏（Lorentz violation）效应和非线性电动力学（nonlinear electrodynamics, NED）共同作用下的黑洞时空几何及其可观测特征（如阴影、霍金辐射）缺乏系统分析。本文旨在填补这一空白，探讨KR场与磁单极荷对黑洞观测特征的影响。

Method: 基于KR场耦合NED的静态球对称黑洞度规，推导有效势、圆轨道能量和角动量的闭式表达式；分析光子球面（photon sphere）与黑洞阴影（black hole shadow）；通过Lyapunov指数计算eikonal似正规振荡频率（quasinormal mode frequencies）；将阴影半径与EHT对M87*和Sgr A*的观测数据进行对比以约束参数空间；计算霍金温度、视界面积及Gray–Visser稀疏参数（sparsity parameter）。

Result: KR场与磁单极荷的共同作用使得霍金辐射稀疏参数从Schwarzschild情形的16π³≈496提升至约1.7×10³，表明霍金级联（Hawking cascade）显著稀疏化；在大部分物理允许的参数范围内，光子环（photon ring）与EHT的1σ观测界限一致。

Conclusion: KR场和磁单极荷会显著改变黑洞的辐射特性和观测信号，使霍金辐射更为稀疏，同时光子环保持在现有观测误差范围内，从而为在EHT数据中检验洛伦兹破坏和NED效应提供了可行的参数空间。

Abstract: We study the timelike and null geodesic structure of a static, spherically symmetric black hole sourced by a Kalb--Ramond (KR) field coupled to nonlinear electrodynamics (NED). The geometry is characterized by the mass $M$, the magnetic monopole charge $q$, and the Lorentz-violating parameters $(γ,λ)$. Closed-form expressions are derived for the effective potential, as well as the specific energy and angular momentum of massive particles on circular orbits. We further analyze the photon sphere, black hole shadow, and the Lyapunov exponent associated with unstable null circular geodesics. The latter determines the eikonal quasinormal-mode frequencies through $ω_{\rm eik}=(\ell+1/2)\,Ω_c-i(n+1/2)\,|λ_L|$. The shadow radius is compared with the Event Horizon Telescope (EHT) observations of M87$^\ast$ and Sgr~A$^\ast$, allowing us to identify the viable region in the $(q,γ)$ parameter space. Finally, we compute the Hawking temperature, horizon area, and the Gray--Visser sparsity parameter. We demonstrate that the combined effects of the KR field and magnetic monopole charge increase the sparsity parameter from the Schwarzschild value $16π^3 \simeq 496$ to nearly $1.7\times10^3$. This indicates a significantly sparser Hawking cascade compared to the Schwarzschild case, while the photon ring remains consistent with the EHT $1σ$ observational bounds across most of the physically allowed parameter range.

</details>


### [194] [Bouncing singularities in Schwarzschild: a geometric origin of the QNM convergence region](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16489)
*Paolo Arnaudo,Benjamin Withers*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文解析地证明，史瓦西时空推迟格林函数的拟正规模展开收敛性由复时间平面上的一个奇点决定。该奇点具有简单几何起源，是AdS/CFT文献中描述的“反弹奇点”，由从黑洞奇点反弹的零测地线引发。该奇点解释了为何实时间下的拟正规模收敛区域被一条在看似平凡点散射的零射线所界定，且同一奇点也决定了史瓦西格林函数在视界附近微扰的早期行为的马祖巴拉模求和收敛环区。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究发现史瓦西时空拟正规模（QNM）的收敛区域存在一个尚未被理解的在实时间下的边界，且该边界与一条零测地线相关，但其深层几何起源尚不清楚。

Method: 采用解析（analytical）方法，通过分析格林函数在复时间平面上的奇点结构，将其与AdS/CFT框架下的反弹奇点（bouncing singularity）几何图像建立联系。

Result: 确定了QNM展开收敛性由复时间平面上的一个奇点决定，该奇点对应从黑洞奇点反弹的零测地线；该奇点解释了QNM收敛区域在实时间的边界，并同时控制了马祖巴拉模态和（Matsubara mode sum）的收敛环区。

Conclusion: QNM展开的收敛性可以追溯到黑洞内部几何结构（反弹奇点）的精确映射，深化了对时空解析结构与微扰收敛性之间关系的理解。

Abstract: We show analytically that the convergence of the QNM expansion of the retarded Green's function of the Schwarzschild spacetime is set by a singularity in the complex time plane. The singularity has a simple geometric origin: it is an example of a `bouncing singularity' in the language of AdS/CFT literature, caused by a null geodesic which bounces from the black hole singularity. Our work explains why the QNM convergence region at real times is bounded by null ray which scatters from the gravitational potential at a seemingly unremarkable point ($r_* = 0$ in the conventions of previous work) -- this ray is the same distance from the origin as the bouncing singularity in the relevant complex plane. The same set of singularities are responsible for an annular region of convergence for the Matsubara mode sum which describes the early time behaviour of the Schwarzschild Green's function for perturbations close to the horizon.

</details>


### [195] [Dynamical quasinormal mode excitation II: propagation and convergence in Schwarzschild](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16492)
*Marina De Amicis,Enrico Cannizzaro,Gregorio Carullo,Adrien Kuntz,Laura Sberna*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于前期工作（Paper I），研究了粒子坠入史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）过程中准正则模（QNMs）的动态激发，给出了更精确的传播方案，确认了“反弹半径”（bounce radius）$r_*=0$的存在，并揭示了QNM信号从准共振态到自由振荡态的转变机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在粒子坠入黑洞的动力学过程中，准正则模（QNMs）的激发机制尚未完全清晰。本文旨在改进Leaver QNM解的高频行为描述，完善从第一性原理出发的环形波建模（ringdown modelling）。

Method: 基于Paper I的理论框架，通过研究Leaver QNM解的高频行为，推导出更精确、更通用的传播方案。将该方案应用于螺旋入（inspiralling）粒子，并对比波形振荡成分以验证方案的有效性。

Result: 确认了新的“反弹半径”（bounce radius）$r_*=0$的存在；QNM信号在反弹半径右侧经历散射，左侧沿光锥直接传播。信号在粒子穿越反弹半径时经历从准共振态（quasi-resonant regime）到自由振荡态（free-oscillator regime）的转变，前者高阶泛音（overtones）反相并相互干扰抵消，后者同相且QNM求和快速收敛。

Conclusion: 研究给出了粒子坠入黑洞过程中QNM集体行为的清晰物理解释，为精确的环形波建模（ringdown modelling）提供了坚实的理论基础。

Abstract: We study the dynamical excitation of quasinormal modes (QNMs) during the plunge of a particle into a Schwarzschild black hole, building on the framework of Phys. Rev. D 113 (2026) 2, 024048 (Paper I). Investigating the high-frequency behavior of Leaver's QNM solutions, we obtain a more accurate and general prescription for their propagation. We confirm the existence of a new "characteristic radius" for QNM excitation, the bounce radius $r_*=0$, in agreement with recent literature. To its right, the QNM signal scatters off this point before reaching the observer; to its left, it propagates directly on the light-cone. Applying the formalism of Paper I to inspiralling particles, and using this refined prescription, we obtain a QNM signal that accurately reproduces the oscillatory component of the waveform after the bounce crossing, yielding an essentially complete first-principles description of the waveform from shortly after the signal peak. The dynamical QNM signal undergoes a transition as the particle crosses the bounce radius: from a quasi-resonant regime, where successive overtones are driven in counter-phase and interfere destructively, to a free-oscillator one, where they are in phase and the QNM sum converges rapidly. These results provide a clear physical interpretation of the collective QNM behavior during the plunge, and a firm theoretical foundation for accurate ringdown modelling.

</details>


### [196] [Rapidly Rotating Neutron Star Collapse in Massive Scalar-Tensor Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16506)
*José Carlos Olvera M.,Daniela D. Doneva,Pablo Cerdá-Durán,José A. Font,Stoytcho S. Yazadjiev*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文开发了一个3D数值演化代码，用于研究大规模标量-张量理论（massive-scalar-tensor theories）中的中子星。该代码嵌入爱因斯坦工具箱（Einstein Toolkit）框架，基于BSN形式加上非最小耦合标量场实现。研究发现，快速旋转的标量化中子星在引力坍缩为黑洞的过程中，其张量引力波（gravitational-wave）发射与广义相对论情形存在观测简并（observational degeneracy），但通过标量辐射（scalar radiation）可打破简并，其能量约为10^-3 M_sun c^2，比四极辐射高数个数量级，可作为修正引力（modified gravity）的观测探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大规模标量-张量理论中，现有研究缺乏对快速旋转标量化中子星（scalarized neutron star）引力坍缩过程的完整3D数值模拟，特别是标量场对动力学过程及引力波信号特征的影响尚不明确。

Method: 在爱因斯坦工具箱框架内开发了3D数值演化代码，采用Baumgarte-Shapiro-Shibata-Nakamura（BSSN）形式（formalism）的修改版本，引入一个非最小耦合（nonminimally coupled）标量场，同时保留标准流体动力学（hydrodynamic）演化方案，以便未来加入更微观物理效应。

Result: 快速旋转的标量化中子星坍缩时，其张量引力波发射与广义相对论中的对应情形存在观测简并；但标量辐射能量约为10^-3 M_sun c^2，远高于四极辐射的约10^-7 M_sun c^2；快速旋转可增强该信号，因为高速旋转星体能维持更大的标量场振幅。

Conclusion: 标量辐射可作为区分标量-张量理论与广义相对论的有效观测探针，尤其通过其远高于张量模式的能量特征来打破简并；快速旋转进一步放大了这一可观测信号。

Abstract: We present a full 3D numerical evolution code to study neutron stars in massive-scalar-tensor theories. The code is embedded in the Einstein Toolkit framework and its implementation constitutes a modified version of the Baumgarte-Shapiro-Shibata-Nakamura formalism with an additional nonminimally coupled scalar field. The approach we follow preserves the standard hydrodynamic evolution for matter fields, allowing eventually for a straightforward inclusion of more microphysical effects and better flexibility. Using this code, we examine the gravitational collapse of rapidly rotating, scalarized neutron stars to a black hole by exploring the influence of the scalar field on the dynamical features of the process and on the gravitational-wave emission. We find that for the configurations studied in this work, there is an observational degeneracy in the tensorial gravitational-wave emission between collapsing scalarized stars and their counterparts in general relativity. However, this degeneracy can be broken through the emission of scalar radiation, which carries an energy of ~10^-3 M_sun c^2. This is orders of magnitude higher than the quadrupolar emission (~10^-7 M_sun c^2) and might be used as an observational probe of modified gravity. We also find that rapid rotation can enhance this signal, since fast rotating stars can sustain larger scalar field amplitudes.

</details>


### [197] [Bidirectional Internal Squeezing for Gravitational-Wave Detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16512)
*Sander M. Vermeulen,Umran Serra Koca,Lee McCuller*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一种用于引力波探测器的双向内挤压（bidirectional internal squeezing）方案，该方案在信号提取腔内设置两个反向传播的光学参量放大（optical parametric amplification）阶段，使腔内真空场被压缩、信号与内部真空场被放大，从而饱和内耗散导致的最低量子噪声下界。研究表明该方案在高频段可解除对腔镜透射率的约束，并通过数值仿真验证了其全量子噪声谱，同时评估了实际实现中的损耗与模失配问题，发现“模式愈合”（mode healing）可抑制失配损耗。该方案有望用于LIGO等引力波观测站升级及其它干涉测量实验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前引力波探测器的灵敏度受到内光学耗散（internal optical dissipation）引入的量子噪声限制，需要寻找一种能够在存在耗散的情况下饱和最低已知量子噪声下界的方案，以突破现有性能瓶颈。

Method: 在信号提取腔（signal-extraction cavity）内引入两个光学参量放大（optical parametric amplification）阶段，分别作用于反向传播的腔内场。通过推导信号参考的量子噪声谱密度（signal-referred quantum noise spectral density）解析表达式，并与其它内挤压和放大方案进行比较，同时采用数值仿真验证全量子噪声谱。

Result: 该方案饱和了内耗散导致的最低已知量子噪声下界；在高频段，信号参考的量子噪声谱密度与臂腔输入透射率和信号提取透射率无关，从而为缓解技术约束和辐射压噪声提供了设计自由度；数值仿真验证了全量子噪声谱；“模式愈合”效应可有效抑制由该方案引入的横向模失配（transverse mode mismatch）损耗。

Conclusion: 双向内挤压方案可作为LIGO等现有引力波观测站的一个潜在升级路径，并有望应用于未来观测站及其它干涉测量实验。

Abstract: We present a bidirectional internal squeezing scheme for gravitational-wave detectors and show that it saturates the lowest known lower bounds on quantum noise from internal optical dissipation. The scheme uses two optical parametric amplification stages inside the signal-extraction cavity that act on intra-cavity fields propagating in opposite directions. Thereby, most vacuum fields entering the interferometer are squeezed, while the signal and internal vacuum fields are amplified so that loss in the readout path adds no further noise. We show that the resulting signal-referred quantum noise spectral density is independent of the arm-cavity input and signal-extraction transmissivities at high frequencies, opening design freedom to mitigate technical constraints and radiation-pressure noise. We derive these results analytically, compare them with other internal squeezing and amplification schemes, and validate the full quantum-noise spectrum through numerical simulations. We also assess realistic implementations, including dissipation mechanisms and transverse mode mismatch introduced by the scheme, and find that 'mode healing' in the signal-extraction cavity can suppress mismatch losses. These results identify bidirectional internal squeezing as a possible upgrade path for gravitational-wave observatories such as LIGO, and the scheme may also benefit future observatories and other interferometry experiments.

</details>


### [198] [Quantum-statistical constraints on Kerr-anti-de Sitter thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16536)
*T. L. Campos,M. C. Baldiotti,C. Molina*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文建立了一个通用框架，用于解释Kerr-反德西特黑洞（Kerr-anti de Sitter black holes, KadS）的热力学描述。研究表明，温度和角速度是与参考系相关的运动学量，而压力-体积贡献则需要规范固定势质量和体积。通过量子统计关系（quantum statistical relation），论文将无穷多种KadS描述限制到特定子类，并确立了与无穷远共转参考系相关的描述以及热力学体积与几何体积一致的描述的唯一性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kerr-反德西特黑洞（KadS）存在多种热力学描述，这些描述服从热力学第一定律和标度性质（scaling properties），但彼此之间的物理解释缺乏统一框架，需要从几何与量子统计角度进行协调。

Method: 论文采用欧几里得形式（Euclidean formalism）识别温度和角速度作为与参考系相关的运动学量；通过规范固定（gauge fixing）处理压力-体积贡献这一动力学项；利用量子统计关系（quantum statistical relation）对无穷多种KadS描述施加限制，并在特定极限下与已知解（Schwarzschild-反德西特和Kerr热力学）进行比对。

Result: 建立了与给定热力学描述对应的观测者直接由生成视界的Killing矢量（Killing vector）编码。量子统计关系将KadS描述的无穷家族限制为在宇宙常数和角动量趋于零时退化为Schwarzschild-反德西特和Kerr热力学的子类。同时确立了与无穷远共转参考系相关的描述以及热力学体积与几何体积一致的描述的唯一性。

Conclusion: 该框架为KadS热力学描述的多样性提供了一致的解释，调和了几何观点与量子统计观点，并明确了不同描述对应的观测者框架。

Abstract: We develop a general framework for interpreting the thermodynamic descriptions of Kerr-anti de Sitter black holes (KadS). These descriptions satisfy a first law and respect the homogeneity required by scaling properties. Additionally, they are subject to restrictions from semiclassical arguments. We show that temperature and angular velocity are kinematic quantities tied to a reference frame, identified through the Euclidean formalism. However, the pressure-volume contribution is a dynamical term that requires a gauge fixing of the potential mass and volume. It is established that the observer associated with a given thermodynamic description is directly encoded in the Killing vector that generates the horizon. We demonstrate that the quantum statistical relation restricts the infinite family of KadS descriptions to a subclass that reduces to Schwarzschild-adS and Kerr thermodynamics in the limits of vanishing cosmological constant and angular momentum. Furthermore, we establish the uniqueness of both the description associated with a frame co-rotating with infinity, and the description whose thermodynamic and geometric volumes coincide. Thus, our framework provides a coherent interpretation of the variety of KadS thermodynamics, reconciling geometric and quantum-statistical considerations.

### [199] [Quantum corrections to cosmic perturbations for a bouncing background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16592)
*Héctor Hernández Hernández,Hugo Morales Técotl,Gustavo Sánchez Herrera*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文在圈量子宇宙学（LQC）框架下，计算了单标量扰动模式与反弹宇宙耦合模型的二阶量子修正（量子色散与关联）。通过有效量子化方法引入量子矩（quantum moments）作为新动力学自由度，推导出引力与标量扇区的期望值与二阶量子矩的耦合运动方程；发现反弹效应导致的领头阶修正被普朗克长度六次幂压制，产生比例依赖的功率谱增强，并通过数值演化揭示了反弹诱导谱的条件性紫外正则化机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在圈量子宇宙学中，量子反弹对大尺度结构扰动谱的影响尚未被充分纳入有效量子修正框架。该研究旨在通过计算二阶量子修正，更精确地描述反弹宇宙中扰动模式的量子行为及其可观测后果。

Method: 采用有效量子化方法，将量子矩作为相空间新自由度扩展经典动力学；在 μ₀ 方案（μ₀ scheme）中通过完整修正（holonomy corrections）纳入宇宙反弹；在测试场近似（test-field approximation）和零标势下，将量子矩方程简化为关于 Mukhanov-Sasaki 变量均方差 G^vv 的三阶常微分方程；将反弹效应作为微扰处理，构造无量纲曲率功率谱的修正。

Result: 领头阶修正被普朗克长度六次幂压制，产生尺度依赖的功率谱增强 δP_R ∝ (k ℓ_Pl)^6，对谱指数修正 δn_s ~ 6(k ℓ_Pl)^6 ≪ 1，与当前观测约束完全一致。数值演化表明引力量子矩产生阻尼机制，压制反弹后标量扰动幅度；跨扇区量子关联在高波数区放大扰动并引入数值不稳定性，揭示二阶截断在紫外区的局限性。

Conclusion: 二阶量子修正对可观测宇宙模式的谱指数影响极小（≪1），符合观测限制。引力量子矩可提供反弹后扰动幅度的有效压制，但跨扇区关联在高波数区破坏二阶近似，提示需更完整的量子动力学框架来处理紫外行为。

Abstract: We compute second-order quantum corrections, as quantum dispersions and correlations, to a cosmological model coupling a single scalar perturbation mode to a bouncing background within Loop Quantum Cosmology (LQC). Using an effective quantization approach in which quantum moments extend the classical phase space as new dynamical degrees of freedom, and incorporating the cosmic bounce through holonomy corrections in the $μ_0$ scheme, we derive a coupled set of effective equations of motion for the expectation values and second-order quantum moments of both the gravitational and scalar sectors evolving with respect to a clock scalar field. Within the test-field approximation and for a vanishing scalar potential, the quantum moment equations reduce to a third-order ordinary differential equation for the mean squared deviation $G^{vv}$ of the Mukhanov-Sasaki variable in a de Sitter background with LQC bounce. Treating the effect of bounce as a perturbation of the solution, we construct the corresponding correction to the dimensionless curvature power spectrum. The leading correction is suppressed by the sixth power of the Planck length, producing a scale-dependent enhancement $δP_{R} \propto (k \ell_{\rm Pl})^6$ that modifies the spectral index by $δn_s \sim 6(k \ell_{\rm Pl})^6 \ll 1$ for all cosmologically observable modes, in full consistency with current observational constraints. Numerical evolution of the full coupled system reveals a conditional ultraviolet regularization of the bounce-induced spectrum: the gravitational quantum moments generate a damping mechanism that suppresses the scalar perturbation amplitude after the bounce. Including cross-sector quantum correlations amplifies perturbation modes and introduces numerical instabilities at high wavenumbers, signaling the limits of the second-order truncation in the ultraviolet.

Abstract: In a very recent paper, we computed the quasibound states of massless acoustic excitations interacting with a new (effective) acoustic geometry with circulation. ### [201] [Classical Dressing of Timelike Naked Singularities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16629)
*Pablo León,G. Alencar,Manuel Gonzalez-Espinoza,Francisco Tello-Ortiz*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究在经典广义相对论（general relativity）中，静态各向异性物质分布是否能在因果上包裹（causally dress）负质量施瓦西型类时裸奇点（timelike naked singularity），给出了视界形成的充分条件，并通过多种密度轮廓示例加以验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典广义相对论中，负质量施瓦西度规包含一个类时裸奇点，其因果结构是否可能被物质分布所修改（即形成事件视界从而屏蔽奇点）是一个尚未明确的基础问题。本文旨在从解析角度给出这一问题的充分条件。

Method: 在球对称（spherically symmetric）框架下求解爱因斯坦场方程（Einstein's equations），引入辅助函数 \(Φ(r)=2m(r)-r\) 分析视界结构，通过总附加质量、物质轮廓局域化程度以及有效紧致度函数（effective compactness function）\(8πr^2ρ(r)\) 的单调性等条件推导视界存在的充分条件。

Result: 非负且充分局域化的密度轮廓（density profile）可以在累积物质贡献超过负裸质量时包裹类时奇点；而非单调的密度轮廓通常会导致多视界（multi-horizon）几何结构。文中通过不连续和光滑幂律轮廓、对数分支以及T-对偶（T-duality）启发极限构型对形式体系进行了验证。

Conclusion: 该研究为类时裸奇点周围视界形成提供了充分条件框架，阐明了物质的径向组织方式如何控制静态广义相对论中的因果可达性（causal accessibility）。

Abstract: We investigate whether a timelike naked singularity of negative-mass Schwarzschild type can be causally dressed by a static anisotropic matter distribution in classical general relativity. Working within a spherically symmetric framework, we solve Einstein's equations for a general density profile \(ρ(r)\) and show that the horizon structure is governed by the auxiliary function \(Φ(r)=2m(r)-r\), whose zeros determine the existence and multiplicity of horizons. We derive sufficient conditions for the formation of a unique outer event horizon in terms of the total added mass, the localization of the matter profile, and the monotonic behavior of the effective compactness function \(8πr^2ρ(r)\). In particular, non-negative and sufficiently localized density profiles can cloak the timelike singularity when the cumulative matter contribution overcomes the negative bare mass, whereas non-monotonic profiles generically lead to multi-horizon geometries. We illustrate the formalism with discontinuous and smooth power-law profiles, logarithmic branches, and T-duality-inspired limiting configurations. These results provide a sufficient-condition framework for horizon formation around timelike naked singularities and clarify how the radial organization of matter controls causal accessibility in static general relativity.

*Gilberto Aguilar-Pérez,Miguel Cruz,Samuel Lepe*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出一种满足热力学第二定律的单模引力（unimodular gravity, UG）扩散模型，利用Pantheon+超新星数据和重子声学振荡（BAO）测量进行联合统计分析，发现该模型偏好闭合空间几何（Ωk0 ≈ -0.109），并能在保持合理宇宙年龄（约13.61 Gyr）的同时显著缓解哈勃常数（Hubble constant）张力，得到H0 ≈ 73.35 km/s/Mpc。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出幂律形式（power-law form）的扩散函数Q(z)=Q0(1+z)^β，并通过要求正熵产生（βQ0 > 0）严格满足热力学第二定律。采用Pantheon+ Ia型超新星（Type Ia Supernova）样本与重子声学振荡（BAO）数据开展联合统计分析（joint statistical analysis），对模型参数空间进行紧密约束。

Conclusion: 单模引力扩散模型是一种热力学一致的现象学替代方案，能够在保持宇宙年龄和声视界尺度的同时有效缓解哈勃常数张力，且数据偏好闭合空间几何。该模型具有类精质有效暗能量行为，为哈勃张力的来源提供了一种新的理论视角。

Abstract: We investigate the cosmological implications of unimodular gravity (UG) featuring energy diffusion and spatial curvature. While standard diffusion models often suffer from thermodynamic inconsistencies, we propose a phenomenologically viable power-law Ansatz for the diffusion function, $Q(z) = Q_0(1+z)^β$, which strictly satisfies the second law of thermodynamics by demanding positive entropy production ($βQ_0 > 0$). Using a joint statistical analysis with the Pantheon+ Type Ia Supernova compilation and Baryon Acoustic Oscillation (BAO) measurements, we tightly constrain the parameter space. We find a diffusion exponent of $β= 0.503_{-0.126}^{+0.118}$ and a slight preference for a closed spatial geometry with $Ω_{k0} = -0.109_{-0.071}^{+0.076}$ at present time. Remarkably, the consideration of spatial curvature and diffusion naturally alleviates the Hubble tension, yielding $H_0 = 73.350_{-0.226}^{+0.221}$ km/s/Mpc while maintaining a consistent cosmic age of $t_0 \simeq 13.61$ Gyr. Furthermore, the constrained diffusion scales as a stable, quintessence-like effective dark energy ($ω_{\text{eff}} \simeq -0.832$). Thus, unimodular diffusion provides a thermodynamically consistent phenomenological alternative that can alleviate the Hubble tension while preserving both the cosmic age and the sound-horizon scale, with a preference for a closed spatial geometry.

We established physical bounds for the non-canonical parameter $α$. To obtain precise parameter constraints, we solved the primordial perturbation equations numerically and conducted a rigorous MCMC analysis by using a comprehensive joint P-ACT-LB-BK18 dataset. Abstract: In this paper, we investigate background-hierarchy bounds in Type~3 of New General Relativity (NGR). We then revisit the perturbative analysis of Type~3 and show that the propagating modes are correctly identified even when the perturbed Lagrangian is not written solely in terms of gauge-invariant variables.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在短距离尺度上对引力平方反比定律（gravitational inverse-square law）进行实验约束，是检验广义相对论（general relativity）及其扩展理论（如额外维模型）的关键手段。现有实验与理论模型之间缺乏统一比较框架，需要一套一致的形式论（consistent formalism）来整合不同尺度下的实验结果。

Method: 采用一致的形式论（consistent formalism）分析短距离引力实验数据，并引入多种模型参数化（model parametrizations）方案，包括额外维模型（extra-dimensional models）；同时将桌面实验结果与高能对撞机实验结果进行对比，分别针对汤川势（Yukawa potential）和幂律势（power-law potential）两种势函数形式。

Result: 提供了过去十年引力平方反比定律实验约束的全面更新，建立了不同实验与理论模型之间的直接比较框架，并展示了桌面实验与高能对撞机实验在汤川势（Yukawa potential）和幂律势（power-law potential）两种情形下的对比结果。

Conclusion: 该工作为短距离引力实验提供了统一的分析框架，促进了实验结果与扩展广义相对论的理论模型之间的直接比较，有助于未来更精确地检验引力平方反比定律（gravitational inverse-square law）及其可能的修正。

Abstract: Experimental constraints on the gravitational inverse-square law at short range are presented, employing a consistent formalism across a wide range of length scales. We provide comprehensive updates from the past decade, building upon our previous review. This work facilitates the direct comparison of experimental results with theoretical models that extend general relativity. Furthermore, a comparison between various model parametrizations, including extra-dimensional models, is introduced. Finally, results from tabletop experiments are compared with those from high-energy collider experiments for both Yukawa and power-law potentials.

Abstract: We investigate the warm inflationary scenario in the Weyl geometric gravity theory, in which the action is constructed by adding matter to the simplest conformally invariant gravitational action in Weyl geometry. The $\tilde{R}^2$ theory can be formulated equivalently as a linear theory supplemented by an additional scalar degree of freedom originating from higher-order curvature terms, with the equations of motion obtained via variational methods. We investigate the cosmological implications of the theory by considering the warm inflationary scenario of the early evolution of the Universe, in which radiation, the inflaton field, and the Weyl vector coexist. We consider the widely studied linear dissipation coefficient model along with a quartic potential, and investigate the influence of the Weyl vector term on the dynamics. We have performed numerical computations for different coupling models, and we have successfully developed a warm inflationary model in which the Universe transitions naturally from an inflationary epoch to a radiation-dominated era. The relevant cosmological observables have been calculated and compared with the latest observational constraints from the ACT data.

### [208] [Boson Stars surrounded by Polish Doughnuts in Scalar-Tensor Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17078)

Method: 采用恒定比角动量（constant specific angular momentum）的平衡模型，在参数空间中对吸积盘结构进行系统性分析，并对比广义相对论与标量化构型之间的相变行为。

Abstract: We investigate thick accretion disks (Polish Doughnuts) around rotating self-interacting boson stars in general relativity and scalar-tensor theories, focusing on spontaneously scalarized solutions and their general relativistic counterparts. Using equilibrium models with constant specific angular momentum, we analyze disk structures across the parameter space, with emphasis on the phase transition between GR and scalarized configurations. We find that scalarization induces qualitative changes in the spacetime that significantly affect disk morphology. In particular, scalarized boson stars can lack innermost circular orbits, allowing stable motion down to the center and enabling highly compact, quasi-spherical disks. For the most massive scalarized solutions, a non-monotonic angular momentum profile further permits two-centered disk configurations connected by a cusp. Overall, disks around scalarized boson stars are more compact and more strongly bound than those in general relativity, highlighting distinctive features that may serve as observational signatures of alternative gravity theories in the strong-field regime.

Abstract: We study the Joule-Thomson expansion and extended thermodynamics of a modified black hole characterised by the parameters $α$, $β$, and $σ$. The deformation parameter $α$ and control parameter $β$ shift the temperature minimum, enlarge the cooling region, and raise the inversion temperature, while $σ$ produces a weaker but consistent influence. The heat-engine analysis reveals that $α$ enhances efficiency, whereas higher $β$ and $σ$ reduce it. Overall, the results demonstrate that geometric deformation and quintessence jointly govern the unified thermodynamic structure of the black hole.

### [210] [Dynamic Aspects of Bumblebee Gravity: Post-Newtonian Approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17516)
*Jie Zhu,Hao Li*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用参数化后牛顿方法（PPN方法）研究了大黄蜂引力（Bumblebee gravity）的动态特征，发现当耦合参数满足 λ = -ξ/2 时，PPN框架在1.5PN阶以内自洽，并导出了非零的优先框架效应参数 α₁、α₂ 及一个新奇的对数增长势 U_B，最终通过脉冲星计时观测给出了对称破缺参数的约束 |ℓ| ≲ 1.6×10⁻⁹。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大黄蜂引力作为一种洛伦兹对称性破缺（Lorentz symmetry breaking）的引力理论，其静态解已有较多研究，但动力学（dynamic）方面尚未充分探讨。本文旨在通过PPN方法系统分析该模型的动力学行为，并考察其与实验观测的一致性。

Method: 采用参数化后牛顿方法（parametrized post-Newtonian method, PPN method）对大黄蜂引力进行后牛顿展开分析，逐阶检查PPN框架的自洽性条件，并推导对称破缺参数的理论与观测约束。

Result: PPN框架自洽至1.5PN阶的条件为 λ = -ξ/2，即大黄蜂场 B_μ 与爱因斯坦张量（Einstein tensor）之间的直接耦合；快子稳定性（tachyonic stability）要求势函数满足 V''(0)=0。在该耦合条件下，PPN度规给出非零的优先框架参数 α₁ 和 α₂，并出现一个具有对数渐近增长行为的新PPN势 U_B。U_B 消失需附加约束 ξ = κ/2 或 V⁽³⁾(0)=0。在小 ℓ 极限下，α₂ ≈ -ℓ₂，结合脉冲星计时观测可得 |ℓ| ≲ 1.6×10⁻⁹。

Conclusion: 上述结果标志着该模型存在优先框架效应（preferred-frame effects），这是洛伦兹对称性破缺的直接后果。脉冲星计时数据对参数 ℓ 给出了数值上限，表明实验观测可有效约束大黄蜂引力模型中的对称破缺强度。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the dynamic aspects of Bumblebee gravity via the parameterized post-Newtonian method. We find that the PPN framework is self-consistent up to 1.5PN order if and only if $λ= -ξ/2$, which corresponds to a direct coupling between the Bumblebee field $B_μ$ and the Einstein tensor. The requirement of tachyonic stability restricts the Bumblebee potential to satisfy $V''(0)=0$. In the specific case where $λ= -ξ/2$, the resulting PPN metric yields non-vanishing values for the parameters $α_1$ and $α_2$, as well as a novel PPN potential $U_B$ that exhibits a logarithmic asymptotic growth. The vanishing of the potential $U_B$ necessitates the additional constraints $ξ= κ/2$ or $V^{(3)}(0) = 0$. These results signify the presence of preferred-frame effects, a direct consequence of the Lorentz symmetry breaking in the model. In the limit of small $\ell$, we obtain $α_2 \simeq -\ell_2$, which yields a constraint of $|\ell| \lesssim 1.6\times 10^{-9}$ based on pulsar timing observations.

</details>


### [211] [Impact of the axion-like self-interactions in gravitational atoms for LISA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17589)
*Samuel Gómez Gómez,Xisco Jimenez Forteza,Carlos Palenzuela Luque*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有自相互作用的超轻玻色子（如类轴子粒子）形成的致密晕（gravitational atoms）对极端及中等质量比旋近（EMRI/IMRI）引力波信号的影响。结果表明，LISA能够在信噪比≤100时区分嵌入此类晕的波形，并探测玻色子质量10⁻¹⁷–10⁻¹⁵ eV与衰变常数10¹⁰–3.2×10¹² GeV的参数空间，无需依赖标准模型耦合即可约束类轴子粒子性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超轻玻色子（ultralight bosons）若具有自相互作用，可在恒星或致密天体周围形成天体物理尺度的玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate），即“引力原子”（gravitational atoms）。本文旨在采用近期提出的动力学形成机制估算这类晕对极端及中等质量比旋近（extreme- and intermediate-mass-ratio inspirals）的影响，并评估LISA在区分波形和约束粒子参数方面的探测能力。

Method: 论文采用一种近期提出的动力学形成机制来模型化晕（halo）的形成，并将其嵌入主黑洞周围；随后计算极端及中等质量比并合双星在此类密度背景下的引力波形，分析由动力学摩擦（dynamical friction）导致的波形退相（dephasing），并与LISA的探测能力进行对比。

Result: 在信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio）≤100时，LISA能够区分嵌入此类晕致密背景中的引力波形；可探测玻色子质量m_dm∼10⁻¹⁷–10⁻¹⁵ eV、衰变常数f_a∼10¹⁰–3.2×10¹² GeV的参数空间，双星总质量M∼10⁴–10⁵ M⊙，暗物质密度取纳瓦罗-弗伦克-怀特（Navarro-Frenk-White, NFW）轮廓中心值。更高背景密度及不同极端质量比构型可进一步扩展可及参数空间。对于M∼10⁴ M⊙、ρ_dm=10³ GeV/cm³、信噪比∼20的构型，粒子质量m_dm∼2.5×10⁻¹⁶ eV与衰变常数f_a∼6.3×10¹⁰ GeV可使动力学摩擦导致的退相最大，从而以百分之一量级的精度恢复粒子参数。

Conclusion: LISA能够在不依赖类轴子粒子（axion-like particles）与标准模型（Standard Model）场额外的耦合条件下，直接对粒子质量及自相互作用强度（通过衰变常数表征）给出约束。这表明引力波观测为探测超轻暗物质粒子提供了一种独立于传统粒子物理实验的新途径。

Abstract: Ultralight bosons with self-interactions, such as axion-like particles, can form astrophysical Bose-Einstein condensates around stars or compact objects, often referred to as gravitational atoms. In this work, we adopt a recently proposed dynamical formation mechanism for these halos and estimate their impact on extreme- and intermediate-mass-ratio inspirals when present around the primary black hole. We show that, for signal-to-noise ratios $\lesssim 100$, LISA can distinguish gravitational waveforms from binaries embedded in such halo overdensities. Our analysis indicates that LISA can probe boson masses $m_\mathrm{dm}\sim10^{-17}$-$10^{-15}\,\mathrm{eV}$ and decay constants $f_a\sim10^{10}$-$3.2 \times 10^{12}\,\mathrm{GeV}$ using binaries with total masses $M\sim10^4$-$10^5\,M_\odot$, assuming conservative DM densities consistent with the central values of Navarro-Frenk-White profiles. Allowing for higher background densities and different extreme-mass-ratio configurations further extends the accessible parameter space. Moreover, we find that for a binary configuration with $M\sim10^4\,M_\odot$, $ρ_\mathrm{dm} = 10^3\,\mathrm{GeV/cm^3}$, and signal-to-noise ratio $\mathrm{SNR}\sim20$, a particle mass of $m_\mathrm{dm}\sim2.5\times10^{-16}\,\mathrm{eV}$ and decay constant $f_a\sim6.3\times10^{10}\,\mathrm{GeV}$ maximize the dephasing due to dynamical friction, enabling the recovery of the particle parameters at the percent level. These results demonstrate that LISA can place constraints on axion-like particle masses and self-interactions without requiring additional couplings to Standard Model fields.

### [212] [Junction Conditions and Gravitational Collapse in Scalar-Tensor-Vector Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17615)
*Debanjan Debnath,Anant Badal,Kaushik Bhattacharya*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文为标量-张量-矢量引力（STVG/MOG）推导了薄壳连接条件，并据此构建了引力坍缩理论。研究发现，在满足连接条件的情况下，引力坍缩可以在有限固有时内形成类Reissner-Nordström（RN）视界，并呈现了两种简化模型：一种坍缩成极端RN类黑洞，另一种趋向坍缩成次极端RN类黑洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为STVG/MOG理论建立严格的连接条件，并以此为基础研究引力坍缩过程，探讨在该修正引力理论中黑洞形成的可能性与特征。

Method: 从标准STVG作用量出发，推导了跨越边界面的连接条件，涉及各场量及其导数的匹配；将内部携带重子物质与暗能量的FLRW时空与外部静态球对称类RN时空通过携带STVG电荷的薄壳进行匹配。

Result: 利用匹配条件与坍缩壳的性质，证明引力坍缩可在当前设定下进行，且能在有限固有时内形成类RN视界；展示了两种简化模型：一种坍缩为极端RN类黑洞，另一种趋向坍缩为次极端RN类黑洞（对无穷远渐近观测者而言）。

Conclusion: STVG/MOG理论中引力坍缩可以产生类RN黑洞，视界形成在有限固有时内发生，且根据参数不同可走向极端或次极端情形。

Abstract: We formulate the junction conditions for Scalar-Tensor-Vector Gravity (STVG/MOG), proposed by J.~W.~Moffat. Using these conditions, the theory of gravitational collapse is constructed. In the collapsing process, an interior Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker (FLRW) spacetime with baryonic matter and dark energy is matched with an exterior static, spherically symmetric Reissner--Nordström (RN)-like spacetime through a shell that carries STVG-charge. Starting from the standard STVG action, we derive the junction conditions across a boundary that relate the values of the various field quantities and their derivatives across the matching surface. Using the matching conditions and the nature of the collapsing shell, it is shown that a gravitational collapse can proceed in the present situation, and one can have RN-like horizon formation in finite proper time. We present two simplified models of gravitational collapse in this article: one ends up as an extremal RN-like black hole, and the other tends to collapse towards a sub-extremal RN-like black hole, as observed by an asymptotic observer at an infinite distance away from the collapsing system.

### [214] [Positive Running of the Spectral Index for Scalar Theory and Modified Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17813)
*S. D. Odintsov,V. K. Oikonomou*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文探讨了宇宙暴涨（inflation）理论中谱指数跑动（running of the spectral index）为正的可能性。基于ACT数据及其他物理迹象，研究在最小耦合标量场引力和修正引力（modified gravity）框架下如何实现正谱指数跑动。结果表明，爱因斯坦-高斯-博内引力（Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet gravity）可较容易地产生正跑动并同时维持可行的暴涨时期，而标量场理论与F(R)引力则面临较大困难。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期ACT数据温和地指出谱指数跑动可能为正，且其他物理迹象也支持这一可能性。若未来宇宙微波背景（cosmic microwave background, CMB）实验确认正跑动，将排除许多流行的暴涨模型，因此有必要探索在何种理论框架下可实现正谱指数跑动。

Method: 研究在最小耦合标量场引力与修正引力两类框架下进行分析。修正引力选取两种源于弦论（string theory）的主流候选理论：F(R)引力（F(R) gravity）和爱因斯坦-高斯-博内引力（Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet gravity）。其中，爱因斯坦-高斯-博内模型还考虑了与引力波事件GW170817的兼容性条件。

Result: 标量场暴涨和F(R)引力暴涨在获得可行的暴涨机制时，难以得到正的谱指数跑动，因此这两类理论大多与Planck数据兼容。但精细调节的标量场场景可与ACT数据兼容并产生正跑动。在兼容GW170817事件的爱因斯坦-高斯-博内理论中，谱指数跑动可以容易地为正，同时保持可行的暴涨时期。

Conclusion: 正的谱指数跑动并非在所有暴涨理论中都能实现。标量场理论和F(R)引力在产生正跑动方面存在困难，而爱因斯坦-高斯-博内引力则提供了更自然实现正跑动的理论框架，提示未来CMB实验对谱指数跑动的测量可能有助于区分不同暴涨模型。

Abstract: In this work we address the possibility of having a positive running of the spectral index in inflationary theories. The recent ACT data indicate mildly that the running of the spectral index might be positive, and several other physical indications point out this possibility. If the running of the spectral index is confirmed to be positive by future cosmic microwave background experiments, this can rule out quite popular inflationary scenarios. We investigate how it is possible to obtain a positive running of the spectral index in the context of minimally coupled scalar field gravity and modified gravity. For the modified gravity we choose two mainstream and of string origin candidate theories, $F(R)$ gravity and Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet gravity. In the case of scalar field inflation and $F(R)$ gravity inflation, we demonstrate the difficulties for obtaining a positive running of the spectral index for a viable inflationary regime, so scalar theories and $F(R)$ gravity are mostly compatible with the Planck data. But nuanced scalar field scenarios can be compatible with the ACT data and produce a positive running of the spectral index. In the context of Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet theories which are compatible with the GW170817 event, the running of the spectral index can easily be positive while in parallel having a viable inflationary era.

### [215] [Pole Skipping, Avoided Crossing, and Resonant Excitation in Kerr Quasinormal Modes near Algebraically Special Frequencies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17840)
*Kei-ichiro Kubota,Hayato Motohash*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过追踪格林函数构建块（Green-function building blocks）在黎曼曲面（Riemann sheets）上的极点和零点，解释了Kerr拟正规模式（quasinormal modes）在代数特殊频率（algebraically special frequencies）附近长期令人困惑的异常行为：分叉（bifurcation）源于避免交叉（avoided crossing）伴随共振激发（resonant excitation），消失（disappearance）源于极点和零点相消导致的极点跳过（pole skipping）。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过在不同黎曼曲面上追踪格林函数构建块的极点和零点，分析拟正规模式极点与松原模式零点（Matsubara-mode zero）之间的相互作用机制。

Result: 发现分叉现象源于避免交叉并伴随共振激发；消失现象源于拟正规模式极点与松原模式零点相互抵消导致的极点跳过。

Conclusion: 成功解析了Kerr拟正规模式在代数特殊频率附近长期存在的异常行为的物理起源。

Abstract: Kerr quasinormal modes near algebraically special frequencies exhibit anomalous behavior, including apparent bifurcation, disappearance, and a nonsmooth connection to the Schwarzschild limit, which has remained puzzling for decades. Tracking poles and zeros of Green-function building blocks across different Riemann sheets, we show that the bifurcation is due to an avoided crossing accompanied by resonant excitation, while the disappearance is due to pole skipping caused by cancellation of a quasinormal-mode pole by a Matsubara-mode zero. This resolves the physical origin of these long-standing anomalies.

### [216] [The impact of seasonality over the sensitivity of Einstein Telescope and the SNR of CBC signals at the Sardinia candidate site](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18135)
*Matteo Di Giovanni,Davide Rozza,Giovanni Diaferia,Andrea Contu,Rosario De Rosa,Carlo Giunchi,Luca Naticchioni,Marco Olivieri,Annalisa Allocca,Enrico Calloni,Giovanni Luca Cardello,Luciano Errico,Giovanni Losurdo,Irene Molinari,Lucia Trozzo,Domenico D'Urso*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 撒丁岛站点的低地震噪声仅导致探测器灵敏度产生微小的季节性变化；即便未采用牛顿噪声抑制措施，信噪比受季节变化的影响也仅限于几个百分点。

Conclusion: 季节性环境波动对致密双星的早期可探测性影响较小，确认了撒丁岛候选址在实现ET低频灵敏度目标方面的适用性。

Abstract: This work investigates the impact of seasonal variations in seismic noise on the low-frequency performance of the Einstein Telescope (ET) at the Sardinia candidate site, focusing on implications for compact binary coalescence observations. Using seismic data collected between 2022 and 2025 in deep boreholes, we characterize monthly noise variations and identify representative best and worst case scenarios, corresponding to July and December. The measured seismic spectra are used to estimate the Newtonian noise contribution in the 2-10 Hz band and to derive modified ET sensitivity curves. These are implemented in a simulation framework to evaluate their effect on the signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) of binary neutron star and intermediate mass black hole signals, assuming the triangular ET configuration. We find that the low seismic noise of the Sardinia site results in only minor seasonal variations in detector sensitivity. The corresponding impact on SNR is limited to a few percent, even without including Newtonian noise mitigation. These results indicate that seasonal environmental fluctuation have a minor effect on the early inspired detectability of compact binaries, confirming the suitability of the Sardinia site for achieving ET low-frequency sensitivity goals.

### [217] [The Case for Astrons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18186)
*Claudio Corianò,Paul H. Frampton,Leonardo Torcellini*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文考察了一类名为“astrons”的原始带电致密天体（fiducial参数：质量~10¹²M⊙、电荷~4×10³² C、间距~Mpc量级），分析了电荷生成、吸积饱和、等离子体屏蔽、Reissner-Nordström与Kerr-Newman几何、透镜效应及Lyman-α吸收探测等议题。主要结论是：大电荷分支无法通过普通吸积饱和获得，且面临等离子体屏蔽、超极端荷质比导致的几何无光子球、以及均匀带电背景能量密度标度率a⁻⁴等严重约束，因此最简单的FLRW完美流体约化无法产生晚期宇宙加速膨胀。任何可行的宇宙学角色必须依赖于超出均匀近似的非均匀Einstein-Maxwell平均问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索一类假设存在的原始带电致密天体（astrons）是否可能具有宇宙学意义，并评估其理论自洽性与观测约束。

Method: 从理论上系统分析astrons的电荷生成机制、吸积饱和过程、在电离介质中的电荷持久性、等离子体屏蔽效应，以及Reissner-Nordström和Kerr-Newman几何框架下的极端荷质比行为；同时探讨透镜效应和Lyman-α吸收谱作为电场探测手段的可能性。

Result: 大电荷分支无法通过普通吸积饱和实现，需视为原始或早期宇宙的电荷集中假设；视界质量估计表明10¹²M⊙的原始天体出现在大爆炸后约数月，与JWST观测的早期结构仅能通过后期重子物质围绕暗种子（dark seeds）组装间接关联。主要约束包括：等离子体屏蔽与中性化问题、超极端（super-extremal）荷质比导致无Reissner-Nordström光子球、以及均匀带电背景的能量密度以a⁻⁴标度，无法产生晚期加速膨胀。

Conclusion: 最简单的FLRW完美流体约化无法让astrons产生晚期宇宙加速膨胀；任何可行的宇宙学角色必须通过受控的非均匀Einstein-Maxwell平均问题，超出均匀近似范围。

Abstract: We examine a proposed population of primordial, electrically charged compact objects, which we call astrons, with fiducial parameters \(M_A\sim10^{12}M_\odot\), \(Q_A\sim4\times10^{32}\,\mathrm{C}\), and megaparsec-scale separations. We analyze charge generation, ordinary accretion saturation, charge persistence in an ionized medium, plasma screening, the Reissner--Nordström and Kerr--Newman geometric regimes, lensing, and the possible use of Lyman-\(α\) absorption as a probe of astron electric fields, and the cosmological interpretation of a sparse charged population. The large-charge branch is not obtained from ordinary accretion saturation; it should be treated as a primordial or early-universe charge-concentration hypothesis. A horizon-mass estimate places a \(10^{12}M_\odot\) primordial object at times of order months after the Big Bang, so any relation to the early structures observed by the James Webb Space Telescope would be indirect, through later baryonic assembly around dark seeds. The main constraints are severe: plasma screening and neutralization must be avoided, the fiducial charge drives the exterior into a super-extremal regime without a Reissner--Nordström photon sphere, and the homogeneous interaction energy of a charged population scales as \(a^{-4}\). Thus the simplest FLRW perfect-fluid reduction does not generate asymptotic late-time acceleration. Any viable cosmological role for astrons must instead come from a controlled inhomogeneous Einstein--Maxwell averaging problem beyond the homogeneous approximation.

### [218] [Natural modification of quantum uncertainty, modified gravity, and cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18203)
*Christian G. Boehmer,Eissa Al-Nasrallah*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过宇宙学中的平直FLRW方程，将广义不确定性原理与修正引力理论联系起来，指出物理模型之间的“自然”扩展方式在不同框架下可能并不一致，并发现Born-Infeld模型是唯一在两种设定中都显得自然的模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物理学和数学中常见的一种方法是引入高阶项或其他非线性项来对理论进行“自然”扩展，但本文指出这种扩展方式需要谨慎对待，因为不同物理模型之间可能以间接方式相互关联，在一个框架中的自然扩展在另一个框架中可能并不自然。

Method: 利用宇宙学中的平直弗里德曼-勒梅特-罗伯逊-沃克（Friedmann-Lemaitre-Robertson-Walker, FLRW）方程，将广义不确定性原理（generalized uncertainty principle）与修正引力理论（modified theories of gravity）联系起来，通过比较同一扩展项在两个框架下的效果进行分析。

Result: 在一个框架中添加简单的额外项，在另一个框架中会导致巨大的复杂性；Born-Infeld模型是唯一在两种设定中都表现自然的模型。

Conclusion: 对于理论和框架的“自然”扩展必须谨慎对待，因为物理模型之间可能存在间接的、非直观的关联方式；Born-Infeld模型在两个不同设定下均保持自然性，具有特殊地位。

Abstract: A common approach in physics and mathematics is to extend and modify theories and frameworks by considering what is often described as a `natural' extension or modification by including higher-order terms or by introducing other non-linearities. We show that such an approach must be taken with care as physical models can be connected in indirect ways. What looks like a natural approach in one setting will likely not be natural in another. We use the flat Friedmann-Lemaitre-Robertson-Walker equations of cosmology to connect the generalized uncertainty principle to modified theories of gravity. A simple additional term in one setting leads to enormous complications in the other. We identify Born-Infeld models as the only ones which appear natural in both settings.

</details>


### [219] [Kerr-like black holes shadow surrounded by dark matter halos: Comparison between various dark matter profiles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18205)
*Malihe Heydari-Fard,Mohaddese Heydari-Fard*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文通过Newman-Janis算法，构建了浸没在King、Hernquist和Moore三种暗物质晕（dark matter halo）中的静态和旋转黑洞解，并系统研究了暗物质特征密度、特征半径及自旋参数对黑洞视界、能层和阴影半径的影响。结果表明，暗物质中旋转黑洞的阴影半径较克尔黑洞（Kerr black hole）有所增大，但不同暗物质晕轮廓（cuspy或cored）对阴影尺寸和形状的影响可忽略，因此黑洞阴影并非区分星系中心暗物质分布性质的有效工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来，浸没于各种暗物质晕（dark matter halo）轮廓中的静态与旋转黑洞阴影研究受到广泛关注。本文旨在系统探究暗物质特征密度、特征半径及自旋参数对黑洞内外视界（horizon）、能层（ergoregion）和阴影半径的影响，并与克尔黑洞（Kerr black hole）及其他暗物质轮廓进行比较。

Method: 考虑浸没在King、Hernquist和Moore三种暗物质晕（dark matter halo）轮廓中的静态黑洞解，采用Newman-Janis算法（Newman-Janis algorithm）推导对应的旋转黑洞解。

Result: 暗物质中旋转黑洞的阴影半径较无暗物质时的克尔黑洞（Kerr black hole）有所增大；但King、Hernquist、Moore三种暗物质晕（dark matter halo）轮廓，以及所有其他考虑的暗物质晕轮廓，对阴影尺寸和形状的影响均可忽略，且此结论与暗物质晕是尖峰型（cuspy）还是核球型（cored）无关。

Conclusion: 至少对于这类类克尔黑洞（Kerr-like black hole），黑洞阴影并非区分星系中心暗物质分布性质的合适工具。

Abstract: The study of shadows of static and rotating black holes immersed in various dark matter halo profiles has gained significant attention in recent years. In this paper, we consider the static black hole solution immersed in three dark matter halo profiles (King, Hernquist, and Moore) and, by using the Newman-Janis algorithm, obtain the corresponding rotating black hole solutions. The main goal of the paper is to study the influence of the characteristic density, characteristic radius, and the spin parameter on the inner and outer horizons, the ergoregion, and the shadow radius, and to compare the results with Kerr black holes and other dark matter profiles. Our findings indicate that the shadow radius of rotating black holes immersed in dark matter increases compared to that of the Kerr black hole in the absence of dark matter; however, the impact on the size and shape of the shadow is negligible for King, Hernquist, and Moore profiles, and for all other dark matter halo profiles considered, and is independent of whether the halo is cuspy or cored. Therefore, at least for these Kerr-like black holes, the black hole shadow is not a suitable tool for distinguishing the nature of the dark matter distribution in galactic centers.

### [220] [Quasinormal modes of a rotating loop quantum black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18249)
*Zhongzhinan Dong,Shulan Li,Dan Zhang,Jian-Pin Wu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文系统计算了有效旋转圈量子黑洞背景上无质量标量场的拟正则模，发现量子引力修正单调降低振荡频率与阻尼率，旋转效应引入非平凡调制并影响高阶泛音谱，为黑洞光谱学和引力波观测提供了理论基准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究旋转效应对圈量子引力（loop quantum gravity）修正黑洞的拟正则模（quasinormal modes）谱的影响，检验有效旋转度规是否保留圈量子引力的核心特征，并为未来黑洞光谱学（black hole spectroscopy）与引力波观测提供理论基准。

Method: 基于协变球模型通过改进的Newman–Janis算法构造有效旋转圈量子黑洞背景；采用连分数法（continued fraction method）计算无质量标量场的基模与泛音模频谱，系统分析频率对量子修正、自旋和扰动角结构的依赖关系。

Result: 量子引力修正使基模的振荡频率和阻尼率均单调下降，表明振荡减慢且衰减延长。旋转导致非平凡调制：球对称扰动下实频随自旋出现交叉，角动量开启后该特征被抑制；方位角分量进一步增大频率并更强地降低阻尼。泛音模中，旋转解保留了球对称情况的泛音爆发（overtone outbursts）与非单调演化特征，但向更弱的量子修正区域移动；非零轨道角动量抑制爆发，方位角自由度提升频率并引发高阶泛音间的新颖谱反转（spectral inversion）。

Conclusion: 有效旋转度精准捕捉了圈量子引力的关键特征，为黑洞拟正则模谱和引力波观测提供了明确的理论基准。

Abstract: We investigate the quasinormal modes of a massless scalar field on an effective rotating loop quantum black hole background, constructed from a covariant spherical model via an improved Newman-Janis algorithm. Using the continued fraction method, we compute the spectrum for both fundamental and overtone modes, and systematically analyze how the frequencies depend on the quantum correction, spin, and angular structure of the perturbation. For all fundamental modes, increasing the quantum gravity correction monotonically reduces both the oscillation frequency and the damping rate, signaling slower oscillations and prolonged decay. Rotation imprints a nontrivial modulation: for a spherically symmetric perturbation, the real frequency displays a crossover as the spin grows, whereas this feature is suppressed once angular momentum is turned on; further activating the azimuthal component enhances the frequency and reduces the damping even more strongly. In the overtone sector, the rotating solution retains the hallmark quantum gravitational signatures of the spherical case - overtone outbursts and non-monotonic evolution - with rotation shifting these phenomena to weaker quantum corrections. Nonzero orbital angular momentum suppresses the outbursts, while the azimuthal degree of freedom boosts the frequency, giving rise to novel spectral inversions among higher overtones. Our results confirm that the effective rotating metric captures essential loop quantum gravity features, providing clear theoretical benchmarks for black hole spectroscopy and future gravitational-wave observations.

</details>


### [221] [Dyonic Black Holes in Lorentz-Violating Gravity with a Background Kalb--Ramond Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18371)
*Yu-Xuan Lin,Jia-Zhou Liu,Yu-Xiao Liu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 论文通过在电磁场与Kalb-Ramond场之间引入非最小耦合，在带有背景Kalb-Ramond场的洛伦兹破缺引力中构造了一个精确的四维静态球对称双荷黑洞解，并系统研究了该解的几何性质、测地线运动、热力学及相变行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在洛伦兹破缺引力（Lorentz-violating gravity）背景下，现有研究中对于带有Kalb-Ramond场与电磁场耦合的黑洞解及其物理性质尚缺乏系统分析，尤其是双荷（dyonic）黑洞解的存在性与性质尚未被探索。

Method: 通过在Kalb-Ramond场与电磁场之间引入非最小耦合（nonminimal coupling），在带有背景Kalb-Ramond场的洛伦兹破缺引力框架下，构造了一个精确的四维静态球对称双荷黑洞解。随后分析了时空曲率不变量、零测地线（null geodesic）与类时测地线（timelike geodesic）运动，得到了光子球半径、阴影半径及最内稳定圆轨道（innermost stable circular orbit, ISCO）。在扩展相空间（extended phase space）中推导了热力学量，并验证了第一定律与Smarr关系。

Result: 曲率不变量显示时空在$r=0$处保留了一个真实的曲率奇点（curvature singularity）。洛伦兹破缺参数与双荷电荷均会显著改变黑洞阴影大小及稳定圆周运动的范围。系统满足黑洞热力学第一定律与Smarr关系，并展现出小黑洞与大黑洞之间的一级相变（first-order phase transition），其相结构受洛伦兹破缺参数和双荷电荷的强烈影响。

Conclusion: 该工作为洛伦兹破缺引力中的双荷黑洞解提供了完整的几何、动力学与热力学描述，揭示洛伦兹破缺参数与双荷电荷在阴影、稳定轨道及相变行为中的关键调控作用。

Abstract: By introducing a nonminimal coupling between the Kalb--Ramond field and the electromagnetic field, we construct an exact four-dimensional static, spherically symmetric dyonic black hole solution in Lorentz-violating gravity with a background Kalb--Ramond field. The curvature invariants show that the spacetime retains a genuine curvature singularity at $r=0$. We then analyze the geodesic motion of null and timelike particles and obtain the photon-sphere radius, the shadow radius, and the innermost stable circular orbit, demonstrating that both the Lorentz-violating parameter and the dyonic charges can appreciably modify the shadow size and the domain of stable circular motion. In the extended phase space, we derive the thermodynamic quantities and verify the first law of black hole thermodynamics together with the Smarr relation. The system also exhibits a first-order phase transition between small and large black holes, and its phase structure is strongly influenced by the Lorentz-violating parameter and the dyonic charges.

### [222] [Traversable Wormholes with Non-Exotic Matter: The Role of Higher Curvature Corrections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18376)
*M Daniel Ranjan,Soumya Chakrabarti,Sanjit Das*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在修正引力理论\(f(R,\Box R)\)中探索了可穿越虫洞（traversable wormhole）解，该理论包含里奇标量（Ricci scalar）\(R\)及其达朗贝尔算子项\(\Box R\)。研究发现，高阶导数修正可以有效贡献于应力-能量张量（stress-energy tensor），从而减少甚至消除虫洞喉部（throat）所需的奇异物质（exotic matter）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机来源于量子修正（quantum corrections）对广义相对论（general relativity）的推广需求。\(f(R,\Box R)\)模型自然拓展了可能引力几何的空间，本文旨在检验在该框架下可穿越虫洞是否存在，并理解高阶曲率项（higher-order curvature terms）在支持虫洞结构中所起的作用。

Method: 首先推导了静态球对称虫洞（static, spherically symmetric wormhole）的场方程（field equations），随后结合解析论证（analytical arguments）和数值方法（numerical methods）对其解进行研究。

Result: 高阶导数修正（higher-derivative corrections）能够有效贡献于应力-能量张量，从而减少虫洞喉部所需奇异物质的量，在某些情况下甚至可以完全消除对奇异物质的需求。

Conclusion: 该修正引力框架可以有效缓解甚至避免经典能量条件（classical energy conditions）的违反问题，为可穿越虫洞的存在提供了一种更自然的理论支持。

Abstract: In this paper, we explore wormhole solutions in a higher-derivative theory of gravity where the action depends not only on the Ricci scalar \(R\), but also on its d'Alembertian, \(\Box R\). Such \(f(R,\Box R)\) models are motivated by quantum corrections to general relativity and naturally extend the space of possible gravitational geometries. Our goal is to examine whether traversable wormholes can exist in this framework and to understand the role of higher-order curvature terms in supporting them. We derive the field equations for a static, spherically symmetric wormhole and study their solutions using both analytical arguments and numerical methods. Particular attention is given to the classical energy conditions, which are usually violated in wormhole physics. We find that the higher-derivative corrections can effectively contribute to the stress-energy tensor, reducing the amount of exotic matter required at the throat, and in some cases eliminating the need for it altogether.

### [223] [Rotating black holes with primary hair in five-dimensional generalized Proca theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17870)
*Mokhtar Hassaine,Ulises Hernandez-Vera*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在五维广义Proca理论中，通过Kerr-Schild拟设导出精确解析旋转黑洞解。该解包含宇宙学常数和两个独立角动量，具有非Killing角坐标的任意函数作为主毛发（primary hair），是Myers-Perry族的重要推广。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高维广义Proca理论中构造精确的解析旋转黑洞解，突破以往数值解或特殊解的局限，并探索矢量场毛发（vector hair）在黑洞几何中的存在性与结构。

Method: 采用Kerr-Schild拟设（Kerr-Schild ansatz），将Proca场置于类光测地线汇（null geodesic congruence）上，使得非线性场方程约化为三个主方程（master equations），并将理论的功能耦合（functional couplings）归结为离散常数，实现全解析处理。

Result: 得到包含宇宙学常数和两个独立角动量的精确解析旋转黑洞解，解具有由非Killing角坐标的任意函数给出的主毛发；存在多个由Proca耦合常数之间代数关系定义的解分支，显著推广了Myers-Perry族。度规形式保持与Myers-Perry表示相同的Kerr-Schild结构，并附加Proca单形（one-form）与其自身的张量积贡献。

Conclusion: 本工作首次在五维广义Proca理论中建立了精确解析旋转黑洞解族，证明了矢量毛发在高维旋转黑洞中的可解存在性，并为研究高维引力理论中的黑洞唯一性（uniqueness）和毛发定理（no-hair theorem）提供了新的检验平台。

Abstract: This work presents a new class of exact analytic rotating black hole solutions within five-dimensional generalized Proca theories. Through a Kerr-Schild ansatz where the Proca field is set along a null geodesic congruence, the non-linear field equations reduce to a consistent set of three master equations. This geometric configuration ensures that the vector field remains light-like on-shell, effectively restricting the theory's functional couplings to discrete constants and allowing for a fully analytic treatment. The resulting solutions, incorporating a cosmological constant and two independent angular momenta, exhibit primary hair given by an arbitrary function of the non-Killing angular coordinate. We identify several solution branches defined by specific algebraic relations between the Proca coupling constants, providing a significant generalization of the Myers-Perry family. Notably, the metric retains a Kerr-Schild form identical to the Myers-Perry representation, with an additional contribution constructed from the tensor product of the Proca one-form with itself.

### [224] [The problem of time: a path integral view](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17935)
*Juan Manuel Diaz,Alejandro Perez*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过路径积分（path integral）视角，论证了在无时间背景的非相对论性封闭量子系统中时间演化的涌现机制，并将其推广到广义协变量子理论（包括量子引力）。研究表明，所谓的“余弦问题”（cosine problem）——即跃迁振幅呈现 $\exp(iS/\hbar) + \exp(-iS/\hbar$ 的形式而非单一正向传播项——并非理论缺陷，而是时间反演不变性（time-reversal invariance）与时间中性边界态的自然结果。一旦识别出合适的时钟自由度并使其处于半经典“好时钟态”（good-clock state），时间箭头便会自发出现，选出正向传播的 $\exp(iS/\hbar)$ 项，无需修改基本动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无时间封闭量子系统中时间演化的涌现机制尚不清晰，尤其在广义协变理论（如圈量子引力中的自旋泡沫模型，spin foam representation）中，路径积分正则化出现“余弦问题”，导致一些研究者试图修改基本振幅以消除反向传播。本文旨在从路径积分角度阐明时间涌现的物理机制，并澄清余弦问题的根源。

Method: 以一个无时间非相对论性封闭量子系统作为广义协变量子理论的简化模型，采用路径积分表示（path integral representation）进行分析。将系统中的一个自由度识别为时钟，并使其处于半经典“好时钟态”，以此考察薛定谔演化（Schrödinger evolution）的涌现条件。

Result: 余弦问题并非路径积分正则化的病态特征，而是时间反演不变的基本动力学与时间中性边界态联合作用的自然结果。当合适的时钟系统被识别并放置于半经典好时钟态时，时间箭头自发涌现，选择出正向传播的 $\exp(iS/\hbar)$ 振幅。

Conclusion: 在合适的条件下时间能够涌现出来；在正则形式（canonical formulation）下，量子引力从根本上说是无时间的（timeless）。余弦问题无需通过修改基本振幅来解决，而是通过时钟系统的识别与半经典态的选择自然消解。

Abstract: We show that the emergence of time evolution in an otherwise timeless nonrelativistic closed quantum system -- viewed as a poor man's model of generally covariant quantum theory -- can be understood from the perspective of the path integral representation. As often happens in the functional integral approach, this viewpoint offers a more intuitive account of features that become cumbersome in the operator/Hilbert-space formulation. We show how Schrödinger evolution emerges once a clock degree of freedom is identified and placed in a suitable semiclassical `good-clock state'.
  Our analysis has a consequence that extends to path integral formulations of generally covariant systems with action $S$ (including gravity). In such theories certain transition amplitudes take the form $\exp(iS/\hbar)+\exp(-iS/\hbar)$ rather than the expected `forward propagating' $\exp(iS/\hbar)$. This feature, known as the {\em cosine problem}, appears in concrete regularizations of the path integral, for example in the spin foam representation defining the physical inner product between spin network states in loop quantum gravity. Both formally and in explicit regularizations, this apparent difficulty has led some authors to seek modifications of the basic amplitudes to eliminate backward propagation.
  Our model shows that the cosine problem is instead a natural consequence of time-reversal invariance of the fundamental dynamics together with the time-neutral boundary states commonly used in transition amplitudes. When a suitable clock system is identified and placed in a semiclassical `good-clock state', it introduces a time arrow selecting the `forward propagating' $\exp(iS/\hbar)$, without modifying the fundamental dynamics.
  The analysis clarifies how time emerges under suitable conditions and emphasizes that, in the canonical formulation, quantum gravity is fundamentally timeless.

</details>


### [225] [Scalar$-$Tensor Gravity as a Probe of Generalized Black Hole Entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18551)
*Hussain Gohar*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过建立广义黑洞熵泛函与 Misner-Sharp 准局域质量及标量-张量引力理论中 Wald Noether 电荷熵之间的几何对应关系，导出各熵模型对应的 Einstein 框架标量势，并在宇宙学与观测约束下验证了该框架的统一性与可检验性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 信息论熵提案（如 Barrow 熵、Tsallis-Cirto 熵）与引力场论之间缺乏统一且具备几何基础的连接机制，现有研究多为分离模型，尚未建立从熵泛函到有效引力理论的系统性映射。

Method: 将广义黑洞熵泛函与标量-张量引力（scalar-tensor theories of gravity）中的 Misner-Sharp 准局域质量（quasilocal mass）和 Wald Noether 电荷熵（Noether-charge entropy）建立直接对应关系，导出标度依赖的有效引力耦合（scale-dependent effective gravitational coupling），并由此推导各熵模型对应的 Einstein 框架标量势（Einstein-frame scalar potential）。

Result: Barrow 熵对应陡峭指数势；Tsallis-Cirto 熵由非广延参数（nonextensivity parameter）控制指数势；量子引力与纠缠诱导修正对应近似线性势。这些势在宇宙学中产生特征性现象学，且框架兼容太阳系测试、大爆炸核合成（big-bang nucleosynthesis）及脉冲星计时（pulsar-timing）观测的现有约束。

Conclusion: 该分析在信息论熵提案与引力场论之间建立了统一且基于几何基础的联系，给出的预测可由未来观测调查检验，为广义熵引力模型的系统性研究提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We develop a geometric realization of a broad class of generalized black hole entropy functionals by establishing their direct correspondence with the Misner$-$Sharp quasilocal mass and the Wald Noether$-$charge entropy in scalar$-$tensor theories of gravity. The resulting models feature a scale-dependent effective gravitational coupling, whose functional dependence is determined by the underlying entropy parameters. Within this framework, we derive explicit Einstein-frame scalar potentials: for Barrow entropy, a steep exponential potential; for Tsallis$-$Cirto entropy, an exponential potential governed by the nonextensivity parameter; and for quantum-gravity and entanglement$-$induced corrections, an approximately linear potential. These distinct potentials generate characteristic cosmological phenomenology, with implications for inflationary dynamics, late-time dark-energy behavior, and non-singular bouncing cosmologies. The framework is compatible with current constraints from solar-system tests, big-bang nucleosynthesis, and pulsar-timing observations, and it yields predictions that can be probed by forthcoming observational surveys. In this way, the analysis establishes a unified and geometrically grounded connection between information$-$theoretic entropy proposals and gravitational field theory.

</details>


### [226] [Emergent Thiemann coherent states in the near-kernel sector of quantum reduced loop gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18625)
*Ilkka Mäkinen,Hanno Sahlmann,Waleed Sherif*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文采用变分蒙特卡洛方法（variational Monte Carlo）结合神经量子态（neural quantum states），对量子约化圈引力（quantum reduced loop gravity）单顶点模型中哈密顿约束算符的近核子区（near-kernel sector）进行了系统性研究。在自旋截断高达$j_{\mathrm{max}}=1001$的截断希尔伯特空间中，通过最小化正二次算符$\hat{\mathcal Q}=\hat C \hat C^\dagger$，发现近核态可分为三类：低截断下的非因子化解，以及两种高截断下的因子化分支，其中一种分支与约化Thiemann相干态（reduced Thiemann coherent states）以近单位保真度相匹配，表明近核子区涌现出半经典组织化结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子约化圈引力中，哈密顿约束算符近核子区的结构尚不清晰，尤其是在包含欧几里得项（Euclidean term）和洛伦兹项（Lorentzian term）的对称哈密顿量作用下，如何从量子态中识别出具有半经典（semiclassical）行为的解是一个关键问题。

Method: 采用变分蒙特卡洛方法（variational Monte Carlo）结合神经量子态（neural quantum states），在自旋截断（spin cutoff）高达$j_{\mathrm{max}}=1001$的截断希尔伯特空间中对正二次算符$\hat{\mathcal Q}=\hat C \hat C^\dagger$进行变分极小化，系统研究近核子区的结构。

Result: 近核态可分为三类：低截断下不跨三个边自由度因子化的解；高截断下的两种因子化分支，均由单边波函数（one-edge wavefunctions）的乘积以极高精度描述，但局域于不同自旋区域。其中一支与约化Thiemann相干态（reduced Thiemann coherent states）以近单位保真度精确匹配，另一支虽高度因子化但因子的单边波函数不能由同一相干态族描述。

Conclusion: 因子化分支的发现，特别是与约化Thiemann相干态的高度匹配，为近核子区的半经典组织化涌现提供了直接证据。

Abstract: We study the near-kernel sector of the Hamiltonian constraint operator in the one-vertex model of quantum reduced loop gravity using variational Monte Carlo methods with neural quantum states. The analysis is based on the symmetric Hamiltonian containing both Euclidean and Lorentzian contributions, and on the variational minimization of the positive quadratic operator $\hat{\mathcal Q}=\hat C \hat C^\dagger$ in truncated Hilbert spaces with spin cutoff up to $j_{\mathrm{max}}=1001$. The resulting near-kernel states are found to organize into three qualitatively distinct classes. At low cutoffs, we find solutions that do not factorize across the three edge degrees of freedom. At larger cutoffs, we find two different factorized branches, both described to very high accuracy by products of one-edge wavefunctions but localized in different spin regimes. One of these branches is matched with near-unit fidelity by reduced Thiemann coherent states, providing evidence for an emergent semiclassical organization of the near-kernel sector. The other is likewise strongly factorized, but its one-edge factors are not well described by the same coherent-state family.

### [227] [Exact classical emergence from high-energy quantum superpositions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.16518)
*Juan A. Cañas,Daniel A. Bonilla,J. Bernal,A. Martín-Ruiz*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于完全解析的傅里叶方法，研究无限深方势阱中高能本征态等概率叠加的对应原理。通过推导量子傅里叶系数的几何级数展开，获得干涉项闭式渐近表达式，证明总概率密度和位置期望值在宏观极限下精确收敛到经典均匀分布和三角轨迹，边界层残余量子偏差在宏观分辨率下可忽略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为孤立束缚系统在静态与动态情境下严格实现经典极限（classical limit）提供解析层面的渐近证明，弥补现有对应原理问题中解析量化分析的不足。

Method: 采用完全解析的傅里叶方法（Fourier-based approach），将干涉项展开为量子傅里叶系数（quantum Fourier coefficients）的几何级数，推导出闭式渐近表达式，并分析其在$n\to\infty$及叠加态数目$\Delta\to\infty$时的收敛行为。

Result: 干涉项表现为功能包络线（functional envelopes），在单个能级渐近极限下不消失但彼此渐近等价；叠加$2\Delta+1$个态的总概率密度在$\Delta\to\infty$时精确收敛到均匀经典分布（uniform classical distribution）；位置期望值渐近复现经典三角轨迹（triangular trajectory）；残余量子偏差被限制在边界层（boundary layers）内，其相对宽度在宏观分辨率下趋于零。

Conclusion: 该工作为孤立束缚系统在静态和动态情境下建立了经典极限的严格渐近实现，证明宏观条件下量子力学与经典力学的一致性。

Abstract: We examine the correspondence principle for an equiprobable superposition of high-energy eigenstates of the infinite square well using a fully analytical Fourier-based approach. We derive a closed-form asymptotic expression for the interference terms $ρ_α^{\text{a}}(x)$ by expanding them into a geometric series of quantum Fourier coefficients. We show these terms act as functional envelopes that do not vanish individually but become asymptotically equivalent in the large-$n$ limit. Furthermore, we prove the total probability density for a superposition of $2Δ+1$ states converges exactly to the uniform classical distribution as $Δ\to \infty$. Dynamically, the expectation value of position reproduces the classical triangular trajectory asymptotically. Residual quantum deviations remain confined to boundary layers whose relative width vanishes under macroscopic resolution. These results establish a rigorous asymptotic realization of the classical limit for isolated bound systems in both static and dynamical contexts.

### [228] [Quantum Error Correction Assisted Axion Search in CMOS Spin Qubit Arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17457)
*Xiangjun Tan,Zhanning Wang*

TL;DR: 本文提出利用量子纠错（quantum error correction, QEC）来抑制固态自旋量子比特中的纵向退相位噪声，从而显著提升轴子（axion）暗物质搜索的灵敏度；通过引入最优重复码QEC与逻辑GHZ纠缠，推导出包含轴子场有限相干时间的量子Fisher信息闭式表达式，表明适度的QEC周期频率即可降低有效退相位率、恢复纠缠增强传感对标准量子极限的超越；在CMOS兼容器件参数下，QEC保护的纠缠传感可使轴子-电子耦合灵敏度提升一个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于固态自旋量子比特（solid-state spin qubits）的轴子与类轴子暗物质搜索受到纵向退相位（longitudinal dephasing）的严重限制，该噪声会迅速抑制纠缠带来的灵敏度增益。

Method: 将最优选择的重复码（repetition code）QEC与逻辑GHZ块纠缠（logical GHZ block entanglement）相结合，推导出显式包含轴子场有限相干时间（finite coherence time）的量子Fisher信息（quantum Fisher information）闭式表达式。

Result: 适度的QEC周期频率即可显著降低有效退相位率（effective dephasing rate），恢复纠缠增强传感对标准量子极限（standard quantum limit, SQL）的超越；在CMOS兼容器件参数下，QEC保护的纠缠传感可将轴子-电子耦合（axion-electron coupling $g_{ae}$）的灵敏度提升至一个数量级。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一条切实可行、理论上可控的路径，利用QEC改善量子比特阵列对标准模型之外物理（physics beyond the Standard Model）的搜索能力。

Abstract: Searches for axion and axionlike dark matter based on solid-state spin qubits are fundamentally limited by strong longitudinal dephasing, which rapidly suppresses the sensitivity gains offered by entanglement. Here we show that quantum error correction (QEC) can substantially enhance axion search sensitivity in realistic semiconductor spin qubit platforms by mitigating this dominant noise source. By integrating an optimally chosen repetition code QEC with logical GHZ block entanglement, we derive closed-form expressions for the quantum Fisher information that explicitly incorporate the finite coherence time of the axion field. Our analysis demonstrates that modest QEC cycle frequencies are sufficient to significantly reduce the effective dephasing rate, thereby restoring a broad parameter regime in which entanglement-enhanced sensing surpasses the standard quantum limit. Projecting these results onto CMOS-compatible device parameters, we find that QEC-protected entangled sensing can revive otherwise inaccessible quantum advantages, yielding up to order-of-magnitude improvements in sensitivity to the axion-electron coupling $g_{ae}$. These results establish a practical and theoretically controlled pathway for using QEC to improve qubit array searches for physics beyond the Standard Model.

</details>


### [229] [Exact nonequilibrium steady states of boundary driven circuit with XYZ gates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17018)
*Xin Zhang,Tomaz Prosen,Vladislav Popkov*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 通过空间非均匀矩阵乘积态（matrix product Ansatz）精确求解了边界驱动XXZ量子电路的多体密度算符，发现了一族相对鲁棒的可分离手性非平衡稳态（NESS），这些稳态是电路的自旋螺旋（spin helix）的椭圆类比，具有实验可观测性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 获取边界驱动量子电路的精确多体密度算符解，特别是针对XXZ相互作用体系，并探索其中可能存在的非平衡稳态及其实验可行性。

Method: 采用形式上的无限键维（infinite bond-dimension）空间非均匀矩阵乘积态Ansatz，结合边界量子比特与复位量子信道（reset quantum channels）的耦合，将边界位点投影到任意纯靶态。

Result: 发现并描述了一族相对鲁棒的可分离手性非平衡稳态（separable chiral nonequilibrium steady states, NESS），这些稳态是电路自旋螺旋的椭圆类比（elliptic analogs of spin helices）。

Conclusion: 该家族的非平衡稳态具有实验可观性（experimentally observable），为边界驱动量子电路中的稳态操控和量子模拟提供了可行方案。

Abstract: We obtain the exact many-body density operator of a boundary-driven XXZ quantum circuit via a spatially inhomogeneous matrix product Ansatz. The Ansatz has formally infinite bond-dimension and generalizes authors' previous construction \cite{2025XXZcircuit} for the XXZ interactions. The boundary qubits are coupled to reset quantum channels that project them toward arbitrary pure target states. We find and describe a family of relatively robust separable chiral nonequilibrium steady states (NESS), which are elliptic analogs of spin helices for the circuit, and which
  are particularly attractive from an experimental perspective.

### [230] [Stable minimum principles for scattering states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17139)
*Scott Lawrence,Yukari Yamauchi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对量子力学散射态（scattering states）提出了一系列稳定的最小原理（minimum principles），能够对非相对论性S矩阵（S-matrix）进行数值计算，并给出了近似解与真实解之间的有界差异估计，适用于动量相关势、长程库仑相互作用以及束缚态的弹性与非弹性散射。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 散射态的数值计算在传统上具有挑战性，尤其是需要满足特定的边界条件以获得S矩阵。为此，作者希望建立一类鲁棒的最小原理，为数值算法提供理论支撑与误差控制。

Method: 提出一个家族性的稳定最小原理，用于构造近似散射态；并通过理论分析证明满足这些原理的近似态与真实散射态之间的差是有界的，从而给出稳定性估计（stability estimates）。

Result: 这些最小原理和稳定性估计可用于获得散射振幅（scattering amplitudes）的严格界限；该方法适用于动量依赖势、长程（库仑）相互作用以及束缚态的弹性或非弹性散射场景。

Conclusion: 所提出的最小原理框架为量子散射态的数值计算提供了理论严谨且应用广泛的工具，尤其对未来非相对论性S矩阵的数值算法具有重要指导意义。

Abstract: Quantum-mechanical scattering states are energy eigenstates obeying particular boundary conditions, whose behavior at infinity encodes the S-matrix which defines the outcoming of scattering experiments. With an eye toward numerical algorithms for computing nonrelativistic S-matrices, we present a family of stable minimum principles for scattering states. States that approximately satisfy these minimum principles are shown to have a bounded difference with the true scattering states. These minimum principles and stability estimates can be used to obtain rigorous bounds on scattering amplitudes. We show that these minimum principles are applicable to momentum-dependent potentials, long-range (Coulomb) interactions, and elastic or inelastic scattering of bound states.

### [231] [Quantum--Fluid Correspondence for Systems of Nonrelativistic Spin-$\frac{1}{2}$ Particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18247)
*Naoki Sato,Michio Yamada*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明带有自旋自由度的荷电流体自然满足非相对论性自旋-1/2粒子的泡利方程 (Pauli equation)，且 n 个此类相互作用流体的集合可重构为 3n 维欧拉流 (Euler flow)，从而将马德隆-量子流体力学图景 (Madelung/quantum-hydrodynamic picture) 推广到多粒子量子系统，并暗示 n 量子比特量子计算机原则上可由 n 个流体的组合或等价的 3n 维欧拉流实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将量子力学的流体力学诠释从单粒子无自旋系统（如马德隆方程）推广到包含自旋自由度的多粒子系统，为量子动力学提供更丰富的经典流体力学表示。

Method: 通过分析带有内禀自旋（internal spin degree of freedom）的荷电流体的动力学方程，证明其与泡利方程在非相对论自旋-1/2粒子情形下的等价性；进一步将 n 个相互作用流体的系统重新表述为 3n 维空间中的欧拉流。

Result: 荷电旋性流体自然导出泡利方程；n 粒子泡利系统对应 3n 维欧拉流；n 量子比特量子计算机原则上可由 n 个流体的组合或 3n 维欧拉流实现。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了流体力学与多粒子量子力学（含自旋）之间的形式对应关系，为量子计算提供了一种基于经典流体或高维欧拉流的替代实现路径。

Abstract: We show that a charged fluid endowed with an internal spin degree of freedom naturally satisfies the Pauli equation for a nonrelativistic spin-1/2 particle, and that a collection of n such interacting fluids can be reformulated as an Euler flow in 3n dimensions, thereby providing a natural representation of a system of n Pauli particles. These results provide a fluid-mechanical derivation of the Pauli equation and extend the Madelung, or quantum-hydrodynamic, picture to many-particle quantum systems. In particular, they imply that an n-qubit quantum computer can, at least in principle, be realized as a suitable combination of n fluids, or equivalently as a 3n-dimensional Euler flow.

### [232] [Emergent supersymmetry in a time-space inverted quantum mechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.17507)
*Marcus W Beims,Arlans JS de Lara*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文发现时间-空间反转量子力学（TSI QM）框架内在地具有超对称结构，通过将算符 $\hat{\mathcal{P}}^{\pm}$（称为动量算符（Momentunian））的平方根结构进行因式分解，直接导出了包含超荷（supercharges）和伙伴哈密顿量（partner Hamiltonians）的超对称代数。研究表明，超对称性在TSI QM中是作为结构属性自然涌现的，而非人为附加的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索时间-空间反转量子力学（time space inverted QM）框架中是否存在内禀的超对称结构，并检验这种超对称性是否源于理论自身的数学结构而非外部引入。

Method: 将TSI QM中生成空间演化的算符 $\hat{\mathcal{P}}^{\pm}$（命名为动量算符（Momentunian））的平方根结构进行因式分解，从而建立超对称代数（supersymmetric algebra），并分析其中零模态（zero-mode states）的性质。

Result: 因式分解直接导出包含超荷（supercharges）和伙伴哈密顿量（partner Hamiltonians）的超对称代数。相对论性动量算符的零模态为瞬衰态（evanescent states），与物理势无关。非相对论与相对论性动量算符的伙伴算符的零模态不再是零能态，而是零动量态。TSI QM中自然出现的1/2阶分数时间导数使超荷将记忆效应（memory effects）引入超对称波函数。

Conclusion: 超对称性在时间-空间反转量子力学中是一种结构属性，内在地涌现于理论框架之中，而非通过唯象方式施加的。

Abstract: This Letter shows that a supersymmetric structure is inherent to the time space inverted (TSI) quantum mechanics (QM) framework, where the spatial evolution of states is generated by the operator $\hat{\mathcal{P}}^{\pm}(\hat{\mathcal{H}},\hat t;q)=\pm\sqrt{2m[\hat{\mathcal{H}}-\mathcal{\hat V}(q)]}$ [\href{https://doi.org/10.1103/PhysRevA.95.032133}{Phys. Rev. A. {\bf 95}, 032133 (2017)}], named here Momentunian, whose square-root structure that can be factorized. Such factorization leads directly to a supersymmetric algebra with supercharges and partner Hamiltonians. For the relativistic Momentunian the zero mode states are shown to be evanescent states, \textit{independent} of the physical potential. Furthermore, the existence of non-relativistic and relativistic Momentunian \textit{partners} is demonstrated, whose zero-mode states are no longer necessarily zero energies, but vanishing momenta states. The natural emergence of the $1/2$-fractional time derivatives in the TSI QM, leads to supercharges which incorporate memory effects into the supersymmetric wave functions. Results indicate that supersymmetry emerges as a structural property of the TSI QM rather than being imposed phenomenologically.

</details>


### [233] [Krylov complexity and fidelity susceptibility in two-band Hamiltonians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18594)
*Rishav Chaudhuri,Ayush Raj,Soham Ray,Sai Satyam Samal*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了两带哈密顿量（two-band Hamiltonians）基态的Krylov扩散复杂度（Krylov spread complexity），给出了基于布洛赫球面（Bloch sphere）几何量的纯几何计算公式，并揭示了该复杂度导数在拓扑相变点的对数发散行为及其与保真度磁化率（fidelity susceptibility）的界限关系，同时在SSH模型中发现了非幺正对偶性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索基态Krylov扩散复杂度在拓扑系统中的行为，特别是其能否作为拓扑相变（topological phase transition）的诊断工具，并挖掘其与已有量子信息量（如保真度磁化率）之间的内在联系。

Method: 利用布洛赫球面上的几何量（geometric formulation）直接计算两带哈密顿量基态的Krylov扩散复杂度，避免了构造电路哈密顿量（circuit Hamiltonian）；通过数值分析SSH模型和解析推导大质量狄拉克哈密顿量（massive Dirac Hamiltonian）来验证复杂度导数的发散行为及边界关系。

Result: 在SSH模型中，对于一般参考态，Krylov扩散复杂度的导数在拓扑相变点呈对数发散；复杂度导数的上界由保真度磁化率给出，该界限适用于任意能隙闭合（gap closing）情形（包括拓扑和非拓扑）。大质量狄拉克哈密顿量在平凡能隙闭合时也验证了这一界限关系。此外，在SSH模型中发现了拓扑相（topological phase）与平凡相（trivial phase）之间的非幺正对偶性（non-unitary duality），该对偶性同时体现在扩散复杂度和保真度磁化率中。

Conclusion: Krylov扩散复杂度的导数可灵敏地探测任何能隙闭合事件，但其发散本身并非拓扑相变的充分条件；该量与保真度磁化率之间的有界关系表明两者在探测量子相变方面具有互补性。SSH模型中的非幺正对偶性进一步揭示了扩散复杂度与拓扑结构之间的深层联系。

Abstract: We investigate Krylov spread complexity for the ground state of two-band Hamiltonians, where the reference state is a generic state on the Bloch sphere. The spread complexity is obtained by using a purely geometric formulation in terms of Bloch sphere data without constructing the circuit Hamiltonian. For generic reference states, the derivative of the spread complexity is logarithmically divergent at the topological phase transition in the Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) model. We demonstrate that the derivative of the spread complexity is bounded by fidelity susceptibility for general two-band models, indicating the sensitivity of the spread complexity to any gap closing (topological or trivial). This is illustrated in the massive Dirac Hamiltonian with a trivial gap closing. Finally, we introduce a non-unitary duality in the SSH model between the topological and trivial phases, which manifests itself in the spread complexity and fidelity susceptibility.

</details>
